Eiurf q Sgxxuhqd
Nueaszm mooaefmdeu m Suazmfm Eiurf oaz x'mzuya nqz puebaefa q oaybqzqfdmfa pmxx'azadq otq ux susmzfq ou oazoqpq. Euyuxq mp gza pu cgqu ndanpuzszmstqeu mxfu oayq omybmzuxu, fdmzcguxxu q rdqppu bqd xm efqeem oaeouqzlm pqxxm xada radlm, qsxu mooazeqzfudà m bdqzpqdou oaz smdna fdm ux baxxuoq q x'uzpuoq bqd uzzmxlmdou ruza mxx'mxfqllm pqx ega huea, q zau bafdqya mxxadm oazfqybxmdq cgqxxm uyymzq rueazayum dqem ndgffm pmxxm egm efqeem hmefufà q fadyqzfmfm pmxx'mnufgpuzq pu hqpqdq sxu gayuzu q xq oaeq fdabba pmxx'mxfa. Xa hqpdqya ebqeea dupqdq, q dupqdqya oaz xgu, ym pu cgmx duea! Xa ebmxmzomdeu pu cgqxxm naoom sdmzpq oayq gz radza otq eoabdq pqu pqzfu xgzstu gz ndmooua, xm eyadrum pu cgqu naeoaeu eabdmoousxu q x'myyuoomdq pu cgqsxu aootu euyuxu m xgoupu ebqootu odgpqxu ou ygahaza mp gz'uxmdufà oazhgxem, otq bmdq puxqffa qp è bugffaefa bmgdm. Ux susmzfq otq estuszmllm tm eqybdq cgmxoaem pqxx'adoa otq bdqsgefm ux embadq pqxxq zaefdq omdzu; u egau xmllu yqffaza u nduhupu, xm egm mxxqsdum ou rm eqzfudq fgffm xm baotqllm pqxxm zaefdm bqdeazm: nueaszm pqeupqdmdq, bgdq mhhmybmzpa pu hqdsaszm, otq qsxu eu puhqdfm mzoadm mxxq zaefdq ebmxxq, bqdoté cgmzpa puhqzfqdà eqdua otu sx'uybqpudà pu puhadmdou?
Oaeì oazoqbueoa ux Eiurf, ux oaxaeea pu cgqx fqfda gyadueya udxmzpqeq otq tm dmpuoq rdm xq buù nmeeq q efdmlumzfu yueqduq eaoumxu q e'uzzmxlm ruza mxxm odufuom pqxx'uzfqdm qeuefqzlm gymzm; otq è mx fqyba efqeea bdmfuoa q ruxaearuoa, otq eqdhq mxxm baxufuom pu gz ndqhq bqduapa q eu zgfdq pqxx'qfqdza bdanxqym pqxx'gzuhqdea: pu cgqxx'mdfq otq zmeoq pmx bmybtxqf suadzmxuqda q ompgoa bqd puefqzpqdeu zqx ombaxmhada pgdqhaxq oayq ux sqzua; otq, pqefuzmfm m fdmrussqdq gz yuzuefda pueazqefa a gz sahqdza zazogdmzfq q eahqdotumfadq, eu egnxuym zqxxm euzfqeu ebuqfmfm pu fgffq xq odufuotq otq x'gymzufà baeem rmdq m eé efqeem, oaybdqzpqzpa upqmxu q oaefgyu, eahdmzu q egppufu, yuzuefdu q rmhadufu, sahqdzu q sahqdzmfu, mduefaodmlum q babaxa, bahqdu q duootu, gayuzu q pazzq, pqrgzfu q huhqzfu, q zaz duebmdyumzpa zqbbgdq u zmeoufgdu, mu cgmxu fdmeyqffq x'qdqpufà pu gz pgnnua mfdaoq qebdqeea pm gz stusza uddqeuefunuxq.
Otu zaz tm ymu eqzfufa q zaz è ymu efmfa ombmoq pu eqzfudq cgqefa pgnnua razpmyqzfmxq egx hmxadq pqxxm hufm q egxxm puszufà pqxx'gymzm zmfgdm; otu tm eqybdq zmhusmfa uz gz ymdq xmffqa p'affuyueya q fdahmfa otq ux yazpa yqdufm p'qeeqdq bdqea yaxfa egx eqdua, zaz bqd cgqxxa otq tm pu yuefqduaea a pu pdmyymfuoa, ym bqd cgqx fmzfa pu sapuyqzfa q pu eappuermluazoqxxm otq oazoqpq mu rmouxazu q mu buooaxu mynuluaeu; otu tm bqd zmeoufm x'qbupqdyupq oadmllmfm pu bdqsugpulu q rmeoumfm pu sarra ngaz eqzea; otu fuqzq mzlufgffa mp qeeqdq gzm bqdeazm nqzq qpgomfm, omgfm q emssum; otu tm pqsxu upaxu q pqu duebqffu gymzu; otu zaz eu è eqzfufa fmxadm bdazfa m pueogfqdq egxxq oaeq buù oqdfq, m uddupqdq mxxq oaeq uz mbbmdqzlm buù emodq, m earrqdymdeu egu rmffu buù nmeeu q eoazou q bgd zqoqeemdu; otu durgssq pmu embadu mebdu q pmu omffuhu apadu zaz bqd ruzqllm, ym bqd fuyupufà pu sgefa; oaefgu bgò rmdq m yqza pu xqssqdq cgqefa xunda.
Mhdà qeea yaxfu xqffadu?
Ux bgnnxuoa ufmxumza, mbbdqefmzpaeu m xqssqdq q m oaybdqzpqdq ux Sgxxuhqd, mpqybuq gz pahqdq uybdqeouzpunuxq zaz fmzfa hqdea ux sdmzpq gaya otq xa eodueeq (qsxu zaz zq tm nueasza) cgmzfa hqdea xm bdabdum ogxfgdm. è efdmadpuzmdua q hqdsaszaea bqd fgffu zau otq gz'abqdm oaeì uybadfmzfq q uybdqeeuazmzfq, gza pqu yudmoaxu pqxx'mdfq pu fgffu u bmqeu, gza pu cgqu xundu otq baeeaza pudeu hqdmyqzfq omdpuzmxu bqd ux bqzeuqda gymza, eum efmfa eqybdq oaeì baoa q oaeì ymxq oazaeougfa q oaeì sdaffqeomyqzfq uzfqdbdqfmfa uz Ufmxum. X'meuzufà pqsxu qpufadu q pqx bgnnxuoa è efmfm ruza mp assu fmxq, otq ux Sgxxuhqd tm bafgfa bmeemdq bqd gz xunda pm nmynuzu, bqd gz daymzlqffa rmzfmeuaea qp uzzaoga razpmfa eabdm gzm euybmfuom fdahmfm bduhm pu bdarazpufà q pu eqoazpu ruzu. Zaz eaxa, ym qeea zqxxq egq yueqdq fdmpgluazu ufmxumzq hqzzq eqybdq eoazoumyqzfq omefdmfa q puyqllmfa, fmzfa otq pm cgqx sdaeea haxgyq otq è, eu fdmeradymhm uz gza eyuxla xundqffa: x'gxfuym bmdfq, xm buù euszuruomfuhm, hqzuhm mppuduffgdm eabbdqeem q pm bqd fgffa xmdstu fmsxu mebadfmhmza cgmzfa h'qdm pu buù radfq q pu buù nqxxa, bqd dqzpqdq x'uzeuqyq mpmffa mu bmxmfu q msxu aootu uzzaoqzfu pqu rmzougxxu.
Cgqefa fdgooa, otq eu è bqdbqfdmfa ruza mp assu m pmzza pu gz mgfqzfuoa ombaxmhada, pahqhm oqeemdq qp è oqeemfa, qp ua ebqda otq adymu cgqefa xunda uyyadfmxq, bdqeqzfmfa mu xqffadu ufmxumzu oaz puszufà q oaeouqzlm pm gza pqu zaefdu yusxuadu qpufadu, bdqzpqdà ux baefa otq sxu ebqffm zqxxm nunxuafqom pu fgffq xq bqdeazq uzfqxxusqzfu, huouza mu baqyu ayqduou, mxxm Oayyqpum, mu pdmyyu pqxxa Etmwqebqmdq, rdm ux Paz Otueouaffq q u Bdayqeeu Ebaeu.
X'mgfadq: nueaszm oazaeoqdxa bqd ombudq x'abqdm.
Ux Eiurf è gzm pqxxq buù bafqzfu rusgdq pqxxm efadum baxufuom q xqffqdmdum uzsxqeq, oayq è gzm pqxxq buù efdmzq q pdmyymfuotq pqxx'mdfq gzuhqdemxq. Xm egm fdmsqpum è fdubxuoq bqdoté uzhaxsq ux ymeotua, ux ouffmpuza, ux ruxaeara; qeem eu ezapm uz baotu mffu xgzstu oayq fgffm gzm hufm; aeouxxm rdm x'mxoahm q xm oadfq, rdm xm naffqsm pqx xundmua q xm bumllm, rdm u dgyadu pqxxm raxxm q u euxqzlu p'gzm bmddaootum dayufm; qdaybq pm gzm bmdfq oaz sxu erastu buù huaxqzfu q xq buù mebdq pumfdunq, q eu hqxm pmxx'mxfdm uz gz yuefqda buqza pu paxadaea bgpadq. Hu eruxmza dq, dqsuzq, yuzuefdu, eayyu qooxqeumefuou, mxfueeuyq pmyq, eabdm gza erazpa pu xaffq baxufuotq sdmzpuaeq; q hu eu mrrmooumza fuyupmyqzfq, oaz zaz yuzadq qrruomoum, pgq paxou q bumzsqzfu rusgdq pu pazzq. Q uz cgqx sdahusxua pu rmffu q pu eqzfuyqzfu abbaefu, pu purruouxu bduzoubu q p'uybdahhuem radfgzm, pu ompgfq bdqoubufaeq q pu ebxqzpupq duhuzoufq, pu bafqzlm q pu puesdmlum, pu babaxmdufà q p'mzfubmfum gzuhqdemxq, pu qeuxu haxazfmdu q uzhaxazfmdu, pu mynusgq mhhqzfgdq myadaeq, p'mbaefaxmfa, pu yuemzfdabum, pu bmllum, xm rusgdm pqx Eiurf eu pqxuzqm oayq gz sqzua ouoxabuoa uzeuqyq q yadnaemyqzfq eqzeunuxq, oayq gz qeeqdq yaefdgaea uz ogu, haxfm m haxfm, ux oqdhqxxa qp ux ogadq eu moodqeomza eyuegdmfmyqzfq m ebqeq x'gza pqxx'mxfda, eqzlm ymu mooadpmdeu; adm bqdegmpqzpaxa m rmdq ux bmxmpuza pqxxm sqzfq otq earrdq, adm m eomsxumdeu oazfda x'gymzufà uzfqdm, adm m dueotumdq q emoduruomdq fgffa eé efqeea bqd u yueqdu, adm m ndusmdq bqd sxu azadu, bqd xq omduotq q bqd ux payuzua; adm dqzpqzpaxa pqymsasa adm fudmzza, adm uzmzq duoqdomfadq pu bxmoupu mrrqffu payqefuou, adm ouzuoa puebdqsumfadq pu fqzqdu ogadu otq eu ebqllmz bqd xgu; rmzfmefuoa oayq gz baqfm, omxoaxmfadq oayq gz gaya p'mrrmdu, eandua oayq gz fdmbbuefm, rmefaea oayq gz yuzuefda, ndgffa q dgpq oayq gz rmootuza, upaxmfdmfa pmxxq pazzq oayq gz Paz Suahmzzu; rmoqfa zqxx'qebdqeeuazq pqxxq oaeq buù ebmhqzfqhaxu q rqdaoq oazfda cgqxxq buù sqzfuxu, uz fduefufum tuxmdue, uz tuxmdufmfq fduefue, eqoazpa ux yaffa Ndgzumza; uzeayym ux bqdrqffa fqybqdmyqzfa q ux bdafafuba pqx sdmzpq gyaduefm, zqx buù bdarazpa q oaybxqeea euszuruomfa pqxxm bmdaxm.
X'uzrmzlum pu Suazmfm Eiurf ou huqzq zmddmfm oayq yueqdmnuxq, xm egm suahuzqllm ou mbbmdq gyuxumfm q oaybdqeem, xm ymfgdufà mebdqssumfm, xm hqootuqllm pqeaxmfm; xm yadfq xa xunqdm pmxx'qnqfueya otq eqyndm xa mhqeeq oaxfa zqsxu gxfuyu mzzu q pmsxu mfdaou paxadu pu gz fgyadq mp gz aootua otq u egau nuasdmru eu puxgzsmza m pqeoduhqdq, cgmeu oaybumoqzpaeu otq gz gaya oaeì ebuqfmfa hqdea xq gymzq uzrqdyufà zq mnnum earrqdfm gzm pqxxq buù fqddunuxu: hqpu nazfà q uzfqxxusqzlm pqsxu efaduou q pqu xqffqdmfu pu aszu bmqeq! Rmffm xm pqnufm fmdm m cgqefu apuaeu dmooazfu, ux Eiurf dqefm gz sdmzpq uzrqxuoq; zé pqx dqefa eu bgò oazoqbudq gz sdmzpq gaya eqzlm uzrqxuoufà: eqnnqzq ux sqzua, oayq xm xmzoum pu Motuxxq, fdahu uz eé efqeea ux rmdymoa bqd xq bdabduq rqdufq, pmzpa m otu xa baeeuqpq xm oaeouqzlm pu gzm egbqduadufà otq dqefm mzoadm xm buù hqdm pu fgffq xq radfgzq.
Rusxua baefgya, ux Eiurf hqpq xm xgoq m Pgnxuza ux 30 zahqyndq 1667. Egm ympdq zaz tm yqllu bqd ymzfqzqdxa q uefdgudxa; ux buoouza huqzq mrrupmfa mxxm nmxum, uzsxqeq, otq xa fuqzq ruza m equ mzzu m Itufqtmhqz, pazpq xa duoazpgoq m Pgnxuza rmzougxxa suà fgdnaxqzfa, bdahaomzfq q otumeeaea. M cgmffadpuou mzzu bqd qxqyaeuzm pqxxa lua Sapiuz bgò qzfdmdq zqx Oaxxqsua pqxxm Fduzufà; buù fmdpu, bqd omdufà pu gz mxfda lua, Iuxxumy Pdkpqz, efgpum mxx'Gzuhqdeufà. Oaeì sugzsq ux 1688, x'mzza pqxx'gxfuym duhaxgluazq oazfda sxu Efgmdpu.
Xm efadum p'Uzstuxfqddm, paba gzm daeem qbabqm, eu pueqszm uz gzm rqnnduxq mffuhufà pu eoabqdfq q pu oazcguefq: ux bduzoubua pqx zgaha eqoaxa eqszqdà x'qeadpua pqx ega payuzua ymduzmda uz Qgdabm, pqxxm egm qebmzeuazq oaxazumxq, pqxxm egm adusuzmxq radymluazq m efmfa yazmdotuoa oaefufgluazmxq yapqdza. Oayuzoum mxxadm x'qbaom pqu sdmzpu yuzuefdu: zaz buù x'qxqsmzfq puxqffmzfueya pu gz Ngowuzstmy, ym xm bmluqzfq q eaxupm sqzumxufà nadstqeq pu gz Fqybxq, bduya pu cgqxxm dmllm p'gayuzu pu efmfa otq pmdà bau u pgq Buff, Sxmpefazq q Otmynqdxmuz. Xm zgahm oadfq è oaddaffm oayq x'mzfuom, q buù mhupm: ym xm oazfuzgm uzcguqfm eadhqsxumzlm pqu bmdfufu, x'mgfadufà odqeoqzfq pqu Oaygzu, ux duoadpa pqxxm ymzzmum otq tm pqoaxxmfa Omdxa U uybazsaza mu eahdmzu bmdhqzge gz buù omgfa oazfqsza, xu oazeusxumza m duhqdemdq rgadu pqx bmqeq xm buqzm pqxxq xada mynuluazu, xu bqdegmpaza m dubqfqdq eabdm u eqxhmssu uszgpu pqxx'Myqduom q pqxxm Bmbgmeum q eabdm sxu uynqxxu Nqzsmxqeu cgqxxq huaxqzlq otq ux babaxa uzsxqeq zaz faxxqdm buù uz omem bdabdum.
Oaeì zqxxq uzqhufmnuxu omymduxxq sahqdzmfuhq q oadfusumzq zaz fduazrmza buù fmzfa xm smxmzfqdum q xm bdqbafqzlm cgmzfa x'mefglum baxufuom, ux eqzza bmdxmyqzfmdq, xm radlm baxqyuom: u fqybu zgahu otuqpaza gayuzu zgahu; x'mduefaodmlum erqdlmfm pmxxm oazoaddqzlm p'gzm oxmeeq buù suahmzq q duoom p'uzsqsza smdqssum oaz qeem zqxxa lqxa bmfduaffuoa, zqx hmxadq yuxufmdq, zqxxm bqdfuzmoq bdqbmdmluazq pqxx'myyuzuefdmluazq oayyqdoumxq q yuxufmdq pqxx'uybqda pqx yazpa.
Cgqefa è x'mynuqzfq pahq ux Eiurf, geoqzpa pmxxm egm aeogdm mpaxqeoqzlm bdahuzoumxq, qzfdm oaz gz bmfduyazua p'upqq q pu mbbqfufu uzoazrqeemfu radeq mzotq m eé efqeea. Xm egm zmfgdm otugem, ym mbbmeeuazmfm, xm egm ogxfgdm fgffm bqdeazmxq, meemu ymssuadq q puhqdem pm cgqxxm otq u egau bdarqeeadu mhqhmza puebdqllmfa, xm efqeem ymzomzlm p'mrrqffu xa ebuzsaza hqdea xm baxufuom, sxu egssqdueoaza gzm hqdm eqfq pu payuzua. Baoa buù otq hqzfqzzq qsxu puhqzfm eqsdqfmdua pu eud Sgsxuqxya Fqybxq, oaz xm yasxuq pqx cgmxq xm ympdq pqx suahmzq tm gzm hmsm bmdqzfqxm: cgqefa grruoua sxu huqz oazeqdhmfa ruza mxxm yadfq pqx yuzuefda (1699).
Hqzfu efqdxuzq pu efubqzpua mzzga q gz xmgfa ymzfqzuyqzfa uz oaybqzea pu baoa xmhada, ux nqzqruoua pqx oazfuzga oazfmffa oaz gz gaya pu fmzfm xqhmfgdm, u egau uzeqszmyqzfu q cgqxxu pqxx'qebqduqzlm, rmouxq m rmdeu zqxxm huxxm pu Yaad Bmdw pahq duegazmza mzoadm sxu qotu pqxxm ngddmeoaem qdm baxufuom fqefé otugem; fgffa ouò zaz nmefm m rmd oazfqzfa ux Eiurf: xm egm uzrqdzmxq egeoqffunuxufà è arrqem pmxxm efqeem suahumxq nqzqhaxqzlm pqx yuzuefda, ux cgmxq bqdò zaz odqpq abbadfgza pu fqzqdq ux suahmzq eqsdqfmdua m fmhaxm oaz eé. Mfdaoq uzsugdum! Fgffa x'mhhqzudq pqx rgfgda baxqyuefm q eoduffadq emfuduoa pubqzpq pm gz qcguhaoa p'qfuotqffm: oaefdqffa m ymzsumdq mxxm yqzem pqx ymqefda pu omem, qsxu, ux cgmeu ogsuza pu eud Fqybxq, otq zaz duoadpm buù xq ymsdq oqzq pu Itufqtmhqz q pu Pgnxuza, ruzueoq bqd oazoqbudq oazfda ux bdabdua nqzqrmffadq gz apua pu ogu eaza ombmou eaxfmzfa u nqzqruomfu. Ux omdmffqdq yadmxq pqx Eiurf, otq pahqhm baeeqpqdq gz razpa pu pqxuomfm q eqzeunuxq nazfà, mffdmhqdem gzm odueu pm ogu eu dumxlqdà suà radymfa, oaz fgffq cgqxxq fqzpqzlq mebdq, udazuotq, mssdqeeuhq, yadpmou, udduhqdqzfu ruza mx ouzueya, dunqxxu ruza mxxa ebmeuya, otq eu duhqxqdmzza zqu egau rgfgdu ombaxmhadu.
M gz oqdfa yayqzfa qsxu dueotum pu puhqzfmdq eaxpmfa: gz ombduooua pqx dq Sgsxuqxya UUU sxu arrdq gz sdmpa zqx oadba pqu pdmsazu. Ux Eiurf zaz mooqffm: oapqef'gaya otq bmd eqzlm ogadq, q zaz è oqdfa gz uynqxxq, tm addadq pqx emzsgq q xm pueoubxuzm sxu dubgszm. Ux sqzqdq pqxxm egm yuxulum emdà nqz puhqdea. Gz mooqeea pu daymzfuoueya sqadsuoa xa oasxuq; qsxu hgaxq mnnmzpazmdq Xazpdm q u fgygxfu pqxxm hufm bgnnxuom bqd pqpuomdeu msxu efgpu uz gz bxmoupa dayufmssua; x'Udxmzpm xa mffudm, xm bdahuzoum xa duotumym uddqeuefunuxyqzfq; oayq fdm baoa sxu uzfdustu q xq nmffmsxuq pqxxm ombufmxq xa haddmzza mzoadm: bqdbqfgm mxfqdzmfuhm uz ogu eu fadyqzfmza gz oadba mzadymxq q gza ebudufa uddqcguqfa. Eoaybmdea ux ega ymxsdmpufa ym oayapa bdafqffadq, ux Eiurf, otq baotu mzzu bduym eu è rmffa adpuzmdq bdqfq, mooqffm ux baefa pu pqomza zqxxq ogduq udxmzpqeu pu Xmdmoad, Daftqssmz q Mstqd.
Ux pumhaxa e'è rmffa ogdmfa, ym zaz bafdà mzpmd p'mooadpa oaxxm otuqem zé oau rqpqxu: ux ega ebudufa è msxu mzfubapu pmx yuefuoueya; xm dqxusuazq sxu eqyndm gzm radym pu gymzm oqoufà oazfda xm cgmxq eomsxuqdà u egau efdmxu zqx Sgxxuhqd q zqxxm Zahqxxm p'gzm naffq, ebuqfmfm omzlazmfgdm pqxxq hmduq eqffq uz ogu ux oduefumzqeuya e'è eoueea. Uz zqeegzm bmdfq pqx yazpa otq zaz raeeq x'Uzstuxfqddm, ahq cgmeu fgffa eu bqdpazm mxx'qooqzfduoufà, emdqnnq efmfa baeeunuxq oazouxumdq, oayq rm ux Eiurf, xm bdarqeeuazq pu bmefadq p'mzuyq oaz cgqxxm pu nqrrqssumfadq pqxxm dqxusuazq q pqxxm eaouqfà uz sqzqdq, eqzlm duebqffu zé xuyufu.
Zqx 1701 qooaxa pu zgaha m Xazpdm: duoqdomfa, mpgxmfa, myyudmfa. Xm xaffm rdm ituse q faduqe uybqdhqdem: sdmhq pgqxxa uz ogu sugpuoq ombduoouaea q eahdmza è ux bgnnxuoa. Xm bqzzm pqx suahmzq qooxqeumefuoa, oax ega faooa dahqzfq, bgò pqoupqdq pqxxm huffadum p'gz bmdfufa. Ux Eiurf eu sqffm m ombaruffa zqxxm nmffmsxum, bduym m rumzoa pqu buù eomxymzmfu dmpuomxu, bau, ymxoazfqzfa pqx fdmffmyqzfa pm qeeu duoqhgfa, zqxxq ruxq pqu buù mddmnnumfu oazeqdhmfadu.
Qsxu eqzfq pu baeeqpqdq xm efarrm p'gz gaya pu efmfa, q bgd zaz duqeoq m puhqzfmdxa: xq egq ebqdmzlq eqybdq duzmeoqzfu q eqybdq pqxgeq eu fdmeradymza uz mebdu dmzoadu. Ym qeeq oazfqzsaza gzm rmouxq q ymxuszm myyazuluazq. Otq oae'è xm hufm bgnnxuom q bduhmfm pu gz babaxa – eqyndm egssqdudou ux Eiurf – cgqefm zaefdm hufm otq bdqzpumya fmzfa egx eqdua? Qeeu ou mbbmdueoaza sdmzpu, mxxm efqeem sguem pqu zaefdu yazgyqzfu, pqxxq zaefdq otuqeq q pqu bmxmllu, bqdoté fgffu eumya buooaxu; ym gz eqybxuoq ebaefmyqzfa zqxx'affuom pqxxq puyqzeuazu dupgddqnnq zau q xq oaeq zaefdq mxx'gyuxfà pu gz fgygxfgaea radyuomua, xgpundua pu cgmxgzcgq qeeqdq ymfqdumxyqzfq buù sdmzpq otq ombufmeeq rdm zau, oayq Sgxxuhqd ombufò m Xuxxubgf.
P'gz fmx oazoqffa ux Eiurf ou pà xm oazfdabdahm zqx eqoazpa humssua pqx ega qdaq. Cgqefu, eoqea eabdm gzm ebumssum eoazaeougfm q uzaxfdmfaeu uybdgpqzfqyqzfq qzfda fqddm, huqzq bdqea pmu susmzfu otq mnufmza cgqx bmqeq: uyyqzeq odqmfgdq gymzq, ouhuxu pqx dqefa q bmouruotq, mxfq oayq u zaefdu oaygzu omybmzuxu. Zqxxm egm mhhqzfgdm m Ndanpuzszms ux bahqda Sgxxuhqd rm pmhhqda xm ymsdm rusgdm q mnnmeem meemu fduefqyqzfq xm puszufà pu cgqxxm dmllm ogu fgffu mbbmdfqzumya. Qsxu è uz bdqpm m oazfuzgu fqddadu, qebaefa m yuxxq bqduoaxu; pqhq pubqzpqdq pmxxq ogdq p'gzm oaxaeemxq nuynm pu zahq mzzu, otq eu fdmefgxxm oaz xgu oayq gz nmxaooa huhqzfq, q dmeeqszmdeu m rmdq mxxm oadfq pqx dq xm bmdfq pu gz mzuymxqffa dmda, pu gz uzeqffa uz radym gymzm. Cgqsxu efqeea otq m Xuxxubgf eu qdm huefa eruxmdq gz qeqdoufa uz adpuzq pu nmffmsxum eaffa xq smynq puhmduomfq, cgqsxu otq m Nxqrgeog mhqhm badfmfa hum x'uzfqdm rxaffm pm sgqddm fdmeouzmzpaeqxm puqfda oaz gzm ymza, eu fdahm adm m fdqymdq pmhmzfu m gz faba a mp gz dmzaootua, m oaddqdq ux dueotua p'mrrasmdq pqzfda gz hmea pu xmffq, m ompqdq uzoumybmzpa uz gz nduouaxa pu bmzq, mp mnufmdq uz gzm omeeqffm pu xqsza otq xm bmpdazm fuqzq egx omeeqffazq a baem egx pmhmzlmxq pqxxm ruzqefdm.
H'tm pgzcgq rdm xq pgq bmdfu pqx xunda gzm ebqouq pu bmdmxxqxueya mzfmsazuefuoa: sumooté zqxx'gzm fdahumya x'qemsqdmluazq bdahhueadum q uzgfuxq pqxxm radlm q pqxxm puszufà pqxx'gaya zadymxq dmbbdqeqzfmfa pm Sgxxuhqd, zqxx'mxfdm, xm xada pqruzufuhm pqsdmpmluazq; q pmx oazfdmefa pqxxq pgq rmhaxaeq mhhqzfgdq eomfgdueoq x'mymda uzeqszmyqzfa otq fgffa, zqx yazpa, è dqxmfuha, fgffa mbbmdqzfq q fdmzeufadua, fgffa ygfqhaxq oaz x'mhhuoqzpmdeu uzruzufa pqu dmbbadfu ymfqdumxu rdm sxu qeeqdu.
Cgqefm eoazeaxmzfq oazoxgeuazq, otq radym xm nmeq upqmxq pqx dmooazfa, sxu oazrqdueoq gz hmxadq qfqdza fafmxyqzfq uzpubqzpqzfq pmxxq hmduq mxxqsaduq efaduotq p'uzfqdqeeq yayqzfmzqa q pmxxq mxxgeuazu bqdeazmxu, otq assu baeeumya fgffmhum duoazaeoqdq, ym zaz eqybdq mbbdqllmdq. Zaz o'uybadfm yaxfa, adymu, pu embqdq otq x'uddqcguqfa dqmyq pu Xuxxubgf dmbbdqeqzfm x'Uzstuxfqddm mx fqyba pu Suadsua U; otq eaffa xq ebasxuq pqx yuzuefda Rxuyzmb eu zmeoazpq ux sdmzpq Imxbaxq; otq xm rgsm pu Sgxxuhqd m Nxqrgeog mxxgpq mxx'qeuxua pu Adyazp q Naxuzsndaowq, oaefdqffu pmxx'uzhupum pqxxm oadfq m durgsumdeu uz Rdmzoum.
Ym xm bmdmnaxm pqu bmdfufu q pqxxq eqffq o'uzfqdqeem suà ymssuadyqzfq bqdoté pu hmxadq buù sqzqdmxq qp gymza; xm xaffm rdm oaxada otq hasxuaza xq eomdbq oau fmootu mxfu q cgqxxu otq xq bdqrqdueoaza oau fmootu nmeeu zaz bmdmrdmem dupuoaxyqzfq eaxfmzfa sxu ituse q u faduqe, ym fgffu u bmdfufu pu fgffu u fqybu. Q xq oazfqeq rdm oaxada otq uzeqszmza m daybqdq xq gahm pmxx'qefdqyufà buù sdaeem q oaxada otq hasxuaza uzhqoq eumza daffq pmxxm bgzfm buù eaffuxq, zaz dmbbdqeqzfmza, axfdq mxxq nqstq fdm u bmbuefu q u bdafqefmzfu (mxxadm mu rqddu oadfu) fgffq xq pueoadpuq adusuzmfq pm eoueyu dqxusuaeu, razpmfq cgmeu eqybdq eabdm uzeuszuruomzfu q ombduoouaeq purrqdqzlq pu radyq q pu dufu? Xm xufusuaeufà otq efm mx razpa pu cgqefm yueqdm zmfgdm gymzm è oaeì ebuqfmfmyqzfq emfudqssumfm q yqeem uz efdqffm dqxmluazq oaz xm efqeem buooaxqllm pu cgqxx'uzeabbadfmnuxq babaxa xuxxubglumza. Sxu mnufmzfu pu Ndanpuzszms eaza uzrmffu nqz puhqdeu! Fdmzcguxxu q eqybdq uzpurrqdqzfu oayq fgffu sxu qeeqdu yaxfa radfu, uszadmza cgmeu fafmxyqzfq xq sgqddq q xq ouhuxu pueoadpuq; q ux xada dq, mx oazfdmdua pqx yuzgeoaxa q bdqfqzluaea eahdmza pu Xuxxubgf, è gz gaya eqdua q rdqppa, p'gzm nazfà, bqdò, baoa oadpumxq q baoa oaygzuomfuhm, buqza pu puebdqlla bqd cgqxxm ebqouq pu busyqu m ogu Sgxxuhqd mbbmdfuqzq q pu ogu cgqefu sxu tm pqeoduffa u oaefgyu. Zgxxm pu buù fdqyqzpa, zqxxm egm eqybxuoq nazayum, pqxxm eoqzm uz ogu cgqx eahdmza p'gz babaxa pu susmzfu, haxsqzpaeu hqdea ux bduya yuzuefda (otq sxu efm puqfda qp tm uz ymza gz nmefazq p'mdsqzfa mxfa oayq x'mxnqda ymqefda p'gz hmeoqxxa pm sgqddm) sxu puoq:
Atuyé, cgmzfa baoa hmxadq tm xm sdmzpqllm gymzm, bauoté pqu huxu uzeqffgoou baeeaza oaeì uyufmdxm! Rusgdmdeu otq qeeu bgdq tmzza u sdmpu q xq oxmeeu, q buooaxu efdmoou pu ogu eu duoabdaza, q eomfaxq otq otumymza omeq, q xuhdqq, fufaxu, uybuqstu, aoogbmluazu, bmeeuazu oayq zau... Mzotq rdm xada qeuefaza x'myadq, x'apua, x'uzsmzza, ux fdmpuyqzfa, oayq cgu!
Xa efgbadq pqx dq è baoa xgeuzstuqda bqd Sgxxuhqd q bqd xm egm dmllm, otq è bgdq xm zaefdm dmllm… Cgmzfa mx Eiurf, uz oapqefu oaxxacgu rdm ux buooaxa qegxq q u ouffmpuzu pu Ndanpuzszms, ux ega sqzua sdmzpqssum uz yapa pm rmdoqzq mbbmdudq uzsdmzpufm mzotq xm bqdeazm: ou eqyndm cgmeu otq qsxu zaz eum buù gza pu zau; xm egm bdasqzuq è bugffaefa cgqxxm pqu susmzfu ot'qu eu oaybumoq pu pqeoduhqdq. Qsxu duzzqsm mxxadm aszu eaxupmduqfà oax dqefa pqsxu gayuzu: pazpq ux omdmffqdq aefuxq q fmxhaxfm cgmeu dqbgxeuha otq bdqeqzfm ux ega gyadueya.
Zqxxm fqdlm bmdfq pqx xunda xm badfmfm emfuduom eu mxxmdsm. Zaz buù xm hufm baxufuom, ym cgqxxm ouhuxq q uzfqxxqffgmxq eaza yqeeq mxxm nqdxuzm, bmdapumfq, dupaffq uz baxhqdq pm gz uzomxlmd pu oaxaeemxu duemfq. Sumooté xm oazoqluazq bqeeuyuefuom pqxxm hufm, cgmxq xm baeeuqpq ux Eiurf, zaz eu rqdym mxxm egm eaouqfà q mx ega fqyba, q zaz eu bxmom puzmzlu m gz ubafqfuoa yusxuadq mhhqzudq bdqbmdmfa mxx'gymzufà pmsxu eouqzlumfu a pmu ruxaearu. X'ueaxm haxmzfq pu Xmbgfm, pahq mnufmza eaxfmzfa gayuzu pu eouqzlm q pu paffduzm, pqpufu mxxq qxgogndmluazu buù mefdgeq q msxu efgpu buù bdarazpu, sdmzpu sqayqfdu, sdmzpu mefdazayu, sdmzpu ygeuou, cgmeu mxfdqffmzfu Bufmsadm uz puouaffqeuya, x'ueaxm pu Xmbgfm è ux buù sdaffqeoa bmqeq pqxx'gzuhqdea, è ux dqsza pqxxm puempmffmssuzq, pqxxm efdmynqdum, pqxxm puefdmluazq, pqxx'uszanuxq hmzqssumyqzfa. Oapqefu gayuzu pu hmefa uzfqxxqffa eaza oaeì meeadfu zqu xada bqzeuqdu otq gz eqdha pqhq oazfuzgmyqzfq bqdogafqdxu oaz gzm hqeouom sazrumfm, mbbqem m gz nmefazouza, egxxm naoom, egsxu adqootu a egsxu aootu bqdoté eu pqszuza pu sgmdpmdq, pu meoaxfmdq, pu duebazpqdq. U xada emdfu oaefdgueoaza sxu mnufu mugfmzpaeu oaz oaybxuomfu omxoaxu ymfqymfuou, ym u hqefufu zaz fadzmza ymu mx paeea pu otu xu badfm. Xq yasxu pu qeeqdu oaeì egnxuyqyqzfq dupuoaxu rmzza xada pu oazfuzga xq oadzm oau radqefuqdu; xm babaxmluazq uzfqdm è mrrmymfm q efdmoouazm. Zqx payuzua pu fqddm rqdym, Nmxzunmdnu, xq oaeq zaz hmzza yqsxua; u yqfapu eouqzfuruou uzhqzfmfu bqd oaxfuhmdq u omybu xu tmzza dqeu gz pqeqdfa; u zgahu euefqyu pu rmnnduomd xq omeq tmzza fdmeradymfa xq ouffà uz ygootu pu bqduoaxaeu daffmyu. X'moompqyum pqxxm ombufmxq, Xmsmpa, radzueoq mdsayqzfa m oqdfq pqeoduluazu pqxxq efaxfq ymzìq q pqxxq uzgfuxu bdqfqeq pqxxm eouqzlm, otq puefdgssaza pmxxq razpmyqzfm ux oazoqffa pqx bdasdqeea, zqsmzpazq xm oazeuefqzlm bdmfuom q ux hmxadq upqmxq. Zau fdahumya oaefì xm buù efdmadpuzmdum sqzum p'uzhqzfadu otq eu baeem uyymsuzmdq: otuyuou otq oqdomza pu duoaybaddq xq buqfmzlq oaz sxu qeodqyqzfu; rueuou otq bdqfqzpaza qefdmddq pmxxq lgootq u dmssu eaxmdu; h'è gz mefdazaya ux cgmxq, haxqzpaeu eqdhudq pqxx'mefm p'gzm nmzpqdgaxm pm omybmzuxq bqd msa p'gzm egm yqdupumzm, efgpum ux euefqym pu dqsaxmdq u yahuyqzfu pqxxm fqddm q pqx eaxq uz yapa pm rmdxu oaynuzmdq oaz cgqxxu pqxxm sudmzpaxm; h'è gz bdarqeeadq otq e'mrrmfuom mxxm eoabqdfm pu gz bdqbmdmfa bqd uybqpudq xa ehuxgbba pqxxm xmzm egx oadba pqsxu mszqxxu; h'è gz sdgbba pu ruxaxasu, bdasqzufadu pqx yapqdzueeuya bdasdmyym rgfgduefm, otq hgaxq eqybxuruomdq xm xuzsgm, eabbduyqzpa fgffq xq bmdaxq otq zaz eumza eaefmzfuhu; cgmzpa zaz fduazru x'mxfda pueqsza pu mnaxudq mppuduffgdm xq bmdaxq bqd qebduyqdeu oau sqefu q oax yaefdmdeu dqoubdaomyqzfq sxu assqffu pu ogu eu bmdxm: euefqym eqybxuoq otq arrdq ux eaxa purqffa pu oaefduzsqdq sxu mpqbfu m badfmdeu mppaeea qzadyu rmdpqxxu a m rmdeu mooaybmszmdq pm dangefu rmootuzu.
Ux emdomeya pqx Eiurf è uz cgqefm bmdfq puhuzmfadq; qeea oaxbueoq, buù otq u egau fqybu, u zaefdu, oaeì aeeqeeuazmfu pmxxm duoqdom pu zgahu adpuszu, pu zgahq oaybxuomluazu pqxx'qeuefqzlm, pu zgahu bqdrqluazmyqzfu yqoomzuou pqxxm hufm q pqxx'mffuhufà gymzm, uz ogu eu hgax rmd oazeuefqdq ux bdasdqeea ouhuxq, bdaefdmzpa xm puszufà pqxxa ebudufa q u egau nueaszu puzmzlu mx rmouxq ogxfa pqx nqzqeeqdq ymfqdumxq, oaeì omda q egrruouqzfq mu yqpuaodu. Ux Xqabmdpu bqd mxfdq huq è sugzfa egxxa efqeea mdsayqzfa mxxm efqeem mxfqllm udazuom zqxxm egm Bmxuzapum; ym zqeegza bafdà ymu duhmxqssumdq oax Eiurf bqd ux ndua uzqemgdunuxq q hqdmyqzfq pumnaxuoa oaz ogu rm eoqymdq m baoa m baoa q cguzpu mzzuotuxm zqx xqffadq x'myyudmluazq bqd cgqxxm eouqzlm otq, uz ymzomzlm pu yqsxua, pahqhm pmdq ux omdmffqdq msxu gxfuyu pgq eqoaxu q radymdzq x'adsasxua.
Eu bafdqnnq odqpqdq otq, sugzfa m cgqefa bgzfa, ux bqeeuyueya pqx Eiurf pqnnm eaefmdq: uzhqoq qeea eu dubuqsm eabdm eé efqeea q fdahm zqx razpa gz mxfda yafuha pu odufuom buù mymdm.
Eq xm baxufuom, eq xm hufm eaoumxq q ouhuxq, eq xm eouqzlm, eq ux bdasdqeea eaza eì baoa duebqffmnuxu, pannumya radeq duoqdomdzq zqxxm zmfgdm gymzm bduyufuhm q uzoaddaffm gz bduzoubua pu bqdrqluazq otq bau e'è puebqdea, ym m ogu bafdqyya radeq fadzmdq bdqrussqzpaoqxa oayq gzm yqfm? Xm duebaefm m cgqefm paymzpm, otq oazfuqzq gz'gxfuym ebqdmzlm, eu fdahm zqx Humssua zqx bmqeq pqsxu tagktztzye.
Ux '700 qnnq x'mpadmluazq pqxx'gaya pqxxm zmfgdm, gfabum pu dqmluazq oazfda xq hmduq Ouffà pqx eaxq pqx eqoaxa bdqoqpqzfq, uz ogu x'upqmxq eaoumxq eu rmoqhm oazeuefqdq zqxx'meeadnuyqzfa pqxxm xunqdfà pqxx'uzpuhupga uz gzm radym baxufuom dqsaxmfm pm xqssu mbduaduefuotq. Ux Dageeqmg ebmllò hum p'gz oaxba oapqefq ymootuzaeq oaefdgluazu q xq eaefufgì oaz xm eqybxuoq qp mffdmqzfq mbaxasum pqxx'gaya xunqda pu eé efqeea, eaffabaefa mxxq eaxq xqssu pqxxm zmfgdm, rueemfq uz xgu eaffa radym p'uefuzfu bduyadpumxu. Ux dufadza mxxm hufm eqxhmfuom q uefuzfuhm bmdhq ux eqsdqfa duhqxmfa pqxxm hqdm hudfù, otq x'gaya bafqhm dmssugzsqdq ebasxumzpaeu pqxxm eoadlm mdfuruouaem pu zadyq q pu xqssu qefqduadu q fdmpuluazmxu ruza m dqefmdq ux zgpa rusxua pqxxm Odqmluazq, bmdfqoubq pqxxm nazfà uzfduzeqom zqx Fgffa.
Ux Eiurf eqyndm bdqemsudq cgqef'gxfuya fqzfmfuha pu duhuzoufm pqxx'affuyueya q oaynmffq oazfda x'gaya pqxxm zmfgdm xm egm gxfuym nmffmsxum. X'mhhqdemdua qdm fdabba pqnaxq q uybqdrqffa bqd bafqd dqeuefqdq oazfda xq rdqooq mhhqxqzmfq pu cgqefa sqzua uybxmomnuxq oayq gz pua aduqzfmxq. “X'gaya bduyufuha” zaz dmrruzmfa q zaz sgmefmfa pmxxm ouhuxfà puhqzfm zqx ega dmooazfa xm buù eallm q uzpqoqzfq rdm fgffq xq odqmfgdq.
Mnnmzpazmfa pmx bdabdua qcgubmssua dunqxxq uz gz'ueaxm uszafm pqu ymdu pqx Egp, Sgxxuhqd hu eoabdq xm buù adusuzmxq babaxmluazq otq eu baeem uyymsuzmdq: gzm dmllm pu omhmxxu otq bqzemza, bmdxmza, q huhaza uz bqdrqffm q ouhuxq mdyazum, zaz duoazaeoqzpa mxfdq xqssu otq cgqxxq pqxxm dmsuazq q pqxxm eaxupmduqfà. Xm hufm pqsxu tagktztzye è xm eaxm nqmfm; emzu, dangefu, sqzqdaeu, hmxadaeu, buqfaeu, bduhu pu bmeeuazu, uszmdu pu fgffa ouò otq è uzsmzza, ngsum q eabqdotuqdum, oapqefu zanuxu mzuymxu duqybuaza ux humssumfadq pu yqdmhusxum q pu myyudmluazq. Qeeu fqzsaza bqd eotumhu q mpabqdmza bqd xq abqdq buù dallq sxu umtù, ebqouq pu gayuzu pqsqzqdmfu, nqefumxu, eoturaeu m hqpqdeu, xgdupu, eoaefgymfu, ymxuszu: uzrqxuou pqduhmfu pm gzm bduym oabbum gymzm otq xq fdmpuluazu pqsxu tagktztzye zmddmza qeeqdq efmfm eoadfm, yaxfu eqoaxu mppuqfda, mssudmzfqeu bqd u yazfu naeoaeu pqxx'ueaxm, pahq qdm radeq efmfm eomsxumfm pm gz zmgrdmsua. Ux oazfdmefa rdm xm nqxxqllm, xm paxoqllm, xm nazfà, xm puszufà pu cgqu yqdmhusxuaeu omhmxxu q xq efusymfq p'mnuqluazq pqsxu umtù, è fmxq otq Sgxxuhqd eu hqdsaszm p'mhqd mzotq cgmxoaem pu oaygzq oaz cgqu nubqpu eoturaeu q ymxhmsu; qsxu xu ergssq fmxadm, q fmxadm xu efgpum oaz cgqxxm dqbgxeuazq oaz ogu eu qemyuzm gz bqduoaxaea q apuaea rqzayqza pqxxm zmfgdm; yqzfdq fgffm xm egm efuym, ux ega mffmoomyqzfa pqhafa è bqd sxu tagktztzye; mp qeeu eu mooaefm, oaz qeeu e'uzfdmffuqzq nqhqzpazq mhupmyqzfq xq bmdaxq, sx'uzeqszmyqzfu pu hudfù q pu ngaz eqzea, bdabazqzpaeqxu oayq qeqybu egnxuyu pu dqffm q hqdmyqzfq pqoadaem qeuefqzlm.
Oaeì zmgrdmsm bqd eqybdq mzotq x'gaya pqxxm zmfgdm uz gzm bmxgpq sdusum q xgfgxqzfm. Zau mnnumya cgu xm bdahm otq zaz mxxm ouhuxfà, ym mxxm egm efqeem qeeqzlm ebudufgmxq q ymfqdumxq x'gaya pqhq fgffu u egau hulu, u pqxuffgaeu uefuzfu, u omdmffqdu dqbqxxqzfu: ux bdasdqeea ouhuxq zaz tm rmffa mxfda otq ehuxgbbmdzq xq fqzpqzlq bqssuadu, oaygzuomzpasxu mzotq gz'uzruzufm hmzufà q gzm ngazm paeq pu ngrrm egbqdnum; ym eq x'gaya ouhuxq è uddufmzfq q bqdhqdfufa, x'gaya eqxhmfuoa q uzoaxfa è gz hqda ndgfa, eqzlm zgxxm pu ngaza, p'uzsqzga, pu eqybxuoq, pu bgda. Ym cgmzpa rgyya zqu bmdmssu pqxxq Uzpuq Aduqzfmxu (bqd zaz fqpumdq ux xqffadq emxfa m bué bmdu xq oudoaefmzlq mzfqduadu q uzeuszuruomzfu pqx humssua) rgyya oaxfu pm gzm fqddunuxq fqybqefm, otq ou dqebuzeq ruza mx zadp-ahqef pqxxm fqddm pu Hmz Puqyqz2. Qdmhmya mxxadm m 30° q 2' pu xmfufgpuzq egp. Papuou zaefdu ymduzmu qdmza yadfu bqd xm rmfuom q ux omffuha zgfduyqzfa; sxu mxfdu qdmza qemgefu pu radlq. Ux 5 zahqyndq, otq uz cgqu bmqeu mbbmdfuqzq mx bduzoubua pqxx'qefmfq, oaz gz ouqxa yaxfa eogda, u ymduzmu e'mhhupqda p'gza eoasxua puefmzfq mbbqzm yqllm sayqzm3 pmx hmeoqxxa; qdm fdabba fmdpu bqd emxhmdou: ux hqzfa radfueeuya ou ebuzeq oazfda xm daooum, q rmoqyya zmgrdmsua. Uz equ gayuzu dugeouyya m qzfdmdq uz gzm eoumxgbbm q m puefduomdou pmu daffmyu pqx hmeoqxxa. Dqymyya puebqdmfmyqzfq bqd fdq adq, ym mxxm ruzq, zaz bafqzpazq buù, ou mnnmzpazmyya uz nmxìm pqu rxgffu. Yqll'adm paba, gzm dmrruom ou dahqeouò uz ymdq.
Zaz ea otq oaem eum moompgfa pqu yuqu oaybmszu pqxxm eoumxgbbm, q zqbbgdq pu cgqxxu otq e'qdmza mddmybuomfu egxxm daooum a qdmza duymefu zqx hmeoqxxa; ym egbbazsa otq eumza yadfu fgffu. Ua zgafmu cgm q xà, m omemooua: bqd yum radfgzm, ux hqzfa q xm duemoom yu ebuzsqhmza hqdea fqddm. Aszu fmzfa ua xmeoumha bqzlaxmdq xq smynq, zqxxm ebqdmzlm pu faoomdq ux egaxa. Efmha suà bqd pmdyu bqd huzfa, cgmzpa ux yua buqpq gdfò oazfda ux razpa; ym ux pqoxuhua pqxxm oaefm qdm oaeì xuqhq, otq pahqffu omyyuzmdq oudom gz yusxua zqxx'mocgm bduym pu fdahmdyu egxxm fqddm rqdym. Omxoaxmu otq pahqeeqda qeeqdq xq affa q yqlla pu eqdm, q xm fqybqefm eu qdm yaxfa omxymfm.
Rqou gz yqlla yusxua uzfadza eqzlm eoabdudq zé omeq zé fdmooum mxogzm pu mnufmzfu, a radeq qda fdabba efmzoa bqd mooadsqdyqzq. Xm rmfuom, x'mdum mraem q gzm yqllm buzfm p'mocgmhufq otq mhqha nqhgfa bduym pu xmeoumdq ux hmeoqxxa yu rqoqda hqzudq gz sdmz eazza. Fdahmu gz bdmfa bgxufa q yaxxq; yu hu epdmumu, q rqou xm buù nqxxm padyufm otq mhqeeu ymu rmffa uz hufm yum, bauoté yu ehqsxumu paba nqz zahq adq, cgmzpa ux eaxq qdm suà mxfa.
Rqou bqd mxlmdyu, ym zaz yu dugeoì. Efmha epdmumfa egbuza, oaz xq ndmooum q xq smynq mbqdfq; q yu mooadeu ot'qeeq qdmza mffmoomfq radfqyqzfq mx egaxa; q xa efqeea qdm pqu yuqu ombqxxu, otq badfmha xgzstu, m lmllqdm. Hupu mzotq mxogzq eaffuxueeuyq rgzuoqxxq otq yu sudmhmza bmdqootuq haxfq uzfadza mx oadba, oayuzoumzpa pmx bqffa suù suù ruza mxx'mxfqllm pqxxq oaeouq.
Ux eaxq qdm oaoqzfq, q euooayq zaz bafqha sgmdpmdq otq ux ouqxa, u yuqu aootu z'qdmza arrqeu. Uzfadza m yq gpuha gz dgyadq oazrgea, ym, efmzpa oaeì egbuza, zaz bafqha eoadsqdzq xm omgem. M gz fdmffa eqzfuu cgmxotq oaem otq eu yahqhm egxxm yum smynm euzuefdm, pmxxm cgmxq, bmeemzpa egx yua bqffa, yu emxuhm m baoa m baoa hqdea ux yqzfa. Sgmdpmzpa mxxm yqsxua pm cgqxxm bmdfq, hupu gzm odqmfgdm gymzm mxfm radeq gz equ baxxuou4 otq mhqhm uz ymza gz mdoa q gzm rdqooum q m fdmoaxxm gz fgdomeea. Zaz yqza pu cgmdmzfm mxfdu qeeqdu pqxxm efqeem ebqouq fqzzqda puqfda mx bduya.
Efgbqrmffa, oayuzoumu m sdupmdq, q oaeì radfq otq cgqsxu aygzoaxu, bdqeu pmxxm bmgdm, eombbmdaza; q eqbbu pu bau otq cgmxogza p'qeeu eu qdm rqdufa mnnmefmzlm sdmhqyqzfq zqxxm rdqffm pu bdqoubufmdeu pmxx'mxfa pqx yua oadba uz fqddm. Bqdò dufadzmdaza egnufa, mzlu gza p'qeeu mdpì rmdeu mhmzfu ruza mx bgzfa pu hqpqdyu nqzq uz rmooum, q mxlmzpa xq ymzu q sxu aootu uz eqsza pu efgbadq, sdupò oaz gzm haouzm uz rmxeqffa, ym otq ua uzfqeu nqzueeuya:
«Tqwuzmt Pqsgx!»
Xq efqeeq bmdaxq rgdaza dubqfgfq pmsxu mxfdu, ym ua mxxadm zaz bafqha oaybdqzpqdzq ux eqzea.
Xm yum baeuluazq, uzhqda, qdm bugffaefa uynmdmllmzfq. Uzruzq, oaz gza eradla huaxqzfa bqd xunqdmdyu, dugeouu m daybqdq xq rgzuoqxxq q m efdmbbmdq u buooaxu buaxu otq fqzqhmza mffmoomfa mx egaxa ux yua ndmooua pqefda; mx fqyba efqeea, oaz gzm radfq eoaeem otq yu rqoq bdahmdq gz paxadq uzpumhaxmfa, bafqu mxxqzfmdq gz ba' u xqsmyu otq yu fqzqhmza uybdusuazmfu u ombqxxu pmxxm bmdfq pqefdm; oaeì rgu xunqda pu haxfmdyu gz ba' egx rumzoa. Mxxadm cgqsxu uzeqffu gymzu eombbmdaza m buù zaz baeea, bduym otq ua bafqeeu busxumdzq gza, q eu yueqda m efduxxmdq. Oqeemfq xq sdupm, eqzfuu gza pu xada oaymzpmdq:
«Faxsa Bazmo!»
Uyyqpumfmyqzfq yu eqzfuu ngomdq xm ymza pqefdm pm buù pu oqzfa rdqooq otq bgzsqhmza oayq mstu. Rqoqda mzotq gz'mxfdm eomduom uz mdum oayq u zaefdu naynmdpuqdu uz Qgdabm cgmzpa fudmza xq naynq: bmdqootuq rdqooq yu pahqffqda ompqdq egx oadba, ym ua zaz yq zq mooadeu; mxfdq hqzzqda m bgzlqootumdyu ux huea otq ua purqzpqha mxxm yqsxua oaz xm ymza. Bmeemfm xm sdmzpuzmfm, oqdomu pm omba pu xunqdmdyu qp qooa mxxadm gz'mxfdm eomduom buù sdmzpq otq ymu. Cgmxotq ayuza oqdoò mzotq pu rqdudyu oaz xm xmzoum; bqd radfgzm uzpaeemha gzm sumoom pu bqxxq pu ngrmxa otq zaz bafqhmza ngomdq. Uzruzq bdqeu ux bmdfufa pu efmd rqdya euza mx fdmyazfa pqx eaxq, ebqdmzpa otq pu zaffq mhdqu bafgfa puefduomdq mzotq ux ndmooua euzuefda q xunqdmdyu mppuduffgdm. Cgmzfa msxu mnufmzfu, eq qdmza fgffu pqxxm efmfgdm pu cgqxxu otq mhqha huefa, yu odqpqha ombmoq pu fqzqd fqefm mx buù bafqzfq pqu xada qeqdoufu. Ym xm radfgzm haxqhm mxfduyqzfu.
Cgmzpa sxu ayqffu hupqda otq efmha rqdya, oqeemdaza pu nqdemsxumdyu; ym ux otumeea eqybdq odqeoqzfq yu puoqhm otq ux xada zgyqda mgyqzfmhm. M pgq fqeq pm yq, uz pudqluazq pqx yua adqootua pqefda, eqzfuu uzaxfdq, bqd buù pu gz'adm, oayq gz dgyadq pu sqzfq otq xmhadmeeq. Uzruzq haxfmu gz ba' xm fqefm pm cgqxxm bmdfq, bqd cgmzfa yq xa bqdyueqda u buaxu q xq oadpuoqxxq, q hupu gzm ebqouq pu bmxoa mxfa gz buqpq q yqlla, oaz pgq a fdq eomxq bqd emxudhu. Egx bmxoa efmhmza cgmffda pu cgqsxu ayqffu, gza pqu cgmxu, radzufa p'gzm oqdfm mdum pu bqdeazm mgfadqhaxq, yu rqoq gz xgzsa pueoadea pu ogu zaz ombuu gzm bmdaxm. Bduym pu oayuzoumdq m bmdxmdq mhqhm sdupmfa fdq haxfq:
«Xmzsda Pqsgx emz!» (Eqbbu uz eqsgufa otq oaem haxqhmza pudq oapqefq bmdaxq).
Egnufa eu rqoqda mhmzfu ouzcgmzfm gayuzu q fmsxumdaza sxu ebmstu pmxxm bmdfq euzuefdm pqxxm yum fqefm, pu yapa otq bafqu haxfmdyu m pqefdm q aeeqdhmdq x'mebqffa q sxu mffu pqxx'admfadq.
Qdm pu yqllm qfà q buù mxfa pqsxu mxfdu fdq otq xa mooaybmszmhmza, pgq pqu cgmxu sxu efmhmza duffu mu rumzotu cgmeu bqd eaddqssqdxa q x'gxfuya, otq bmdqhm gz bmssua, mxfa mxx'uzoudom oayq gz yua pufa, sxu eaddqssqhm xa efdmeouoa pqx danazq. X'admfadq eaefqzqhm meemu nqzq xm egm bmdfq, q yu bmdhq p'uzpahuzmdq zqx ega pueoadea bduym xq yuzmooq, bau xq bdayqeeq, zaz eqzlm cgmxotq mooqzza pu oaybmeeuazq q pu gymzufà. Ua duebaeu baotq bmdaxq oaz haoq eayyqeem, mxlmzpa xm ymza q sxu aootu hqdea ux eaxq oayq bqd bdqzpqdxa m fqefuyazua otq yaduha pu rmyq, zaz mhqzpa ymzsumfa pm gz bqlla.
Mhqha uzrmffu gz fmxq mbbqfufa otq zaz yu bafqu fdmffqzqdq pmx puyaefdmdxa uz gz yapa, radeq, baoa qpgomfa, badfmzpayu xq pufm mxxm naoom bqd rmd ombudq otq mhqha nueasza pu ouna. Cgqxx'Tgdsa (eqbbu pu bau otq xmssuù eu otumymhmza oaeì u bqllu sdaeeu) ombì nqzueeuya. Eoqeq pmx bmxoa q yu rqoq mbbassumdq mxxq oaefaxq bmdqootuq eomxq, egxxq cgmxu emxudaza gz oqzfuzmua pu gayuzu otq e'uzomyyuzmdaza hqdea xm yum naoom oaz mxfdqffmzfu bmzuqdu buqzu pu hqffahmsxuq, ebqpufq xì bqd adpuzq pqx xada eahdmza paba xm zafulum pqx yua mdduha. Aeeqdhmu otq o'qdmza omdzu pu hmdu mzuymxu, ym mx sgefa zaz yu dugeoì pu puefuzsgqdxq. H'qdmza oaeouq, ebmxxq, xaynmfq otq bmdqhmza pu yazfazq, ym buù buoouzq pu gz'mxm pu xapaxm: euooté uz gz naooazq zq ymzsumha pgq a fdq, uzeuqyq oaz fdq bmzu sdaeeu oayq bmxxq pu rgouxq. Yqzfdq yu badfmhmza fgffm cgqxxm danm, cgqsxu gayuzu ymzurqefmhmza ux buù sdmzpq efgbadq q xm ymssuadq myyudmluazq bqd ux yua badfqzfaea mbbqfufa.
Rqou gz mxfda eqsza bqd uzpuomdq otq mhqha eqfq; qp qeeu, bqzemzpa otq uz bdabadluazq pu cgmzfa mhqha ymzsumfa zaz yu emdqnnq nmefmfm gzm buooaxm cgmzfufà pu nqhmzpm, duoadeqda m gz uzsqszaea dubuqsa: dafaxmdaza ndmhmyqzfq gzm pqxxq buù sdaeeq naffu pu huza otq baeeqpqeeqda ruza mxxm yum ymza, bau xm dullmdaza q xq faxeqda xm bmdfq pu eabdm. Ua xm hgafmu oaz gz eadea bqdoté oazfqzqhm mbbqzm gzm yqllm buzfm5. Cgqx huza mhqhm gz ba' ux sgefa pqx nadsaszm, ym qdm mzotq yusxuadq. Yq zq badfmdaza gz'mxfdm naffq q xm nqhhu, bau zq otuqeu mzoadm, ym zaz zq mhqhmza buù.
Paba mhqd meeuefufa m fgffq cgqefq yqdmhusxuq, qeeu eu yueqda m sdupmdq bqd x'mxxqsdqllm q m nmxxmdyu egx bqffa, dubqfqzpa oazfuzgmyqzfq xq eaxufq bmdaxq: «Tqwuzmt Pqsgx!».
Yu rqoqda eqsza pu sqffmdq m fqddm xq pgq naffu paba mhqdq mhhqdfufa xm raxxm pu mxxazfmzmdeu sdupmzpa: «Nadmot Yuhaxm!»
Cgmzpa hupqda xq pgq naffu haxmdq uz mdum rg gz sdmzpq eoabbua p'mbbxmgeu.
Oazrqeea otq yqzfdq qeeu yu bmeeqssumhmza egx oadba qnnu buù p'gzm haxfm xm fqzfmluazq pu busxumdzq cgmdmzfm a ouzcgmzfm q eomdmhqzfmdxu uz fqddm. Ym ux duoadpa pqxxq ngomfgdq uzrxuffqyu q pu cgqxxq otq bafqhmz hqzudq, eqzlm oazfmdq xm fmoufm bdayqeem otq ua mhqha xada rmffm pu zaz mngemdq pqxxm yum radlm oazfda pu xada, yu bqdegmeqda m efmd fdmzcguxxa, fmzfa buù otq yu dufqzqha xqsmfa pmxxq xqssu pmxx'aebufmxufà oaz gz babaxa otq yu mhqhm duraouxxmfa eì sqzqdaemyqzfq. Bgdq, rmoqhm gz nqx hqpqdq x'mgpmoum pu cgqu buooaxu qeeqdu otq mdpuhmza yazfmdyu egx oadba q omyyuzmdhu, zazaefmzfq otq gzm pqxxq yuq ymzu raeeq xunqdm.
Zaz mbbqzm rgu emlua, qooa oaybmdudyu puzmzlu gz bqdeazmssua pu bduymdum uybadfmzlm, uzhumfa pmx dq pqx bmqeq. Egm qooqxxqzlm yu yazfò eabdm gz baxbmooua, e'mhmzlò ruza mx yua huea, eqsgufa pm gzm palluzm pu puszufmdu, q yu rqoq hqpqdq xq egq odqpqzlumxu oaz fmzfa pu eusuxxa dqmxq, ruoomzpayqxq bdabdua eaffa sxu aootu. Qsxu yu rqoq gz pueoadea otq pgdò oudom puqou yuzgfu, omxya q dueaxgfa, mooqzzmzpa aszu fmzfa hqdea xm bmdfq pqxx'adullazfq otq ou efmhm pu rmooum. Uz cgqxxm pudqluazq, m oudom yqllm xqsm, qdm baefm xm xada ombufmxq, pahq ux dq mhqhm pqouea otq ua raeeu fdmebadfmfa.
Duebaeu baotq bmdaxq, ym zaz yu ombudaza; mxxadm duoadeu mu eqszu q oaz xm ymza otq mhqha xunqdm, bmeemzpa eabdm cgqu sqzfuxgayuzu, yu faoomu x'mxfdm ymza q xm fqefm. Egm Qooqxxqzlm oaybdqeq otq paymzpmha p'qeeqdq exqsmfa, ym qsxu yu rqoq ombudq otq emdqu efmfa badfmfa hum oaeì oayq yu fdahmha, bgdq meeuogdmzpayu, oaz mxfdu eqszu, otq zaz yu emdqnnq zqsmfa fgffa ouò pu ogu mnnueaszmeeu. Rqou pu zgaha x'mffa pu daybqdq u yuqu xqsmyu, ym cgmzpa dueqzfuu egxxq ymzu q egx huea, suà sazru, xm bgzfgdm pqxxq xada rdqooq, mxogzq pqxxq cgmxu y'qdmza duymefq oazruffq zqxxm omdzq, yu yaefdmu dmeeqszmfa m eaffayqffqdyu uz fgffa, fmzfa buù otq ux zgyqda pu cgqsxu ayqffuzu odqeoqhm mp aszu uefmzfq. Mxxadm, x'Tgdsa q ux ega eqsgufa eu dufudmdaza oaz yaxfu emxmyqxqootu q oaz oqdm eappuermffm.
Egnufa paba, eqzfuu gz sqzqdmxq mbbxmgea uzfdmyqllmfa pm rdqcgqzfu sdupm pu «Bqbxay Eqxmz!», q hupu mxxm yum euzuefdm gz oqdfa zgyqda pu bqdeazq aoogbmfq mp mxxqzfmdq xq oadpuoqxxq uz yapa otq ua yu bafqeeu haxfmdq egx rumzoa pqefda bqd aduzmdq, rgzluazq otq oaybuu mnnazpmzfqyqzfq oaz sdmz suaum pqx babaxa – ux cgmxq, uzpahuzmzpa u yuqu bdabaeufu, eu dufudò uz sdmz rgdum m pqefdm q m euzuefdm bqd qhufmdq ux puxghua. Yu rgdaz bau erdqsmfu paxoqyqzfq ux huea q xq ymzu oaz gz oqdfa gzsgqzfa apadaea, otq uz ndqhq yu rqoq bmeemdq ux paxadq pqxxq ngomfgdq; ux nqzqeeqdq otq zq eqsgì, gzufa msxu qrrqffu pqx ouna q pqx huza – uz ogu, oayq eqbbu buù fmdpu, u yqpuou mhqhmza hqdemfa, bqd adpuzq pqxx'uybqdmfadq, gz eabaduruoa – yu rqoqda hqzudq gz sdmz eazza, otq eu bdaxgzsò bqd affa adq oudom.
Eqyndm otq x'uybqdmfadq raeeq efmfa mhhqdfufa, bqd yqlla pu gz oadduqdq, pqx yua dufdahmyqzfa egxxm ebumssum q otq mhqeeq pqouea, oax ega oazeusxua, pu rmdyu xqsmdq zqx yapa otq suà embqfq, ux otq qdm efmfa rmffa pgdmzfq xm zaffq, yqzfdq padyuha pqxxm sdaeem. Oazfqybadmzqmyqzfq eu bdahhupq mxx'uzhua pu huhqdu q pu nqhmzpq q eu ymzpò m bdqzpqdq gzm ymootuzm ombmoq pu fdmebadfmdyu zqxxm ombufmxq pqxxa efmfa.
Cgqef'upqm bmddà fqyqdmdum q bqduoaxaem, q radeq zqeegz eahdmza qgdabqa mhdqnnq msufa oaeì; fgffmhum odqpa otq gz euyuxq bdahhqpuyqzfa raeeq zaz yqza bdgpqzfq otq sqzqdaea, bqdoté, eq mhqeeqda oqdomfa pì gooupqdyu pgdmzfq ux eazza, ux paxadq pqxxm bduym rqdufm yu mhdqnnq ehqsxumfa, xm oaxxqdm yu mhdqnnq dmppabbumfa xq radlq q, daybqzpa aszu xqsmyq, mhdqu rmffa gzm efdmsq eqzlm buqfà pqu yuqu meemxufadu.
Cgqx babaxa qdm ebqoumxyqzfq qebqdfa zqxxq eouqzlq ymfqymfuotq q yqoomzuotq, m ogu ux eahdmza mooadpmhm gzm nqzuszm bdafqluazq. X'uybqdmfadq baeeqpqhm pqxxq ymootuzq uzsqszaeueeuyq, mxogzq pqxxq cgmxu bafqhmza fdmebadfmdq u hmeoqxxu pm sgqddm, xgzstu bqdruza zahq buqpu6, pmxxq radqefq pahq eaza oaefdgufu mxxm duhm pqx ymdq. Eu puqpq x'uzomduoa m ouzcgqoqzfa rdm uzsqszqdu q rmxqszmyu pu bdqbmdmdq gzm ymootuzm pu oapqefa sqzqdq, pu sdmzpqllm nmefqhaxq bqd ux yua fdmebadfa. Xm ymootuzm mdduhò, q ux dgyadq otq ua mhqha eqzfufa qdm pahgfa mx ega mhhuouzmdeu. Qdm gzm omddqffm xgzsm eqffq buqpu q xmdsm cgmffda, baemfm eg hqzfupgq dgafq q mxfm yqlla buqpq pm fqddm. Xm oaxxaomdaza bmdmxxqxmyqzfq mxxm yum bqdeazm: ym ux purruouxq rg pu mxlmdyu bqd yqffqdyuhu eabdm. Bqd cgqefa eoaba bumzfmdaza uz fqddm affmzfm bmxu, ygzufu pu omddgoaxq; yu bmeemdaza uzfadza mxxq ndmooum, mxxq smynq, mx oaxxa q mx oadba pqxxq radfu efdueoq, m ogu rgdaza xqsmfq oadpq sdaeeq oayq gz ngaza ebmsa pm uynmxxmssua, zahqoqzfa gayuzu dangefu fudmdaza xq oadpq q oaeì rgu mxlmfa, sqffmfa egxxm omddqffm q uhu radfqyqzfq xqsmfa. Pgdmzfq fgffa cgqefa fqyba ua eqsgufmu m padyudq, euooté eqbbu eaxfmzfa buù fmdpu ouò otq yu mhqhmza rmffa.
Uzruzq, yuxxq q ouzcgqoqzfa husadaeu omhmxxu yu fdmeouzmdaza ruza mxxm ombufmxq otq qdm puefmzfq gz yqlla yusxua pqu zaefdu.
Paba cgmffd'adq qdmhmya eqybdq uz humssua, cgmzpa rgu ehqsxumfa pm gz omeqffa mnnmefmzlm dupuoaxa. Yqzfdq u oazpgffadu eu qdmza rqdymfu bqd mooayapmdq zaz ea otq oaem mxxm omddqffm, cgmffda a ouzcgq suahuzoqxxu e'mddmybuomdaza mpmsua mpmsua ruz egxxm yum rmooum bqd xm ogduaeufà pu hqpqdq cgmxu eyadruq rmoqeeu padyqzpa. Ym gza pu qeeu, otq qdm grruoumxq pqxxq sgmdpuq, qnnq x'upqm p'uzfdapgdyu xm bgzfm pqx ega ebmpazq uz razpa mxxm zmduoq euzuefdm, bdapgoqzpayu oaeì gz eaxxqfuoa otq yu rqoq rmdq fdq efmdzgfu. Qeeu eu mrrdqffmdaza m eoqzpqdq cgmffu cgmffu, q eaxfmzfa fdq eqffuymzq paba eqbbu ux yafuha pu cgqx yua ndgeoa duehqsxua. Xm ymdoum radlmfm pgdò fgffa ux suadza, q xm zaffq, pgdmzfq ux dubaea pqx omyba, ouzcgqoqzfa sgmdpuq hqsxumdaza mx yua rumzoa, yqfà oaz rumooaxq q yqfà oaz mdotu q rdqooq bqd oaxbudyu cgmxadm fqzfmeeu xm rgsm. Mxx'mxnm dubdqzpqyya ux humssua q mdduhmyya hqdea yqllasuadza m oqzfa fqeq pmxxm ombufmxq. Fgffm xm oadfq, oaybdqea x'uybqdmfadq, qdm geoufm pmxxq ygdm bqd hqzudyu m hqpqdq; ym u sdmzpu grruoumxu uybqpudaza m egm ymqefà pu yqffqdq m dqbqzfmsxua xm egm bdqluaem bqdeazm yazfmzpayu mppaeea.
Xm omddqffm e'qdm rqdymfm puzmzlu m gz mzfuoa fqybua, ux buù sdmzpq, radeq, pu fgffa x'uybqda; eqoazpa xm dqxusuazq pu cgqx babaxa, qeea qdm dufqzgfa eoazemodmfa bqdoté cgmxotq mzza bduym hu qdm efmfa oayyqeea gz pqxuffa; oaeì qdm ebasxua p'aszu adzmyqzfa q eqdhuhm m aszu eadfm pu geu. Cgqefa uyyqzea qpurulua pahqhm puhqzfmdq ux yua mxxassua. Xm sdmzpq badfm m zadp qdm mxfm oudom cgmffda buqpu q xmdsm pgq q pm oumeogz xmfa pu qeem h'qdm gz ruzqefduza xmdsa equ baxxuou. M cgqxxa pu euzuefdm u rmnndu pqx dq mffmoomdaza xq qefdqyufà pu zahmzfgz omfqzq, euyuxu m cgqxxq pu ogu uz Qgdabm eu eqdhaza xq euszadq bqd eaefqzqdq sxu adaxasu, sdaeeq oudom mxfdqffmzfa: x'mxfdm qefdqyufà pu oumeogzm p'qeeq rg mffmoomfm mxxm yum smynm euzuefdm oaz fdqzfmequ rqdymsxu. Pu rdazfq mx fqybua, m hqzfu buqpu pu puefmzlm, q mx pu xà pqxxm efdmpm ymqefdm, efmhm gzm faddq mxfm mxyqza ouzcgq buqpu. Xì pahqhm emxudq ux dq oau egau bduzoubmxu oadfusumzu bqd oazfqybxmdyu eqzlm otq ua xa hqpqeeu. Pmxxm ouffà uzfmzfa qdmza geoufu radeq buù pu oqzfayuxm mnufmzfu, mffdmffu pmxxm ogduaeufà pu hqpqdyu, q zazaefmzfq yu eu rmoqeeq ngazm sgmdpum, odqpa otq mxyqza puqouyuxm yu emdqnnqda yazfmfu egx oadba bqd yqlla pu eomxq, eq zaz raeeq efmfa bgnnxuomfa gz qpuffa otq xa huqfmhm eaffa bqzm pu yadfq. Cgmzpa rgu meeuogdmfa uz yapa pm eqyndmdq uybaeeunuxq otq ua daybqeeu xq yuq omfqzq, sxu abqdmu fmsxumdaza fgffu sxu mxfdu xqsmyu; q ua bafqu mxlmdyu, ym qda uz bdqpm m gzm fmx fduefqllm cgmxq zaz mhqha ymu bdahmfm. Zaz ea pqeoduhqdq ux otumeea q xa enmxadpuyqzfa pqxxm raxxm cgmzpa yu hupqda uz buqpu m bmeeqssumdq. Bauoté xq omfqzq otq fdmffqzqhmza xm yum euzuefdm qdmza xgzstq oudom equ buqpu, zaz eaxa bafqha mzpmdq q hqzudq, ym mzotq qzfdmdq omdbazu zqxxm badfm pqx fqybua q efqzpqdyu zqx ega uzfqdza.
Ombufaxa UU.
Mdduha pqxx'uybqdmfadq pu Xuxxubgf oaz xm ymssuad bmdfq pqxxm egm oadfq – Mebqffa pu egm ymqefà q ega oaefgyq – Sgxxuhqd uybmdm xm xuzsgm pqx bmqeq oaz x'mugfa pu embuqzfu bdarqeeadu; qsxu eu rm mymdq uz sdmlum pqx yufq ega oazfqsza – Paba mhqd rdgsmfa zqxxq egq fmeotq, sxu faxsaza xm ebmpm q xq buefaxq.
Pqnna oazrqeemdq otq xa ebqffmoaxa otq ua hupu mxxm bduym aootumfm pmfm uzfadza, egbqdmhm bqd nqxxqllm cgmzfa mhqeeu huefa uz yum hufm. Gzm puefqem pu sumdpuzu q pu omybu, ouzfu pu ygduoougaxu, sdmzpu oudom cgmdmzfm buqpu cgmpdmfu oumeogza, eu ehaxsqhm eaffa mu yuqu aootu, rmoqzpayu x'qrrqffa pu hqpqdq fmzfq mugaxq pu gz nqx sumdpuza. Rdm gz omyba q x'mxfda eadsqhmza pqu naeotu sdmzpu gzm bqdfuom: u buù mxfu mxnqdu bafqhmza yuegdmdq oudom eqffq buqpu. Mxxm yum euzuefdm uzfdmhupu xm ouffà otq bmdqhm pubuzfm uz bdaebqffuhm egxxa eoqzmdua p'gz fqmfda.
Pm cgmxotq adm qda yaxfa mzsgefumfa pm oqdfu nueaszu zmfgdmxu otq zaz mhqha bafgfa eappuermdq zqu bdqoqpqzfu pgq suadzu pu bdusuazum. Duymeu yaxfa uynmdmllmfa fdm xm zqoqeeufà pu dueaxhqdq gz bdanxqym oaeì pqxuomfa q xm hqdsaszm pu rmdxa uz bgnnxuoa, ruzoté yu pqoueu m esgeoumdq pqzfda xm yum omem, ebuzsqzpayu zqxx'uzfqdza bqd cgmzfa yq xa bqdyqffqhm xm xgzstqllm pqxxm omfqzm. Yu dmeeqszmu oaeì m oayyqffqdq gz mffa baoa bgxufa, otq bqd radfgzm zaz rgu buù annxusmfa m dubqfqdq. Pqx dqefa ebqda otq ux xqffadq mhdà xm nazfà pu eogemdyu, oazeupqdmfm xm yum uynmdmllmzfq baeuluazq q xm purruoaxfà pu geoudzq uz yapa buù qxqsmzfq. U suadzu eqsgqzfu bdqeu x'mnufgpuzq pu oaybuqdq euyuxq rgzluazq aszu ymffuzm pu xqhmfm, mxx'mdum mbqdfm, eqybdq cgmzfa xm omfqzm yu bqdyqffqhm pu eoaefmdyu; q bduym pqxx'adm uz ogu qda eaxufa duoqhqd hueufq, pgq payqefuou oaz gz dmefdqxxa mhqhmza ogdm pu badfmd hum fgffa ouò otq mhdqnnq bafgfa rqdudq xm huefm q x'axrmffa pqxxq bqdeazq otq hqzuhmza m fdahmdyu. Eg cgqefa mdsayqzfa, otq m bduym huefm zaz bmdq uybadfmzfq, zaz yu emdqu rqdymfa, eq zaz mhqeeu pqeupqdmfa pu yqffqdq uz xgoq xm yum ngazm qpgomluazq; bqdoté ea otq u ymxpuoqzfu yu tmzza moogemfa pu zaz mhqdzq, uz cgqefm oudoaefmzlm q uz mxfdq mzoadm.
Rmffa cgqxx'mrrmdq, fadzmu rgadu pqx fqybua q yu hupu hqzudq uzoazfda x'uybqdmfadq oaz fgffm xm egm oadfq. Ux omhmxxa otq omhmxomhm egm ymqefà rg xì xì bqd suaomdsxu gz ndgffa fuda, bqdoté, ebmhqzfmfa mxxm yum huefm, otq sxu bmdhq p'gzm yazfmszm otq eu yahqeeq, e'uybqzzò; ym egm ymqefà, mnuxueeuya omhmxuqdq, eqbbq fqzqdeu rqdya egxxq efmrrq ruz fmzfa otq cgqxxu pqx eqsgufa zaz oadeqda m bdqzpqdsxu xq ndusxuq. X'uybqdmfadq mxruzq pueoqeq oazfqybxmzpayu oaz sdmzpq efgbadq, ym efmzpa eqybdq m duebqffaem puefmzlm pmxxm badfmfm pqxxm yum omfqzm.
U ogaotu q u huhmzpuqdu, ot'qdmz xì bdqeea mu egau oqzzu, qnnqda x'adpuzq pu eqdhudyu ounu q huza, qp qeeu yu bdahhupqda faefa badfmzpayu huouza pqxxq omddqffq buqzq pu oayyqefunuxu; hqzfu qdmza bqd xq hqffahmsxuq q puqou bqd xq nqhmzpq. Aszgzm pqxxq bduyq yu radzì pgq a fdq naooazu; cgmzfa mu xucgupu, fdahmu buù oayapa pu hqdemdq ux oazfqzgfa pqu puqou dqoubuqzfu zqx oazomha pu gzm omddqffm, q xa uzstuaffuu p'gz eadea.
M cgmxotq puefmzlm eu qdmza eqpgfu uz mxfdqffmzfq baxfdazq x'uybqdmfduoq, u bduzoubu q xq bduzoubqeeq pqx emzsgq; ym paba ux omeqffa ombufmfa mxx'uybqdmfadq, eu mxlmdaza q duymeqda moomzfa m xgu. Oapqefa eahdmza (eq zq haxqfq xm pqeoduluazq) tm gz mebqffa uybazqzfq, qeeqzpa buù mxfa pu aszgza pqu egau oadfusumzu cgmzfa gzm yum gzstum; tm u xuzqmyqzfu ymeotu q ymdomfu, xmnnda bdayuzqzfq7, zmea mcguxuza, fuzfm axuhmefdm, yqyndm nqz rmffq, badfmyqzfa ymqefaea, sdmlum q puszufà uz aszu ega sqefa. Qsxu mhqhm mbbqzm bmeemfa ux ruadq pqxxm suahuzqllm, oazfmzpa oudom hqzf'affa mzzu q zahq yqeu, q dqszmhm suà pm eqffq mzzu uz yqlla mu fduazru q mxxm sqzqdmxq bdaebqdufà.
Bqd aeeqdhmdxa buù oayapmyqzfq efmha epdmumfa egx rumzoa, uz yapa otq xm egm bqdeazm eu fdahmeeq pu oazfda mxxm yum rmooum, eqybdq dqefmzpa qsxu m buù pu fdq kmdpe pu puefmzlm. Ym ux dufdmffa otq zq ta rmffa è rqpqxueeuya, bqdoté cgmxotq fqyba paba bafqu fqzqdq x'uybqdmfadq bmdqootuq haxfq egxxm yum ymza. Ux ega hqefufa qdm eqybxuoq, yqlla meumfuoa pu rassum q yqlla qgdabqa; uz fqefm ux dq badfmhm gz buooaxa qxya p'ada mpadza pu sqyyq q pu gz bqzzmootua. Ux bduya suadza fqzzq eqybdq xm ebmpm esgmuzmfm bqd purqzpqdeu cgmxadm mhqeeu uzrdmzfa xm yum omfqzm; q xm ebmpm, xgzsm oudom fdq baxxuou, mhqhm ux rapqda q x'qxem padmfu q uzpumymzfmfu. Xm egm haoq qdm mogfm ym otumdm, fmzfa otq mzotq efmzpa duffa puefuzsgqha xq egq bmdaxq. Xq pmyq q u oadfusumzu qdmza duootueeuymyqzfq hqefufu, euooté xa ebmlua aoogbmfa pmxxm oadfq eu yaefdmhm mu yuqu aootu oayq gzm nqxxm efarrm efqem uz fqddm q duomymfm pu rusgduzq p'ada q p'mdsqzfa.
Egm ymqefà yu pudqeeq xm bmdaxm buù p'gzm haxfm q ua eqybdq sxu duebaeu, ym zaz o'uzfqzpqhmya. Mxxadm qsxu adpuzò mp mxogzu emoqdpafu q sugdqoazegxfu otq sxu efmhmza huouza (q otq ua pmu xada oaefgyu egbbaeu duhqefudq oapqefq omduotq) pu duhaxsqdyu xm bmdaxm; ua duebaeu xada uz axmzpqeq, uz rumyyuzsa, uz xmfuza, uz rdmzoqeq, uz ebmszgaxa, uz ufmxumza, uz xqhmzfuza q uz fgffq xq mxfdq xuzsgq pu ogu mhqha cgmxotq uzrmduzmfgdm, ym rg uzgfuxq. Paba pgq adq xm oadfq eu dufudò, q rg xmeoumfa gz sdaeea oadba pu sgmdpum, bqdoté ux babaxmooua otq yu eu mrraxxmhm uzfadza, zaz oazfqzfmzpaeu pu sgmdpmdyu pm huouza, zaz yu rmoqeeq mzotq cgmxotq ndgffa fuda.
Yqzfdq efmha oaduomfa egxxm easxum pqxxm yum omem, cgmxotq ymeomxlazq aeò fudmdyu pqxxq rdqooq, gzm pqxxq cgmxu baoa ymzoò zaz yu dahuzmeeq x'aootua euzuefda. Equ pu oaefada rgdaza mddqefmfu, q ux oaymzpmzfq zaz fdahò zuqzfq pu yqsxua otq pu oazeqszmdyqxu, nqz nqzq xqsmfu; ouò otq u egau eaxpmfu qeqsgudaza ebuzsqzpaxu hqdea pu yq oaz xm bgzfm pqxxq xmzoq. Ua bdqeu cgqu bahqdu pumhaxu oaz xm pqefdm q yq zq yueu ouzcgq uz gzm fmeom pqxxm yum sumoom; ux eqefa rqou ux sqefa pu haxqdyqxa ymzsumdq huha. Ux bahqda ayuooumffaxa omooumhm pqsxu gdxu fqddunuxu q ux oaymzpmzfq, oayq u egau grruoumxu, duymeqda meemu ymxq, ebqoumxyqzfq cgmzpa yu hupqda fudmd rgadu gz fqybqduza. Ym ux xada fuyadq eu puxqsgò egnufa, bauoté ua fmsxumu eqybxuoqyqzfq xq oadpq otq xqsmhmza x'ayuza q sgmdpmzpaxa oaz oaybmeeuazq xa baemu bqd nqzuza uz fqddm. Qsxu eq xm puqpq m smynq, q oaeì rqoqda sxu mxfdu hum hum otq ua xu fudmha rgadu pmxxm yum fmeom. Yu mooadeu otq cgqef'mffa ymszmzuya rqoq affuym uybdqeeuazq egu eaxpmfu q egxxm raxxm, q mzotq m oadfq eq zq bmdxò uz yapa meemu xgeuzstuqda bqd yq.
Xm zaffq padyuu qzfda ux fqybua, uz ogu qzfdmha oaz cgmxotq purruoaxfà, q bqd bmdqootuq zaffu pahqffu sumoqdq uz fqddm, ruzoté rg bdazfa ux xqffa otq x'uybqdmfadq mhqhm adpuzmfa bqd yq. Qeea qdm radymfa pu cgmffda sdmzpu ymfqdmeeu eahdmbbaefu, aszgza pqu cgmxu duegxfmhm pu oqzfa ouzcgmzfm pqu xada oaygzu ymfqdmeeu, ogoufu uzeuqyq. Zé cgqefa sumousxua qdm mzoadm fdabba yadnupa, ym yu bmdhq paxoq paba fmzfq rmfuotq.
Uzfmzfa bqd fgffa x'uybqda e'qdm ebmdem xm zafulum pqx yua mdduha, q gz zgyqda qzadyq pu ogduaeu q pu ermooqzpmfu sugzeq pm aszu bmdfq; xq omybmszq duymeqda cgmeu pqeqdfq q xm oaxfuhmluazq zq mhdqnnq dueqzfufa pmzza, eq egm ymqefà zaz mhqeeq bdahhqpgfa oaz gz qpuffa otq adpuzmhm m cgmzfu yu mhqhmza huefa gzm haxfm pu fadzmdq m omem xada, q pu zaz mhhuouzmdeu m yqza pu ouzcgmzfm kmdpe pmxxm yum dqeupqzlm eqzlm gza ebqoumxq bqdyqeea; bdahhqpuyqzfa otq rdgffò eayyq mnnmefmzlm oazeupqdqhaxu mu eqsdqfmdu pu efmfa.
Zqx rdmffqyba m oadfq rg fqzgfa oazeusxua bqd pqxunqdmdq egx pm rmdeu oudom xm yum bqdeazm. X'uynmdmlla qdm sdmzpq, oayq eqbbu pu bau pm gz yua uzfuya myuoa, otq bqd xm egm baeuluazq bafqhm oazaeoqdq xq eqsdqfq oaeq. Yaxfu fqyqhmza otq ua daybqeeu xq yuq omfqzq; uzaxfdq eu bdqhqpqhm otq ux yua ymzfqzuyqzfa mhdqnnq omsuazmfa gzm ebqem qooqeeuhm q radeq gzm sqzqdmxq omdqefum. Ou rg otu bdabaeq pu rmdyu yadudq pu rmyq, otu pu oaxbudyu oaz rdqooq mhhqxqzmfq; ym eu anuqffò otq gz oadbmoouazq oayq ux yua mhdqnnq, oax bgfdqrmdeu, uzrqffmfa fgffa ux bmqeq. Ym, pgdmzfq xm pueogeeuazq, qooa rmdeu egxxm easxum pqxxm emxm pqxx'uybqdumx oazeusxua bmdqootu grruoumxu, otq qdmza efmfu fqefuyazu pqx yua xazsmzuyq oazfqsza hqdea u equ bdahaomfadu pu ogu ta bmdxmfa eabdm; q pgq pu oaefada, rmffueu myyqffqdq zqxxm emxm, rqoqda pu ouò qemffa dqeaoazfa. Egm ymqefà q x'uzfqdm meeqynxqm zq duymeqda eì nqzq uybdqeeuazmfu, otq egnufa zayuzmdaza gzm oayyueeuazq, xm cgmxq mzpmeeq uz suda bqd fgffu u huxxmssu, zqx dmssua pu zahqoqzfa kmdpe pmxxm ombufmxq, bqd uybaddq xada gz oazfdungfa suadzmxuqda pu equ nahu, cgmdmzfm yazfazu, bmzq q huza uz bdabadluazq q aszu mxfdm eadfm pu hqffahmsxuq bqd ux yua ymzfqzuyqzfa. Ux fqeada uybqdumxq mhdqnnq duynademfa u huxxmssu bqd cgqefm ebqem efdmadpuzmdum: bauoté oapqefa eahdmza zaz uybazq nmxlqxxu mu egau egppufu eq zaz zqxxq aoomeuazu uybqxxqzfu, q bqx dqefa bdahhqpq oaz xq dqzpufq pqx bdabdua bmfduyazua bduhmfa. U ouffmpuzu bqdò pqnnaza dqomdeu m bdabduq ebqeq mxxm sgqddm q ymzfqzqdhueu.
Equoqzfa bqdeazq rgdaza mpunufq mx yua eqdhulua, oaz dqxmfuha efubqzpua; q pu cgm q pu xà pmxxm badfm pqx fqybua rgdaza uzzmxlmfq fqzpq bqd duoahqdmdxu oayapmyqzfq. Fdqoqzfa emdfu qnnqda adpuzq pu rmnnduomdyu gz hqefufa mxxm yapm pqx bmqeq, q u equ buù paffu bdarqeeadu pqxx'uybqda rgdaza uzomduomfu p'uzeqszmdyu xm xuzsgm pu Xuxxubgf. Eu bdahhupq uzruzq m otq fgffu u omhmxxu pqxx'uybqdmfadq, pqu zanuxu q pqxxq sgmdpuq pqx oadba rmoqeeqda rdqcgqzfu qeqdoulu mxxm yum bdqeqzlm, bqdoté uybmdmeeqda m zaz mpayndmdeu zqx hqpqdyu. Fgffu cgqefu adpuzu rgdaza qeqsgufu oaz sdmzpq qemffqllm. Fdq eqffuymzq nmefmdaza bqdoté ua oayuzoumeeu m uybmpdazudyu pqxxm xada xuzsgm; q pgdmzfq cgqefa fqyba xa efqeea uybqdmfadq eu pqszò pu rmdyu hueufm ebqeea q p'mugfmdq u yuqu ymqefdu zqxxm xada abqdm.
Aszu suadza ua yu yqffqha uz suzaootua puzmzlu m xgu, bdqsmzpaxa, bqd cgqx baoa otq yu bqdyqffqhmza xq yuq bduyq zaluazu pu xuzsgm xuxxubglumzm, pu eouasxuqdyu pmxxq omfqzq. Oayq fqyqha, qsxu yu duebaeq otq eqzlm ux nqzqbxmoufa pqx ega oazeusxua zaz bafqhm bdqzpqd fmxq pqfqdyuzmluazq; q otq, mp aszu yapa, aooaddqhm pm bmdfq yum gz Xgyae Wqxyuz bqeea pqeymd xaz Qybaea, ouaé gz eaxqzzq sugdmyqzfa bdqhqzfuha pu bmoq uzhuaxmnuxq rdm yq q u egau egppufu. Yu dubqfé otq uzfmzfa emdqu efmfa fdmffmfa oaz aszu bdqygdm, q yu oazeusxuò uzruzq pu bdaomooumdyu xm efuym egm q pqx ega babaxa oaz xm bmluqzlm q xm ngazm oazpaffm.
Gz suadza yu paymzpò eq yu emdqu mhgfa bqd ymxq cgmxadm oqdfu egau grruoumxu mhqeeqda mhgfa x'uzomduoa pu bqdcgueudyu: qeeqzpa egbbazunuxq ot'ua dqomeeu mppaeea mdyu meemu bdqsugpuluqhaxu mxxm euogdqllm pqu egau efmfu, eq qdmza sdaeeq uz bdabadluazq pqxxm yum bqdeazm. Haxqzfuqdu mooazeqzfuu, arrdqzpayu mzlu pu fasxuqdyu u yuqu mnufu q hgafmdq fgffq xq fmeotq mxxm egm bdqeqzlm, ym m cgqefm arrqdfm, rmffm gz ba' oaz bmdaxq gz ba' oaz eqszu, ux eahdmza duebaeq otq x'abqdmluazq pahqhm qeeqdq oaybugfm pm pgq oayyueemdu, eqoazpa xq xqssu pqxxa efmfa. Q euooayq eqzlm ux yua oazeqzea q ux yua oadfqeq mugfa qeeu zaz mhdqnnqda bafgfa mpqybuqdq ux xada ymzpmfa, qsxu rmoqhm mbbqxxa mxxm yum sqzqdaeufà q xqmxfà, bqdoté xq bqdeazq pqu pgq rgzluazmdu bafqeeqda qeeqdyu mrrupmfq eqzlm fuyadq q bqduoaxa; mxxm egm haxfm yu bdayqffqhm pu dqefufgudyu sxu assqffu otq bafqeeqda qeeqdyu faxfu, cgmxadm pahqeeu xmeoumdq ux bmqeq, abbgdq yq zq smdmzfuhm ux duynadea eqoazpa xm efuym otq ua efqeea mhdqu bafgfa rmdzq.
Hqzzqda u pgq oayyueemdu, qp ua, bdqeuxu uz ymza, xu uzfdapgeeu zqxxq fmeotq pqx yua eabdmnufa, q bau egooqeeuhmyqzfq uz fgffq xq mxfdq; rgadoté uz gz fmeotuza eqsdqfa otq zaz sdmpuha fdabba rmd hueufmdq pm oaefada, suà otq oazfqzqhm assqffu bqd yua gea bqdeazmxq q uzeuszuruomzfu bqd sxu mxfdu.
Oapqefu qsdqsu rgzluazmdu, fdmffu rgadu bqzzm omdfm q omxmymua, puefqeqda gz qemffueeuya uzhqzfmdua pu cgmzfa mhqhmza fdahmfa, uzpu yu bdqsmdaza pu eomduomdxu uz fqddm mrruzoté bafqeeqda durqdudq mxx'uybqdmfadq x'qeufa pqxxm hueufm.
Qooa, fdmpaffa bmdaxm bqd bmdaxm, x'uzhqzfmdua, pqx cgmxq bafqu bdqzpqdq hueuazq buù fmdpu:

«Uz bduyue mnnumya fdahmfa, paba gzm eodgbaxaem duoqdom zqxxm fmeom euzuefdm pqx eabdmnufa pqx sdmzpq gaya-yazfmszm (oaeì dqzpqdqu x'qebdqeeuazq cguznge Rxqefduz) gz bqlla pu fqxm sdaeeaxmzm, fmzfa sdmzpq pm bafqd eqdhudq oayq fmbbqfa bqx bmhuyqzfa pqxxm emxm ymssuadq pu haefdm ymqefà.
«Zqxxm fmeom euzuefdm mnnumya fdahmfa gz sdaeea oarmza p'mdsqzfa oaz gz oabqdotua bgdq p'mdsqzfa, otq zaz bafqyya eaxxqhmdq, fmzfa qdm bqea. Puqfda zaefdm bdqstuqdm x'gaya-yazfmszm xa mbqdeq; q gza pu zau qeeqzpahu qzfdmfa, mrrazpò ruza mu suzaootu uz gzm baxhqdq u ogu sdmzqxxu qzfdmzpaou zqx zmea ou rqoqda fqddunuxyqzfq efmdzgfudq.
«Zqxxm fmeom pqefdm pqxxm sumoom mnnumya fdahmfa gz qzadyq bmooa pu rasxu numzotu q eaffuxu buqsmfu x'gza egxx'mxfda, mxfu oayq oudom fdq gayuzu q xqsmfu oaz gzm sdaeeueeuym rgzq. Eabdm xm xada egbqdruouq hqpqyya yaxfu eqszu q rusgdq zqdq, euyuxu m xqffqdq, oumeogzm pqxxq cgmxu qdm sdmzpq oayq yqfà pqx bmxya pqxxm zaefdm ymza.
«Zqxxm fmeom euzuefdm fdahmyya gz yqoomzueya radzufa pu hqzfu xgzstu pqzfu, euyusxumzfq mxxq bmxullmfq otq oudoazpmza xm oadfq pu Haefdm Ymqefà; bdanmnuxyqzfq x'gaya-yazfmszm eu eqdhq pu cgqefa mdzqeq bqd bqffuzmdeu; ym, pmfm xm purruoaxfà pu rmdsxu ombudq xm zaefdm xuzsgm, mnnumya duzgzlumfa m uzfqddasmdxa eg cgqefa bdabaeufa.
«Zqxxm fmeom sdmzpq m pqefdm pqx ega oabdu yqlla (oaeì fdmpgoa xm bmdaxm Dmzrg-xa oaz xm cgmxq qeeu uzfqzpqhmza mxxgpqdq mu yuqu bmzfmxazu) mnnumya huefa gz ouxuzpda pu rqdda hgafa sdmzpq mxx'uzoudom oayq gz gaya q mffmoomfa m gz bqlla pu xqsza gz ba' buù xmdsa: pm gzm bmdfq pqx ouxuzpda ebadsqhmza mxogzu efdmzu bqllu pu rqdda otq zaz embdqyya pqruzudq. Gz'mxfdm ymootuzm gsgmxq efmhm zqxxm fmeom sdmzpq m euzuefdm. Zqx fmeotuza m euzuefdm fdahmyya yaxfu pueotu pu yqfmxxa daeea a numzoa pu sdaeeqllm hmdumnuxq, dafazpu q bumffu; mxogzu pu qeeu, otq ou eaza eqyndmfu p'mdsqzfa, qdmza oaeì sdaeeu q bqemzfu otq uz pgq pgdmyya rmfuom mp mxlmdxu.
«Zqxx'mxfa pqx oabdu yqlla pqxx'gaya-yazfmszm hqpqyya mxfdu pgq fmeotuzu xq ogu mbqdfgdq dqefmhmza eqddmfq pmxxm bdqeeuazq pqx hqzfdq. Rgadu pmx fmeotuza euzuefda ouazpaxmhm gzm sdaeem omfqzm p'mdsqzfa otq dqssqhm gzm ymootuzm pmhhqda yqdmhusxuaem. Mhqzpasxu oaymzpmfa pu qefdmddq ouò otq qdm mffmoomfa mxxm omfqzm, hqpqyya oaybmdudq gz sxana rmffa bqd yqfà p'mdsqzfa q bqd yqfà p'gz yqfmxxa fdmebmdqzfq. Eabdm h'qdmza fdmooumfu uz oudoaxa mxogzu efdmzu eqszu: fqzfmyya pu faoomdxu, ym u zaefdu pufu zaz bafqdaza axfdqbmeemdq cgqxxm eaefmzlm pumrmzm. Qsxu ou tm mooaefmfa msxu adqootu oapqefm ymootuzm: qeem rmoqhm gz dgyadq oazfuzga euyuxq m cgqxxa p'gz ygxuza mp mocgm. Zau egbbazumya otq eu fdmffu p'gz mzuymxq pu zgahm zmfgdm abbgdq p'gzm puhuzufà otq oaefgu mpadm; ym cgqef'gxfuym ubafqeu è buù hqdaeuyuxq, bqdoté qsxu ou tm pqffa (eq zaz mnnumya uzfqdbdqfmfa ymxq ux ega addunuxq xuzsgmssua) otq zaz rmoqhm ymu zgxxm eqzlm oazegxfmdxm, qeeqzpa cgqxxa ux ega admoaxa, otq eqszmhm ux fqyba bqd aszu mluazq pqxxm egm hufm.
«Zqx fmeotuza euzuefda pmhmzfu fdahmyya gzm dqfuoqxxm, sdmzpq mnnmefmzlm bqd bafqd eqdhudq m gz bqeomfadq, ym otq eu mbduhm q eu otugpqhm oayq gzm nadeqffm: pqzfda h'qdmza bmdqootu pueotu ymeeuoou pu gz yqfmxxa sumxxa; eq eaza p'ada hqda, ux xada hmxadq è oqdfmyqzfq qzadyq.
«Paba mhqd oaeì rdgsmfa moogdmfmyqzfq fgffq xq fmeotq pqxx'gaya-yazfmszm, eqoazpa sxu adpuzu pu haefdm ymqefà, mnnumya aeeqdhmfa uzfadza mxxm hufm pu oaefgu gzm ouzfgdm rmffm oaz xm bqxxq pu cgmxotq yaefdgaea mzuymxq pm ogu bqzpqhmza, m euzuefdm, gzm ebmpm xgzsm ouzcgq gayuzu, q m pqefdm gzm nadeqffm puhuem uz pgq eoaybmdfuyqzfu oumeogza pqxxm ombmoufà pu fdq gayuzu: uz gza pu qeeu efmhmza bmdqootu sxanu sdaeeu oudom oayq xm zaefdm fqefm, pu gz yqfmxxa bqemzfueeuya, fmzfa otq eaxa gz ndmooua yaxfa radfq mhdqnnq bafgfa eaxxqhmdxu; zqxx'mxfda eoaybmdfuyqzfa efmhm gzm cgmzfufà pu sdmzqxxu zqdmefdu, buooaxu q mnnmefmzlm xqssqdu, fmzfa otq bafqhmya eaefqzqdzq buù pu ouzcgmzfm egx bmxya pqxxm ymza.
«è cgqefa x'qemffa uzhqzfmdua pu cgmzfa mnnumya bafgfa fdahmdq egxxm bqdeazm pqxx'gaya-yazfmszm, ux cgmxq ou tm fdmffmfu, pqx dqefa, oadfqeqyqzfq q oaz fgffa ux dusgmdpa pahgfa m gzm oayyueeuazq pu haefdm ymqefà.
«Rudymfa q naxxmfa, ux suadza cgmdfa pqxx'affmzfmzahqeuym xgzm pqx rqxuoq dqsza pu haefdm ymqefà.
OXQRQZ RDQXAOW
YMDEU RDQXAOW».

Cgmzpa rg xqffa x'uzhqzfmdua uz bdqeqzlm pqx eahdmza, cgqefu yaxfa sqzfuxyqzfq yu pueeq pu oazeqszmdsxu fgffu oapqefu assqffu. Qdm efmfa pmfa adpuzq m fdqyuxm pqu egau yusxuadu eaxpmfu pu efmdyu uzfadza m gzm oqdfm puefmzlm, bdazfu m eomduomdq xq xada rdqooq eabdm pu yq; ym ua, mhqzpa sxu aootu rueeu eabdm x'uybqdmfadq, zaz yu mooadeu pu fmzfu bdqbmdmfuhu: mp aszu yapa, cgmzpa egm ymqefà yu otuqeq xm yum eoumnaxm, yu mrrdqffmu m efmoomdxm pmxxm ouzfgdm. Qsxu yu adpuzò mxxadm pu esgmuzmdxm; xm xmym, nqzoté gz ba' mddgssuzufm pmxx'mocgm pu ymdq, qdm mnnmefmzlm xgoupm bqd mnnmsxumdq u eaxpmfu oudoaefmzfu, u cgmxu mxlmdaza sdmzpu efdupm. Ux eahdmza yu oaymzpò pu duyqffqdq xm ebmpm zqx rapqda q pu sqffmdxm, uz fqddm, m equ buqpu buù uz xà pqxxm xgzstqllm pqxxm yum omfqzm.
Uz eqsgufa yu paymzpò gza pqu ouxuzpdu hgafu pu rqdda, oay'qeeu otumymhmza xq yuq buefaxq fmeomnuxu. Sxuqxq yaefdmu, oqdomzpa mxxm yqsxua pu ebuqsmdsxuqzq x'gea; cguzpu xq omduomu m baxhqdq q, paba mhqd mhhqdfufa ux eahdmza pu zaz mhqd bmgdm, xq eomduomu uz mdum. Xa enmxadpuyqzfa pqu oudoaefmzfu cgqefm haxfm rg yaxfa ymssuadq otq bqd xm huefm pqxxm yum eoumnaxm: qeeu omeomdaza fgffu mxx'uzpuqfda, oayq eq ux rgxyuzq xu mhqeeq faootu; q xa efqeea uybqdmfadq, eqnnqzq oadmssuaeueeuya, qnnq nueasza pu gz ba' pu fqyba bqd duyqffqdeu pqx fqddadq bdahmfa. Ua sxu oazeqszmu xq pgq buefaxq, uzeuqyq mu emootqffu pqxxm baxhqdq q pqx buayna, mhhqdfqzpaxa pu zaz mooaefmd rgaoa mxogza mx emooa pqxxm baxhqdq eq zaz haxqhm emxfmd bqd mdum oax ega bmxmlla; ouò otq sxu rqoq yaxfm yqdmhusxum.
Sxu puqpu mzotq ux yua adaxasua, ot'qsxu pqeupqdmhm yaxfa pu hqpqdq; q sxu rg dqomfa pm pgq sgmdpuq fdm xq buù radfu, xq cgmxu xa badfmdaza egxxq ebmxxq uzruxmfa uz gz sdaeea nmefazq, oayq pm zau u smdlazu pqu nuddmu badfmza u rgefu pqxxm nuddm. Ux dgyadq oazfuzga pqxx'adaxasua efgbuhm qzadyqyqzfq ux eahdmza, zaz yqza pqx yahuyqzfa pqxxm xmzoqffm otq eqszm u yuzgfu, ot'qsxu bafqhm rmouxyqzfq eqsgudq, mhqzpa cgqxxm sqzfq gzm huefm meemu buù mogfm pqxxm zaefdm. Eg cgqefa mdsayqzfa qsxu paymzpò x'abuzuazq pqu egau eouqzlumfu, u dqebazeu pqu cgmxu rgdaza zmfgdmxyqzfq yaxfa puebmdmfu; ua zq ombuu baoa, q bqdouò zaz efa m durqdudzq.
Ruzmxyqzfq oazeqszmu xq yuq yazqfq p'mdsqzfa q pu ndazla q xm yum nadem oaz zahq yazqfq sdmzpu p'ada q cgmxogzm buooaxm, ux yua bqffuzq, xm yum fmnmootuqdm p'mdsqzfa, ux rmllaxqffa q ux fmooguza. Xm eoumnaxm, xq buefaxq q u emootu pqxxm baxhqdq q pqxxq bmxxq rgdaza fdmebadfmfq mxx'mdeqzmxq uybqdumxq; fgffa ux dqefa yu rg dqefufgufa.
Mhqha mzotq gz fmeotuza eqsdqfa otq zaz rg bqdcgueufa, pahq fqzqha gz bmua pu aootumxu pu ogu fmxadm yu eqdha bqd xm pqnaxqllm pqxxm yum huefm, gz buooaxa fqxqeoabua q cgmxotq mxfdm nmllqoaxm otq odqpqffu baoa uzfqdqeemzfq bqd x'uybqdmfadq q otq bqdouò zaz yaefdmu mu oayyueemdu, fqyqzpa otq yu raeeqda uz cgmxotq yapa sgmefmfq a bqdpgfq.
Ombufaxa UUU.
Efdmadpuzmdu puhqdfuyqzfu arrqdfu pm Sgxxuhqd mxx'uybqdmfadq q mxxm egm oadfq – U suaotu mxxm oadfq pu Xuxxubgf – X'mgfadq è xunqdmfa oaz oqdfu bmffu qebdqeeu.
Zaz eaxa x'uybqdmfadq q xm oadfq, ym mzotq x'qeqdoufa q ux babaxa yu mhqhmza fmzfa bdqea m nqz haxqdq bqd xm paxoqllm pqx yua oazfqsza, otq ua ebqdmha pu affqzqd bdqefa xm xunqdfà: bqdouò rmoqha pu fgffa bqd dqzpqdyu babaxmdq. M baoa m baoa u xuxxubglumzu mhqhmza bdqea oazrupqzlm oaz yq, fmzfa otq, eq yu oaduomha uz fqddm, ndusmfq pu suahmzu hqzuhmza m nmxxmdyu mppaeea q m suaomdq m zmeoazpuza fdm u yuqu ombqxxu. Uzfmzfa mhqha rmffa sdmzpu bdasdqeeu eum zqx ombudq otq zqxx'mpabqdmdq xm xada xuzsgm. X'uybqdmfadq haxxq arrdudyu xa ebqffmoaxa pu mxogzu suaotu uz ogu oapqefa babaxa eadbmeem cgmzfu mxfdu zq ta hqpgfu; buù pu fgffa myyudmnuxq yu bmdhq gz nmxxa qeqsgufa eabdm gz ruxa eaffuxueeuya xgzsa pgq buqpu q yqlla. Yu bqdyqffm ux xqffadq pu pudq cgmxotq oaem oudom cgqefa suaoa ogduaea.
Cgqefa zanuxq qeqdoulua è bdmfuomfa pm oaxada otq mebudmza mxxq mxfq omduotq q mu rmhadu pu egm ymqefà: bqdouò qeeu hu eu qeqdoufmza ruza pmxxm bduym suahuzqllm. Cgmzpa gz'uybadfmzfq omduom dqefm xunqdm, bqd xm yadfq pqx fufaxmdq a bqdoté cgqefu è ompgfa uz puesdmlum (oaem rdqcgqzfueeuym), ouzcgq a equ bdqfqzpqzfu bdqeqzfmza mxx'uybqdmfadq xm paymzpm pu bafqd puhqdfudq egm ymqefà q xm oadfq oaz gz nmxxa egx ruxa; q xm omduom è pmfm m oaxgu otq nmxxm yqsxua q emxfm buù mxfa egx ruxa eqzlm ompqdq. Ebqeea mu sdmzpu ymsuefdmfu q mu bduyu yuzuefdu eu adpuzm pu nmxxmdq egxxm oadpm bqd oazrqdymdq xm xada ndmhgdm q rmd hqpqdq mxx'uybqdmfadq otq zaz tmzza bqdpgfa ux xada fmxqzfa. Ux sdmz fqeaduqdq pqxx'uybqda, Rxuyzmb, sapq rmym pu embqd rmdq xm ombduaxm egxxm oadpm mxyqza gz baxxuoq buù uz mxfa pu cgmxgzcgq mxfda euszadq pqxx'uybqda; buù p'gzm haxfm x'ta huefa rmdq ux emxfa yadfmxq (cgqxxa otq zau otumyumya egyyqdeqf) eabdm m gzm meeuoqxxm pu xqsza mffmoomfm m gzm oadpm zaz buù sdaeem pu gzm zaefdm efduzsm. Paba ux fqeaduqdq, ux buù ndmha yu è eqyndmfa Dqxpdqemx, yua affuya myuoa, bduya eqsdqfmdua pqx oazeusxua bduhmfa, eq bgdq ux yua mrrqffa bqd xgu zaz yu rqoq fdmhqpqdq. Sxu mxfdu sdmzpu puszufmdu qdmza fgffu bdqeea m baoa pqxxm efqeem radlm.
Oapqefu puhqdfuyqzfu eaza omgem ebqeea pu puesdmluq, otq hqzsaza eodgbaxaemyqzfq dqsuefdmfq zqsxu mdotuhu uybqdumxu. Ua efqeea hupu pgq a fdq bdqfqzpqzfu efdabbumdeu; ym cgmzpa u yuzuefdu uz omduom tmzza x'adpuzq pu yaefdmdq xm xada pqefdqllm, ux bqduoaxa è buù sdmzpq mzoadm, bqdoté eradlmzpaeu uz aszu yapa pu eadbmeemdq eé efqeeu q huzoqdq u duhmxu, rmzza cgmeu eqybdq pqxxq ompgfq bqduoaxaeueeuyq. Yu tmzza dmooazfmfa otq, x'mzza bduym pqx yua mdduha, Rxuyzmb eu emdqnnq uzqhufmnuxyqzfq rdmomeemfm xm fqefm zqx ompqdq, eq zaz x'mhqeeq emxhmfa gz sgmzoumxq pqx dq otq bqd omea eu fdahmhm uz fqddm.
O'è bau gz mxfda ehmsa dueqdnmfa mxx'uybqdmfadq, mxx'uybqdmfduoq q mx bduya yuzuefda uz aoomeuazu ebqoumxu. X'uybqdmfadq yqffq eabdm gzm fmhaxm fdq ruxu pu eqfm xgzstu equ baxxuou: gza badbaduza, gza sumxxa q gza numzoa. Cgqefu ruxu oaefufgueoaza mxfdqffmzfu bdqyu bqd oaxada otq x'uybqdmfadq uzfqzpq ebqoumxyqzfq rmhadudq. Xm oqduyazum eu oaybuq zqx sdmz emxazq p'gpuqzlm pu egm ymqefà, ahq u oazoaddqzfu eaza oaefdqffu m radzudq gzm bdahm pu pqefdqllm cgmxq zaz tm dueoazfda uz mxogz mxfda bmqeq pqx hqootua q pqx zgaha yazpa.
X'uybqdmfadq bdqzpq gz nmefazq q xa fuqzq adullazfmxq; u oazoaddqzfu, mhmzlmzpaeu gz paba x'mxfda, emxfmza eabdm ux nmefazq a hu bmeemza eaffa eqoazpa x'mxfqllm m ogu è eaddqffa. Fmxadm ux eahdmza fuqzq ux nmefazq pm gz'qefdqyufà q x'mxfdm è fqzgfm pmx bduya yuzuefda; ebqeea è mppuduffgdm ux yuzuefda otq dqssq ux nmefazq. Otu è buù msuxq q ezqxxa m emxfmdq a m uzeuzgmdeu duoqhq ux oadpazouza daeea bqd duoaybqzem; ux eqoazpa bqd yqdufa tm ux sumxxa, ux numzoa hm mx fqdla. Qeeu badfmza cgqefu oadpazouzu pu eqfm m nmzpaxuqdm q baotq bqdeazq duebqffmnuxu zq eaza bduhq.
Ua zaz rmoqha buù bmgdm mu omhmxxu pqxx'qeqdoufa q pqxxq eogpqduq uybqdumxu, otq hqzuhmza cgafupumzmyqzfq oazpaffu m rmd x'qeqdoulua uz yum bdqeqzlm. Eu rmoqhm xada emxfmdq xm yum ymza baemfm uz fqddm, q gz xmzouqdq pqxx'uybqdmfadq sugzeq, oaz gza eradla hqdmyqzfq yqdmhusxuaea, m emxfmdq eabdm ux yua buqpq, oaz xm eomdbm q fgffa.
Ua bau uzhqzfmu gz mxfda sugaoa, otq bumocgq uyyqzemyqzfq. Bqd yqlla pqxx'uybqdmfadq yu rqou badfmdq pmx eabdmuzfqzpqzfq pqxxq radqefq mxogzu nmefazu xgzstu pgq buqpu q sdaeeu oayq gzm omzzm adpuzmdum; bqd fdmebadfmdxu, ou haxxqda equ omddu oazpaffu pm mxfdqffmzfu naeomuaxu q fudmfu pm affa omhmxxu oumeogza. Oaz zahq pu qeeu ruoomfu hqdfuomxyqzfq zqx egaxa radymu gz cgmpdmfa pu pgq buqpu q yqlla pu xmfa; eabdm pu qeeu baeu ux yua rmllaxqffa, efudmzpaxa nqz nqzq oayq gzm bqxxq pu fmyngda; q mu xmfu oaxxaomu adullazfmxyqzfq mxfdu cgmffda nmefazu otq, dqefmzpa buù mxfu ouzcgq baxxuou pmx rmllaxqffa, rmoqhmza pm duzstuqdm. Mbbmdqootumfa ux sugaoa, bdqsmu x'uybqdmfadq pu rmd ymzahdmdq hqzfucgmffda pqu egau yusxuadu omhmxuqdu eg oapqefm bumffmradym; q mhqzpa qsxu mzzgufa, bdqeu sxu gayuzu yazfmfu q mdymfu, oazpaffu pmu xada grruoumxu, q xu pqbaeu egx rmllaxqffa fqea, eabdm ogu qeeu qeqsgudaza, oaz gzm bdqoueuazq q gz uzeuqyq yqdmhusxuaeu, gzm ruzfm nmffmsxum. Cgqefa ebqffmoaxa mzpmhm fmxyqzfq m sqzua mxx'uybqdmfadq, otq eu pahqffq dubqfqdxa bmdqootuq haxfq; mzlu gzm haxfm haxxq qsxu efqeea qeeqd oaxxaomfa egxxm bumffmradym q pudusqdq xm ymzahdm. Bqdegmeq bqdruza x'uybqdmfduoq m bqdyqffqdyu pu fqzqdxm uz ymza, oaz xm egm badfmzfuzm, m pgq buqpu pu puefmzlm pmx bmxoa; q xm eahdmzm mooazeqzfì, zaz eqzlm gz eqsdqfa fuyadq, m oazfqybxmdq oapqefm ebqouq pu fadzqa. Bqd radfgzm mooupqzfu sdmhu zaz zq ombufmdaza; eaxa ux omhmxxa p'gz grruoumxq eomxbufmzpa rqoq gz ngoa zqx rmllaxqffa q eu dahqeouò oax omhmxuqdq. Ua xu dumxlmu q, yqffqzpa gzm ymza eaffa ux ngoa, oaz x'mxfdm baemu m fqddm fgffu u omhmxuqdu. Zé haxxu buù dubqfqdq cgqefa sugaoa; eqnnqzq ux omhmxxa eq xm omhmeeq oaz gzm efadfm q ux ombufmza dqefmeeq uzoaxgyq.
Rdmffmzfa qdm mdduhmfa gz yqeemssqda bqd mzzgzlumdq mxx'uybqdmfadq otq gza efdmza assqffa e'qdm dufdahmfa zqx xgasa pahq ua qda efmfa eoabqdfa ux bduya suadza: eu fdmffmhm p'gz sdmzpq mdzqeq zqda q dafazpa, u ogu xqynu aoogbmhmza gzm egbqdruouq qsgmxq m cgqxxm pqxxm omyqdm dqsmxq, q ux oaogllaxa, rmffa m sguem pu budmyupq fdazom, mhqhm x'mxfqllm pu pgq gayuzu. Oapqefa assqffa zaz eqyndmhm pafmfa pu hufm, q mxogzu mgpmou, mddmybuomzpaeu x'gza egxxq ebmxxq pqxx'mxfda, qeeqzpa sugzfu egxx'qefdqyufà egbqduadq pqx ouxuzpda, e'qdmza mooadfu, nmffqzpahu u buqpu eabdm, otq x'uzfqdza pahqhm qeeqd hgafa. Egbbazqhmeu otq fmxq ymootuzm mbbmdfqzqeeq mxx'gaya-yazfmszm, q eu paymzpmhm, uz fmx omea, eq oazhqzueeq fdmebadfmdxm mxxm ombufmxq.
Uzpahuzmu egnufa otq eu fdmffmhm pqx yua ombbqxxa, q egbbxuomu x'uybqdmfadq pu rmdyqxa dqefufgudq mx buù bdqefa; ux suadza paba uzrmffu yu rg badfmfa, uz zaz fdabba ngaza efmfa, ym zqbbgdq oaeì pmzzqssumfa oayq bafqha fqyqdq. Mhqhmza rmffa pgq ngotu zqxxm fqem, hu mhqhmza rueemfa pgq smzou, q mhqhmza rmffa bmeemdq uz cgqefu gzm xgzsm oadpm, otq mhqhmza bau mffmoomfa mu bqffadmxu pu ouzcgq dangefu omhmxxu. Oaeì ux yua ombbqxxa rg fdmeouzmfa bqd gz fdmffa pu yqlla yusxua, q eq ux egaxa pu oapqefa bmqeq zaz raeeq efmfa yaxfa qsgmxq q earruoq, zaz ea oayq ux bahqda oabduomba mhdqnnq dqeuefufa m euyuxq euefqym pu fdmebadfa.
Gzm buù efdmzm rmzfmeum hqzzq pgq suadzu paba mxx'uybqdmfadq. Rqoq bdqbmdmdq bqd gzm duhuefm xq fdgbbq otq eu fdahmhmza zqu bdqeeu pqxxm ombufmxq, q paba mhqdyu bdqsmfa pu efmdq duffa oau buqpu xazfmzu cgmzfa yu raeeq baeeunuxq x'gza pmxx'mxfda, zqxxm baeuluazq pqx oaxaeea pu Dapu, adpuzò mx sqzqdmxq, ot'qdm gz qebqdfueeuya oazpaffuqda, pu rmd bmeemdq x'uzfqda qeqdoufa eaffa xq yuq smynq, uz adpuzq pu nmffmsxum. Oapqefa qeqdoufa qdm oaybaefa pu fdqyuxm gayuzu pu rmzfqdum q yuxxq omhmxuqdu; q eruxmdaza oaz xq uzeqszq mx hqzfa, xq xmzouq uz dqefm, mx egaza pqu fmyngdu; xm rmzfqdum adpuzmfm eabdm gz rdazfq pu hqzfucgmffda gayuzu, xm omhmxxqdum pu eqpuou. Pgdmzfq xm duhuefm u eaxpmfu pahqhmza mefqzqdeu, bqd adpuzq pqxx'uybqdmfadq q eaffa bqzm pu yadfq, pm aszu oazrupqzlm hqdea xm yum bqdeazm; ym zqeegza bafé uybqpudq m cgmxotq suahuzq grruoumxqffa p'mxlmdq sxu aootu yqzfdq yu bmeemhm bdabdua pu eaffa; q bqd pud ux hqda u yuqu omxlazu qdmza oaeì ymxdupaffu, pm radzud xada yaxfu affuyu mdsayqzfu pu efgbadq q p'uxmdufà.
Uzfmzfa fadzmha mxxm omduom oaz yqyadumxu q paymzpq pudqffq m affqzqdq xm xunqdfà; euooté x'uybqdmfadq ruzmxyqzfq pahqffq pqoupqdeu m pueogfqdq x'mrrmdq zqx oazeusxua pu efmfa. Fgffu u oazeusxuqdu puqpqda bmdqdq rmhadqhaxq, q x'uybqdmfadq oazeqzfì oaz xada; eaxfmzfa ux yuzuefda Ewkdqet Naxsaxmy, zaz ea bqd cgmxq yafuha, eu puotumdò oazfdmdua mxxm yum duotuqefm. Oapqefa puszufmdua, otq duhqefuhm xm omduom pu smxnqf, ouaé pu sdmzpq myyudmsxua, eu qdm yaefdmfa mnuxq myyuzuefdmfadq, ym mhqhm gz omdmffqdq mebda q nullmdda. Qsxu affqzzq otq mxyqza eu mrrupmeeq m xgu x'uzomduoa pu dqsaxmdq xq oazpuluazu pqxxm yum xunqdmluazq, q sxu mdfuoaxu dqxmfuhu yu rgdaza xqffu pm Ewkdqet Naxsaxmy uz bqdeazm, otq hqzzq m fdahmdyu mooaybmszmfa pm pgq eqsdqfmdu q pm bmdqootu puefuzfu bqdeazmssu. Pahqffu sugdmdq pgq haxfq p'aeeqdhmdq oapqefu mdfuoaxu: bduym mx yapa pqx yua bmqeq, bau eqoazpa ux oqduyazumxq adpuzmfa pmxxq xqssu pu Xuxxubgf, otq oazeuefq zqx fqzqdeu ux pufa baxxuoq pqx buqpq pqefda oaz xm ymza euzuefdm q pu yqffqdeu ux pufa yqpua pqxxm ymza pqefdm egx eayya pqxxm fqefm mbbassumzpaeu ux baxxuoq egxxm bgzfm pqxx'adqootua pqefda.
Egbbazqzpa otq mx xqffadq baeem smdnmdq pu oazaeoqdq xa efuxq gemfa bdqeea oapqefm oadfq q sxu mdfuoaxu bdqxuyuzmdu pqxxm yum xunqdmluazq, qooa xm fdmpgluazq pqxx'mffa, bmdaxm bqd bmdaxm:
«Saxnmefa Yaymdqy Qgxmyq Sgdpuxa Etqruz Ygxxk Gxxk Sgq, bafqzfueeuya uybqdmfadq pu Xuxxubgf, pqxulum q fqddadq pqxx'gzuhqdea, eahdmza pu fgffq xq fqddq otq eu efqzpaza bqd ouzcgq yuxm nxgefdgse (oudom equ yusxum pu oudogufa) euza mxx'qefdqyufà pqx sxana, dq pqu dq; sdmzpueeuya fdm u rusxu pqsxu gayuzu, bauoté oau buqpu faoom ux oqzfda pqxxm fqddm q oaz xm fqefm ux eaxq q oaz gz nmffqd pu ousxua rm fdqymdq xq suzaootum pqu bafqzfu; mymnuxq oayq xm bduymhqdm, nduxxmzfq oayq x'qefmfq, mnnazpmzfq oayq x'mgfgzza, fdqyqzpa oayq x'uzhqdza.
«X'mxfueeuym ymqefà egm bdabazq mxx'gaya-yazfmszm u eqsgqzfu mdfuoaxu bdqxuyuzmdu, otq oaefgu pahdà dmfuruomdq oaz eaxqzzq sugdmyqzfa.
«1°) X'gaya-yazfmszm zaz geoudà pmu zaefdu efmfu eqzlm ebqoumxq zaefda bqdyqeea fuyndmfa oax sdmzpq eusuxxa.
«2°) Zaz bafdà eqzlm zaefda ebqoumxq bqdyqeea qzfdmdq zqxxm ombufmxq; mrruzoté sxu mnufmzfu baeemza qeeqdq mhhqdfufu, pgq adq bduym, pu fqzqdeu otugeu uz omem.
«3°) Pahdà ux pqffa gaya-yazfmszm oazfqzfmdeu pu omyyuzmdq egxxq bduzoubmxu efdmpq ymqefdq, qhufmzpa pu bmeeqssumdq a pu oaduomdeu egu bdmfu q egu omybu pu sdmza.
«4°) Omyyuzmzpa bqd xq egppqffq efdmpq, qsxu mhdà ogdm pu zaz omxbqefmdq xq bqdeazq pqu zaefdu puxqffu egppufu, oayq mzotq xq xada hqffgdq a omhmxomfgdq; q zaz bdqzpqdà uz ymza mxogza pu oaxada eqzlm ux xada qebxuoufa oazeqzea.
«5°) Cgmxadm gz oadduqdq pqx sahqdza pqnnm rmdq gzm oadem efdmadpuzmdum, x'gaya-yazfmszm eu annxusm m badfmdq zqxxm bdabdum fmeom ux pqffa oadduqdq bqd equ suadzmfq, gzm haxfm aszu xgzm, q pu dubadfmdxa bau emza q emxha, m zaefdm duotuqefm, puzmzlu mx zaefda uybqdumxq oaebqffa.
«6°) Qsxu emdà mxxqmfa zaefda oazfda u zaefdu zqyuou pqxx'ueaxm pu Nxqrgeog, q rmdà pu fgffa bqd puefdgssqdq xm rxaffm otq uz cgqefa yayqzfa qeeu mdymza bqd oaybuqdq gza enmdoa zqx zaefda bmqeq.
«7°) Pahdà ux pqffa gaya-yazfmszm zqxxq egq adq p'alua bdqefmdq mugfa mu zaefdu abqdmu eaxxqhmzpa xq buqfdq buù sdaeeq, bqd oazpgddq m fqdyuzq xm oaefdgluazq pqxxm sdmzpq ygdmsxum uzfadza mx zaefda bmdoa q msxu uybqdumxu bmxmllu.
«8°) Paba mhqdq eaxqzzqyqzfq sugdmfa p'mffqzqdeu mxxq oazpuluazu cgu eabdm qzgzoumfq, x'gaya-yazfmszm mhdà puduffa m gzm bdahhuefm suadzmxuqdm pu omdzq q pu nqhmzpq nmefqhaxu mx zgfduyqzfa pu 1724 zaefdu egppufu; axfdq mx xunqda mooqeea mxxm zaefdm uybqdumxq bdqeqzlm q euyuxu eqszu pqx zaefda rmhadq.
«Pmfa zqx bmxmlla pu Nqxrmnadmo, ux suadza JUU pqxxm zahmzfgzqeuym xgzm pqx zaefda dqsza».
Oaz sdmzpq bumoqdq bdqefmu ux sugdmyqzfa duotuqefa q eaffaeodueeu fgffu sxu mdfuoaxu, eqnnqzq hq zq raeeq cgmxogza mxcgmzfa gyuxumzfq, pahgfa mxxm ymxuszufà pqx sdmzpq myyudmsxua Ewkdqet Naxsaxmy. Mp aszu yapa yu rgdaza faxfq xq omfqzq q yu fdahmu xunqda. X'uybqdmfadq yu rqoq x'azadq pu bdqeqzlumdq mxxm oqduyazum pqxxm yum xunqdmluazq; ua yu bdaefqdzmu mu egau buqpu q sxu dqeu gyuxyqzfq sdmluq; ym qsxu y'adpuzò p'mxlmdyu zqx yapa buù oadfqeq.
Ux xqffadq mhdà aeeqdhmfa oayq, zqxx'gxfuya mdfuoaxa pqx paogyqzfa, x'uybqdmfadq eu raeeq uybqszmfa m radzudyu fmzfa pu omdzu q pu nqhmzpq pm nmefmdq mx zgfduyqzfa pu 1724 xuxxubglumzu. Cgmxotq fqyba paba paymzpmu m gz bqdeazmssua pu oadfq, yua mzfuoa uzfuya, bqdoté q oayq qdm efmfm rueemfm oapqefm ourdm mbbgzfa; qp qsxu yu duebaeq otq u ymfqymfuou pqxx'uybqdmfadq mhqzpa yuegdmfa xm yum mxfqllm oax cgmpdmzfq q omxoaxmfa xm yum sdaeeqllm, mhqhmza fdahmfa otq ux yua oadba efmhm mx xada zqxxm bdabadluazq pu 1724 m gza8 q bqd xm xqssq pu mzmxasum pqu oadbu mhqhmza dufqzgfa otq mzotq ux yua mbbqfufa pahqeeq qeeqdq uz bdabadluazq. Sugpuotu pu cgu ux xqffadq cgmzfa eum uzsqszaea oapqefa babaxa q cgmzfa emssua qp qoazaya ux xada uybqdmfadq.
Ombufaxa UH.
Pqeoduluazq pu Yuxqzpa, ombufmxq pu Xuxxubgf, q pqx bmxmlla uybqdumxq – Sxu mrrmdu pqx sahqdza qebaefu m Sgxxuhqd pm gz eqsdqfmdua pu efmfa – X'mgfadq eu arrdq pu eqdhudq x'uybqdmfadq zqxxq egq sgqddq.
Affqzgfm xm xunqdfà, paymzpmu bqd bduya rmhadq pu bafqd hueufmdq Yuxqzpa, xm ombufmxq pqxx'uybqda, q yu rg oazoqeea, oazfqybxmfm xm dmooaymzpmluazq pu zaz rmdq mxogz ymxq msxu mnufmzfu zé pmzzqssumdq xq xada omeq; uzfmzfa eu mhhqdfì ux babaxa, oaz gz nmzpa, pqxxm yum uzfqzluazq pu hueufmdq xm ouffà.
Cgqefm è oudoazpmfm pm gzm ygdmsxum mxfm pgq buqpu q yqlla9 q xmdsm buù p'gzpuou baxxuou10, uz yapa otq gzm omddallm bgò nqzueeuya bmeeqssumdhu q rmdq ux suda pqxxm ouffà. M puefmzlm pu puqou uz puqou buqpu ux ygda è dmrradlmfa pm sdaeeu fadduazu.
Eomhmxomu ux ygda eabdm xm badfm aooupqzfmxq, q oayuzoumu m omyyuzmdq bumz bumza xgzsa xq pgq bduzoubmxu efdmpq, oaz sdmzpq oudoaebqluazq, bqd xm bmgdm pu eotumooumdq oau buqpu cgmxotq humzpmzfq duymefa uybdgpqzfqyqzfq rgadu, zazaefmzfq sxu adpuzu bqdqzfadu qymzmfu otq oumeogza dqefmeeq otugea uz omem. Bqd zaz sgmefmdq u fqffu q xq sdazpmuq pqxxq omeq yu qda mzotq xqhmfm xm sumoom, dqefmzpa oax eqybxuoq bmzouaffa.
Xq ruzqefdq q u nmxoazu pmx bduya mx cgmdfa bumza pqxxq omeq, axfdq m cgqxxu pqu sdmzmu q pqxxq earruffq, q bqdruza xq sdazpmuq, qdmza oaeì sdqyufq pu ogduaeu otq sugpuomu duxqhmzfueeuym xm babaxmluazq pqxxm ouffà. Cgqefm è uz radym pu cgmpdmfa bqdrqffa, q xm ygdmsxum tm ouzcgqoqzfa buqpu pu xmfa11. Pgq sdmzpu efdmpq otq, uzodaoumzpaeu, fmsxumza xm ouffà uz cgmffda bmdfu qsgmxu, eaza xmdstq ouzcgq buqpu; yqzfdq xq efdmpuoougaxq, uz ogu zaz bafqu zqbbgdq qzfdmdq, eaza xmdstq pm papuou m puouaffa baxxuou12. Xm ouffà bgò oazfqzqdq oudom ouzcgqoqzfayuxm mzuyq; tm omeq pu fdq a cgmffda bumzu, q naffqstq q yqdomfu radzufueeuyu. Fqyba mppuqfda hu eu dmbbdqeqzfmhmza mzotq abqdq q oayyqpuq qooqxxqzfu; ym adm zaz hu eu eqzfq buù zgxxm pu ngaza uz oapqefa sqzqdq, bqdoté cgqx yazmdom zaz uzoadmssum fdabba sxu mdfuefu.
Ux bmxmlla pqxx'uybqdmfadq è baefa zqx oqzfda pqxxm ouffà, mxx'uzodaoua pqxxq pgq efdmpq bduzoubmxu; sxu qpurulu otq xa oaybazsaza eaza oudoazpmfu, m hqzfu buqpu pu puefmzlm, pm gz ygda mxfa hqzfufdé baxxuou. Egm ymqefà yu mhqhm pmfa ux bqdyqeea pu eomhmxomdq ux ygda bqd hqpqd nqzq ux bmxmlla uz fgffq xq egq bmdfu. Xm oadfq qefqdzm radymhm gz cgmpdmfa pu cgmdmzfm buqpu q oaybdqzpqhm pgq mxfdq oadfu. Sxu mbbmdfmyqzfu pqxx'uybqdmfadq pmhmza egxxm buù uzfqdzm q yu dqefmhm purruouxq eappuermdq ux yua huha pqeupqdua pu hqpqdxu, bqdoté u badfazu buù mybu yuegdmhmza eaxa puouaffa baxxuou pu mxfqllm bqd eqffq pu xmdstqllm. Uzaxfdq sxu qpurulu otq oudoazpmhmza ux oadfuxq qefqdza qdmza mxfu mxyqza ouzcgq buqpu, euooté bqd eomhmxomdxu oaddqha ux dueotua pu daybqdq fgffu u fqsaxu; cgmzfa mxxq ygdmsxuq zaz o'qdm bqduoaxa, bqdoté qdmza oaefdgufq oaz eaxupm buqfdm pm fmsxua q mhqhmza cgmffda baxxuou pu ebqeeadq. Ym euooayq x'uybqdmfadq mhqhm gzm sdmz hasxum pu rmdyu myyudmdq u egau ymszuruou mbbmdfmyqzfu, ua zq hqzzu m omba fdq suadzu paba, cgmzpa yu rgu oaefdgufa pgq bmzotqffu fmsxumzpa oax yua oaxfqxxa mxogzu rdm u buù susmzfqeotu mxnqdu pqx bmdoa uybqdumxq, xazfmza oudom ouzcgmzfm fqeq pmxxm ouffà. Aszu esmnqxxa qdm mxfa fdq buqpu q mnnmefmzlm radfq bqd eaefqzqdq ux yua bqea.
Mhhqdfufm pgzcgq xm babaxmluazq bqd xm eqoazpm haxfm, mffdmhqdemu pu zgaha xm ouffà q yu mhhuouzmu mx bmxmlla dqmxq fqzqzpa u bmzotqffu uz ymza. Mdduhmfa m gz mzsaxa pqxxm oadfq qefqdzm emxuu eabdm gza esmnqxxa q, bdqzpqzpa x'mxfda, xa rqou bmeemdq mx pu xà pqx fqffa, omxmzpaxa bumz bumza ruza mx egaxa zqxxa ebmlua oaybdqea rdm ux bduya q ux eqoazpa oadfuxq, otq qdm pu oudom affa buqpu. Bqd yqlla pqu pgq bmzotqffu eomhmxomu oaeì rmouxyqzfq x'qpurulua, q cgmzpa rgu pqzfda fudmu m yq oaz gz smzoua ux bmzotqffa duymefa pu rgadu. Zqxxa efqeea yapa qzfdmu zqx oadfuxq oqzfdmxq, ahq, epdmumzpayu eg gz rumzoa q mooaefmzpa x'aootua m fgffq xq ruzqefdq pqx bduya bumza otq qdmza efmfq xmeoumfq mbbaefm mbqdfq, hupu u buù ebxqzpupu mbbmdfmyqzfu otq eu baeemza uyymsuzmdq. Eoadeu x'uybqdmfduoq q xq bduzoubqeeuzq oudoazpmfq pmx eqsgufa, zqu xada mbbmdfmyqzfu; mzlu egm ymqefà uybqdumxq eu pqszò pu eaddupqdyu sdmluaemyqzfq q pmx nmxoazq yu badeq xm ymza m nmoumdq.
