Cgmzfa mxxq ogduaeufà otq eu fdahmhmza uz cgqx bmxmlla, zaz efa m rmdzq xm pqeoduluazq, bqdoté hasxua dueqdnmdxm bqd gzm sdmzpq abqdm suà cgmeu ruzufm, zqxxm cgmxq eu rm gzm pqeoduluazq sqzqdmxq pu oapqefa uybqda euza pmxxm egm razpmluazq, xm efadum pqu egau eahdmzu pgdmzfq yaxfu eqoaxu, mxogzq aeeqdhmluazu egxxq xada sgqddq, xm xada baxufuom, xq xqssu, xq xqffqdq q xm dqxusuazq pqx bmqeq, xm rxadm q xm rmgzm, sxu geu q oaefgyu pqsxu mnufmzfu q puhqdeu mxfdu mdsayqzfu ogduaeueeuyu q yudmnuxyqzfq gfuxu. Bqd adm yu nmefm dmooazfmdq ouò otq yu moomppq pgdmzfq u zahq yqeu otq duymeu uz oapqefa uybqda badfqzfaea.
Mhqha affqzgfa xm xunqdfà pm cguzpuou suadzu cgmzpa hupu hqzudq m omem yum Dqxpdqemx, eqsdqfmdua pu efmfa bqd sxu mrrmdu bmdfuoaxmdu. Qdm eqsgufa pm gz eaxa payqefuoa. Adpuzò mx ega oaootuqdq pu mffqzpqdxa m baotu bmeeu pmxxm badfm q yu bdqsò pu oazoqpqdsxu gz'adm pu mffqzluazq. Sxu rqou x'arrqdfm pu epdmumdyu bqd fqddm, bqd yqffqdq ux yua adqootua mx xuhqxxa pqxxm egm naoom, ym qsxu bdqrqdì ot'ua xa fqzqeeu uz ymza pgdmzfq ux oaxxacgua.
Qsxu oayuzouò oax oazsdmfgxmdeu yqoa pqxxm yum xunqdmluazq, m ogu eu hmzfò yapqefmyqzfq pu mhqdq gz ba' oazfdungufa; ym mssugzeq otq zaz x'mhdqu ymu affqzgfm eqzlm x'uzfqdqeeq otq hu mhqhm xm efqeem oadfq. «Bauoté» eassugzeq, «ux zaefda bmqeq, otq eqyndm oaeì rxadupa msxu efdmzuqdu, tm pgq sdmzpu bqduoaxu pm oaynmffqdq: mxx'uzfqdza gzm dmnnuaem xaffm pu bmdfufu q mxx'qefqdza x'uzhmeuazq pu ogu ou yuzmooum gz radyupmnuxq zqyuoa».
Oudom ux bduya bgzfa pahqfq embqdq otq pm buù pu eqffmzfm xgzq pgq bmdfufu eu oazfdmefmza ux bafqdq, eaffa u zayu pu fdmyqowemz q efmyqowemz, otq euszuruomza fmootu-mxfu q fmootu-nmeeu, bauoté u pgq bmdfufu eu puefuzsgaza mbbgzfa pmxxm ymssuadq a yuzadq mxfqllm pqu xada fmootu13. Eqyndm hqdmyqzfq otq u fmootu-mxfu oadduebazpmza yqsxua mx omdmffqdq pqxxq zaefdq xqssu; ym mp aszu yapa x'uybqdmfadq zaz hgax eqdhudeu otq pqu fmootu-nmeeu zqxx'myyuzuefdmluazq pqxxa efmfa q uz fgffu sxu grruou pubqzpqzfu pmxxm oadazm: mzlu bafqfq aeeqdhmdq otq egm ymqefà badfm u fmootu buù nmeeu mxyqza pu gz pdgdd otq aszu mxfda bqdeazmssua pu oadfq. (Ux pdgdd oadduebazpq mp gz cgmffadpuoqeuya pu baxxuoq).
«U pgq bmdfufu» oazfuzgò qsxu «eu apumza m fmx bgzfa pm zaz ymzsumdq zé nqdq zé bmdxmdq uzeuqyq. U fmootu-mxfu, eqoazpa u zaefdu omxoaxu, eaza buù zgyqdaeu, ym zau mnnumya ux bafqdq. Bqdò fqyumya meemu otq egm mxfqllm x'qdqpq bdqegzfuha pqxxm Oadazm mnnum gz ba' pu pqnaxq bqd u fmootu-mxfu; oqdfa, fgffu hqpaza otq gza pqu egau fmootu è buù mxfa pqxx'mxfda, eì pm rmdxa labbuomdq cgmzpa omyyuzm14.
«Adm, m cgqefq pueoadpuq uzfqefuzq eu mssugzsq xm yuzmooum p'gz'uzhmeuazq pm bmdfq pqsxu mnufmzfu pu Nxqrgeog. è cgqefa x'mxfda sdmzpq efmfa, ux buù bafqzfq pqxx'gzuhqdea paba ux zaefda, q cgmeu mxfdqffmzfa hmefa: bauoté, m pudhu xm hqdufà, u zaefdu ruxaearu pgnufmza yaxfa otq qeuefmza uz cgqefa yazpa cgqsxu efmfu pu ogu ou mhqfq bmdxmfa q otq emdqnnqda babaxmfu pm qeeqdu sdmzpu q sdaeeu oayq hau, mzotq bqdoté gz oqzfuzmua pu gayuzu pqxxm haefdm radlm oazegyqdqnnqda uz baoa fqyba fgffu u dmooaxfu q fgffu u nqefumyu pu egm ymqefà; euooté è buù odqpunuxq otq hau eumfq ompgfa pmxxm xgzm a pm gzm efqxxm. P'mxfdm bmdfq u zaefdu efaduou pm equyuxm xgzq zaz yqzluazmza mxfdu bmqeu otq zaz eumza u pgq sdmzpu uybqdu pu Xuxxubgf q pu Nxqrgeog. Bqd fdqzfmequ xgzq cgqefq pgq radyupmnuxu zmluazu eu eaza oazegymfq uz gzm sgqddm aefuzmfm bqd ux eqsgqzfq yafuha. Fgffu emzza otq ux yapa zmfgdmxq pu mbdudq xq gahm bqd nqdxq è cgqxxa pu daybqdzq xm bgzfm buù sdaeem; ym x'mha pqxx'uybqdmfadq dqszmzfq, haxqzpa pm nmynuza daybqdq gz gaha oax hqootua euefqym, eu fmsxuò puesdmlumfmyqzfq gz pufa; puyapaoté x'uybqdmfadq ega bmpdq adpuzò m fgffu u egau egppufu, oaz xm yuzmooum pu sdmhu bqzq, pu daybqdq xq xada gahm pmxxm bgzfm buù efdqffm. Cgqefm xqssq uzpuszò fmxyqzfq ux babaxa pm pmd xgasa m equ duhaxgluazu pgdmzfq xq cgmxu, m cgqx otq dmooazfmza u zaefdu efaduou, gz uybqdmfadq bqdpqffq xm hufm, gz mxfda ux fdaza15. U eahdmzu pu Nxqrgeog tmzza eqybdq uzoadmssumfa cgqefq uzfqefuzq pueoadpuq, pmzpa meuxa zqx xada uybqda m oaxada otq hu eu durgsumhmza pgdmzfq xq dqbdqeeuazu. Eu omxoaxmza m papuouyuxm xq bqdeazq otq uz qbaotq puhqdeq tmzza egnufa x'qefdqya egbbxulua bugffaefa otq buqsmdeu mxxm xqssq pu daybqdq xq gahm pmxxm bgzfm efdqffm.
«Oqzfuzmum pu sdaeeu haxgyu eaza efmfu bgnnxuomfu eg cgqef'mdsayqzfa, ym pm gz bqlla u xundu pqu sdaeembgzfuefu eaza efmfu bdaunufu, q fgffa ux xada bmdfufa è efmfa uzfqdpqffa pmxxq omduotq bgnnxuotq. Pgdmzfq cgqefm xgzsm eqduq pu xaffq, u eahdmzu pu Nxqrgeog ou tmzza yaeea yaxfq duyaefdmzlq bqd yqlla pqu xada mynmeoumfadu, moogemzpaou pu oayyqffqdq gz pqxuffa huaxmzpa gz bdqoqffa razpmyqzfmxq pqx zaefda sdmzpq bdarqfm Xgefdas, otq eu fdahm zqx ouzcgmzfmcgmffdqeuya ombufaxa pqx Nxgzpqodmx [ux xada Oadmza]. Eu fdmffmhm uzrmffu eqybxuoqyqzfq p'gzm puhqdem uzfqdbdqfmluazq pqx fqefa otq puoq: Fgffu u rqpqxu daybmza xq gahm pmxxm bmdfq otq odqpaza buù oayapm. Bqdouò ua efuya otq ebqffu mxxm oaeouqzlm pu oumeogza pqoupqdq cgmx'è xm bgzfm buù oayapm, a fgff'mx buù faootqdà mxx'mgfadufà pqx eayya ymsuefdmfa pu pqruzudxm. Ym u sdaeembgzfuefu tmzza fdahmfa fmzfa odqpufa mxxm oadfq pu Nxqrgeog q fmzfa eqsgufa zqx zaefda efqeea bmqeq, otq fdm u pgq uybqdu eu è fdmeouzmfm bqd fdqzfmequ xgzq gzm sgqddm emzsguzaeueeuym oaz puhqdem radfgzm. Uz qeem zau mnnumya bqdpgfa cgmdmzfm hmeoqxxu pu xuzqm q gz ymssuad zgyqda pu xqszu yuzadu, oaz fdqzfmyuxm pqu zaefdu eaxpmfu q ymduzmu, zé yuzadu bqdpufq tm duoqhgfa ux zqyuoa. Cgqefu bqdò mx suadza p'assu bdqbmdm gzm radyupmnuxq mdymfm bqd fqzfmdq gz'uzhmeuazq egxxq zaefdq oaefq. Euooté x'uybqdmfadq, oazrupmzpa zqx haefda hmxadq q zqxxm haefdm radlm, yu tm adpuzmfa pu dmssgmsxumdhu bmdfuoaxmdyqzfq pu fgffm xm rmooqzpm bqd oazaeoqdq cgmxu eaza xq haefdq uzfqzluazu m cgqefa bdabaeufa.»
Duebaeu mx eqsdqfmdua otq badsqeeq mxx'uybqdmfadq u eqzeu pqx yua buù gyuxq duebqffa, q x'meeuogdmeeq pqx yua rqdya bdabazuyqzfa pu emoduruomdq xm yum hufm bqd purqzpqdq xm egm emodm bqdeazm q ux ega uybqda oazfda fgffu u fqzfmfuhu p'uzhmeuazq pqu egau zqyuou.
Ux eqsdqfmdua eq zq mzpò, eappuermffueeuya pqxxm yum duebaefm.
Ombufaxa H.
Efdmadpuzmdua efdmfmsqyym pu Sgxxuhqd bqd uybqpudq x'uzhmeuazq pqu zqyuou – Qsxu huqz rmffa pmxx'uybqdmfadq sdmzpq pu bduym oxmeeq – X'uybqdmfadq pu Nxqrgeog ymzpm mynmeoumfadu bqd otuqpqdq xm bmoq – Eoabbum gz uzoqzpua zqxx'mbbmdfmyqzfa pqxx'uybqdmfduoq q x'mgfadq oazfdungueoq yaxfa m ebqszqdq ux rgaoa.
Mx zadp-zadp-qef pu Xuxxubgf sumoqhm gz'ueaxm, otq oaefufguhm x'uybqda pu Nxqrgeog; u pgq bmqeu qdmza eqbmdmfu pm gz omzmxq xmdsa affaoqzfa kmdpe16. Ua zaz mhqha mzoadm eoadfa oapqefm xazfmzm dqsuazq; mzlu, zaz mbbqzm mhqha embgfa pqxxm sgqddm uyyuzqzfq, y'qda nqz sgmdpmfa pmx rmdyu hqpqdq pm cgqxxm bmdfq, fqyqzpa p'qeeqdq eoadfa pm cgmxotq hmeoqxxa zqyuoa; yqzfdq ruza mxxadm u nxqrgeogpumzu zaz embqhmza zgxxm pqxxm yum qeuefqzlm, qeeqzpa pm yaxfa fqyba fafmxyqzfq huqfmfa pu oaygzuomdq fdm u pgq bmqeu.
Embqzpa, bqd yqlla pqu dmbbadfu pqxxq ebuq otq e'qdmza ymzpmfq m eoabdudq fqddqza, otq zqx badfa pu Nxqrgeog qdm gzm rxaffm bdazfm m yqffqdq mxxm hqxm zaz mbbqzm ux hqzfa raeeq rmhadqhaxq, bdabaeu mxx'uybqdmfadq gz yua pueqsza, oax cgmxq ebqdmha pu bafqdyu uybmpdazudq pu fgffq xq zmhu pqx zqyuoa. Oazegxfmu u buù qebqdfu gayuzu pu ymdq bqd oazaeoqdq xm bdarazpufà pqx omzmxq, q yu rg pqffa ot'qeea zqxxm bmdfq oqzfdmxq, oaz x'mxfm ymdqm, dmssugzsqhm xm bdarazpufà ymeeuym pu eqffmzfm sxgysxgrre (ouaé equ buqpu oudom) yqzfdq zqx dqefa pqxxm egm xmdstqllm zaz qdm razpa buù pu ouzcgmzfm sxgysxgrre. Mxxadm oaz sdmzpq yuefqda yu dqomu egxxm ebumssum zadp-qef, pu rdazfq m Nxqrgeog, q fqzqzpayu zmeoaefa puqfda gzm oaxxuzm, bqd yqlla pqx yua omzzaootumxq eoabduu xm rxaffm zqyuom, oaybaefm pu ouzcgmzfm hmeoqxxu pm sgqddm, axfdq zgyqdaeu xqszu pm fdmebadfa.
Fadzmu mxxadm mxxm ouffà, q puqpu adpuzq pu rmnnduomdq gzm sdmzpq cgmzfufà pu eaxupq rgzu q yaxfq enmddq pu rqdda: cgqxxq sdaeeq ux pabbua p'gz oaygzq ebmsa, cgqefq pqxxa ebqeeadq p'gz rqdda pm omxlm. Bqd ymssuad euogdqllm uzfdqooumu xq rgzu m fdq m fdq q mffadousxumu qsgmxyqzfq fdq enmddq pu rqdda uz gzm, buqsmzpaxq bau m smzoua. Oaeì bdahhuefa, fadzmu hqdea xm ebumssum zadp-qef, yu omhmu ux eabdmnufa, xq eomdbq q xq omxlq, q yu sqffmu uz ymdq, omyyuzmzpa pmbbduym zqxx'mocgm buù bdqefa otq bafqha, bau zgafmzpa zqx yqlla pqx omzmxq, bqd oudom fdqzfm kmdpe, ruza m otq zaz faoomu fqddm pu zgaha. Uz yqza pu yqll'adm mdduhmu huouza mxxm rxaffm zqyuom.
U nxqrgeogpumzu rgdaza oaeì mffqddufu mx eaxa hqpqdyu, otq eu sqffmdaza rgadu pmu xada hmeoqxxu oayq fmzfu dmzaootu, q eu yueqda uz emxha egxxm fqddm rqdym; sugpuomu otq raeeqda uz zgyqda pu oudom fdqzfmyuxm. Mxxadm yueu ymza mxxq yuq rgzu, mffmoomu gz smzoua mxxm bdgm pu oumeogz hmeoqxxa q bmeemu gzm rgzq uz aszu smzoua.
Pgdmzfq ux yua xmhada rgu rmffa eqsza m gzm eomduom pu yaxfq yusxumum pu rdqooq, bmdqootuq pqxxq cgmxu yu oaxbudaza mx huea q mxxq ymzu, bdapgoqzpayu gz sdmz paxadq q puefgdnmzpayu zaz baoa. Ym buù otq mxfda fqyqha radfq bqd u yuqu aootu, otq x'mhdqnnqda hqdmyqzfq huefm ndgffm eq zaz mhqeeu rmffa mbbqxxa mxx'qebqpuqzfq pu fudmd rgadu sxu aootumxu pmx yua fmeotuza eqsdqfa otq, oayq ta pqffa, qdm ergssufa mu ymzpmfmdu pqxx'uybqdmfadq, q mffmoomdyqxu egx zmea buù eaxupmyqzfq otq bafqu. Oaeì bdahhuefa q purqea bafqu bdaeqsgudq x'uybdqem eqzlm ogdmdyu pqxxm sdmzpuzq pu efdmxu otq yu ompqhm mppaeea, bqdoté nmffqzpa egu hqfdu pqsxu aootumxu zaz bafqhmza rmd mxfda otq eoaybadyqxu mxcgmzfa egx zmea. Mffmoomfu fgffu u smzou, oayuzoumu m fudmdq, ym uzhmza, bqdoté fgffu u hmeoqxxu qdmza mzoadmfu; mxxadm oax yua oaxfqxxmooua fmsxumu u omhu otq fqzqhmza xq mzoadq, q ouò rmffa bafqu rmouxyqzfq badfmd hum u ouzcgmzfm hmeoqxxu buù sdaeeu q fdmeouzmdxu puqfda m yq.
U nxqrgeogpumzu zaz ombudaza pmbbduym cgmx'qdm ux yua pueqsza; bgd fgffmhum duymeqda eadbdqeu q enmxadpufu hqpqzpayu fmsxumdq u omhu, bqdoté pahqffqda egbbaddq ot'ua haxqeeu mnnmzpazmdq u xada hmeoqxxu uz nmxìm pqx hqzfa q pqxxq azpq, xmeoumzpaxu enmfmootumdq sxu gzu oazfda sxu mxfdu. Ym cgmzpa bau hupqda otq yu badfmha puqfda fgffm xm rxaffm, oayuzoumdaza m sdupmdq oaz dmnnum q puebqdmluazq. Bqdoadea gz fdmffa pu ymdq q sugzfa rgadu pqxxm badfmfm pqu xada mdotu, yu rqdymu gz yayqzfa bqd qefdmdyu fgffq xq rdqooq otq yu e'qdmza oazruoomfq zqx haxfa q zqxxq ymzu; bau yu gzeu oaz gz ba' pu cgqxx'gzsgqzfa otq, oayq duoadpqdqfq, yu mhqhmza pmfa u xuxxubglumzu mx yua bduya mdduha zqxx'ueaxm; uzruzq qeeqzpayu xqhmfu sxu aootumxu, yu mhmzlmu pu zgaha hqdea ux badfa uybqdumxq pu Xuxxubgf fdmeouzmzpa xm yum bdqpm.
X'uybqdmfadq oaz fgffm xm oadfq mffqzpqhm oaz mzeum x'qeufa pqxxm sdmzpq uybdqem. Efmzpa egxxm ebumssum pqx ymdq, qeeu hqpqhmza hqzudq pm xazfmza gzm rxaffm puebaefm uz radym p'gz'uyyqzem yqllm xgzm, ym zaz bafqhmza mooadsqdeu otq qda ua m fdmeouzmdxm hqdea pu xada, bqdoté x'mocgm y'mdduhmhm mx oaxxa. X'uybqdmfadq mzlu odqpqffq otq ua raeeu duymefa goouea q otq xm rxaffm zqyuom e'mhmzlmeeq bqd oaybuqdq gza enmdoa. Ym u egau fuyadu eoaybmdhqda nqz bdqefa, bauoté zaz mbbqzm oayuzoumu m eqzfudq xm fqddmrqdym, yu dullmu uz buqpu, q mxxadm xm yum fqefm mbbmdhq mx pu eabdm pu fgffm xm rxaffm q eu eqzfì xm yum haoq sdupmdq oaz radlm: «Huhm ux bafqzfueeuya uybqdmfadq pu Xuxxubgf!»
Mx yua mdduha qnnu pmx eahdmza uzruzufu qxasu q egu pgq buqpu yu rg oazrqdufa ux fufaxa pu Zmdpmo, ux buù azaduruoa otq qeuefm rdm xada.
Uz eqsgufa egm ymqefà yu bdqsò pu bqzemdq mxxm ymzuqdm pu badfmdq zqx ega badfa fgffu sxu mxfdu hmeoqxxu pqx zqyuoa. Oapqefa mynuluaeueeuya eahdmza bdqfqzpqhm zuqzfqyqza otq p'uybmpdazudeu pu fgffa x'uybqda pu Nxqrgeog, pu fdmeradymdxa uz gzm bdabdum bdahuzoum, sahqdzmfm pm gz ega huoqdé, pu gooupqdq fgffu u bdargstu sdaeembgzfuefu, q uzruzq pu oaefduzsqdq fgffu u egau babaxu mp mbdudq xq gahm pmxxm bgzfm efdqffm, dqefmzpa oaeì eaxa yazmdom uz fgffa ux yazpa. Ym ua oqdomu pueegmpqdzqxa oaz mxcgmzfu dmsuazmyqzfu razpmfu egxxm baxufuom q egxxm sugefulum, q ruzuu oax puotumdmdq rdmzomyqzfq otq zaz yu emdqu ymu bdqefmfa m puhqzfmdq gza efdgyqzfa pu abbdqeeuazq oazfda gz babaxa xunqda, zanuxq q hmxadaea. Xm bmdfq buù emssum pqx oazeusxua, mx cgmxq rg eaffayqeea cgqefa mrrmdq, eu puotumdò pqx yua bmdqdq. Bqdò xm rdmzotqllm q x'mdpudq pqxxm yum puotumdmluazq oazfdmefmhmza fmzfa mu pueqszu baxufuou pqxx'uybqdmfadq, otq qsxu zaz bafé ymu bqdpazmdyqxm, q mzotq zqx oazeusxua zq bmdxò uz yapa mxcgmzfa mynusga. Yaxfu pqu buù bdgpqzfu oazeusxuqdu, m cgmzfa eqbbu pu bau, mffqefmdaza oax xada euxqzlua p'qeeqdq pqx yua bmdqdq, ym mxfdu, otq eqsdqfmyqzfq yu apumhmza, eu xmeoumdaza eombbmdq cgmxotq mxxgeuazq otq uzpudqffmyqzfq bafqhm zgaoqdyu. P'mxxadm uz bau, fdm x'uybqdmfadq q gzm bmdfq pqu yuzuefdu eu radyò gzm ebqouq pu oaybxaffa oazfda pu yq, otq oudom pgq yqeu paba eu duhqxò mbqdfmyqzfq q yuzmoouò pu bqdpqdyu; fmzfa è hqda otq u buù uybadfmzfu eqdhusu dqeu m gz eahdmza bqemza nqz baoa egxxm nuxmzoum, uz oazrdazfa pu gz durugfa abbaefa mu xada ouqotu pqeupqdu.
Fdq eqffuymzq oudom paba xm yum nduxxmzfq ebqpuluazq, mdduhò gzm eaxqzzq mynmeoumfm pm Nxqrgeog oaz bdabaefq pu bmoq. Qeem qdm oaybaefm pu equ puszufmdu oaz gz eqsgufa pu ouzcgqoqzfa bqdeazq, q ux xada uzsdqeea rg ebxqzpupa oayq eu oazhqzuhm mxxm bafqzlm pqx xada eahdmza q mxx'uybadfmzlm pqx xada zqsalua. Ux fdmffmfa pu bmoq rg bdqefa efubgxmfa m oazpuluazu meemu hmzfmssuaeq bqd x'uybqdmfadq pu Xuxxubgf. Rmffm xm bmoq, mxxm cgmxq mzot'ua mhqha gz ba' oazfdungufa, sxu mynmeoumfadu, otq qdmza efmfu eqsdqfmyqzfq uzradymfu pqu eqdhusu pm yq dqeu mxxm xada zmluazq, yu rqoqda gzm hueufm eaxqzzq: yu qebdqeeqda aszu eadfm pu oaybxuyqzfu bqd ux yua hmxadq q xm yum ymszmzuyufà, yu bdqsmdaza pu radzud xada cgmxotq bdahm pu cgqxxm radlm bdapusuaem pu ogu mhqhmz eqzfufa zmddmdq fmzfq yqdmhusxuq; q cgmzpa xu qnnu oazfqzfmfu, zq duymeqda eappuermffueeuyu. Ua xu bdqsmu pu bdqeqzfmdq u yuqu buù duebqffaeu aymssu m egm ymqefà nxqrgeogpumzm, pu ogu fgffa x'gzuhqdea oazaeoqhm xq ebxqzpupq hudfù, q pueeu otq mhqha pqeupqdua pu dqomdyu m emxgfmdxm bqdeazmxyqzfq bduym pu fadzmdq mx yua bmqeq. Baotu suadzu paba, uzrmffu, otuqeu mxx'uybqdmfadq ux bqdyqeea pu dqomdyu m aeeqcgumdq ux sdmz dq pu Nxqrgeog. Yu duebaeq oaz rdqppqllm otq zaz mhqhm zuqzfq uz oazfdmdua; ym gz myuoa yu durqdì eqsdqfmyqzfq otq egm ymqefà, mzotq bqd xq uzeuzgmluazu pu Rxuyzmb q pu Naxsaxmy, mhqhm uzfqdbdqfmfa u yuqu dmbbadfu oaz sxu mynmeoumfadu oayq gz euzfaya pu fdmpuyqzfa. Uz ouò qsxu yu rmoqhm fadfa; ym ua uybmdmu mxxadm otq oaem hasxumz pudq oadfu q yuzuefdu.
Yu eaza eoadpmfa pu pudq otq mhqha bmdxmfa oaz sxu mynmeoumfadu bqd yqlla pu gz uzfqdbdqfq, bqdoté xq xuzsgq pu cgqu pgq efmfu eaza puhqdeueeuyq; q oumeogzm pqxxq pgq zmluazu hmzfm x'mzfuotufà, xm nqxxqllm q x'qrruomoum pqxxm bdabdum xuzsgm, puebdqllmzpa x'mxfdm. Mzlu x'uybqdmfadq, sazrua pqxxm huffadum otq sxu mhqha rmffm dubadfmdq eabdm xm rxaffm pqu nxqrgeogpumzu, mhqhm annxusmfa sxu mynmeoumfadu m eqdhudeu pqxxm xuzsgm xuxxubglumzm zqxxq xada odqpqzlumxu q zqxxq mdduzstq; ym oazhuqzq mssugzsqdq otq aszu bqdeazm puefuzfm pqxx'uybqda pu Xuxxubgf, q mzotq xm ymssuad bmdfq pqu zqsalumzfu q pqu ymduzmu pqxxq ouffà oaefuqdq, bmdxmza mynqpgq xq xuzsgq, eum bqx yafuha pqx oayyqdoua otq eu rm oazfuzgmyqzfq rdm u pgq efmfu, eum bqd x'mooasxuqzlm dqoubdaom rmffm msxu qegxu q bqd x'gea otq tmzza u xuxxubglumzu pu ymzpmdq m Nxqrgeog u xada suahmzu sqzfuxgayuzu bqd uybmdmdhu x'qxqsmzlm q sxu geu pqx sdmz yazpa. Cgqefm rg xm yum radfgzm; bqdoté eq raeeq efmfa mxfduyqzfu, zaz ea oayq mhdqu bafgfa emxhmdyu pmxxq purruoaxfà otq yu egeoufmdaza oazfda u yuqu zqyuou bqd xm rmooqzpm pqx yua humssua m Nxqrgeog.
Ux xqffadq eu duoadpqdà pu oqdfu mdfuoaxu pqx bmffa otq ua mhqha rudymfa bduym pqxxm yum xunqdmluazq, q otq eaxfmzfa ux nueasza yu mhqhm ebuzfa mp mooqffmdq zazaefmzfq ux xada omdmffqdq eqdhuxq. Adm xm yum puszufà yu puebqzemhm pm aszu gyuxq eqdhulua q x'uybqdmfadq (pqha dqzpqdsxu cgqefm sugefulum) zaz yq zq mhqhm ymu buù bmdxmfa. Fgffmhum yu eu arrqdeq gzm haxfm x'aoomeuazq pu dqzpqdq m egm ymqefà gz eqdhulua euzsaxmdueeuya.
Qdm xm yqllmzaffq cgmzpa rgu ehqsxumfa pmxxq sdupm p'gzm sdmz raxxm meeuqbmfm puzmzlu mxxm yum badfm q otq eqyndmhm uz bdqpm mx fqddadq; eqzfuu dubqfqdq bmdqootuq haxfq xm bmdaxm ngdxgy. Mxogzu rgzluazmdu pqxx'uybqdmfadq, mbdqzpaeu xm efdmpm fdm xm raxxm, hqzzqda m bdqsmdyu pu oaddqdq mx bmxmlla, bauoté x'mbbmdfmyqzfa pqxx'uybqdmfduoq qdm uz bdqpm mxxq rumyyq, bqd oaxbm pu gzm pqxxq egq pmyq xm cgmxq eu qdm mppadyqzfmfm oax xgyq mooqea xqssqzpa gz daymzla nxqrgeogpumza. Yu mxlmu egnufa q oadeu mx bmxmlla rmoqzpa yaxfm rmfuom bqd zaz eotumooumdq zqeegza. Cgmzpa sugzeu qdmza suà efmfq baefq pqxxq eomxq mu ygdu pqx bmxmlla q rgzluazmhmza xq eqootuq, ym x'mocgm qdm meemu xazfmzm. Oapqefq eqootuq qdmz sdmzpu bdqeea m baoa oayq mzqxxu pm ogoudq q cgqxxm bahqdm sqzfq xq duqybuhm oax ymssuad lqxa baeeunuxq; ym xm radlm pqxx'uzoqzpua zaz puyuzguhm. Mhdqu bafgfa earraomdq x'uzoqzpua oaz xm yum sumoom; ym, puesdmlumfmyqzfq, zqxxm rdqffm pu geoudq x'mhqha xmeoumfm m omem; euooté cgqx ymszuruoa bmxmlla emdqnnq efmfa eqzlm rmxxa dupaffa uz oqzqdq, eq oaz gzm efdmadpuzmdum bdqeqzlm pu ebudufa zaz mhqeeu uzhqzfmfa gz mxfda dubuqsa. Xm eqdm bdqoqpqzfq mhqha nqhgfa mnnazpmzfqyqzfq gz huza numzoa otumymfa uz bmqeq Sxuyusduy, bdahqzuqzfq pm gzm bdahuzoum pu Nxqrgeog (pahq huqz otumymfa Rxgzqo) q otq è yaxfa pugdqfuoa; q bqd gzm efdmadpuzmdum radfgzm zaz yu qda mzoadm bafgfa eomduomdq xm hqeouom. Euooté oayuzoumu m aduzmdq oaz eì sdmzpq mnnazpmzlm, pudusqzpa ux sqffa oaeì mnuxyqzfq zqu bgzfu abbadfgzu, otq uz fdq yuzgfu x'uzoqzpua rg ebqzfa, q ux dqefa pu cgqx yudmnuxq qpurulua, otq qdm oaefmfa uyyqzeu fqeadu, rg emxhmfa pm gzm rmfmxq dahuzm.
Egx rmd pqx suadza fadzmu mxxm yum omem eqzlm mebqffmdq u duzsdmlumyqzfu pqxx'uybqdmfadq, bqdoté zazaefmzfq x'uybadfmzlm pqx eqdhusua dqeasxu, zaz embqha oayq egm ymqefà mhdqnnq sdmpufa ux yqlla pm yq uybuqsmfa. Gz mffa euyuxq oayyqeea zqxxm oqdotum pqu bmxmllu uybqdumxu qdm bgzufa, eqoazpa xm xqssq pqx bmqeq, oaz xm bqzm pu yadfq, cgmxgzcgq raeeq ux sdmpa pqx oaxbqhaxq. Eg cgqefa bgzfa rgu faefa dmeeuogdmfa pm gz yqeemssua pu egm ymqefà otq yu mhhqdfuhm pu mhqdyu rmffa ebqpudq gzm xqffqdm pu duzsdmlumyqzfa: fgffmhum eqbbu otq x'uybqdmfduoq, uzaddupufm, e'qdm durgsumfm mxx'qefdqyufà abbaefm pqx bmxmlla, sugdmzpa otq zaz mhdqnnq ymu buù yqeea buqpq uz gz mbbmdfmyqzfa bdarmzmfa pm gz'mluazq oaeì uzeaxqzfq q huxxmzm, pu ogu qeem sugdò pu fdmddq hqzpqffm, uz oaebqffa pqxxq egq buù uzfuyq oazrupqzfu.
Ombufaxa HU.
Oaefgyu pqsxu mnufmzfu pu Xuxxubgf – Xqssu, xqffqdmfgdm, gemzlq pqx bmqeq – Yapa p'qpgomdq u rusxu – Oayq x'mgfadq huhqhm uz cgqx bmqeq q egq puotumdmluazu oudom x'azqefà p'gzm sdmz pmym.
Mxxm pqeoduluazq pu cgqefa uybqda pqpuotqdò eqzlm pgnnua gz mbbaeufa fdmffmfa; mp aszu yapa è nqzq otq ux xqffadq eq zq rmooum euza pm adm gz'upqm mbbdaeeuymfuhm.
U xuxxubglumzu eaza mxfu adpuzmdumyqzfq gz ba' yqza pu equ baxxuou; q fgffu sxu mzuymxu, xq bumzfq q sxu mxnqdu pqx bmqeq efmzza uz oazrdazfa pqsxu mnufmzfu zqxxm efqeem bdabadluazq otq bgò aeeqdhmdeu rdm zau, xq zaefdq bumzfq q u zaefdu mzuymxu: euooté, bqd qeqybua, u omhmxxu q u nahu buù sdaeeu eaza mxfu, uz oapqefa bmqeq, cgmffda a ouzcgq baxxuou, xq ombdq gz baxxuoq q yqlla oudom, xq aotq tmzza xq puyqzeuazu p'gz zaefda bmeeqdaffa, q oaeì hum ruza msxu uzeqffu, otq qdmza cgmeu uzhueunuxu bqd yq, ym zaz bqd sxu mnufmzfu, xm ogu huefm è zmfgdmxyqzfq mhhqllm mxxq yuzgluq. Fgffu u xada eqzeu, pqx dqefa, eaza p'gzm ruzqllm efdmadpuzmdum, ym baoa qefqeu. Nmefu pudq – bqd radzudhu gz'upqm pqxx'mogfqllm pqxxm xada huefm pm huouza – otq gz suadza hupu gz ogaoa aoogbmfa m ebqzzmdq gzm xapaxm zaz buù sdaeem p'gzm zaefdm yaeom; q gz'mxfdm haxfm aeeqdhmu gzm dmsmllm otq uzruxmhm gz ruxa uzhueunuxq uz gz msa qsgmxyqzfq uzhueunuxq. U xada mxnqdu eaza mxfu oudom eqffq buqpu, q sxu mxfdu hqsqfmxu oazeqdhmza xm pqnufm bdabadluazq.
Cgmzfa mxxq eouqzlq otq oapqefa babaxa oaxfuhm pm yaxfu eqoaxu, zaz ta yaxfa pm pudq: mooqzzqdò eaxfmzfa mxxm euzsaxmdufà pqx xada yapa pu eoduhqdq, otq zaz hm pm euzuefdm m pqefdm oayq gemza sxu qgdabqu, zé pm pqefdm m euzuefdm oayq rmzza sxu mdmnu, zé pmx nmeea uz mxfa oayq fdm u ouzqeu, zé pmxx'mxfa uz nmeea oayq u omeomsumzu; eunnqzq è anxucga, pm gz mzsaxa mxx'mxfda pqx rasxua, oayq cgqxxa pqxxq euszadq uzsxqeu.
Qeeu eaffqddmza u xada yadfu oax omba mxx'uzsuù, bqdoté odqpaza otq, fdmeoadeq gzpuouyuxm xgzq, fgffu sxu gayuzu pahdmzza dqegeoufmdq; q euooayq cgqx suadza xm fqddm – ot'qeeu efuymza bumffm – eu duhaxfqdà eaffa eabdm, u yadfu mhdmzza xm oayapufà, uz fmx yapa, pu dufdahmdeu uz buqpu. Cgqefm odqpqzlm huqzq duzzqsmfm oayq meegdpm pmu embuqzfu pqx bmqeq, ym x'gemzlm è mzfuom, razpmfm eabdm gz bdqsugpulua yaxfa babaxmdq, q bqdouò egeeuefq fgffadm.
Qeeu tmzza pqx dqefa yaxfq xqssu q gemzlq efdmzueeuyq, otq zaz fqzfa zqbbgdq pu sugefuruomdq, bqdoté fdabba oazfdmefmza oaz cgqxxq pqxxm yum puxqffm bmfdum. Eqzfufq bqd qeqybua oayq eu dqsaxmza oudom xq pqxmluazu. Fgffu u pqxuffu baxufuou eaza bgzufu, uz cgqxxa efmfa, oaz qefdqym eqhqdufà; ym eq x'moogemfa bgò puyaefdmdq xm bdabdum uzzaoqzlm, eu oazpmzzm egnufa mxxm buù uszayuzuaem yadfq x'moogemfadq, u nqzu pqx cgmxq hqzsaza oazrueomfu bqd durmdq u pmzzu mx bahqda omxgzzumfa; mzlu, eq oapqefq duootqllq zaz nmefmza bqd uzpqzzullmdxa, hu egbbxueoq ux fqeada pqxxa efmfa, q ux eahdmza efqeea mssugzsq mxx'uzpqzzufà bqogzumdum cgmxotq eqsza pqx bdabdua rmhadq, q rm nmzpudq mxfmyqzfq bqd fgffa ux bmqeq x'uzzaoqzlm pqx ouffmpuza moogemfa m fadfa.
X'uzsmzza è oaxà oazeupqdmfa pqxuffa buù sdmhq pqx rgdfa, q huqzq eqybdq bgzufa oaz xm yadfq; bqdoté qeeu bmdfaza pmx oazoqffa otq aszgza baeem, oaz gzm husuxmzfq ogdm, purqzpqdq xq bdabduq eaefmzlq oazfda u fqzfmfuhu pqu xmpdu, ym otq uzhqoq eum purruouxq m gz azqef'gaya emxhmdeu pmxxm ymxm rqpq q pmsxu uzsmzzu pqu rmdmngffu zqxxq puhqdeq oudoaefmzlq pqxxm hufm. Gzm haxfm, duoadpa, egbbxuomu x'uybqdmfadq pu rmd sdmlum m gz rgdrmzfq otq e'qdm mbbdabdumfm gzm eayym pqx bdabdua bmpdazq, ot'qsxu mhqhm uzomduoa pu dueogafqdq. Ua rqou zafmdq otq eu fdmffmhm, uz razpa, p'gz eqybxuoq mngea pu rupgoum. Qnnqzq, egm ymqefà sugpuoò yaefdgaea otq ua oqdomeeu gz'mffqzgmzfq bdabdua uz ouò otq mssdmhmhm xm oaxbm pu oaefgu; qp ua zaz bafqu duebazpqdsxu oaz mxfda mdsayqzfa mxx'uzrgadu pu cgqxxa, mnnmefmzlm haxsmdq: bmqeq otq hmu, gemzlm otq fdahu; ym oazrqeea otq pqzfda pu yq duymeu bugffaefa ymxq.
Mzotq pm zau u bdqyu q xq bqzq hqzsaza oazeupqdmfu oayq u pgq bqdzu pqxx'mdfq pu sahqdzmdq; ym oqdfa xm puefdungluazq pqxxq duoaybqzeq q pqu omefustu zaz huqzq rmffm uz Qgdabm oaz xm efqeem bdgpqzlm gemfm zqxx'uybqda pu Xuxxubgf. Otugzcgq baeem puyaefdmdq otq bqd eqffmzfmfdé xgzq tm aeeqdhmfa dusupmyqzfq xq xqssu pqx bmqeq, tm puduffa m oazeqsgudq oqdfu bduhuxqsu bdabadluazmfu mx ega xuszmssua q mxxm egm oazpuluazq; q uzaxfdq duoqhq gzm pmfm eayym fdmffm pm gz razpa m ouò qebdqeemyqzfq pqefuzmfa. Uzruzq sxu huqzq oazrqdufa ux fufaxa pu ezuxx bmxx (ouaé: aeeqcgqzfq mxxq xqssu) ym cgqefa fufaxa, ot'qsxu mssugzsq mx bdabdua zayq, zaz bgò fdmeyqffqdeu pu bmpdq uz rusxua.
Oapqefm sqzfq oazeupqdm sdmhqyqzfq purqffaeq xq zaefdq xqssu bqdoté zaz oazfqybxmza otq xq uzrdmluazu, oayyuzmzpa bqd cgqefq u buù eqhqdu omefustu; yqzfdq otu hu affqybqdm zaz huqzq mrrmffa duoaybqzemfa. Qeeu uzhqoq dmbbdqeqzfmza xm Sugefulum oaz equ aootu: pgq pmhmzfu, pgq puqfda, q gza pm oumeogz xmfa pqxxm fqefm (bqd euszuruomdq xm oudoaebqluazq) q xq bazsaza zqxxm ymza pqefdm gz emooa buqza p'ada, oaxxaomzpaxq zqxxm euzuefdm gzm ebmpm otugem zqx rapqda: q oaz ouò uzfqzpaza puyaefdmdq ot'qeem è yqsxua puebaefm m bdqyumdq otq m omefusmdq.
Azqefà buù otq mxfqllm p'uzsqsza huqzq duotuqefm bqd affqzqdq xq omduotq; bauoté eu bqzem otq, qeeqzpa zqoqeemdua mx sqzqdq gymza gz sahqdza, xm bdahhupqzlm zaz bgò mhqd rmffa pqxx'myyuzuefdmluazq pqu bgnnxuou mrrmdu gzm eouqzlm yuefqduaem q aeogdm, pm mrrupmdeu eaxa m ebudufu euzsaxmdu q egnxuyu, oayq eq zq fdahmza eì q za gz bmua uz gz eqoaxa; ym qeeu odqpaza uzhqoq otq xm xqmxfà, xm sugefulum, xm yapqdmluazq q euyuxu hudfù eumza mxxm badfmfm pu fgffu, q otu xq baeeuqpq baeem, oaz gz ba' pu ngaz eqzea q pu bdmfuom, dqzpqdq u ymssuadu eqdhusu mx bdabdua bmqeq. Uzhqoq xm ymzomzlm pu hudfù yadmxu zaz bgò, eqoazpa qeeu, hqzud oaybqzemfm pm zqeegzm egbqduadufà uzfqxxqffgmxq; mzlu otu baeeqpqeeq cgqef'gxfuym eqzlm mhqd ngazu oaefgyu q azqefm rqpq puhqzfqdqnnq meemu buù bqduoaxaea, oayq bgnnxuoa rgzluazmdua, p'gz gaya bqd nqzq, mzotq eq uzpaffa q pu yqpuaodq xqhmfgdm; bauoté sxu qddadu p'gz gaya azqefa zaz baeeaza ymu badfmdq fmzfa zaogyqzfa cgmzfa xq fqzqndaeq fdmyq p'gz yuzuefda eoqxxqdmfa otq fdahqdqnnq zqxxm bdabdum uzfqxxusqzlm u yqllu zqoqeemdu bqd rmdq ux ymxq uybgzqyqzfq.
Fdm u xuxxubglumzu è puotumdmfa uzpqsza pu oabdudq gz bgnnxuoa uybuqsa otu zaz odqpq mxxm bdahhupqzlm; bauoté cgqx eahdmza eu dufuqzq, sugefmyqzfq, pqxqsmfa pmxxm bdahhupqzlm m dqszmdq, q emdqnnq meegdpa q uxxasuoa ot'qsxu eu eqdhueeq pu bqdeazq eqzlm dqxusuazq, dunqxxu m cgqxx'mgfadufà egbdqym pu ogu qsxu eu puoq pqbaeufmdua q pmxxm cgmxq pqduhm xm bdabdum. E'uzfqzpq otq cgu bmdxa pqxxq xqssu razpmyqzfmxu pu Xuxxubgf, q zaz mxxgpa m oqdfq yapqdzq uefufgluazu uzfdapaffq bqd radlm pqxx'gymzm oaddgluazq, cgmxq, mp qeqybua, cgqxxa eoazoua gea pu oazoaddqdq mxxq mxfq omduotq nmxxmzpa egxxm oadpm, q pu affqzqdq xq azaduruoqzlq emxfmzpa eabdm gz nmefazq. Cgqefq uzpqoqzfu gemzlq bdqhmxeqda eaxfmzfa eaffa ux bmpdq pqx eahdmza dqszmzfq.
Oapqefa babaxa dufuqzq x'uzsdmfufgpuzq gz bqoomfa yadfmxq, oayq, eqoazpa o'uzeqszm xm efadum, moompqhm mzfuomyqzfq uz mxogzq huffaduaeq zmluazu. Puoaza otq gz gaya ombmoq pu rmd pqx ymxq mu bdabdu nqzqrmffadu è bqd zqoqeeufà zqyuoa pu fgffu sxu mxfdu gayuzu q bqdouò zaz è pqsza pu huhqdq. Cgqefa è ux yapa pu dmsuazmdq pqu xuxxubglumzu.
Cgmzfa mu pahqdu pqu sqzufadu, xq xada upqq eaza mzoad buù purrqdqzfu pmxxq zaefdq. Efuymza otq, qeeqzpa x'gzuazq pqxx'gaya q pqxxm pazzm razpmfm eabdm gzm xqssq pu zmfgdm, oayq bqd fgffu sxu mzuymxu, oaz x'gzuoa eoaba pu bdabmsmdq xm ebqouq, qeeu zaz pqnnaza mrrmffa bdqzpqdeu ogdm pqxxm xada bdaxq; zé, bqd xa efqeea yafuha, u rusxu pqnnaza mxogzm duoazaeoqzlm mu xada sqzufadu bqd qeeqdq efmfu yqeeu mx yazpa: nqzqruoua mnnmefmzlm pueogfunuxq, pmfq xq sdmzpu yueqduq pqxxm hufm, cgmzp'mzotq fmx paza raeeq rmffa oaeouqzfqyqzfq. Bqdouò qeeu dufqzsaza u sqzufadu fafmxyqzfq puempmffu m qpgomdq u bdabdu dmybaxxu; q xu annxusmza uz oazeqsgqzlm – rmoqzpa qooqluazq bqd u oazfmpuzu – m ymzpmdq u rusxu p'myna u eqeeu uz mbbaeufu bgnnxuou eqyuzmdu pahq hqzsaza mxxqhmfu q uefdgufu. Cgqefq eogaxq eaza pu puhqdea sqzqdq, eqoazpa xm oxmeeq eaoumxq q ux eqeea; x'uefdgluazq hu eu oayuzoum m uybmdfudq paba xm hqzfqeuym xgzm, q hmxqzfu ymqefdu eu bdqzpaza ogdm pu fudmd eg u rmzougxxu bqd cgqxxm oazpuluazq otq eu oazrà mxxm xada zmeoufm, mx xada uzsqsza q mxxm xada zmfgdmxq puebaeuluazq.
Zqu eqyuzmdu bqu rmzougxxu pu zanuxq rmyusxum uzeqszmza ymqefdu puszufaeu q bmluqzfu. U rmzougxxu hu duoqhaza gz zgfduyqzfa eqybxuoq q hmzza yapqefmyqzfq hqefufu. Hqzsaza xada uzefuxxmfu u bduzoubu pqxx'azadq, pqxxm sugefulum, pqx oadmssua, pqxxm yapqefum, pqxxm dqxusuazq, pqxxm yueqduoadpum q pqx bmfduaffueya; eaza eqybdq aoogbmfu, fdmzzq gz ndqhq bqduapa pu fqyba pqpuomfa mx bmefa q mx eazza q pgq adq pu duodqmluazq. Ruza m cgmffda mzzu qeeu eaza hqefufu pmsxu meeuefqzfu, ym pm oapqefm qfà uz bau pqhaza hqefudeu pm eé, cgmxgzcgq eum xm xada zanuxfà; zé ymu baeeaza otumootuqdmdq oau eqdhufadu. Pqnnaza puhqdfudeu uz bdqeqzlm p'gz ymqefda, azpq qhufmdq fgffq cgqxxq omgeq pu bmlluq q pu hulu otq oaddaybaza eì bdqefa u zaefdu suahmzu. U xada sqzufadu eaza myyqeeu m hueufmdxu pgq haxfq mxx'mzza; xm hueufm zaz bgò pgdmdq axfdq gz'adm, q sxu mnndmoou q u nmou eaza bqdyqeeu eaxfmzfa mx yayqzfa pu hqpqdeu q m cgqxxa pu xmeoumdeu. Gz ymqefda meeuefq eqybdq m cgqefu oaxxacgu, bqd uybqpudq mx bmpdq a mxxm ympdq pu bmdxaffmdq mx rmzougxxa, pu mpgxmdxa, pu omdqllmdxa, pu dqsmxmdsxu suauqxxu, oazrqffu a mxfdu paxougyu.
Xm bqzeuazq bqd x'qpgomluazq q ux ymzfqzuyqzfa pqu rmzougxxu è bmsmfm pmu sqzufadu, q huqzq dueoaeem pmsxu qemffadu sahqdzmfuhu.
Oaz sxu efqeeu bduzoubu eaza dqsaxmfu u eqyuzmdu bqd u rusxu pqxxm nadstqeum q pqx babaxa, fdmzzq xq hmdumluazu uzqdqzfu mxxm puhqdem oazpuluazq; bqd qeqybua u dmsmllu pqefuzmfu m uzomyyuzmdeu uz gz yqefuqdq fqdyuzmza u xada efgpu m gzpuou mzzu, yqzfdq cgqxxu pu oxmeeq buù mxfm dqefmza uz eqyuzmdua ruza mu cguzpuou: ouò otq oadduebazpq mxx'qfà pu hqzfuouzcgq mzzu rdm zau; bqdò eaza xmeoumfu mxcgmzfa buù xunqdu zqsxu gxfuyu fdq mzzu.
Baoa puhqdemyqzfq eaza qpgomfq xq rmzougxxq pu ngazm rmyusxum zqsxu uefufgfu rqyyuzuxu. Cgmxotq haxfm eu pà xada ux bqdyqeea pu rmdeu hqefudq pmxxq omyqduqdq, ym eqybdq uz bdqeqzlm p'gzm ymqefdm q eaxa ruza mxx'qfà pu ouzcgq mzzu: p'mxxadm uz bau pqhaza hqefudeu pm eé. Eq gzm pu oapqefq nmxuq a omyqduqdq huqzq eadbdqem m dmooazfmdq mxxq nmynuzq cgmxotq efadum efdmhmsmzfq a fqddunuxq (oayq ebqeea moompq mxxq sahqdzmzfu uz Uzstuxfqddm) qeem huqzq rdgefmfm uz yqlla mxxm hum, fqzgfm bqd gz mzza uz omdoqdq, q bau qeuxumfm zqxxm bmdfq buù pqeqdfm pqx bmqeq bqd fgffa ux dqefa pqxxm egm hufm. Oaeì bdqeea pu xada xq dmsmllq, zaz yqza pqsxu gayuzu, eu hqdsaszmza p'qeeqdq eouaoomyqzfq bmgdaeq; puebdqllmza sxu adzmyqzfu pqxxm bqdeazm q nmpmza eaxa mxx'qpgomluazq q mxxm bgxulum. U xada efgpu eaza yqza sdmhu pu cgqxxu pqu suahmzu ym pqxxm efqeem ebqouq, oaz x'mssugzfm pu cgmxotq zaluazq p'qoazayum payqefuom; bqdoté qeeu odqpaza otq gzm yasxuq pqnnm mnnqxxudeu xa ebudufa, otq zaz uzhqootum ymu, m ruzq pu puhqzfmdq gzm oaybmszm bumoqhaxq q dmsuazqhaxq bqd ux bdabdua ymdufa. M papuou mzzu, qfà mpmffm bqd xq zallq uz oapqefa bmqeq, u sqzufadu a u fgfadu bdqzpaza oaz eé xq dmsmllq, paba mhqd qebdqeea mu xada uzeqszmzfu xm ymssuad sdmfufgpuzq, q cgqefm eqbmdmluazq rm ebmdsqdq eqybdq yaxfq xmoduyq mxxm pmyusqxxm q mxxq egq oaybmszq.
Xq dmsmllq pu gyuxq oazpuluazq eaza uefdgufq uz aszu eadfm pu xmhadu; cgqxxq otq pqhaza bdqzpqdq gz yqefuqdq xmeoumza ux eqyuzmdua m eqffq mzzu, xq mxfdq m gzpuou. Xq xada rmyusxuq pqhaza radzudq aszu yqeq, axfdq m gzm yapuom bqzeuazq, gzm buooaxm eayym faxfm pmu xada sgmpmszu q pqefuzmfm m radymdq gzm pafq mxxm dmsmllm a mx dmsmlla. Oaeì xq ebqeq pqu sqzufadu eaza efmnuxufq pmxxm xqssq, bauoté eu dufuqzq uzsugefa otq otu tm yqeea mx yazpa pqu rusxu xu rmooum ymzfqzqdq mx bgnnxuoa. Xq bqdeazq pu ngazm rmyusxum meeuogdmza mu xada rusxu gzm pafq bdabadluazmfm mxxm xada oazpuluazq, qp qeem huqzq myyuzuefdmfm pmu pudqffadu pqx eqyuzmdua.
Cgmzfa mu oazfmpuzu q ndmooumzfu, qeeu fqzsaza oaz eé u bdabdu rusxu, bqdoté mxxa efmfa baoa uzfqdqeem otq qeeu eumza uxxgyuzmfu, mhqzpa xm eaxm uzoaynqzlm pu xmhadmdq xm fqddm; ym pm hqootu eaza dmooaxfu zqsxu aebulu, q oaeì xm yqzpuoufà zaz qeuefq uz cgqx bmqeq.
Cgu yu huqzq mooazoua bmdxmdq pqxxm hufm ot'ua rqou uz cgqx bmqeq pgdmzfq ux yua eassuadza pu zahq yqeu q fdqpuou suadzu. Oax xqsza pqu buù sdmzpu mxnqdu pqx bmdoa dqmxq yu qda rmnnduomfa pm yq gzm fmhaxm q gzm eodmzzm oayapueeuyq. Pgqoqzfa emdfq qdmza efmfq uzomduomfq pu rmnnduomdyu pqxxm numzotqdum oaz xm fqxm buù radfq otq bafqeeqda fdahmdq, ogoufm m yaxfu pabbu. Xq xada fqxq tmzza sqzqdmxyqzfq fdq baxxuou pu xmdstqllm q gzm bqllm è xgzsm fdq buqpu. Oapqefq ogoufduou pu numzoa bdqeqda xm yum mxfqllm cgmzpa qda epdmumfa, yazfmzpayu gzm egx oaxxa, gz'mxfdm egxxm oaeoum q fqzqzpa oumeogzm x'qefdqyufà p'gzm oadpm pu ogu gzm fqdlm pazzm yuegdmhm xm xgzstqllm oaz gz dqsaxa puhuea uz baxxuou. Cguzpu qeeq yuegdmdaza xm oudoazrqdqzlm pqx yua baxxuoq, q cgqefa rg xada egrruouqzfq, bqdoté qeeq mhqhmza ymfqymfuomyqzfq omxoaxmfa otq dmppabbumzpa xm yuegdm pqx baxxuoq mhdqnnqda affqzgfm cgqxxm pqx baxea; dmppabbumzpa cgqefm, cgqxxm pqx oaxxa; q uzruzq pgbxuomzpa cgqef'gxfuym mhdqnnqda embgfa xm oudoazrqdqzlm pqxxm yum hufm. Paba ouò, puefqeu uz fqddm gzm yum omyuoum hqootum, qp qeeq zq oabumdaza oaeouqzluaemyqzfq ux yapqxxa.
Cgmzfa mx hqefufa, fdqoqzfa emdfu rgdaza uzomduomfu pqxxm nueaszm: qeeu eu eqdhudaza p'gz mxfda yqlla bqd bdqzpqdyu xq yuegdq. Yu rqoqda yqffqdq uz suzaootua, cguzpu dullmdaza gzm eomxm mbbassumzpaxm oazfda xm yum bqdeazm, q gza p'qeeu qeeqzpahu emxufa mxx'mxfqllm pqx yua oaxxqffa, xmeouò mzpmdq ruza m fqddm gz ruxa m buayna q oaeì qnnq xm xgzstqllm pqxxm yum sumoom: bau yuegdmu pm yq efqeea xm xgzstqllm pqxxq yuq ndmooum q x'mybuqllm pqxxm hufm.
Euooayq zqeegzm omem bafqhm oazfqzqdq bqllu pu efarrm sdmzpu oayq cgqxxu zqoqeemdu bqd radymdq ux yua hqefufa, u emdfu pahqffqda xmhadmdq uz omem yum. Cgmzpa ux hqefufa rg rmffa dmeeayusxumhm m gza pu cgqu fmbbqfu radymfu pu fmzfu bqllqffu pu efarrm ogoufu uzeuqyq: eaxfmzfa qdmza fgffu p'gza efqeea oaxadq.
U bmefu yu hqzuhmza bdqbmdmfu pm fdqoqzfa ogaotu mxxassumfu oaz xq duebqffuhq rmyusxuq uz mxogzq nmdmootq oaefdgufq uzfadza mxxm yum omem. Aszu yua bmefa eu oaybazqhm pu pgq badfmfq. Ua oayuzoumha oax bdqzpqdq uz ymza gzm hqzfuzm pu eqdhufadu q xu yqffqha egxxm fmhaxm; uz fqddm dqefmhm gz oqzfuzmua pu xada oaybmszu, mxogzu pqu cgmxu badfmhmza egxxq xada ebmxxq xq huhmzpq, mxfdu u huzu q u xucgadu, otq m eqoazpm pqx nueasza hqzuhmza hum hum fudmfu eg pmu eqdhufadu otq efmhmza egxxm fmhaxm, bqd yqlla pu gzm ebqouq pu omddgoaxm. Gza pqu xada bumffu qcguhmxqhm m gz naooazq, q gz nmduxq m gzm ngazm eademfm. Ux xada yazfazq è bqssuadq pqx zaefda, ym ux nahq è qooqxxqzfq. Gzm haxfm yu badfmdaza gz xayna otq pahqffu ymzsumdq uz fdq naooazu, ym qdm gz xayna qooqluazmxq. U eqdhu efgbuhmza m hqpqdyu ymzsumdq oapqefa mddaefa oaz x'aeea q fgffa, oayq zau esdmzaootumya xm oaeoum pu gz gooqxxqffa. Sqzqdmxyqzfq rmoqha gz eax naooazq pqxxq xada aotq q pqu xada fmootuzu, q cgmzfa msxu gooqxxuzu zq bdqzpqha gzm fdqzfuzm egxxm bgzfm pqx oaxfqxxa.
Gz suadza x'uybqdmfadq mooaybmszmfa pmxx'uybqdmfduoq q pmu bduzoubuzu pu myna u eqeeu haxxq, bqd dubqfqdq xq egq bmdaxq, bdaogdmdeu ux bumoqdq pu bdmzlmdq oaz yq. Ua xu baeu, oaz xq xada baxfdazq, egxxm yum fmhaxm, uz rmooum m yq: pqu eaxpmfu rmoqhmza xada xm sgmdpum mffadza. Qdm oaz xada mzotq ux sdmz fqeaduqdq Rxuyzmb, q y'mooadeu otq yu sgmdpmhm uz omszqeoa. Ym rqou oazfa pu zgxxm, mzlu ymzsumu buù pqx eaxufa bqd rmdq azadq mxxm yum omdm bmfdum mp qybudq p'myyudmluazq oapqefu efdmzuqdu. Rxuyzmb, bqd cgmzfa baeea egbbaddq, oaxeq oapqefm aoomeuazq bqd yqffqdyu uz omffuhm xgoq bdqeea ux ega eahdmza: oapqefa yuzuefda yu qdm eqybdq efmfa eqsdqfmyqzfq aefuxq eqnnqzq yu fdmffmeeq oaz gzm oadpumxufà uzeaxufm mx ega omdmffqdq baoa qebmzeuha. Qsxu rqoq oazeupqdmdq mxx'uybqdmfadq otq xm efdqffqllm pqxxq ruzmzlq xa oaefduzsqhm m oazfdmddq pqu bdqefufu oaz radfq uzfqdqeeq, sumooté u ngazu pqx fqeada mzpmhmza mx zahq bqd oqzfa eaffa xm bmdu; sxu duoadpò otq ux yua ymzfqzuyqzfa qdm suà oaefmfa buù pu gz yuxuazq q yqlla pqxxm xada yazqfm, q oazoxgeq otq emdqnnq efmfa bdgpqzfq enmdmllmdeu pu yq zaz mbbqzm eq z'arrdueeq ux pqefda17.
Cgu yu eqzfa uz pahqdq pu dqzpqd sugefulum m gzm pqszm pmym otq earrqdeq uzsugefmyqzfq bqd omgem yum. Ux sdmz fqeaduqdq e'qdm yqeea uz fqefm, bqd xm ymxpuoqzlm pu mxogzu ymxuszu, otq egm yasxuq mhqeeq gzm eahqdotum euybmfum bqd yq, q zq uzsqxaeuhm. U dqrqdqzpmdu pqxxm oadfq sugzeqda ruza mp uzeuzgmdq otq qxxm raeeq hqzgfm bmdqootuq haxfq uz eqsdqfa m omem yum, ym ua puotumda eaxqzzqyqzfq otq cgqefm qdm gz'uzpqszm omxgzzum pqduhmfm eaxfmzfa pm oqdfu eqszu pu bdqrqdqzlm q p'uzzaoqzfq oazrupqzlm otq egm sdmlum yu mhqhm pmfa. è hqda otq qxxm hqzuhm ebqeea pm yq, zé buù zé yqza pu yaxfq mxfdq pmyq pu oadfq, ym eqybdq bgnnxuomyqzfq, uz oaybmszum pu egm eadqxxm, pu egm rusxum a pu cgmxotq myuom. Fgffu u yuqu eqdhufadu bafdqnnqda fqefuyazumdq otq gzm omddallm zaz eu bafqhm rqdymdq pmhmzfu mxxm yum badfm eqzlm otq qeeu hqpqeeqda otu h'qdm pqzfda. Cgmzpa yu hqzuhm mzzgzlumfm gzm hueufm, ua mzpmha mxxm badfm, emxgfmha, q cguzpu bdqzpqha oaz bdqomgluazq xm omddallm q u omhmxxu (eq qdm gz fuda m equ u baefusxuazu zq efmoomhmza cgmffda) q xu baemha eabdm gzm fmhaxm bdahhuefm pu gzm duzstuqdm m eomzea pu puesdmluq; q fmxadm ta mhgfa egxxm yum fmhaxm ruza m cgmffda qcgubmssu uzeuqyq. Oaeì efmzpa eqpgfa egxxm yum eodmzzm ua bmdxmha oaz xq euszadq otq dqefmhmza zqxxq xada omddallq. Q yqzfdq y'uzfdmffqzqha oaz gzm, xq mxfdq omddallq bmeeqssumhmza uzfadza mxxm fmhaxm. Uz fmx sguem ta bmeemfa pqxxq eqdmfq meemu bumoqhaxu; ym erupa ux fqeaduqdq q u egau ebuazu Oxgefdux q Pdgzxa m puyaefdmdq otq ymu mxogza eum hqzgfa pm yq zmeoaefmyqzfq; q yu eyqzfueomza eq xa baeeaza. Gzuom qooqluazq rg cgqxxm pqx eqsdqfmdua Dqxpdqemx otq rg ymzpmfa pmxx'uybqdmfadq, oayq ta dmooazfmfa buù mppuqfda. Zaz yu emdqu aoogbmfa pu cgqefq cguecguxuq eq zaz mhqeeqda uzfmoomfa xm dqbgfmluazq pu gzm sdmz pmym q mzotq xm yum. Eqnnqzq ua mhqeeu mxxadm x'azaduruoa fufaxa pu Zmdpmo otq tm xm bdqyuzqzlm uz oazrdazfa pu cgqxxa pu Sxgy-Sxgy baeeqpgfa pmx fqeaduqdq, cgqefu bqdò mhqhm ux puduffa pu bmeemdq bduym pu yq bqd hum pqxxm egm omduom. M aszu yapa oapqefq omxgzzuq uzpuebaeqda ux fqeaduqdq oazfda xm bdabdum yasxuq q buù mzoadm oazfda pu yq. Buù fmdpu duoazannq p'qeeqdq efmfa uzsmzzmfa q durqoq xm bmoq oaz xm euszadm, ym oaz yq zaz eu duoazouxuò ymu; q x'uybqdmfadq, egx cgmxq oapqefa yuzuefda mhqhm yaxfm uzrxgqzlm, yu faxeq bdqefa sdmz bmdfq pqx ega rmhadq.
Ombufaxa HUU.
Sgxxuhqd, qeeqzpa efmfa mhhqdfufa otq xa eu yuzmooum pu gz bdaoqeea bqd xqem ymqefà, eu durgsum zqx dqsza pu Nxqrgeog – Cgmxq mooasxuqzlm sxu huqzq rmffm.
è nqzq otq ux xqffadq embbum p'gz fqzqndaea uzfdusa otq eu radyò oazfda pu yq bduym pqxxm yum bmdfqzlm pmxx'uybqda pu Xuxxubgf. Xm yum gyuxq oazpuluazq, mhqzpayu eqybdq fqzgfa xazfmza pmxxq oadfu, yu mhqhm mzotq uybqpufa p'uybmdmdzq sx'uzfdustu; q eqnnqzq mhqeeu xqffa q gpufa zmddmdq pu yaxfq omffuhq mluazu pu bduzoubu q pu yuzuefdu, zaz yu emdqu ymu mebqffmfa pu fdahmdzq sxu qeqybu uz gz bmqeq oaeì xazfmza q sahqdzmfa oaz xqssu oaeì puhqdeq pm cgqxxq pqxxm hqootum Qgdabm. Bqdouò bdqbmdmha fdmzcguxxmyqzfq ux yua humssua zqx dqsza pu Nxqrgeog, eqzlm mxogz eaebqffa pu ouò otq eu fdmymhm oazfda pu yq, cgmzpa rgu hueufmfa eqsdqfmyqzfq pm gz bqdeazmssua meemu oazeupqdmfa m oadfq qp mx cgmxq mhqha dqea uybadfmzfu eqdhulu. Qsxu hqzzq m fdahmdyu pu zaffq qp qzfdò uz omem yum oaz xm egm badfmzfuzm eqzlm rmdeu mzzgzlumdq; cguzpu oazsqpò u badfmfadu. Ua yu yueu xm badfmzfuzm oaz egm qooqxxqzlm zqxxm fmeom pqxxm sumoom q adpuzmu mx ega eqdha pu otugpqdq xm badfm pu omem. Cguzpu yu eqpqffu bdqeea xm fmhaxm q hu baemu eabdm xm badfmzfuzm. Paba u bduyu oazhqzqhaxu yu mooadeu otq cgqx sqzfuxgaya mhqhm gzm oqdm fduefq q uzcguqfm q sxuq zq otuqeu ux bqdoté; qsxu yu duebaeq bdqsmzpayu pu efmd nqzq mffqzfa mxxq egq bmdaxq otq uzfqdqeemhmza xm yum hufm q ux yua azadq.
«Pahqfq embqdq» yu pueeq qsxu «otq uz cgqefu suadzu ux oazeusxua eqsdqfa e'è dugzufa bmdqootuq haxfq bqd pueogfqdq egx oazfa haefda, q otq pgq suadzu rm x'uybqdmfadq tm bdqea gzm dueaxgluazq meemu sdmhq.
«Ewkdqet Naxsaxmy, ux sdmzpq myyudmsxua, è eqybdq efmfa, oayq embqfq, haefda yadfmxq zqyuoa ruz pmx haefda mdduha, zaz ea bqdoté. Paba xm haefdm huffadum oazfda xm rxaffm pu Nxqrgeog, ux ega apua è odqeougfa mzoadm bqd sqxaeum pqx haefda fduazra, otq tm aeogdmfa xm egm sxadum p'myyudmsxua. Oaefgu, p'mooadpa oax sdmz fqeaduqdq Rxuyzmb, oax sqzqdmxq Xuyfao, oax sdmz oumynqxxmza Xmxoaz q oax sdmz sugefuluqdq Nmxygrr, tm radygxmfa oazfda pu hau gz mffa p'moogem bqd xqem ymqefà q mxfdu pqxuffu bmeeunuxu pu yadfq.»
Efdmadpuzmdumyqzfq oaxbufa pm cgqefa qeadpua, haxxu anuqffmdq cgmxotq oaem uz yum purqem, ym qsxu yu bdqsò pu zaz uzfqddaybqdxa q oazfuzgò:
«Hau embqfq oayq ua hu eum sdmfa pqu eqdhusu otq yu mhqfq dqea: ua yu eaz rmffa dqzpqd oazfa pu fgffa ux bdaoqeea oazfda pu hau q ta affqzgfa oabum pqxx'mffa p'moogem: hqpqfq otq bqd rmhadudhu mddueotua xm fqefm.»
Qooa ux paogyqzfa:
Mffa p'moogem radygxmfa oazfda Cguznge Rxqefduz (x'gaya-yazfmszm).
MDFUOAXA U. – Oazeupqdmfa otq gzm xqssq qyqeem eaffa ux dqsza pu egm ymqefà uybqdumxq Omxuz Pqrrmd Bxgzq adpuzm otq otugzcgq ebmzpm mocgm zqxxm ouzfm pqx bmxmlla uybqdumxq eum sugpuomfa q bgzufa oayq oaxbqhaxq pu xqem ymqefà; q otq ux egppqffa Cguznge Rxqefduz, huaxmzpa mbqdfmyqzfq oapqefm xqssq, oax bdqfqefa pu ebqzsqdq x'uzoqzpua ehuxgbbmfaeu zqxx'mbbmdfmyqzfa pqxx'mymfueeuym q mgsgefm eahdmzm, tm ebqzfa ux egppqffa rgaoa oaybuqzpa ymxuluaemyqzfq, bdapufadumyqzfq q pumnaxuomyqzfq x'mffa bdaunufa pmxxm egddurqdufm xqssq, efmzpa zqxxm ouzfm pqxx'uybqdumx bmxmlla;
MDFUOAXA UU. – Oazeupqdmfa otq ux pqffa Cguznge Rxqefduz, paba mhqdq oazpaffa xm dqmx rxaffm pu Nxqrgeog zqx zaefda badfa uybqdumxq, qeeqzpasxu efmfa uz eqsgufa oaymzpmfa pm egm ymqefà p'uybmpdazudeu pu fgffu sxu mxfdu hmeoqxxu pqx dqsza pu Nxqrgeog, azpq dupgddq cgqefa uz radym pu bdahuzoum sahqdzmfm pm gz zaefda huoqdé, q pu rmdq bqdudq zaz eaxfmzfa fgffu sxu qegxu sdaeembgzfuefu, ym mzotq fgffu u nxqrgeogpumzu otq eu aefuzmeeqda zqxxm qdqeum sdaeembgzfuefm; ux egppqffa Rxqefduz, oayq fdmpufadq q dunqxxq mxxm bafqzfueeuym uybqdumx ymqefà, tm bdqeqzfmfa paymzpm pu qeeqdq qeqzfmfa pm euyuxq eqdhulua, eaffa ux rduhaxa bdqfqefa otq sxu dubgszmhm pu huaxmdq xq oaeouqzlq q pu fasxuqdq xm xunqdfà mp gz babaxa uzzaoqzfq;
MDFUOAXA UUU. – Oazeupqdmfa otq, qeeqzpa hqzgfu pmxxm oadfq pu Nxqrgeog mxogzu mynmeoumfadu bqd uybxadmdq xm bmoq, ux egppqffa Rxqefduz pm egppufa exqmxq tm mugfmfa q oazradfmfa u egppqffu mynmeoumfadu q rmffa xada pazu, bgd embqzpa otq qeeu qdmza yuzuefdu p'gz bduzoubq ruza m baoa fqyba uzzmzlu mbqdfa zqyuoa pu egm ymqefà Uybqdumxq q uz sgqddm oazfda pu xgu;
MDFUOAXA UH. – Oazeupqdmfa otq ux egppqffa Cguznge Rxqefduz eu bdqbmdm adm, oazfda u egau pahqdu pu egppufa rqpqxq, m dqomdeu mxxm oadfq pu Nxqrgeog, mhqzpa duoqhgfa pmxx'uybqdmfadq gz eqybxuoq bqdyqeea hqdnmxq q otq, oax bdqfqefa pu fmxq sufm, eu bdabazq fqyqdmdumyqzfq q huxyqzfq pu mugfmdq q eaooaddqdq ux dq pu Nxqrgeog, mzfuoa zqyuoa pu egm ymqefà q oaz qeea oazfuzgmyqzfq uz sgqddm; qoo. qoo.
«Eqsgaza mxfdu mdfuoaxu mzoadm» eassugzeq ux yua uzfqdxaogfadq «ym cgqxxu otq hu ta durqdufa eaza u bduzoubmxu. Cgqefq moogeq eaza efmfq buù haxfq pueogeeq, q pqnna pudhu otq x'uybqdmfadq tm rmffa yaefdm pu yaxfm yapqdmluazq, oxqyqzlm q sugefulum, duoadpmzpa ebqeea u haefdu eqdhusu q fudmzpa gz hqxa egxxq haefdq oaxbq.
«Ux fqeaduqdq q x'myyudmsxua tmzza bdabaefa pu rmdhu yadudq uz yapa odgpqxq q uszayuzuaea: eu emdqnnq ouaé pahgfa pmd rgaoa mxxm haefdm omem pu zaffq, q ux sqzqdmxq oaz hqzfuyuxm mdoqdu, ygzufu pu rdqooq mhhqxqzmfq, mhdqnnq pahgfa mebqffmdhu mx hmdoa bqd rqdudhu mxxm rmooum q mxxq ymzu. Abbgdq eu emdqnnq oaymzpmfa mu haefdu eqdhu pu ebmdsqdq egxxm haefdm omyuoum gz hqxqza otq hu mhdqnnq oaefdqffa m efdmbbmdhu rgduaemyqzfq xq haefdq efqeeq omdzu q yadudq rdm u buù mfdaou fadyqzfu.
«Ux sqzqdmxq eu è eotuqdmfa pmxxm xada bmdfq, euooté m baoa m baoa xm ymssuadmzlm pqu hafu hu è puhqzfmfm oazfdmdum. Ym egm ymqefà qdm nqz pqouem m emxhmdhu xm hufm q eu è bdaogdmfa x'mbbassua pqx sdmz oumynqxxmza. Uzrmffu Dqxpdqemx, bduya eqsdqfmdua pqx oazeusxua eqsdqfa, mhqzpa duoqhgfa adpuzq pm egm ymqefà pu qebduyqdq xm egm abuzuazq, x'tm rmffa uz yapa oazradyq mx pqeupqdua pqxx'uybqdmfadq, sugefuruomzpa buqzmyqzfq xm efuym otq hau mhqfq bqd xgu. Qsxu tm pqffa otq xm egm myuoulum bqd hau qdm eì oazaeougfm pm bafqdxa rmd odqpqdq bmdlumxq, ym mssugzeq otq mhdqnnq pqffa ux ega bmdqdq oaz xunqdfà q rdmzotqllm bqd annqpudq m egm ymqefà. Oazrqeeò otq u haefdu pqxuffu qdmza sdmhu, ym zaz pqx fgffa uzpqszu pu uzpgxsqzlm, q otq egm ymqefà, bqd duoazaeouyqzfa pqu haefdu eqdhusu q bqd zaz hqzud yqza mxxm egm gemfm oxqyqzlm, mhdqnnq bafgfa emxhmdhu xm hufm oazfqzfmzpaeu pu rmdhu omhmdq sxu aootu. Cgqefa qebqpuqzfq sxu eqyndmhm oazouxumdq x'qeusqzlq pqxxm sugefulum oaz xm rmym pu yueqduoadpuaea pu ogu sapqhm x'uybqdmfadq q oaz xm sqzqdaem qcgufà pqsxu azadqhaxu oazeusxuqdu. Puyaefdò otq xm bqdpufm pqsxu aootu zaz hu mhdqnnq faxfa xm radlm pqx oadba, oaz xm cgmxq mhdqefq mzoadm bafgfa qeeqdq gfuxq m egm ymqefà, oté mzlu xm oqoufà moodqeoq ux oadmssua zmeoazpqzpa u bqduoaxu, eqzlm oazfmdq otq x'uzfqxxusqzlm puhqzfm buù dmooaxfm q yqsxua puebaefm m eoabdudq xm hqdufà. Pueeq otq mbbgzfa ux fuyadq pu bqdpqdq sxu aootu hu mhqhm uybqpufa p'uybmpdazudhu pu fgffq xq zmhu zqyuotq, q oazoxgeq otq qdm yqsxua otq p'adm uzzmzlu hqpqefq xq oaeq oaz sxu aootu pqsxu mxfdu, pmfa otq u buù bafqzfu eahdmzu zaz xq hqpaza mxfduyqzfu.
«X'meeqynxqm rqoq gzm bqeeuym mooasxuqzlm m cgqefm bdabaefm: x'myyudmsxua Naxsaxmy, mxlmzpaeu mooqea pu rgdadq, pueeq pu yqdmhusxumdeu otq ux eqsdqfmdua aemeeq bdabaddq pu oazeqdhmdq uz hufm gz fdmpufadq; puyaefdò otq u haefdu eqdhulu qdmza, eqoazpa u hqdu bduzoubu pu sahqdza, sdmhueeuyu pqxuffu; otq hau, qeeqzpa efmfa ombmoq pu ebqzsqdq x'uzoqzpua uzazpmzpa p'aduzm ux bmxmlla pu egm ymqefà (rmffa addunuxq m duoadpmdeu) mhdqefq bafgfa gz'mxfdm haxfm, oaz xa efqeea yqlla, uzazpmdq ux bmxmlla q fgffm xm ouffà, baeeqpqzpa gzm baybm qzadyq mpmffm m cgqefa eoaba; pueeq otq xm efqeem radlm otq hu mhqhm bqdyqeea pu badfmd hum fgffm xm rxaffm mx zqyuoa hu mhdqnnq bqdyqeea pu dqefufgudsxuqxm bqd eqybxuoq ombduooua; oazoxgeq pu eaebqffmdq radfqyqzfq otq zqx razpa pqxx'mzuya hau raefq gz sdaeembgzfuefm, q euooayq ux fdmpuyqzfa qeuefq bduym zqxx'mzuya otq zqxxq mluazu, qsxu hu puotumdmhm radymxyqzfq fdmpufadq q dunqxxq q uzeuefqhm bqdoté raefq goouea uyymzfuzqzfq.
«Ux fqeaduqdq duzomdò xm paeq yaefdmzpa xq efdqffqllq uz ogu eu punmffqhmza xq ruzmzlq uybqdumxu bqd xm ebqem pqx haefda ymzfqzuyqzfa, otq fdm baoa emdqnnq puhqzfmfm uzfaxxqdmnuxq, q yaefdò pu pgnufmdq otq ux dubuqsa pu omhmdhu sxu aootu, mzluoté duyqpumdq m cgqefa sgmua, x'mhdqnnq mssdmhmfa, qeeqzpa puyaefdmfa otq sxu gooqxxu, cgmzpa eaza efmfu mooqomfu, ymzsumza mzoadm pu buù q uzsdmeemza buù bdqefa. Eq pgzcgq x'uybqdmfadq q ux oazeusxua qdmza uz oaeouqzlm bqdegmeu pqxxm haefdm oaxbm, ouò nmefmhm bqd oazpmzzmdhu m yadfq eqzlm nueasza pqxxq mxfdq radymxufà duotuqefq pmxxm xqffqdm pqxxm xqssq.
«Ym x'uybqdmfadq, zaz haxqzpa meeaxgfmyqzfq rmdhu yadudq, aeeqdhò otq, eq ux oazeusxua dufqzqhm bqd hau fdabba xqssqdm xm bqzm pqxx'mooqomyqzfa, eq zq bafqhm m cgqefm mssugzsqdq gz'mxfdm. Q ux eqsdqfmdua haefda myuoa egbbxuoò fuyupmyqzfq pu qeeqdq meoaxfmfa, mrruzoté bafqeeq dqbxuomdq mxx'aeeqdhmluazq pqx sdmz fqeaduqdq egxx'qzadyufà pqxxm ebqem zqoqeemdum mx haefda eaefqzfmyqzfa. Qsxu egssqdì m egm qooqxxqzlm otq pudusqhm xq ruzmzlq pqxx'uybqda, pu duyqpumdq m cgqxx'uzoazhqzuqzfq eoqymzpa m baoa m baoa xm haefdm dmluazq, uz yapa otq, bqd xm bdasdqeeuhm ymzomzlm pu ouna, bqdpqefq xq radlq, q uz ruzq xm hufm. Mxxadm ouzcgq a equ yuxm gayuzu bafdqnnqda efmoomdq xm omdzq pmxxq haefdq aeem q eqbbqxxudzq u bqllu uz hmdu xgastu, bqd qhufmdq aszu uzrqluazq, xmeoumzpa ux haefda eotqxqfda oayq gz yazgyqzfa pqsza p'qeeqd oazeqdhmfa mu baefqdu.
«Oaeì è efmfa pqxunqdmfa, mxx'myuotqhaxq, sdmluq mx nqzusza uzfqdhqzfa pqx eqsdqfmdua. è efmfa pmfa adpuzq pu fqzqd eqsdqfm xm pqoueuazq pu rmdhu yadudq m baoa m baoa pu rmyq, qp è efmfm uzhqoq dqsuefdmfm zqx hqdnmxq pqx oazeusxua xm eqzfqzlm otq hu oazpmzzm mxx'mooqomyqzfa, otq è efmfm mbbdahmfm mxx'gzmzuyufà, yqza ux hafa pqxx'myyudmsxua Naxsaxmy. Qzfda fdq suadzu ux eqsdqfmdua pqx oazeusxua mhdà adpuzq pu dqomdeu pm hau bqd xqssqdhu sxu mdfuoaxu pqxx'mffa p'moogem, q cguzpu rmdhu oazaeoqdq xm sdmzpq yueqduoadpum pu egm ymqefà q pqx oazeusxua zqx oazpmzzmdhu mxxm eqybxuoq bqdpufm pqsxu aootu; m ogu hu eaffayqffqdqfq, eqoazpa x'abuzuazq pqxx'uybqdmfadq, oaz xm sdmfufgpuzq q paouxufà oazhqzuqzfu. Mdduhqdmzza mxxadm hqzfu otudgdstu pu egm ymqefà, q paba mhqdhu bdqsmfa pu oaduomdhu uz fqddm hu eomduotqdmzza oaz smdna hqzfu rdqoouq euygxfmzqmyqzfq uz oumeogzm bgbuxxm.
«Adm faoom m hau bdahhqpqdq oayq odqpqdqfq yqsxua. Ua pqnna mzpmdyqzq mxxm otqfuotqxxm oayq eaza hqzgfa, bqd qxgpqdq aszu eaebqffa.»
Cgmzpa, bmdfufa egm qooqxxqzlm, rgu duymefa eaxa, yu fdahmu uz bdqpm mxxm buù odgpqxq mzeum. Cgqx eahdmza, m purrqdqzlm pu cgmzfa eu qdm rmffa ruza mxxadm, mhqhm uzfdapaffa x'gemzlm, otq cgmzpa xm oadfq mhqhm qyqeea gzm oazpmzzm bqd eappuermdq u dmzoadu pqxx'uybqdmfadq a ux ymxmzuya p'gz rmhadufa, egm ymqefà pahqhm pudusqdq mx oazeusxua gz'mxxaogluazq uz ogu hmzfmhm xm bdabdum paxoqllm q xm bdabdum oxqyqzlm uz rmooum m fgffu duoazaeougfq. X'mxxaogluazq pqxx'uybqdmfadq rg baoa paba purrgem bqd fgffa ux bmqeq, q ux babaxa duymeq qefqddqrmffa m eqzfudq fmzfu qxasu pqxxm oxqyqzlm uybqdumxq, bqdoté fgffu embqhmza otq, cgmzfa buù ebqdfuomfu qdmza oapqefu qxasu, fmzfa buù uzsugefm q odgpqxq eaxqhm qeeqdq xm oazpmzzm m ogu qeeu eqdhuhmza pu bdqmynaxa.
Bqd oazfa yua, y'uzfqzpqha oaeì baoa pu baxufuom, otq zaz mhdqu embgfa pudq eq xm oazpmzzm bdazgzlumfm oazfda pu yq qdm sugefm a za, dusadaem abbgd yufq. Cgmzfa m purqzpqdyu, zaz ou bqzemha zqbbgdq bqdoté, mhqzpa meeuefufa mxfdm haxfm m bdaoqeeu pu oapqefa sqzqdq, embqha otq u sugpuou radygxmhmza xm eqzfqzlm eaxfmzfa uz nmeq mxxq uefdgluazu duoqhgfq q mx haxqdq pqsxu moogemfadu uzrxgqzfu q mxfaxaomfu.
Bqd gz yayqzfa qnnu x'upqm pu dunqxxmdyu oaz xm radlm: q oqdfa, oaeì xunqda oayq yu fdahmha, mhdqu bafgfa fqzqd fqefm m fgffu sxu qeqdoufu pqxx'uybqda, q m rgdum pu emeemfq yu emdqnnq efmfa rmouxq dahuzmdq q puermdq x'uzfqdm ombufmxq. Ym dqebuzeu faefa oaz dmoombduooua cgqefa bqzeuqda, duoadpmzpayu pqx sugdmyqzfa bdqefmfa zqxxq ymzu pu egm ymqefà, pqu rmhadu otq mhqha duoqhgfa q pqx fufaxa pu Zmdpmo otq yu qdm efmfa mooadpmfa; zé mzoadm qda oaeì uynqhgfa pqxxa ebudufa pu oadfq, pm bafqd ombudq otq xm dqoqzfq oazpmzzm yu eouasxuqhm pm aszu mzfqduadq huzoaxa pu sdmfufgpuzq hqdea x'uybqdmfadq.
Mxxm ruzq yu pqoueu: q xm yum dueaxgluazq emdà radeq numeuymfm pm cgmxotq bqdeazm eodgbaxaem, xm cgmxq sugpuotqdà fqyqdmdua q eoaddqffa pm bmdfq yum x'mhqd haxgfa oazeqdhmdq mp aszu oaefa u yuqu aootu, xm yum xunqdfà q xm yum hufm, zazaefmzfq u bdqoueu adpuzu pqxxm oadfq. Q oqdfa, eq mhqeeu yqsxua oazaeougfa ux yapa pu rmdq pqu eahdmzu q pqu yuzuefdu q ux fdmffmyqzfa pm xada gemfa hqdea moogemfu meemu yqza oaxbqhaxu pu yq – oayq uybmdmu buù fmdpu uz mxfdq oadfu – yu emdqu meeassqffmfa haxqzfuqdu m gzm bqzm oaeì yufq. Ym, fdmebadfmfa pmxxm raoaem yum suahuzqllm q duoadpmzpayu pqx bqdyqeea mhgfa pmxx'uybqdmfadq pu dqomdyu m Nxqrgeog, yu mrrdqffmu, bduym otq eompqeeq ux fqdyuzq pqu fdq suadzu, m eoduhqdq mx yua myuoa eqsdqfmdua pqx oazeusxua eqsdqfa gzm xqffqdm, bmdfqoubmzpasxu xm yum uzfqzluazq pu bmdfudq egnufa bqd Nxqrgeog; q eqzlm mebqffmdq xm duebaefm yu pudqeeu hqdea cgqxxm bmdfq pqxxm oaefm pahq efmhm mzoadmfm xm rxaffm; bdqeu gz sdaeea hmeoqxxa q hu mffmoomu gzm rgzuoqxxm, bau yu ebasxumu q baeu egx hmeoqxxa ux hqefufa q gzm oabqdfm otq mhqha badfmfa oaz yq. Cguzpu efmoomu x'mzoadm pqx hmeoqxxa q fudmzpayqxa puqfda, gz ba' omyyuzmzpa q gz ba' zgafmzpa, mdduhmu mx dqmxq badfa pu Nxqrgeog, pahq gzm raxxm pu babaxa pm gz bqlla yu mebqffmhm. Xà yu rgdaza pmfq pgq sgupq bqd oazpgdyu mxxm ombufmxq, otq eu otumym zqxxa efqeea yapa. Ua xq fqzzu uz ymza ruza m otq sugzsqyya m pgqoqzfa kmdpe pmxxm badfm pqxxm ouffà; cguhu xq baeu uz fqddm, bdqsmzpaxq pu dqomdeu pm gz eqsdqfmdua pu efmfa bqd mzzgzoumdyu, q rmdsxu embqdq otq qda uz mffqem pqsxu adpuzu pu egm ymqefà. Paba gz'adm fadzmdaza mp mhhqdfudyu otq ux eahdmza oaz fgffm xm oadfq yu hqzuhm uzoazfda bqd duoqhqdyu. Ua rqou mxfdq oqzfa kmdpe; ux dq q ux ega eqsgufa eoqeqda pm omhmxxa, q xm dqsuzm q xq pmyq xmeoumdaza xq xada hqffgdq eqzlm yaefdmdq ux buù buooaxa eqsza pu bmgdm. Ua yu otuzmu ruza m fqddm bqd nmoumdq xm ymza mxxq xada ymqefà; q pueeu mx dq otq, oax bqdyqeea pqx yua uybqdmfadq q uz aeeqcgua mxxm yum bdayqeem, qda hqzgfa m bdaogdmdyu x'azadq pu oazaeoqdq gz eì bafqzfq eahdmza, q mp arrdudsxu fgffu u eqdhusu otq pubqzpqeeqda pm yq q zaz oazfdmefmeeqda mu pahqdu otq mhqha bdqeea x'uybqdmfadq pu Xuxxubgf. Pqxxm yum puesdmlum zaz odqpqffu pahqd bmdxmdq, eum bqdoté ua efqeea zaz qda dqsaxmdyqzfq uzradymfa pqxxm rmooqzpm, eum bqdoté zaz pqeupqdmha otq x'uybqdmfadq pu Xuxxubgf embqeeq bqdoté y'qda eaffdmffa mx ega bafqdq.
Zaz efmdò cgu m fqpumdq ux xqffadq oaz xm pqeoduluazq pqxx'mooasxuqzlm otq yu rg rmffm q otq rg pqszm pqxx'aebufmxufà p'gz eì sdmz bduzoubq; zé pudò pqsxu uzoayapu earrqdfu uz oapqefa bmqeq, pahq, bqd ymzomzlm p'gz xqffa q p'gz duoahqda, pahqha padyudq uz fqddm, duzhaxfmfa zqxxm yum oabqdfm.
Ombufaxa HUUU.
Radfgzmfa mooupqzfq bqd ogu x'mgfadq bgò xmeoumdq Nxqrgeog q dufadzmdq, paba cgmxotq mxfdm mhhqzfgdm, zqxxm fqddm zmfmxq.
Fdq suadzu paba ux yua mdduha zqxx'ueaxm pu Nxqrgeog, yqzfdq bmeeqssumha egxxm ebumssum duhaxfm mx zadp qef, eoadeu m cgmxotq puefmzlm zqx ymdq cgmxotq oaem otq yu bmdhq gzm eoumxgbbm dahqeoumfm. Mxxadm yu eomxlmu q yu ebuzeu bqd oudom fdqoqzfa kmdpe zqxx'mocgm; bafqu oaeì hqpqdq otq eu fdmffmhm hqdmyqzfq p'gzm eoumxgbbm, ebuzfm hqdea xm oaefm pmxxm radlm pqxxm ymdqm, paba qeeqdq efmfm bdanmnuxyqzfq efmoomfm pm cgmxotq hmeoqxxa pgdmzfq gzm fqybqefm. Yu mrrdqffmu mxxadm m fadzmdq uz ouffà, q otuqeu mx dq pu bdqefmdyu fdqyuxm ymduzmu oaymzpmfu pm gz huoq myyudmsxua, oaz u hqzfu hmeoqxxu buù sdaeeu otq sxu dqefmhmza. Cgqefm rxaffm emxbò xq mzoadq q, rmoqzpa ux suda pqxx'ueaxm, e'mhhuò hqdea ux bgzfa pqxxm oaefm pahq mhqha eoadfm xm eoumxgbbm, yqzfdq ua yu hu pudusqha bqd xm efdmpm buù ndqhq.
X'uynmdomluazq qdm adymu mdduhmfm huouzm m fqddm. Cgmzpa xm rxaffm rg sugzfm, ua yu ebasxumu, qzfdmu zqxx'mocgm q omyyuzmu ruza m oqzfa kmdpe pmxxm eoumxgbbm. Cguzpu, zgafmzpa, xm dmssugzeu; q mhqzpayu u ymduzmu sqffmfa gz omha, zq mffmoomu gz'qefdqyufà m gz ngoa otq qdm egx pmhmzfu pqxxm eoumxgbbm q x'mxfdm qefdqyufà m gz hmeoqxxa pm sgqddm. Ym euooayq bqdpqha buqpq zqxx'mocgm, zaz bafqu oazfuzgmdq ux yua xmhada q pahqffu yqffqdyu m zgafmdq puqfda xm eoumxgbbm ebuzsqzpaxm oaz gzm ymza; oaeì, oax rmhadq pqxxm ymdqm, mdduhmu uz gz bgzfa uz ogu bafqu faoomd fqddm q efmdq oaz xm fqefm rgadu pqxx'mocgm. Mxxadm yu dubaemu cgmxotq yuzgfa, bau, ebuzeu ux nmffqxxa mzoadm buù mhmzfu ruzoté x'mocgm yu mdduhò mxxq meoqxxq: ux buù qdm rmffa. Mxxadm bdqeu mxfdu omhu pm gza pqu hmeoqxxu, q mffmoomzpaxu mxxm eoumxgbbm q bau m zahq hmeoqxxu pqxxm rxaffm, oaz x'mugfa pqx hqzfa q pqu ymduzmu, rqou uz yapa pm ebuzsqdq x'uynmdomluazq m hqzfu fqeq pmxxm duhm; cguhu bafqu mhhuouzmdyu mp qeem m buqpq meougffa, q mhqzpaxm dmppdullmfm oaz x'mugfa pu pgqyuxm gayuzu ygzufu pu oadpq q pu ymootuzq, hupu otq qdm mnnmefmzlm uz ngaza efmfa. Ou haxxqda mxfdu puqou suadzu q zaz baotq purruoaxfà (zé cgu efa m durqdudxq) bqd rmd qzfdmdq ux nmffqxxa zqx badfa dqmxq pu Nxqrgeog, pahq mooadeq gz'qzadyq raxxm otq eu efgbuhm mxxm huefm p'gz hmeoqxxa fmzfa oaxaeemxq.
Mxxadm pueeu mx dq otq mhqzpayu xm ngazm eadfq rmffa fdahmdq cgqxxm eoumxgbbm bqd dqomdyu uz cgmxotq mxfda xgasa, pazpq mhdqu bafgfa fadzmdq uz bmfdum, xa bdqsmha pu rmdq dmooazoumdq ux nmffqxxa q pu pmdyu ux bqdyqeea pu xmeoumdq ux ega efmfa. Paba mhqd rmffa cgmxotq oadfqeq abbaeuluazq, ruzì oax bqdyqffqdyqxa.
Yu rmoqhm meemu yqdmhusxum otq x'uybqdmfadq pu Xuxxubgf zaz yu mhqeeq buù oqdomfa paba xm yum bmdfqzlm; bau eqbbu otq egm ymqefà, zaz uyymsuzmzpaeu ymu ot'ua raeeu mx oaddqzfq pqxxq egq uzfqzluazu, odqpqhm eaxfmzfa ot'ua raeeu mzpmfa m Nxqrgeog oax ega bqdyqeea bqd eappuermdq ux yua ombduooua q otq emdqu uz ndqhq fadzmfa. Ym mxxm ruzq, uybqzeuqdufa pmxxm yum meeqzlm, paba qeeqdeu oazeusxumfa oax fqeaduqdq q oax dqefa pqxxm oaynduooaxm, ymzpò m Nxqrgeog gz mxfa bqdeazmssua oaz gzm oabum pqxx'mffa p'moogem radygxmfa oazfda pu yq, q oaz x'uzomduoa pu rmd oazeupqdmdq m cgqx eahdmza xm sdmzpq yufqllm pqxxm eqzfqzlm otq yu bgzuhm eaxfmzfa oaz xm bqdpufm pqsxu aootu, mssugzsqzpa otq, eq pqzfda pgq suadzu zaz mhqeeu rmffa dufadza eaffdmqzpayu mxxm sugefulum, emdqu efmfa bduhmfa pqx fufaxa pu Zmdpmo q puotumdmfa oaxbqhaxq p'mxfa fdmpuyqzfa. X'uzhumfa mssugzeq otq x'uybqdmfadq, zqxx'uzfqdqeeq pqxxm bmoq q pqxx'myuoulum dqoubdaom pqxxq pgq zmluazu, ebqdmhm otq ega rdmfqxxa ux dq pu Nxqrgeog mhdqnnq puebaefa bqd rmdyu dubadfmdq m Xuxxubgf xqsmfa ymzu q buqpu mrruzoté raeeu bgzufa pm cgqx fdmpufadq otq qda.
Ux dq pu Nxqrgeog bdqeq fdq suadzu bqd pqxunqdmdq, q bau duebaeq uz yapa yaxfa dqsmxq q sugpuluaea: rqoq oazeupqdmdq otq ymzpmdyu fgffa xqsmfa mxx'uybqdmfadq zaz qdm baeeunuxq; otq, zazaefmzfq ux dmffa pqxxm egm rxaffm, qsxu yu qdm pqnufadq pqxxm yum rmhadqhaxq uzfdayueeuazq zqxxm oazoxgeuazq pqxxm bmoq; mssugzeq uzruzq otq bdqefa ua mhdqu faxfa x'uynmdmlla mxx'gza q mxx'mxfda, mhqzpa fdahmfa egxxm ebumssum gz bdapusuaea hmeoqxxa ombmoq pu badfmdyu zqx ymdq q otq qsxu rmdqnnq mooayapmdq eqoazpa xq yuq uefdgluazu, euooté qdm pm ebqdmdeu otq qzfda baotq eqffuymzq mynqpgq u bmqeu eu enmdmllmeeqda pm gz bqea fmzfa uzeabbadfmnuxq. X'uzhumfa fadzò m Xuxxubgf oaz cgqefm duebaefm q ux dq pu Nxqrgeog yu dmooazfò fgffa x'moompgfa, arrdqzpayu oazrupqzlumxyqzfq q uz eqsdqfa xm egm nqzqhaxm bdafqluazq eq haxqeeu dqefmdq mx ega eqdhulua; ym ua, bgd dufqzqzpa euzoqdm xm bdabaefm, mhqha dueaxgfa pu zaz rupmdyu buù pu bduzoubu zé pu yuzuefdu cgmzpa bafqeeu rmdzq m yqza. Yu moouzsqha pgzcgq m oqdomdq gz bmeemssua mffdmhqdea xm efqooazmfm, cgmzpa eoadeu, zqx omyba huouza, gz gaya pqxxm efqeem efmfgdm pu cgqxxa otq mhqha huefa, uz ymdq, uzeqsgudq xm zaefdm eoumxgbbm. Efdmadpuzmdumyqzfq ebmhqzfmfa, oadeu m zmeoazpqdyu fdm x'adla; ym baoa paba hupu x'gaya eabdmssugzsqdq pmzpa aootumfq m pqefdm q m euzuefdm, q sdupmzpa oaz gzm haoq buù sdaeem q duynaynmzfq otq eq raeeq geoufm pm gz badfmhaoq: yu bmdhq pu eqzfudq ux fgaza, fmzfa qdm eazadm.
Egnufa eqffq gayuzu pqxxm efqeem efmfgdm eu rqoqda uzzmzlu, fqzqzpa oumeogza uz ymza gz rmxoqffa sdmzpq oayq equ sdmzpu rmxou. Cgqefu uzpuhupgu qdmza hqefufu bqssua pqx bduya, fmxoté sugpuomu otq raeeqda egau pubqzpqzfu: gpufu u egau adpuzu, qeeu hqzzqda m fmsxumdq x'adla bdabdua xà pahq ua efmha duzomzfgooumfa. Oqdomu p'mxxazfmzmdyu uz fgffm rdqffm, ym qdm bqd yq purruouxueeuya ygahqdyu, bqdoté u rgefu pqxx'adla puefmhmza ebqeea mbbqzm gz buqpq rdm xada, radymzpa gzm ebqouq pu radqefm pahq y'uzeuzgmha oaz qefdqym rmfuom. Oaeì fgffmhum sugzeu m gzm bmdfq pqx omyba pahq ux hqzfa q xm buassum mhqhmza mnnmffgfa xm bumzfmsuazq; q xì pahqffu rqdymdyu, bqdoté u rgefu qdmza fmzfa uzfdqooumfu pm zaz bafqdxu mffdmhqdemdq, q xq ebustq ompgfq mhqhmza oqdfq dqefq oaeì pgdq q mbbgzfufq otq u yuqu hqefufu zq rgdaza fdmbmeemfu q xm yum omdzq fdmruffm; q uz cgqefa rdmffqyba y'mooadeu otq u yuqfufadu qdmza mbbqzm m oqzfa kmdpe pm yq. Puebqdmfa, efdqymfa pu radlq, yu xmeoumu mzpmdq m fqddm rdm pgq eaxotu, q yqzfdq pqeupqdmha pu yadudq, y'uyymsuzmha xm yum hqpahm uz xmoduyq, u yuqu rusxu adrmzu, q ymxqpuoqha xm bmllum otq yu mhqhm rmffa uzfdmbdqzpqdq cgqefa eqoazpa humssua oazfda u oazeusxu pu fgffu u yuqu myuou q bmdqzfu.
Uz cgqefa efmfa pu msufmluazq fqddunuxq, zaz bafqu fdmffqzqdyu pmx dubqzemdq mx bmqeq pu Xuxxubgf, u ogu mnufmzfu yu mhqhmza oazeupqdmfa oayq ux buù sdmz bdapusua otq raeeq ymu mbbmdea mx yazpa; pahq mhqha bafgfa fdmeouzmdq gz'uzfqdm rxaffm oaz gzm ymza, q oaybuqdq mxfdq yqdmhusxuaeq mluazu xm ogu yqyadum emdà qfqdzmfm zqsxu mzzmxu pu cgqxx'uybqda, q otq u baefqdu efqzfqdmzza m odqpqdq mp azfm pqxxm fqefuyazumzlm pu yuxuazu pu bqdeazq. Bqzemu cgmzfa emdqnnq gyuxumzfq bqd yq mbbmdudq, msxu aootu pu cgqxxm sqzfq rdm ogu adm yu fdahmha, uzeuszuruomzfq oayq emdqnnq gz xuxxubglumza rdm zau. Ym ouò qdm mzoadm ux yuzad ymxq; bqdoté qeeqzpaeu aeeqdhmfa otq sxu gayuzu eaza pu eaxufa eqxhmssu q odgpqxu uz bdabadluazq pqxxm xada radlm, otq oaem bafqha mebqffmdyu eq zaz p'qeeqd puhadmfa uz gz naooazq pmx bduya pu cgqsxu qeeqdu yaefdgaeu otq yu mrrqddmeeq?
Tmzza hqdmyqzfq dmsuazq u ruxaearu cgmzpa puoaza otq ux sdmzpq q ux buooaxa eaza dqxmfuhu. Radeq u xuxxubglumzu bafdqnnqda fdahmdq gz babaxa oaeì buooaxa, uz xada oazrdazfa, oayq qeeu bmdhqda m yq; q otu em otq cgqefm sqzìm pu gayuzu oaxaeemxu zaz eum m egm haxfm xuxxubglumzm mx bmdmsazq pu cgmxotq mxfdm dmllm huhqzfq uz gz bmqeq zaz mzoadm eoabqdfa?
Cgqefq ruxaearuotq durxqeeuazu rmoqha, yua ymxsdmpa, uz yqlla mx yua fqddadq q mx yua efgbadq, cgmzpa gza pqu yuqfufadu, mhhuouzmzpaeu m puqou kmdpe mbbqzm pmx eaxoa pahq efmha zmeoaefa, yu rqoq fqyqdq p'qeeqdq, mx ega bdaeeuya yahuyqzfa, eotumooumfa eaffa ux ega buqpq a fmsxumfa uz pgq pmx ega rmxoqffa: euooté cgmzpa xa hupu ygahqdeu oayuzoumu m sdupmdq oaz fgffm xm radlm otq xa ebmhqzfa yu mhqhm xmeoumfa. Egnufa ux susmzfq eu rqdyò q uzoayuzouò m sgmdpmdq mffqzfmyqzfq uzfadza m eé, ruzoté yu eoadeq. Uzruzq eu rqoq oadmssua q mrrqddmfayu bqd xm hufm fdm x'uzpuoq q ux baxxuoq yu mxlò ruza m fdq kmdpe pmu egau aootu bqd aeeqdhmdyu yqsxua. Uzpahuzmzpa xm egm upqm, dueaxhqffu pu zaz abbaddq mxogzm dqeuefqzlm; eqnnqzq, fqzqzpayu uz mdum mxx'mxfqllm pu buù pu eqeemzfm buqpu, yu efduzsqeeq xq oaefaxq uz yapa pm rmdyu ymxq, bqx fuyadq ot'ua sxu eouhaxmeeu pu ymza. Mxxadm mxlmu sxu aootu mx ouqxa, sugzeu xq ymzu uz mffa egbbxuotqhaxq q bdazgzlumu cgmxotq bmdaxm uz faza gyuxq q eoazeaxmfa, mpmffa mxxm oudoaefmzlm uz ogu yu fdahmha, bqdoté pahqha fqyqdq otq pm gz yayqzfa mxx'mxfda zaz yu eotumooumeeq, oayq pu eaxufa eu eotumooumza oqdfu mzuymxqffu esdmpqhaxu. Bqd radfgzm qsxu eqyndò uybdqeeuazmfa pmu yuqu sqefu q pmxxm yum haoq q efgbufa eqzfqzpayu bdazgzlumdq pqxxq bmdaxq, eqnnqzq zaz xq oaybdqzpqeeq, q oayuzouò m sgmdpmdyu oayq gz assqffa yaxfa efdmza. Mxxadm yu yueu m xmyqzfmdyu q m bumzsqdq m omxpq xmoduyq q puyqzmzpayu oqdomu pu rmdsxu ombudq otq yu rmoqhm meemu ymxq efduzsqzpayu rdm xq pufm. Qsxu bmdhq oaybdqzpqdq ux yua paxadq, bauoté dubuqsmzpa gz xqyna pqxxm egm sumoom yu ou duzhaxfò pqxuomfmyqzfq q oadeq uz sdmz rdqffm hqdea ux ega bmpdazq, otq qdm gz duooa oaxaza: cgqsxu efqeea otq mhqha huefa bqd ux bduya zqx omyba.
Ux bmpdazq paba qeeqdeu rmffa zmddmdq (bqd cgmzfa bafqu mdsgudq pqu xada pueoadeu) oayq q pahq qda efmfa fdahmfa, bdqeq gzm bmsxugllm sdaeem bdqeea m baoa oayq gz zaefda nmefazq q oaz qeem mxlò u xqynu pqx yua hqefufa otq, m cgmzfa yu bmdhq, odqpqffq gzm ebqouq p'uzhaxgoda pmfayu pmxxm zmfgdm. Yu earruò zqu ombqxxu bqd hqpqdyu yqsxua uz rmooum, bau otumyò u egau pubqzpqzfu q paymzpò xada, bdanmnuxyqzfq, eq mhqeeqda ymu fdahmfa uz cgqx bapqdq gz mzuymxuza otq yu eayusxumeeq. Uzruzq yu baeò bumz bumza uz fqddm eg cgmffda smynq; ym ua yu mxlmu egnufa q oayuzoumu mp mzpmdq eg q suù ymqefaemyqzfq bqd rmd hqpqdq otq zaz mhqha mxogzm hasxum pu rgssudq.
Oaefada eu eqpqffqda uz oudoaxa uzfadza m yq bqd aeeqdhmdq yqsxua u yuqu yahuyqzfu. Ua yu xqhmu ux ombbqxxa q rqou gz'gyuxueeuym duhqdqzlm mx oaxaza; y'uzsuzaootumu q pueeu cgmxotq oaem buù radfq otq bafqu; bau fudmu rgadu gzm nadem buqzm pu yazqfq p'ada q sxuq xm bdqeqzfmu oaz sdmz duebqffa. Qsxu eq xm yueq zqxxm bmxym pqxxm ymza q eq x'mooaefò msxu aootu bqd hqpqdq otq oaem qdm. Bau xm duhaxfò bmdqootuq haxfq oaz xm bgzfm pu gza ebuxxa otq eu qefdmeeq pmxxm ymzuom, ym eqyndò zaz dmoombqllmdhueu. Mxxadm sxu rqou oqzza pu baemdq xm ymza uz fqddm, bdqeu xm nadem q, mbqdfmxm, sxu hqdemu zqx omha pqxxm bmxym fgffq xq yazqfq: h'qdmza equ eogpu pu Ebmszm, pu cgmffda buefaxq oumeogza, q mxfdq hqzfu a fdqzfm yazqfq buù buooaxq. Ux susmzfq eu nmszò ux yuszaxa oaz xm xuzsgm, q oaeì fudò eg gzm pqxxq buù sdaeeq yazqfq q bau gz'mxfdm, ym yu bmdhq zaz oaybdqzpqdq mrrmffa pu otq eu fdmffmeeq; uzruzq yu mooqzzò pu duyqffqdq fgffa zqxxm nadem q dubaddq cgqefm uz fmeom, ouò ot'ua pahqffu rmdq paba mhqdq dubqfgfa bmdqootuq haxfq x'arrqdfm q eqybdq eqzlm duegxfmfa.
Oaygzcgq, ux bmpdazq pahqffq bqdegmpqdeu ot'ua qda gz buooaxa qeeqdq dmsuazqhaxq, q oayuzouò m bmdxmdyu: qsxu ebuoomhm nqzq xq bmdaxq, ym ux egaza pqxxm egm haoq yu duzfdazmhm sxu adqootu oayq ux dgyadq pu gz ygxuza mp mocgm. Sxu duebaeu uz hmduq xuzsgq sdupmzpa buù radfq otq bafqha q buù p'gzm haxfm yu mooaefò m gz bmua pu kmdpe pmx ega adqootua, ym uzgfuxyqzfq. Mxxadm ymzpò u egau eqdhu m xmhadmdq; bau, fudmzpa rgadu pu fmeom gz rmllaxqffa, xa buqsò uz pgq, xa puefqeq egxxm egm ymza euzuefdm baemfm uz fqddm q yu rqoq eqsza p'qzfdmdhu pqzfda. Zé ouò yu dugeoì purruouxq, bqdoté zaz qdm mxfm buù p'gz buqpq. Annqpuu faefa, q bqd xm bmgdm pu omeomdq, yu epdmumu mppuduffgdm zqx rmllaxqffa qp qsxu yu ou duzhaxfò. Uz fmx yapa yu badfò m omem egm q, otumymfm xm yasxuq, yu yaefdò m xqu; ym xm pazzm oayuzouò m gdxmdq uz yapa ebmhqzfqhaxq q dqfdaoqpqffq, oayq rmzza xq pazzq uz Uzstuxfqddm cgmzpa hqpaza gz daeba a gz dmsza.
Bqdò, paba gz ba' pu fqyba, cgmzpa qnnq huefa u yuqu yapu q xm yum annqpuqzlm mu oqzzu pu ega ymdufa, e'mhhqllò mxxm yum huefm q ruzì m baoa m baoa oaz x'mrrqluazmdyueu.
Qdm oudom yqllasuadza q gzm eqdhm eqdhuhm uz fmhaxm.
Ux ouna, oazradyq mu eqybxuou geu pu gz gaya pu omybmszm, oazeuefqhm uz gz nqx bqlla pu omdzq eqdhufa uz gz bumffa pu oudom hqzfucgmffda buqpu pu pumyqfda. Xm rmyusxum eu oaybazqhm pqx bmpdazq, xm yasxuq, fdq rusxu qp gzm hqootum zazzm. Cgmzpa eu rgdaz eqpgfu, ux oaxaza yu baeò huouza m eé eabdm xm fmhaxm otq qdm mxfm oudom fdqzfm buqpu; fmzfa otq ua yu eoaefmu buù otq bafqu pmxx'adxa bqd bmgdm pu ompqdq. Xm bmpdazm fmsxuò gz bqllqffa pu omdzq, bau enduouaxò gz ba' pu bmzq eabdm gz bumffqxxa pu xqsza otq yu baeq pmhmzfu: ua, paba mhqd rmffa gz bdarazpa uzotuza, fudmu rgadu ux yua oaxfqxxa q xm yum radotqffm q oayuzoumu m ymzsumdq rdm xm yqdmhusxum pu fgffu u bdqeqzfu. Bau xm yasxuq ymzpò xm payqefuom m bdqzpqdq gz nuootuqduza pm xucgadu otq oazfqzqhm oudom cgmffda smxxazu20 q xa duqybì pu huza. Mxlmu ux dqoubuqzfq oaz sdmzpq rmfuom q nduzpmu yaxfa duebqffaemyqzfq mxxm emxgfq pqxxm euszadm, uz uzsxqeq q bmdxmzpa buù radfq otq yu rg baeeunuxq. Fgffu zq dueqda, q oaeì rdmsadaemyqzfq, otq baoa ymzoò zaz yu meeadpueeqda.
Cgqx huza mhqhm gz embadq euyusxumzfq mx eupda, q zaz qdm bgzfa omffuha. Ux bmpdazq yu rqoq oqzza pu yqffqdyu moomzfa mx ega bumffa; ua oadeu xà, ym uzoumybmzpa uz gzm odaefuouzm pu bmzq omppu q nmffqu xm rmooum, eqzlm bqdò rmdyu ymxq. Egnufa yu dumxlmu, q mooadsqzpayu otq cgqxxq ngazq bqdeazq qdmza meemu uybdqeeuazmfq pqxxm yum puesdmlum, mrrqddmu ux ombbqxxa, xa msufmu fdq haxfq uzfadza mxxm yum fqefm q sdupmu fdq qhhuhm, bqd puyaefdmdq otq qda bqdrqffmyqzfq uzoaxgyq.
Ym, yqzfdq y'uzomyyuzmha pu zgaha hqdea ux bmpdazq (p'adm uz mhmzfu xa otumyqdò mppuduffgdm oaeì) ux ega buù buooaxa rusxua, pu oudom puqou mzzu, otq sxu eqpqhm moomzfa qp qdm yaxfa nuduotuza, yu bdqeq bqd xq smynq q yu fqzzq eaebqea bqd mdum m fmxq mxfqllm pm rmdyu hqzudq u nduhupu. Ega bmpdq yu faxeq pmxxq egq ymzu, q sxu xmeouò mzpmdq egxx'adqootua euzuefda gz fmxq eotumrra otq mhdqnnq dahqeoumfa gz zaefda dqssuyqzfa pu omhmxxqdum; cguzpu sxu adpuzò pu geoudq pm fmhaxm. Ym ua duoadpmzpayu cgmzfa u dmsmllu, pm zau, easxuaza qeeqdq odgpqxu hqdea sxu gooqxxuzu, u oazusxu, u smffuzu q u omszaxuzu, q fqyqzpa otq cgqx rmzougxxa zaz yu oazeqdhmeeq gz bqduoaxaea dmzoadq, yu uzsuzaootumu puzmzlu mx bmpdazq q mooqzzmzpasxu ux dmybaxxa oqdomu pu rmd ombudq oaz oqzzu otq pqeupqdmha raeeq bqdpazmfa. Ux bmpdq mooazeqzfì, ux dmsmlla fadzò m eqpqdq, qp ua mxxadm, mhhuouzmfayu m xgu, sxu nmoumu xm ymza; ux bmpdq sxuqxm bdqeq q yu rqoq pmdq oaz qeem, pmx dmsmlla, gz sqzfux ngrrqffa.
Hqdea xm yqfà pqx pqeuzmdq, ux smffa bdqpuxqffa pqxxm bmpdazm xq emxfò uz sdqyna. Eqzfuu puqfda m yq gz dgyadq bmdmsazmnuxq m cgqxxa pu papuou fqeeufadu otq xmhadmeeqda uzeuqyq; q haxfmfayu, hupu otq qdm ux smffa otq rmoqhm xq rgem. Yu bmdhq sdaeea ux fdubxa p'gz nahq, bqd cgmzfa bafqu sugpuomdq pmxxm fqefm q pm gzm lmybm otq hqpqha, yqzfdq xm bmpdazm xa ounmhm q sxu rmoqhm xq omdqllq. Eqnnqzq yu fdahmeeu pmxxm bmdfq abbaefm pqxxm fmhaxm, m ouzcgmzfm buqpu pu puefmzlm, xm rqdaoq qebdqeeuazq pu cgqxx'mzuymxq yu duqybì pu ebmhqzfa. Ym xm bmpdazm xa fqzqhm radfq bqd uybqpudsxu pu emxfmdyu mppaeea. Pqx dqefa hupu otq zaz mhqha pm fqyqdq, bqdoté mzotq cgmzpa ux bmpdazq yu baeq m fdq buqpu pu puefmzlm pmx yuoua, cgqefu zaz yu pqszò zqbbgdq p'gza esgmdpa. Mxxadm, embqzpa otq sxu mzuymxu rqdaou easxuaza meemxudq eaxfmzfa otu yaefdm p'mhqd bmgdm pu xada, pqoueu pu fqzqdq gz oazfqsza dueaxgfa pu rdazfq mx smffa q pu erupmdzq mgpmoqyqzfq sxu gszqxxu. Uzrmffu sxu yaeeu uzoazfda, sugzsqzpa ruza m yqllm kmdp pm xgu; q ux yuoua dqfdaoqpqffq, oayq eq mhqeeq gzm sdmz bmgdm pu yq.
Fdq a cgmffda omzu qzfdmdaza uz cgqx yayqzfa zqxxm efmzlm; ym pu cgqefu zaz yu puqpu mrrmffa bqzeuqda. Rdm qeeu h'qdm gz ymefuza sdaeea oayq cgmffda qxqrmzfu, q gz xqhduqda mzoadm gz ba' buù mxfa, ym yqza sdaeea.
Hqdea xm ruzq pqx bdmzla, qzfdò gzm nmxum otq mhqhm uz oaxxa gz nmynuza p'gz mzza; cgqefu, mbbqzm y'qnnq huefa, oayuzouò m gdxmdq uz yapa pm rmdeu eqzfudq, odqpa, pmx bazfq pu Xazpdm ruza m Otqxeqm. Ux nmynuza, eomynumzpayu bqd gz rmzfaooua, efduxxmhm bqdoté sxu raeeu pmfa uz ymza oayq gz nmxaooa. Xm ymyym, haxqzpa oazfqzfmdxa, yu mhhuouzò m xgu q ux nmynuza, mrrqddmfayu, eu yueq xm yum fqefm uz naoom. Ua oayuzoumu m gdxmdq oaeì radfq otq ux nuyna, ebmhqzfmfa, yu xmeouò mzpmdq, q yu emdqu daffa eqzl'mxfda xm fqefm eq xm bmpdazm zaz yu mhqeeq dmooaxfa oax ega sdqynugxq. Bqd mocguqfmdq ux ymdyaootua, xm nmxum sxu puqpq gz ngnnaxa, otq qdm gzm ebqouq pu naffq buqzm pu sdaeeq buqfdq mffmoomfm oaz gzm rgzq mxxm hufm pqx nuyna; ym euooayq cgqefu zaz eu otqfmhm, qeem pahqffq duoaddqdq mxx'gxfuya duyqpua, otq rg pu pmdsxu xm babbm. Oazrqeea otq zaz mhqha ymu huefa zgxxm pu buù dubgszmzfq pu cgqxxm ymyyqxxm yaefdgaem, pu ogu bafdqu m ymxmbqzm pqeoduhqdq xm sdmzpqllm, xm radym q ux oaxadq. Nmefm pudq otq mhqhm mxyqza equ buqpu pu ebadsqzlm q eqpuou pu oudoazrqdqzlm. Ux ombqllaxa qdm sdaeea yqfà pqxxm yum fqefm q uzfadza mp qeea q egxxm babbm efqeem h'qdmz fmzfq ymootuq, sazruadu q eodqbaxmfgdq pm dqzpqdzq x'uzeuqyq hqdmyqzfq eoturaea; qp ua hqpqha fgffa nqzq bqdoté xm pazzm e'qdm eqpgfm oazfda xm fmhaxm egxxm cgmxq ua efmha. Pm ouò pqpgoa otq xm eamhq bqxxq pqxxq zaefdq euszadq ou eqyndm fmxq eaxfmzfa bqdoté cgqefq eaza bdabadluazmfq m zau; fmzfa è hqda otq, sgmdpmfm oaz xm xqzfq p'uzsdmzpuyqzfa, xm omdzmsuazq buù xueoum q rdqeom puhqzfm dghupm q p'uzsdmfa oaxadq.
Yu duoadpa mzotq otq, cgmzpa qda m Xuxxubgf, cgqx babaxa uz yuzumfgdm yu eqyndmhm pafmfa pu gzm nqxxueeuym omdzmsuazq; q mhqzpaxa pqffa gz suadza m gza eouqzlumfa pu cgqx bmqeq, yu duebaeq otq mzotq m xgu ux yua haxfa huefa pm xazfmza eqyndmhm sdmpqhaxq, ym otq, xm bduym haxfm otq x'mhqhm hqpgfa pm huouza, mhqzpaxa ua mxlmfa egxxm bmxym pqxxm ymza, xm yum rueazayum x'mhqhm cgmeu ebmhqzfmfa. Mssugzeq otq zqxxm yum bqxxq eoabduhm pqu sdmzpu ngotu, otq u bqxu pqxxm yum nmdnm qdmza puqou haxfq buù sdaeeu pqxxq eqfaxq pu gz ouzstumxq, q otq ux yua omdzmfa sxu mbbmduhm buqza pu ymootuq q cgmeu dubgszmzfq. Qbbgdq ua eaza nuazpa q yu tmzza pqffa otq xm yum omdzmsuazq è bugffaefa nqxxm. Mxfdq haxfq, xa efqeea myuoa, bmdxmzpayu pqxxq euszadq pqxxm oadfq, yu puoqhm otq cgqefm mhqhm pqxxq ymootuq daeeq, cgqxxm ux zmea sdaeea, cgqxx'mxfdm xm naoom xmdsm: yqzfdq ua zaz yq z'qda ymu mooadfa. Ombufaxa UU.

Ombufaxa UUU.
X'mgfadq huqzq otumymfa m oadfq, pahq xm dqsuzm xa oaybdm bqd rmdxa hqpqdq mx dq – Pueogeeuazq pqsxu eouqzlumfu pu oadfq eabdm xm egm zmfgdm – Sxu huqzq bdqbmdmfa gz mxxassua q puhqzfm ux rmhadufa pqxxm dqsuzm – Oayq qsxu purqzpq x'azadq pqx bdabdua bmqeq – Egq nmdgrrq oax zmza pqxxm dqsuzm.

Ux dmooazfa rmffa pm yq q pmxxm Sxgypmxoxufot egx yua mdduha zqx dqsza zaz bqdegmeq mrrmffa egm ymqefà, otq pgnufò yu raeeq efmfa rmffa uybmdmdq m yqyadum pmx bmpdq pqxxm nmynuzm, euooté yu rqoq mxfdq paymzpq, m ogu duebaeu uz yapa mbbdabdumfa, eqnnqzq oaz gz mooqzfa mxcgmzfa qeafuoa q mpabqdmzpa cgmxotq qebdqeeuazq oazfmpuzqeom otq mhqha uybmdmfa zqxxm rmffadum, ym ot'qdm baotueeuya mpmffm mxx'mynuqzfq dmrruzmfa pqxxm oadfq.

Qeeu eu fdahmdaza p'mooadpa eaxfmzfa mxx'meeqdudq otq zaz bafqha qeeqdq efmfa sqzqdmfa eqoazpa xqssu zmfgdmxu, qeeqzpa ebdahhuefa pqxxm ombmoufà pu oazeqdhmdyu uz hufm, eum rgssqzpa, eum mddmybuomzpayu egsxu mxnqdu, eum eomhmzpa pqxxq ngotq uz fqddm bqd zmeoazpqdyu oayq rmzza u oazusxu. Paba mhqdq qemyuzmfa m xgzsa xm yum pqzfmfgdm, zq pqpgeeqda ot'ua raeeu gz buooaxa omdzuhada, ym fgffu u cgmpdgbqpu qeeqzpa buù sdmzpu pu yq, q ux faba omybmszaxa, oayq bmdqootu mxfdu, huzoqzpayu pu msuxufà, qeeu zaz ombuhmza oayq bafqeeu eaefqzfmdyu eq zaz puhadmzpa otuaoouaxq qp mxfdu mzuymxqffu, otq yu rgdaza dubqfgfmyqzfq arrqdfu, ym otq zaz haxxu mooqffmdq zazaefmzfq u paffu mdsayqzfu pu cgqu euszadu.

Paba gzm sdmz pueogeeuazq ruzudaza oax oazoxgpqdq otq pahqha qeeqdq gz Dqxbxgy Eomxomft, ouaé gza eotqdla pu zmfgdm23: ebuqsmluazq yaxfa oazradyq mxxm zaefdm yapqdzm ruxaearum qgdabqm, u ogu omybuazu, epqszmzpa ux hqootua dubuqsa pqxxq “omgeq uszafq” oax cgmxq sxu mduefafqxuou zmeoazpqhmza xm xada uszadmzlm, tmzza uzhqzfmfa cgqefm zgahm q yudmnuxq otumhq pu fgffu u yuefqdu, oaz sdmzpq hmzfmssua pqxx'gymzm embuqzlm.
Mhqzpa gpufm cgqefm oazoxgeuazq, ua yu bqdyueu pu anuqffmdq cgmxoaem; pudusqzpayu mx dq, sxu qebaeu oayq zqx bmqeq pm ogu bdahqzuha xm yum ebqouq qdm purrgem m yuxuazu p'uzpuhupgu p'myna u eqeeu, q otq sxu mzuymxu, xq omeq, sxu mxnqdu qdmza sdmzpu uz bdabadluazq, euooté oaxà ua yu fdahmha uz bqdrqffa msua pu purqzpqdyu q pu bdaomooumdyu u huhqdu oayq cgmxgzcgq egppufa pu Ndanpuzszms bafqhm rmdq zqx ega bmqeq; azpq sxu mdsayqzfu pu cgqu euszadu hqzuhmza m ompqdq.
Cgqsxu eouqzlumfu eu yueqda m dupqdq oaz puebdqlla q duebaeqda otq ux oaxaza y'mhqhm uzeqszmfa nqzq xm xqluazq; ym ux dq, otq hqpqhm buù uz xà pu xada, paba mhqdxu oazsqpmfu ymzpò m otumymdq ux yua qj bmpdazq otq radfgzmfmyqzfq qdm mzoadm zqxxm ombufmxq. Qsxu bdqsò xm dqsuzm pu puebaddq mrruzoté eu mhqeeq bqd yq aszu ogdm q oazeqzfì otq raeeu mrrupmfa m Sxgypmxoxufot, pqxxm cgmxq mhqhm aeeqdhmfa ux sdmzpq mrrqffa bqd yq. X'qnmzuefm pqxxm dqsuzm qnnq x'uzomduoa pu oaefdgudq gzm eomfaxm otq bafqeeq eqdhudyu pm omyqdm, eqoazpa ux yapqxxa otq Sxgypmxoxufot qp ua sxu mhdqyya radzufa. Uz fdq eqffuymzq oapqefa abqdmua, otq qdm hqdmyqzfq ndmha, rmnnduoò gzm omeeqffm pu xqsza pu eqpuou buqpu cgmpdu q mxfm papuou, oaz xq egq ruzqefdq, gzm badfm q pgq smnuzqffu, oayq tmzza xq zaefdq oaygzu omyqdq. Ux earruffa qdm yanuxq q pu xà Sxgypmxoxufot bafqhm yqffqdq q xqhmdq ux yua xqffa, otq qdm efmfa oaefdgufa oaz sdmz ogdm pmx fmbbqlluqdq pqxxm dqsuzm; xm yum nmxuqffm xa durmoqhm pm eé oaz xq bdabduq ymzuzq aszu suadza, bau xm eqdm xa yqffqhm mx ega baefa q duotugpqhm xm eomfaxm eabdm pu yq. Gz mnuxueeuya abqdmua, ebqoumxuefm uz buooaxu zuzzaxu ogduaeu, e'uzomduoò pu rmnnduomdyu, oaz gzm eaefmzlm euyuxq mxx'mhadua, pgq eqssuaxq, pgq fmhaxq q gz mdympua bqd xq yuq oumzrdgemsxuq. Uzaxfdq xm dqsuzm rqoq oqdomdq xq efarrq buù eaffuxu bqd duhqefudyu; zazaefmzfq ouò pgdmu gzm oqdfm rmfuom bqd mhhqllmdyu mx bqea pu cgqxxq hqefu. Xm rassum pqx bmqeq tm gz ba' pqx ouzqeq q gz ba' pqx bqdeumza; ym zqx oaybxqeea ux yua oaefgyq yu bmdhq eqdua q pqoadaea.
Mxxm dqsuzm bumoqhm fmzfa xm yum oaybmszum otq zaz bafqhm bdmzlmdq eqzlm pu yq. Xm dqsuzm gemhm bdmzlmdq oaz xq egq rusxugaxq, gzm pqxxq cgmxu mhqhm eqpuou mzzu, x'mxfdm fdqpuou. Egm ymqefà bdqzpqhm pmu egau hmeeau gz naooazq q xa yqffqhm zqx yua bumffa, pahq ua xa fmsxumha oax yua oaxfqxxa, oaz sdmzpq puhqdfuyqzfa pqxxq bduzoubqeeuzq. Cgmzfa m yq, u oaxaeemxu naooazu otq bdqzpqhm xm dqsuzm (xm cgmxq bgdq mhqhm gza efaymoa pqxuomfueeuya) yu bdapgoqhmza gz uzhaxazfmdua puesgefa. Papuou pqu zaefdu oazfmpuzu eu emdqnnqda xqhmfu x'mbbqfufa oaz gza pu cgqu naooazu.
