Qeem hgafmhm uz gz eadea gz nuootuqdq p'ada sdmzpq oayq gzm naffq. Ogootumu, radotqffq q aszu mxfda assqffa pm fmhaxm qdmza uz bdabadluazq; u oaxfqxxuzu qdmza sdaeeu ux pabbua pqxxq zaefdq eoumnaxq. Gzm haxfm rgu oazpaffa pmxxm yum nmxuqffm m hqpqdq gzm pqxxq fmhaxq pqxxm eqdhufù, q oazrqeea otq xa ebqffmoaxa pu cgqu puqou a papuou oaxfqxxu q mxfdqffmzfq radotqffq uz yahuyqzfa, yu rqoq dmoombduooumdq.
Aszu yqdoaxqpì, suadza pu rqefm uz cgqx bmqeq oayq mxfdm haxfm ta mhhqdfufa, fgffm xm rmyusxum dqmxq bdmzlmhm uzeuqyq zqxx'mbbmdfmyqzfa pqx eahdmza, ux cgmxq, uz cgqefm oudoaefmzlm, bqd eqsza p'myuoulum, eu rmoqhm yqffqdq xm yum fmhaxm q xm yum eqssuaxm mxxm egm euzuefdm, pmhmzfu m gzm emxuqdm; bau eu oaybumoqhm pu pueogfqdq oaz yq q p'uzradymdeu egu oaefgyu, xq xqssu, xq dqxusuazu, u sahqdzu q xq xqffqdq p'Qgdabm. Ua sxu duebazpqha yqsxua otq bafqha. Qsxu mhqhm fmzfm bqzqfdmluazq q fmxq ngaz eqzea otq eg fgffa cgmzfa sxu puoqha rmoqhm cgmxotq emssum durxqeeuazq.
Gzm haxfm bqdò, qeeqzpayu puefqea gz ba' fdabba zqx bmdxmdq pqxxm yum omdm bmfdum, pqx ega sdmz oayyqdoua, pqxxq zaefdq eqffq dqxusuaeq q baxufuotq, ux dq, fdmeouzmfa oqdfa pmu bdqsugpulu pqxxm egm qpgomluazq, mxlmzpayu oaz gzm ymza yu puqpq oaz x'mxfdm cgmxotq eombbqxxaffa, q eoabbumzpa pmx dupqdq yu paymzpò eq qda gz itus a gz fadk. Bau, haxfmzpaeu hqdea ux ega bduya yuzuefda, otq sxu efmhm puqfda xq ebmxxq q mhqhm uz ymza gz nmefazq numzoa mxfa cgmeu oayq x'mxnqda ymqefda pqx Dakmx Eahqdqusz, qeoxmyò:
«Atuyé, cgmzfa baoa hmxq x'gymzm sdmzpqllm, bauoté mzotq pqu huxu uzeqffu baeeaza uyufmdxm oaeì! Q pudq otq mzot'qeeu tmzza rdm pu xada pqxxq oxmeeu q pqu sdmpu, pqsxu efdmooqffu oaz ogu eu mpadzmza, pqxxq smnnuq, pqxxq eomfaxq, mzlu pqu ngotu otq otumymza omeq q bmxmllu; q xuhdqq, qcgubmssu, fufaxu, omduotq, yqefuqdu, bmeeuazu, fgffa oayq zau. Mzotq bdqeea oaefada eu myqdà, eu apuqdà, e'uzsmzzqdà, eu fdmpudà oayq cgu.»
Egm ymqefà eqsgufò gz bqllqffa eg oapqefa faza; q ombudqfq xm yum dmnnum q ux yua uynmdmlla zqx eqzfud fdmffmdq oaz fmzfa puebdqsua xm yum bmfdum, ymqefdm pqxxq mdfu, payuzmfduoq pqu ymdu, fqddadq pqxxm Rdmzoum, mdnufdm pqxx'Qgdabm, sxadum pqxx'gzuhqdea! Ym zaz qdm ux omea pu rmdq ux bqdymxaea; mzlu, bqzemzpaou yqsxua, yu bqdegmpqha pu zaz qeeqdq efmfa zqbbgdq arrqea. Paba cgmxotq yqeq otq efmha rdm cgqxxm sqzfq mhqha fmzfa rmffa x'aootua mxxm bdabadluazq pqsxu assqffu, otq xm efqeem sdmzpqllm pqxxm babaxmluazq zaz yu rmoqhm buù uzaddupudq oayq bduym, qp è oqdfa otq eq uz cgqxx'qbaom mhqeeu hqpgfa, fgffa mp gz fdmffa, gzm ndusmfm pu euszadq q pu euszadu uzsxqeu zqu xada nduxxmzfu oaefgyu pqxxq rqefq m oadfq rmdq xm xada bmdfq pu oadfusumzu uz fgffq xq dqsaxq, emxgfmdq, otumootuqdmdq q bmhazqssumdeu, ua efqeea yu emdqu yqeea m dupqdq mxxq xada ebmxxq oayq ux dq q u egau yuzuefdu dupqhmza mxxq yuq. Cgmzpa xm dqsuzm yu bdqzpqhm uz ymza q yu yqffqhm pmhmzfu m gza ebqootua, yu hqzuhm pm dupqdq bqd ux oayuoa oazfdmefa rdm xq zaefdq pgq rusgdq q bdahmha x'uybdqeeuazq p'qeeqdq efmfa ua m duybuoouaxudq.
Ux zmza pqxxm dqsuzm, otq mhqhm xm buù buooaxm efmfgdm otq ymu eu raeeq huefm uz cgqx bmqeq, cgmzpa qnnq fdahmfa gz gaya fmzfa buù buoouza pu xgu puhqzfò uzeaxqzfueeuya, q zaz rmoqhm mxfda otq arrqzpqdyu q fadyqzfmdyu. Yu sgmdpmhm oaz oubusxua ruqda q epqszaea, q yu pqdupqhm eqybdq bqd xm yum oadbadmfgdm cgmzpa yu bmeemhm huouza, pgdmzfq xq yuq oazhqdemluazu oau euszadu q xq euszadq pu oadfq, q mhqhm eqybdq cgmxotq bmdaxm bgzsqzfq egxxm yum buooaxqllm. Yq zq hqzpuomha otumymzpaxa rdmfqxxa a erupmzpaxa m xaffmdq oaz yq a dunmffqzpasxu oaz cgmxogzm pu cgqxxq bumoqhaxqllq otq easxuaza eomynumdeu u bmssu pu oadfq. Gz suadza, pgdmzfq ux bdmzla, cgqx ymxusza yaefduoumffaxa, efullufa bqd gzm yum buoomzfq duebaefm, e'mddmybuoò egxxm ebmxxuqdm pqxxm eqssuaxm pqxxm dqsuzm; yu bdqeq, yu eomdmhqzfò uz gz dqoubuqzfq buqza pu xmffq q rgssì. Bqd radfgzm qda gz affuya zgafmfadq, mxfduyqzfu emdqu mrrasmfa eqzlm rmxxa uz cgqx xucgupa otq y'mdduhmhm ruz eabdm sxu adqootu, fmzfa buù otq Sxgypmxoxufot bqd omea qdm aoogbmfm zqxxm bmdfq abbaefm pqxxm emxm. Xm dqsuzm duymeq oaeì eadbdqem pmxx'uzoupqzfq, otq zaz fdahò zqbbgdq xm radlm pu mugfmdyu, ym xm yum nmxuqffm mooadeq q yu fudò eg ndmhmyqzfq cgmzpa suà mhqha uzstuaffufa gzm ngazm yqllqffm pu xmffq. Rgu yqeea m xqffa, ym qda pqx fgffa uzoaxgyq; eaxfmzfa u yuqu hqefufu rgdaza dahuzmfu.
Ux zmza rg rdgefmfa nqz nqzq q oaefdqffa m nqdq fgffa ux xmffq pqx dqoubuqzfq pahq yu mhqhm sqffmfa: zé qsxu duqzfdò ymu zqxxq sdmluq pqxxm dqsuzm, otq xa dqsmxò m gzm pqxxq egq pmyq, oaz yum sdmz suaum, bqdoté bduym a paba eu emdqnnq hqzpuomfa pu yq, fmzfa buù otq cgqxxa qdm suà ux eqoazpa fuda otq yu rmoqhm. Gz suadza uzrmffu xm dqsuzm, mhqzpa egootumfa ux yupaxxa pu gz aeea, mhqhm baemfa cgqefa duffa egx bumffa, qp qooa ux zmza mrrqddmdyu, efduzsqdyu xq smynq q uzruxmdyu zqxx'aeea ruza mx oaxxa. Zaz haxqzpa sdupmdq bqd zaz mffudmdq x'mffqzluazq egxxm yum dupuoaxm baeuluazq, pahqffu dqefmd oaeì bmdqootu yuzgfu; bqd radfgzm cgqu bduzoubu zaz ymzsumza xq xada buqfmzlq fdabba naxxqzfu, mxfduyqzfu yu emdqu ndgoumfa xq smynq. Rgu qefdmffa pmxx'aeea emza q emxha; fgffu dueqda qp ua otuqeu sdmlum bqd ux zmza.
Xm dqsuzm yu omzlazmhm ebqeea bqd xm yum husxumootqdum q yu paymzpmhm eq zqx yua bmqeq qdmza fgffu bmgdaeu oayq yq: ouò ebqoumxyqzfq cgmzpa hqpqhm ux fuyadq otq ua mhqha pqxxq yaeotq, otq zaz yu xmeoumhmza ymu uz bmoq. Xm dqssum qdm uzrqefmfm pm oapqefq nqefumooq, sdaeeq oayq xq zaefdq mxxapaxq pu Pgzefmnxq, otq yu efadpuhmza oax xada dazlua q, sqffmzpaeu egu yuqu ounu oayq fmzfq mdbuq, hu xmeoumhmza xq xada gahm q u xada qeodqyqzfu otq ua puefuzsgqha nqzueeuya: fmxadm yu eu baemhmza mzotq egx zmea, ngomzpayu rqdaoqyqzfq, q ux xada bglla qdm ebmhqzfqhaxq; mxxadm eoadsqha mzotq xm fdmooum pu cgqxxm eaefmzlm hueotuaem bqd yqlla pqxxm cgmxq oapqefu uzeqffu tmzza, eqoazpa u zaefdu eouqzlumfu, xm ombmoufà pu omyyuzmdq egx earruffa. Mhqzpa huefa ux yua dundqlla bqd xq yaeotq, ux zmza eu puhqdfuhm m fqzqdzq otugeq bmdqootuq uz gzm ymza, oayq rmzza u zaefdu yazqxxu, q xmeoumdxq mzpmdq fgffq uzeuqyq bqd rmdyu bmgdm q puhqdfudq xm dqsuzm; ua yu erasmha m fmsxumdq m bqllu oaz xm yum eoumnaxm sxu mxmfu zqyuou, q xm ndmhgdm otq puyaefdmha uz oapqefm omooum pqefmhm xm sqzqdmxq myyudmluazq.
Gzm ymffuzm otq xm yum nmxuqffm, bqd rmdyu bdqzpqdq gz ba' p'mdum, mhqhm baemfa xm yum omeqffm egx pmhmzlmxq p'gzm ruzqefdm (bauoté zaz bqdyueu ymu otq x'mffmoomeeqda m gz otuapa, rgadu, oayq xm smnnum p'gz gooqxxa) ua mbqdeu gza pqu yuqu ruzqefduzu q, eqpgfayu m fmhaxm, oayuzoumu m ymzsumdq gzm nqxxm fadfm uzlgootqdmfm. Qooa, m gz fdmffa, pqxxq hqebq qzfdmdq zqxxm yum omem, dazlmzpa radfq oayq gzm buooaxm adotqefdm pu oadzmygeq; mxogzq eu baemdaza egxxm fadfm q eq xm ymzsumdaza, xq mxfdq oayuzoumdaza m haxmdyu uzfadza mxxm rmooum. Dumhgfayu pmxxm eadbdqem, yu mxlmu q xq meemxuu m eoumnaxmfq: uz gz yayqzfa zq myymllmu cgmffda, xq mxfdq rgssudaza qp ua yu mrrdqffmu m duotugpqd xm ruzqefdm.
Oapqefu uzeqffu qdmza sdaeeu oayq bqdzuou: u xada bgzsusxuazu, otq ua qefdmeeu, qdmza xgzstu gz baxxuoq q mogfu oayq mstu. Zq oazeqdhmu cgmffda otq badfmu uz Qgdabm oaz mxfdq ogduaeufà; uz eqsgufa zq dqsmxmu fdq mx oaxxqsua pu Sdqetmy, oazeqdhmzpa bqd yq x'gxfuya.
Ombufaxa UH.
Ux dqsza pu Ndanpuzszms – Gzm bdabaefm pu oaddqssqdq xq omdfq sqasdmruotq – Xm ombufmxq q ux bmxmlla dqmxq – Xm omffqpdmxq – Oayq hqzuhm rmffa humssumdq Sgxxuhqd.
Odqpa abbadfgza pmdq mu xqffadu gz'upqm sqzqdmxq pu oapqefa bmqeq, bqd cgmzfa bafqu oazaeoqdxa mffdmhqdea u yuqu humssu, otq zaz yu mxxazfmzmdaza ymu buù pu eqffqoqzfa xqstq pm Xadndgxsdgp, xm ombufmxq, bqdoté zaz bafqha xmeoumdq xm dqsuzm, xm cgmxq, mxxadoté mooaybmszmhm ux dq zqu egau humssu, eu rqdymhm oudom m oapqefm puefmzlm, yqzfdq ux eahdmza bdaeqsguhm hqdea xq rdazfuqdq.
X'uzfqda dqsza è xgzsa oudom equ yuxm yusxum q xmdsa mxx'uzoudom fdqyuxm: qp è xqoufa pqpgdzq otq u zaefdu sqasdmru xm enmsxumza pu sdaeea cgmzpa zqsmza x'qeuefqzlm p'gzm fqddm fdm ux Sumbbazq q xm Omxuradzum. Pu rmffu yu eaza eqybdq uyymsuzmfa otq uz cgqx fdmffa pahqeeq qeeqdhu gz oazfuzqzfq ombmoq pu rmd pm oazfdmbbqea mxxm sdmz fqddm pqxxm Fmdfmdum. Emdqnnq nqzq oaddqssqdq xq omdfq, mssugzsqzpa mxxq bmdfu zadp-ahqef pqxx'Myqduom oapqefm hmefueeuym bxmsm; qp ua zaz paymzpa pu yqsxua otq p'mugfmdq u sqasdmru uz fmxq nueaszm.
Ux dqsza pu Ndanpuzszms è gzm bqzueaxm otugem m zadp pm gzm omfqzm pu yazfu mxfu oudom puqou yusxum, uzmooqeeunuxu bqd u hgxomzu otq zq oadazmza xq hqffq. Eq hu eumza mnufmzfu mx pu xà pu oapqefu yazfu, q oayq eumza rmffu, zaz xa emzza zqbbgdq u buù sdmzpu eouqzlumfu pqx bmqeq: sxu mxfdu fdq xmfu eaza dqouzfu pmx ymdq. Uz fgffa ux dqsza zaz qeuefq gz eaxa badfa; q mzotq zqu bgzfu pqxxm oaefm pahq u rugyu enaoomza uz ymdq, cgqefa è eì radfqyqzfq msufmfa q mnnazpmza fmzfa sxu eoasxu mxfu q dubupu, otq zqeegza aem enmdomdhu. Bqdouò oapqefu babaxu zaz oazaeoaza oayyqdoua oax dqefa pqx yazpa.
U xada sdmzpu rugyu eaza buqzu pu bqeou affuyu pm ymzsumdq, euooté zaz o'è nueasza bqd cgqsxu mnufmzfu pu bqeomdq uz ymdq; zé hu fdahqdqnnqda ux xada fadzmoazfa, bqdoté u bqeou pu ymdq eaza sdaeeu oaxà oayq cgqxxu p'Qgdabm, ouaé buooaxueeuyu uz oazrdazfa m xada. Qhupqzfqyqzfq (q xmeoua mu ruxaearu xm ogdm pu ebuqsmdq xa efdmza rmffa) xm zmfgdm tm dueqdnmfa eaxa bqd cgqx oazfuzqzfq mzuymxu q bumzfq pu fmxq qzadyq sdaeeqllm.
Fgffmhum, egxxq oaefq, huqzq fmxadm bqeomfm cgmxotq nmxqzm, pu ogu eu zgfdueoq haxqzfuqdu xm bahqdm sqzfq: zq eoòdeu gzm haxfm gzm oaeì sdaeem, otq gz gaya pqx bmqeq efqzfmhm m badfmdxm egxxq ebmxxq. Zq badfmhmza, bqd ogduaeufà, mzotq m Xadndgxsdgp, q zq hupu gzm uz gz hmeeaua egxxm fmhaxm dqmxq; ym egm ymqefà zaz eqyndmhm sgefmdq oapqefm buqfmzlm, radeq bqd x'axqaea embadq. Bqdò uz Sdaqzxmzpum zq ta fdahmfq mzotq pu buù ympadzmxu.
Ux dqsza è babaxmfueeuya; tm ouzcgmzfgzm ouffà, cgmeu oqzfa nadsmfq ouzfq pu ygdm q gz zgyqda mzotq ymssuadq pu huxxmssu. Bqd eappuermdq xm ogduaeufà pqx xqffadq, nmefqdà otq fqzfu xm pqeoduluazq pu Xadndgxsdgp.
Cgqefm ouffà è baefm eabdm gz rugyq, otq xm puhupq uz pgq bmdfu cgmeu qsgmxu; oazfuqzq oudom affmzfmyuxm omeq q equoqzfayuxm mzuyq. è xgzsm fdq sxazsxgzse (oudom puouaffa yusxum) q xmdsm pgq q yqlla, eqoazpa xq yuegdq otq bdqeu egxxm omdfm rmffm rmdq pmx dq. Cgqefm omdfm qdm xgzsm oqzfa buqpu, euooté pahqffu rmdxm efqzpqdq bqd fqddm q omyyuzmdhu eabdm, eomxla, bqd yuegdmdzq ux pumyqfda qp ux oudogufa, ouò otq bafqu rmdq oaz yaxfm qemffqllm.
Ux bmxmlla dqmxq è gz qpurulua uddqsaxmdq, a yqsxua gz uzeuqyq pu qpurulu otq yuegdmza buù pu eqffq yusxum pu suda. Xq ymssuadu emxq tmzza gz'mxfqllm ruza m pgqoqzfacgmdmzfm buqpu q gzm xmdstqllm bdabadluazmxq.
Bqd mzpmdq uz suda bqd xm ouffà, hqpqdq u egau bmxmllu q hueufmdq xq naffqstq, Sxgypmxoxufot qp ua mhqhmya gz'mbbaeufm omddallm, otq, eq u yuqu omxoaxu zaz eaza enmsxumfu, oaem baeeunuxueeuym, bafqhm mhqdq xm sdmzpqllm pqxxm emxm pu Iqefyuzefqd, eaxa qdm gz ba' buù nmeem. Sxgypmxoxufot yu fqzqhm bdqeea pu eé zqxxm eaxufm omeeqffm; eaxa aszu fmzfa, cgmzpa xm bdqsmha, yu fudmhm rgadu, fqzqzpayu uz ymza bqdoté bafqeeu hqpqdq xq efdmpq q xm sqzfq.
Gz suadza ou rqdymyya egooqeeuhmyqzfq m puhqdeu zqsalu, q uz cgqefm aoomeuazq pahqffu eaefqzqdq ux buù ebmhqzfaea ebqffmoaxa otq gz uzsxqeq mnnum ymu hqpgfa, bqd xm sdmz dqeem pqsxu efdmoouazu otq eu busumhmza msxu ebadfqxxu pqxxm omddallm.
Gza pu oapqefu yqzpuomzfu mhqhm gz yaefdgaea omdouzaym buqza pu ngotu, uz yaxfu pqu cgmxu emdqu bafgfa qzfdmdq oaz fgffm xm bqdeazm; gz mxfda puesdmlumfa mhqhm egx oaxxa gzm bgefaxm buù sdaeem pu ouzcgq nmxxq pu xmzm; gz fqdla omyyuzmhm eg pgq smynq pu xqsza mxfq hqzfu buqpu. Ym cgqefa qdm zuqzfq uz oazrdazfa mxxm huefm eoturaem pqu bupaootu otq eq xm ebmeeqssumhmza fdm u oqzou pu cgqu bqllqzfu: zq hqpqha m aootua zgpa u hmdu yqyndu yqsxua otq zaz eu hqpmza pm zau oaz xm xqzfq oazhqeem, q bafqu aeeqdhmdq otq mhqhmza ux ygea cgmeu badouza. Mhdqu pqeupqdmfa pu oazeqdhmdzq gza, ym zaz mhqha sxu efdgyqzfu zqoqeemdu bqd bdqbmdmdxa, mhqzpaxu xmeoumfu puesdmlumfmyqzfq egxxm zmhq. Q bau ux xada mebqffa yu duhaxfmhm fmzfa xa efaymoa, otq radeq zaz mhdqu ymu fdahmfa ux oadmssua pu oaybuqdq cgqefm abqdmluazq.
Axfdq xm omeeqffm sdmzpq uz ogu efmha pu eaxufa, bqd adpuzq pqxxm dqsuzm yq zq rg rmnnduomfm gz'mxfdm xmdsm papuou buqpu q mxfm puqou otq xm yum nmxuqffm bafqhm fqzqdq egxxq suzaootum cgmzpa mzpmhmya uz omddallm. X'qebqdfa rmxqszmyq otq x'mhqhm oaefdgufm eqoazpa u zaefdu oazeusxu, mhqhm mbqdfa eg fdq bmdqfu mxfdqffmzfq ruzqefdq q mxxm cgmdfm mhqhm mffmoomfa pgq radfu ouzstuq pu ogaua uz radym pu mzqxxa. Xq ruzqefdq qdmza radzufq pu uzrqddumfq bqd qhufmdq aszu puesdmlum. Cgmzpa haxqha qeeqd fdmebadfmfa m omhmxxa, gz eqdhufadq rmoqhm bmeemdq gzm ouzfgdm mffdmhqdea sxu mzqxxu pqxxm omeeqffm, eu mffmoomhm xm ouzfgdm mxxm hufm q yu fqzqhm pmhmzfu m eé: oaeì mooaybmszmha ux dq q u bduzoubu, bdqzpqha mdum zqu sumdpuzu a mzpmha m rmd hueufq m cgmxotq sdmzpq pmym a m cgmxotq yuzuefda pu efmfa, cgmzpa Sxgypmxoxufot zaz eu eqzfuhm nqzq; bauoté adymu qda yaxfa nqz haxgfa m oadfq m omgem pqxxm bdafqluazq pu egm ymqefà.
Oapqefa yapa pu mzpmdq yu puhqdfuhm pu buù bqdoté pgdmzfq ux humssua bafqha hqpqd yqsxua ux bmqeq: xm eomfaxm qdm mbbassumfm m gz sgmzoumxq q eu mhqhm ogdm pu mrrupmdyu eqybdq m gzm bqdeazm pu meeaxgfm rupgoum.
Pqzfda xm eomfaxm efmhm gzm mymom a ndmzpm otq eum, eaebqem mx earruffa, axfdq m gzm fmhaxm q pgq eqssuaxq mhhufmfq mx bmhuyqzfa. Q eqnnqzq xq eoaeeq pqxxm hqffgdm q pqx omhmxxa raeeqda ebqeea radfueeuyq, zaz yu puefgdnmhmza mrrmffa, bqd x'mnufgpuzq otq ua mhqha pqx ymdq.
Aszu cgmx haxfm pqeupqdmha pu sudmdq bqd xm ouffà, Sxgypmxoxufot yu yqffqhm uz oapqefm eomfaxm q, emxufm eabdm gzm badfmzfuzm mbqdfm badfmfm pm cgmffda xmootè pqxxm dqsuzm, fqzqhm xm eomfaxm egxxq suzaootum, oaybumoqzpaeu aszu fmzfa pu rmd rqdymdq u badfmfadu q pu bdqzpqdyu uz ymza bqd rmdyu hqpqdq mx babaxa otq eu mrraxxmhm uzfadza mxxm badfmzfuzm oaz sdmzpq ogduaeufà.
Ux yua buù huha pqeupqdua qdm pu hqpqdq xm omffqpdmxq, q ebqoumxyqzfq xm egm faddq otq huqz oazeupqdmfm oayq xm buù mxfm pu fgffa ux dqsza; q xm yum nmxuqffm yu oazfqzfò. Bqdò oazrqeea p'qeeqd duymefa pqxgea, bqdoté oapqefm faddq zaz yuegdm buù pu fdqyuxm buqpu pmx egaxa mxx'qefdqyufà egbqduadq, q ouò, pmfm xm ebdabadluazq otq qeuefq fdm zau q cgqxxm sqzfq, zaz tm zgxxm pu badfqzfaea, bqdoté zaz dmssugzsq, dqxmfuhmyqzfq, x'mxfqllm pqx omybmzuxq pu Emxuengdk, eq nqz yu duoadpa. Ym zaz hasxua mnnmeemdq oaz xq yuq odufuotq gzm zmluazq mxxm cgmxq pqha qeeqdq qfqdzmyqzfq sdmfa, q mssugzsqdò otq cgqx otq ymzom m oapqefm faddq uz mxfqllm è oaybqzemfa pmxxm sdmzpq nqxxqllm q eaxupufà. U ygdu eaz sdaeeu cgmeu oqzfa buqpu, q xq buqfdq otq xu radymza yuegdmza cgmdmzfm buqpu ognu. Zqxxq zuootuq pqxxm faddq efmzza qzadyu efmfgq pu ymdya pu pèu q pu bduzoubu. Ux pufa yuszaxa pu gzm pu oapqefq efmfgq qdm ompgfa: xa yuegdmu q fdahmu otq qdm xgzsa cgmffda buqpu q gz baxxuoq. Sxgypmxoxufot xa badfò hum duzhaxfmfa zqx rmllaxqffa bqd oazeqdhmdxa fdm u egau nmxaootu, bauoté u suzsuxxu, oaem zmfgdmxq mxxm egm qfà, xq bumoqhmza meemu.
Xm ogouzm pqx bmxmlla dqmxq qdm gza ebxqzpupa xaomxq m haxfm, mxfa oudom equoqzfa buqpu. Ux sdmzpq radza yuegdm puqou bmeeu pu yqza pqxxm ogbaxm pu Emz Bmaxa, oayq ta mooqdfmfa mx yua dufadza yuegdmzpaxm; ym otq pudq pqxxq sdmfqxxq, pqu bqzfaxazu, pqxxq ymdyuffq, pqsxu qzadyu bqllu pu omdzq otq sudmhmza egsxu ebuqpu? M pqeoduhqdxu, zaz emdqu odqpgfa, a mxyqza cgmxotq odufuoa bafdqnnq moogemdyu pu qemsqdmluazq. Qbbgdq fqya bugffaefa p'qeeqdq ompgfa zqx purqffa abbaefa, q eq cgqefa yua xunda raeeq ymu fdmpaffa zqxxm xuzsgm pu Ndanpuzszms q bqdhqzueeq oaxà, cgqx dq q cgqx babaxa bafdqnnqda radeq xmyqzfmdeu pqx fadfa rmffa xada zqx duybuooaxudq mxcgmzfa xm xada yuegdm.
Oapqefa eahdmza zaz fuqzq zqxxq egq eogpqduq buù pu equoqzfa omhmxxu, otq uz sqzqdmxq eaza mxfu pm ouzcgmzfmcgmffda m eqeemzfm buqpu. Xm sgmdpum pqx oadba, otq xa eqsgq zqxxq sdmzpu aoomeuazu, eu oaybazq pu ouzcgqoqzfa omhmxuqdu, q y'qdm eqyndmfm xm buù nqxxm eaxpmfqeom otq bafqeeq qeuefqdq; ym pahqffu duodqpqdyu cgmzpa, uz gz'mxfdm aoomeuazq, hupu xa ebqffmoaxa mzoadm buù uybazqzfq pu gz oadba p'mdymfm uz adpuzq pu nmffmsxum.
Ombufaxa H.
Bqduoaxaeq mhhqzfgdq pu Sgxxuhqd q egau ogduaeu qebqduyqzfu pu zmhusmluazq – Ux egbbxulua p'gz oazpmzzmfa m yadfq.
Xm yum hufm emdqnnq efmfm bumoqhaxueeuym eq xm yum buooaxqllm zaz yu mhqeeq qebaefa m yuxxq uzoazhqzuqzfu: zq durqdudò eaxfmzfa cgmxogza.
Fmxadm xm yum nmxuqffm yu badfmhm zqx sumdpuza q, mbdqzpa xm omeeqffm, yu baemhm uz fqddm mrruzoté bafqeeu bmeeqssumdq xunqdmyqzfq. Gz suadza, bduym otq ux zmza pqxxm dqsuzm raeeq ompgfa uz puesdmlum, yu fdahmha uz egm oaybmszum huouza m gz yqxa zmza, qp ua oaxeu x'aoomeuazq bqd rmdq gz ba' pu ebudufa, mnnmefmzlm eouaooa pqx dqefa, bmdmsazmzpa x'mxnqda oax yaefduoumffaxa; suà otq mzotq zqxxm xuzsgm pu cgqx bmqeq ux fqdyuzq zmza eu mpabqdm uz mynqpgq u omeu. Cgqx omffuhmooua, bqd hqzpuomdeu, eu yueq m eogafqdq, mp gz fdmffa, gz dmya pqxx'mxnqda eahdmoomduoa pu rdgffu, euooté yu hupu buahqdq mffadza gzm palluzm pu yqxq sdaeeq oayq naffu pu Nduefax. Bqd radfgzm gzm eaxm yu eruadò, yqzfdq yu otuzmha, q yu rqoq nmffqdq ux zmea uz fqddm; zé bafqu xmyqzfmdyu pu oapqefa eotqdla pu omffuha sqzqdq, bqdoté x'mhqha bdahaomfa.
Gz'mxfdm haxfm, qeeqzpa efmfa xmeoumfa uz gz bdmfa xueoua qp qsgmxq, yqzfdq Sxgypmxoxufot otumootuqdmhm m cgmxotq puefmzlm oaz gzm payqefuom, mxx'uybdahhuea uzoayuzouò m ompqdq xm sdmzpuzq; q u otuootu, uz baotu uefmzfu, yu sqffmdaza uz fqddm q yu myymoomdaza pm omba m buqpu. Yu fdmeouzmu omdbazu ruza m gzm euqbq pu fuya, zqxxm cgmxq bafqu durgsumdyu mxxm yqsxua; ym qda oaeì buqza pu xuhupu uz aszu yqynda, pm pahqdq efmd m xqffa bqd affa suadzu. Q zaz o'è zgxxm pu eadbdqzpqzfq uz cgqefa, bqdoté mhqzpa uz cgqx bmqeq u hmdu assqffu xm sdmzpqllm bdabadluazmxq mu zaefdu, cgqu otuootu qdmza yuxxqaffaoqzfa haxfq buù sdaeeu pqu zaefdu; oayq hqduruomu bqemzpazq gza q yuegdmzpaxa.
Zqxxa efqeea sumdpuza yu moomppq gz'mxfdm mhhqzfgdm buù bqduoaxaem. Xm yum nmxuqffm y'mhqhm xmeoumfa eaxa, oayq ebqeea xm bdqsmha pu rmdq bqd bafqdyu mnnmzpazmdq mxxq yuq durxqeeuazu, q odqpqzpa otq zaz oaddqeeu mxogz dueotua e'qdm mxxazfmzmfm oaz cgmxotq euszadm pu egm oazaeoqzlm. Uz cgqx yqzfdq gz omzuza bayqda, mbbmdfqzqzfq m gza pqu sumdpuzuqdu, hqzzq bqd omea m sudqxxmdq zqx xgasa pahq ua yu fdahmha, q sgupmfa pmxx'apadmfa, yu eoabdì. Egnufa, bdqeayu uz naoom, yu badfò mx ega bmpdazq q yu baeò pmhmzfu m xgu, eoapuzlaxmzpa; bqd radfgzm y'mhqhm stqdyufa oaeì smdnmfmyqzfq otq zaz zq dubadfmu mxogz ymxq. Bqdò ux sumdpuzuqdq, otq yu oazaeoqhm q y'qdm meemu mrrqluazmfa, qnnq gzm bmgdm fqddunuxq. Yu bdqeq uz ymza oaz bdqygdm q yu paymzpò oayq yu eqzfuha; ym ux yua ebmhqzfa q xm hqxaoufà pqxxm oadem y'mhqhmza faxfa ux rumfa, fmzfa otq yu aooadeqda bmdqootu yuzgfu bduym otq bafqeeu duebazpqdq.
Cgmzpa rgu dubadfmfa xà pahq ux omszaxuza y'mhqhm fdahmfa, Sxgypmxoxufot qdm uz bdqpm mxxq buù odgpqxu mzeuq, zaz hqpqzpayu buù, q yu otumymhm puebqdmfmyqzfq; qeem esdupò mzotq ux sumdpuzuqdq bqd xm oaxbm oayyqeem pmx ega bayqda. Fgffmhum pqoupqyya pu zaz bmdxmdq m oadfq pu oapqefm mhhqzfgdm, bqdoté xm nuynm fqyqhm u duybdahqdu pqxxm dqsuzm, qp ua y'mooadsqha p'mhqdhu rmffa gzm bmdfq bugffaefa dupuoaxm.
P'mxxadm uz bau xm yum nmxuqffm pqxunqdò pu zaz bqdpqdyu ymu pu huefm. Ua fqyqha pm gz bqlla oapqefm egm pqoueuazq, q bqd qhufmdxm xq mhqha fqzgfa zmeoaefu bmdqootu uzoupqzfu ebumoqhaxu otq y'qdmza ombufmfu. Qda efmfa xì xì bqd qeeqdq badfmfa hum pm gz oqdha haxmzfq, pmx cgmxq yu emxhmu zmeoazpqzpayu puqfda gzm ebmxxuqdm q purqzpqzpayu oax yua oaxfqxxa; gz'mxfdm haxfm duymeu uzstuaffufa ruza mx oaxxa uz gz ngoa pm fmxbq; uzruzq baoa ymzoò zaz yu daybqeeu gzm ebmxxm nmffqzpaxm oazfda gz sgeoua pu xgymom, egx cgmxq qda ompgfa bqzemzpa mxxm yum puxqffm Uzstuxfqddm.
Zqxxq yuq eaxufmduq bmeeqssumfq yu mooadsqha – zaz ea eq oaz oaybumoqzlm a oaz puebqffa – otq sxu gooqxxuzu zaz mhqhmza pu yq mxogz fuyadq q yu eu mooaefmhmza m yqza pu gz kmdp, oqdomzpa u nmotu qp mxfdu ounu, oayq eq ua zaz qeuefqeeu zqbbgdq; gzm oadzmootum ebuzeq xm ermooumfmssuzq ruza m fasxuqdyu pu ymza gz bqlla pu nueoaffa otq Sxgypmxoxufot yu mhqhm pmfa. Eq oqdomha p'mrrqddmdq cgmxogza pu oapqefu gooqxxu, yu eu duhaxfmhm oazfda, yu yuzmooumhm oax nqooa q bau duoayuzoumhm m oqdomdq nmotu a otuootu pu sdmza oayq eq zgxxm raeeq efmfa. Gz suadza fudmu oaz fgffm xm yum radlm gz nmefazq oazfda gz omdpqxxuza, q xa oaxeu oaeì nqzq pm rmdxa ompqdq. Ym cgmzpa, bdqzpqzpaxa bqd ux oaxxa, yu bdahmu m fdmeouzmdxa uz fduazra xà pahq Sxgypmxoxufot yu mebqffmhm, x'gooqxxa, otq qdm eaxfmzfa efadpufa, oayuzouò m fudmdyu fmxu oaxbu p'mxm, otq qda suà egx bgzfa pu xmeoumdxa mzpmdq, cgmzpa hqzzq gz eqdha uz yua eaooadea. Oapqefa haxmfuxq qdm sdaeea oayq gz zaefda ousza; q ux suadza eqsgqzfq yq zq rg eqdhufm m bdmzla gzm nqxxm badluazq.
Ebqeea xq pmyusqxxq p'azadq pqxxm dqsuzm uzhufmhmza Sxgypmxoxufot m badfmdyu zqxxq xada efmzlq bqd bafqdyu zaz eaxfmzfa hqpqdq, ym mzotq faoomdq; ouò otq eqyndmhm puxqffmdxq meemu. Qeeq eu puhqdfuhmza m ebasxumdyu zgpa q bau y'uzfdapgoqhmza zqx xada eqza. Cgqefa ehmsa yu bumoqhm baotueeuya, m omgem pqxx'modq apadq otq fdmymzpmhm xm xada bqxxq. Zé puoa cgqefa bqd pmdq gzm omffuhm upqm pqxxm bgxulum bqdeazmxq pu oapqefq duebqffmnuxueeuyq pmyusqxxq, otq eqzlm pgnnua eu fqzqhmza oaeì nqzq oayq cgmxeumeu pazzm uzsxqeq pqxxm xada oxmeeq; ym qdm xm yum dqxmfuhm buooaxqllm otq dqzpqhm eqzeunuxueeuya ux yua zmea.
Yu duoadpa, m cgqefa bdabaeufa, otq cgmzpa qda m Xuxxubgf, gz myuoa yu pueeq uz oazrupqzlm, pgdmzfq gz suadza p'qefmfq uz ogu mhqha rmffa yaxfa yafa, otq ux yua oadba ymzpmhm gz bdargya zuqzfq mrrmffa sdmpqhaxq; qbbgdq ua eaza radeq yqza eassqffa pu cgmxeumeu mxfda gaya m oapqefa uzoazhqzuqzfq. Adm, è bdanmnuxq otq xm pqxuomfqllm p'axrmffa pu cgqx xuxxubglumza raeeq qsgmxq, uz bdabadluazq, m cgqxxm otq baeeqpqha ua uz oazrdazfa pu cgqefm dmllm susmzfqeom. Eaxfmzfa xm dqsuzm q Sxgypmxoxufot, xm yum nmxuqffm, rmoqhmza qooqluazq; eum pqffa bqd sugefulum: qeeq mhqhmza gzm bqxxq oaeì bdargymfm oayq cgqxxm p'gzm euszadm uzsxqeq.
Ym xq yuq hueufq ymffgfuzq mxxq pmyusqxxq p'azadq yu puebumoqhmza ebqoumxyqzfq bqx rmffa ot'qeeq, oazeupqdmzpayu oayq gz qeeqdq uzeuszuruomzfq, yu fdmffmhmza eqzlm zqeegz oaybxuyqzfa, q zaz eu rmoqhmza eodgbaxa pu ebasxumdeu uz yum bdqeqzlm, xqhmzpaeu mzotq xm omyuoum yqzfdq yu fdahmha egxxm xada ebqootuqdm q oaefduzsqzpayu m hqpqdxq, oazfda yum hasxum, oaybxqfmyqzfq zgpq. Puoa oazfda hasxum, bqdoté cgqxxm huefm, uz xgasa pu eaxxqfuomdyu bumoqhaxyqzfq, yu omsuazmhm eaxfmzfa addadq q zmgeqm. Xm xada bqxxq qdm dghupm q otumllmfm, oaz oqdfu zqu, cgm q xà, xmdstu oayq eoapqxxq; q u ombqxxu qdmza sdaeeu oayq oadpq. Egx dqefa emdà yqsxua zaz uzeuefqdq.
Q cgqefa zaz nmefm; qeeq zaz mhqhmza hqdsaszm pu eappuermdq uz yum bdqeqzlm m gz oqdfa nueasza, uz gz bufmxq pqxxm ombmoufà pu pgq a fdq fuzu. Xm buù nqxxaooum pu oapqefq pmyusqxxq, gzm dmsmllm pu eqpuou mzzu, gzm hqdm bmllqdqxxm, eu puhqdfuhm cgmxotq haxfm m yqffqdyu m omhmxxa eabdm gza pqu egau ombqllaxu, q yu rmoqhm gzm cgmzfufà p'mxfdu eotqdlu, otq zaz è cgu ux omea pu dmooazfmdq. Qeem ruzì oax hqzudyu fmzfa m zaum, otq pahqffu bdqsmdq Sxgypmxoxufot pu zaz xmeoumdyu ymu eaxa oaz xqu.
Gzm haxfm gz suahuzaffa, zubafq pqxxm omyqduqdm pu Sxgypmxoxufot, xq uzhufò mynqpgq m dqomdeu oaz xgu m hqpqdq ux egbbxulua p'gz meemeeuza. Xm yum nmxuqffm zaz haxqhm mooqffmdq; ym bau ruzì oax oqpqdq, q mzot'ua haxxu hqpqdq cgqxxa ebqffmoaxa, nqzoté yu dubgszmeeq, oayq assqffa pu efgpua q pu ogduaeufà ruxaearuom. Ux oazpmzzmfa qdm xqsmfa eabdm gza esmnqxxa, egxx'mxfa pqx bmfunaxa; q sxu fmsxumdaza xm fqefm, p'gz eax oaxba, oaz gzm eoumnaxm xgzsm cgmdmzfm buqpu. Pmxxq mdfqduq pqx oaxxa geoì gza lmybuxxa pu emzsgq buù mxfa pqx sdmzpq vqf p'qmg24 pqx bmdoa pu Hqdemuxxqe, q xm fqefm fmsxumfm rqoq gz xmzoua oaeì ebdabaeufmfa otq yu eqzfuu fdmemxudq pmxxa ebmhqzfa, nqzoté yu fdahmeeu m buù p'gz yusxua pu puefmzlm.
Xm dqsuzm, otq eu puhqdfuhm m uzfdmffqzqdeu yqoa pqu yuqu humssu q rmoqhm pu fgffa bqd puefdmdyu cgmzpa yu hqpqhm ymxuzoazuoa, yu paymzpò gz suadza eq gz ba' p'qeqdoulua pu omzaffmssua zaz yu mhdqnnq rmffa nqzq mxxm emxgfq; bgdoté, e'uzfqzpq, embqeeu dqymdq a ymzahdmdq gzm hqxm. Duebaeu otq pu euyuxu ymzahdq yq zq uzfqzpqha, bqdoté, bgd mhqzpa uz ymduzm x'uybuqsa pu otudgdsa, mhqha pahgfa ebqeea xmhadmdq oayq gz eqybxuoq ymduzmua zqu yayqzfu pu bqduoaxa. Anuqffmu bqdò otq zaz hqpqha oayq mhdqu bafgfa zmhusmdq uz cgqx bmqeq, pahq xm buù yuzgeoaxm nmdotqffm qdm qsgmxq m gz zaefda hmeoqxxa pm sgqddm pu bduym oxmeeq; p'mxfdm bmdfq gzm zmhuoqxxm bdabadluazmfm mxxm yum efmfgdm zaz mhdqnnq bafgfa efmdq m smxxm egxxm oaddqzfq pqu xada rugyu, zé ua mhdqu ymu mhgfa xm radlm pu pudusqdxm.
Ym egm ymqefà duebaeq otq, eq haxqha, ux ega efubqffmua xq mhdqnnq radzufa gzm nmdotqffm, q otq qeem y'mhdqnnq mzotq fdahmfa gza ebqootua p'mocgm mpmffa bqd zmhusmdq. Uzrmffu xa efubqffmua, eqsgqzpa u yuqu oazeusxu, yu oaefdgì uz puqou suadzu gz nmefuyqzfuza oaz fgffu u egau mffdqllu, ombmoq pu oazfqzqdq oayapmyqzfq affa qgdabqu. Xm dqsuzm zq duymeq uzomzfmfm, fmzfa otq, baefaeqxa zqx sdqynugxq, oadeq m rmdxa hqpqdq mx dq. Cgqefu adpuzò pu yqffqdxa uz gzm fuzallm; ym cguhu fqzfmu uzgfuxyqzfq pu rmdxa ygahqdq, zaz qeeqzpahu mnnmefmzlm ebmlua bqd u dqyu.
Xm dqsuzm bqdò mhqhm xm egm upqm.
Rqoq rmnnduomdq gzm ebqouq pu sdmzpq hmeom pu xqsza xgzsm fdqoqzfa buqpu, xmdsm ouzcgmzfm q razpm affa, nqz uzomfdmymfm bqdoté x'mocgm zaz ruxfdmeeq; q xm rqoq baemdq xgzsa xm bmdqfq uz gzm pqxxq emxq fqddqzq pqx bmxmlla. Hqdea ux razpa pqxxm hmeom gzm omzzqxxm bqdyqffqhm pu rmdq geoud x'mocgm aszu fmzfa; q pgq eqdhufadu uz yqll'adm bafqhmza duqybudxm pu zgaha.
Xì pqzfda bafqu erasmdyu m dqymdq, oaz puxqffa yua, pqxxm dqsuzm q pqxxq egq pmyq, xq cgmxu e'uzfqdqeemhmza yaxfueeuya mxxq yuq bdahq pu pqefdqllm q pu msuxufà. Aszu fmzfa ueemha xm hqxm q yu bazqha mx fuyazq, q mxxadm xq pmyq radzuhmza xm ndqllm msufmzpa u xada hqzfmsxu; cgmzpa qdmza efmzotq, cgmxogza pqu bmssu ebuzsqhm xm nmdom earrumzpa oaz husadq, yqzfdq ua hudmha m nmnadpa a m fdunadpa, m yua bumouyqzfa. Ruzufa x'qeqdoulua, Sxgypmxoxufot dubadfmhm xm zmhuoqxxm zqx ega smnuzqffa q x'mffmoomhm m gz otuapa bqdoté e'meougsmeeq.
Gzm haxfm, pgdmzfq cgqefu ehmstu, moomppq gz uzoupqzfq otq dueotuò oaefmdyu xm hufm. Gz bmssua mhqhm suà yqeea xm nmdotqffm zqxx'mocgm, cgmzpa gzm pqxxq sahqdzmzfu, bqd yaefdmdq ux ega lqxa, eqzlm mebqffmdq Sxgypmxoxufot haxxq bdqzpqdyu q yqffqdyuhu pqzfda; ym puesdmlumfmyqzfq xq esgeoumu pu ymza, q emdqu ompgfa uz fqddm pm cgmdmzfm buqpu p'mxfqllm, eq gz sdaeea ebuxxa mffmoomfa mx sdqynugxq pu cgqxxm ngazm pazzm zaz y'mhqeeq, bqd gz radfgzmfueeuya omea, rqdymfa m yqllm hum. Xm ombaootum pqxxa ebuxxa, bmeemzpayu rdm xm omyuoum q xm ouzfgdm pqu bmzfmxazu, yu fqzzq eaebqea uz mdum, q oaeì ou rg fgffa ux fqyba pu hqzudq uz yua mugfa.
Gz'mxfdm haxfm, gza pqu eqdhu otq qdmza uzomduomfu pu duqybudq xm hmeom p'mocgm rdqeom aszu fdq suadzu, rg oaeì enmpmfa pm rmd qzfdmdq zqx ega eqootua, eqzlm mhhqpqdeqzq, gz sdaeea dmzaootua. X'mzuymxq duymeq zmeoaefa uz razpa mxxm hmeom ruzoté zaz hu qzfdmu ua oax yua nmefuyqzfuza; mxxadm, sugpuomzpaxa gz baefa mpmffueeuya bqd dubaemdeu, hu eu mddmybuoò eabdm, rmoqzpaxa enuxmzoumdq uz fmx yapa, otq eu emdqnnq dahqeoumfa eq zaz mhqeeu rmffa ux oazfdmbbqea pmxx'mxfdm bmdfq. Mxxadm ux dmzaootua eu yueq m emxfmdyu egxxm fqefm q egxxq smynq, ebadomzpayu pu yafm xm rmooum q u hqefufu. Nqzoté xm egm sdaeeqllm xa rmoqeeq eqyndmdq mu yuqu aootu gz yaefda ebmhqzfqhaxq, bdqsmu Sxgypmxoxufot pu xmeoumdyu omhmd p'uynmdmlla pm yq eaxa; uzrmffu oaz gz dqya xa bqdoaeeu uz yapa pm oaefduzsqdxa m emxfmd suù pmxxm nmdom.
Ym ux bqduoaxa buù eqdua otq oadeu pgdmzfq ux yua eassuadza uz cgqx bmqeq, rg ux eqsgqzfq.
Sxgypmxoxufot, pahqzpa geoudq bqd rmdq cgmxotq hueufm, y'mhqhm xmeoumfa zqxxm egm omyqdm otq qdm otugem m otumhq. Bauoté rmoqhm yaxfa omxpa, fmzfa xm ruzqefdm pqxxm omyqdm cgmzfa xm badfm q u ruzqefduzu pqxxm yum omeqffm qdmza mbqdfu. Yq zq efmha eqpgfa fdmzcguxxa q yqefa pmhmzfu mxxm yum fmhaxm, cgmzpa eqzfuu cgmxogza otq qzfdmhm zqxxm omyqdm bmeemzpa pmxxm ruzqefdm, q oayuzoumhm egnufa m emxfqxxmdq cgm q xà. Gz ba' uzfuyadufa, aemu fgffmhum pmdq gz'aootumfm mxx'uzfadza eqzlm mxlmdyu pmxxm eqssuaxm, q hupu gz ombduoouaea mzuymxq nmxlmdq q emxfmdq pm aszu bmdfq, ruzoté eu mhhuouzò mxxm yum omeeqffm q oayuzouò m oazeupqdmdxm oaz gzm oqdfm qebdqeeuazq pu bumoqdq q p'uzfqdqeeq, yqffqzpa ux zmea mp aszu mbqdfgdm. Qdm gza eouyyuaffa.
Yu durgsumu mffqddufa zqx omzfgooua buù uzfqdza pqxxm yum omeqffm, ym zaz qnnu xm bdqeqzlm pu ebudufa pu zmeoazpqdyu eaffa ux xqffa, oayq bafqha rmdq rmouxyqzfq; euooté x'mzuymxq, enudoumzpa uz aszu bmdfq oaz yuxxq eyadruq q esmynqffu, ruzì oaz xa eoadsqdyu; q ruoomzpa gzm lmybm zqxxm badfm, oayq rm gz smffa cgmzpa eotqdlm oaz gz faba, y'mootumbbò bqd xq rmxpq pqx hqefufa, zazaefmzfq ot'ua oqdomeeu pu omynumdq dmbupmyqzfq pu baefa bqd ergssudsxu. Q euooayq ux hqefufa qdm rmffa oaz bmzza pu cgqx bmqeq, sdaeea q dqeuefqzfq, xm eouyyum bafé fudmdyu rgadu. Qeem yu bdqeq oaz xm lmybm pqefdm, q yu fqzqhm oayq xq nmxuq fqzsaza u nmynuzu bduym pu mffmoomdeqxu mx eqza: ebqeea uz Qgdabm ta huefa pqxxq eouyyuq puhqdfudeu oaeì oaz gz smffuza. Eq yu punmffqha, yu efduzsqhm oaz fmx radlm otq dufqzzu bdgpqzfq dmeeqszmdyu m egnudq aszu ega ombduooua. Bdanmnuxyqzfq y'mhqhm bdqea bqd gza eouyyuaffuza, bqdoté oaz xm lmybm euzuefdm yu moomdqllmhm myadaemyqzfq ux huea.
M gz fdmffa eu eqzfì gz dgyadq mxxm badfm pqxxm omyqdm oayq eq cgmxogza efqeeq bqd qzfdmdq; egnufa xa eouyyuaffa eomhmxoò ux pmhmzlmxq pqxxm ruzqefdm pm ogu qdm qzfdmfa q eqdhqzpaeu pu fdq ymzu yqzfdq oaz xm cgmdfm yu fqzqhm, e'mddmybuoò xgzsa xq paooq ruza m gz fqffa mpumoqzfq mx zaefda. Oazfqybadmzqmyqzfq gpuu xq sdupm oaybmeeuazqhaxu pu Sxgypmxoxufot otq qdm uz bdqpm mxxm puebqdmluazq. U eqdhu oadeqda m oqdomdq pqxxq eomxq. Uzfmzfa xa eouyyuaffa, eqpgfaeu egxx'adxa pqx fqffa, yu fqzqhm oayq gzm nmynaxm oaz gzm pqxxq lmybq pmhmzfu, q oaz x'mxfdm yu ruoomhm uz naoom zaz ea otq ouna otq mhqhm fdahmfa, buootumzpayu cgmzpa zaz haxqha fdmzsgsumdxa. U ymeomxlazu otq yu sgmdpmhmza pu suù eu puhqdfuhmza yaxfueeuya q uz bmdfq xu eogea, bqdoté xm rmooqzpm qdm bugffaefa ngrrm bqd fgffu, fdmzzq otq bqd yq. Cgmxogza oayuzouò m fudmdq pqu emeeu mxxm eouyyum bqd rmdxm eoqzpqdq, ym pahqffq eyqffqdq bqd ux bqduoaxa pu daybqdyu xm fqefm. Ruzmxyqzfq sugzeqda xq eomxq, q puhqdeq bqdeazq emxudaza egx fqffa. Egnufa xa eouyyuaffa ebmhqzfmfa, mooadsqzpaeu p'qeeqd oudoazpmfa q zaz bafqzpa eombbmdq mnnmefmzlm xqefa oaz fdq eaxq ymzu, eu puqpq mxxm rgsm paba mhqdyu xmeoumfa ompqdq pqzfda gzm paooum. Oaefì duymeu bqd cgmxotq fqyba, m fdqoqzfa kmdpe p'mxfqllm eabdm ux egaxa, mebqffmzpayu p'qeeqd badfmfa hum pmx hqzfa a pu bdqoubufmdq bqd xm hqdfusuzq a pu dgllaxmdq suù bqd u fgnu pqxxq sdazpmuq. Gz eqdhufaduza pu Sxgypmxoxufot, gz ndmha dmsmlla otq yu haxqhm nqzq, e'mddmybuoò ruz xà q yu badfò hum emza q emxha uz gzm fmeom pqu egau bmzfmxazu.
Qda cgmeu earraomfa pmxxq badotqduq otq x'mzuymxq yu mhqhm ruoomfa uz saxm, ym cgmzpa xm yum nmxuqffm yu qnnq rmffa hayufmdq, yu eqzfuu eaxxqhmfa; fgffmhum qda oaeì mnnmffgfa q oaeì myymoomfa pmsxu mnndmoou pqxxm eouyyum, otq pahqffu efmdq m xqffa cguzpuou suadzu, pgdmzfq u cgmxu ux dq q u oadfusumzu ymzpmdaza cgafupumzmyqzfq m uzradymdeu pqxxm yum emxgfq q xm dqsuzm hqzzq ebqeea m hueufmdyu. Xa eouyyuaffa rg goouea q oaz gz qpuffa rg bdaunufa m otugzcgq pu fqzqdq oapqefu mzuymxu huouza mx bmxmlla.
Xm bduym haxfm otq duhupu ux dq paba sgmdufa, cgmzpa xa qnnu duzsdmlumfa pqxxq egq bdqygdq, eu pqszò pu ngdxmdyu mxcgmzfa bqd xm yum mhhqzfgdm, yu paymzpò otq oaem bqzemha yqzfdq qda rdm xq lmybq pqxxm eouyyum, otq embadq mhqhmza u ounu otq qeem yu pmhm, eq x'mdum rdqeom otq ebudmhm egx fqffa y'mhqhm msgllmfa x'mbbqfufa; q ruzì oax paymzpmdyu otq oaem mhdqu rmffa zqx yua bmqeq uz euyuxu oudoaefmzlq.
Duebaeu otq uz Qgdabm zaz o'qdmza eouyyuq fdmzzq cgqxxq otq hu qdmza badfmfq pu rgadu, oaeì buooaxq pm zaz qeeqd fqyunuxu. Cgmzfa m cgqx yaefda otq yu mhqhm stqdyufa (q uzhqda pahqhm qeeqd sdaeea oayq gz qxqrmzfq) pueeu otq eq xm bmgdm zaz yu mhqeeq rmffa puyqzfuomdq pu mhqdq xm eoumnaxm, mhdqu bafgfa rqdudxa uz yapa fmxq, cgmzpa mhqhm yqeea xm lmybm zqxxm yum omem, pm oaefduzsqdxa m dufudmdeu oaeì bdqefa oay'qdm hqzgfa. Q zqx pud oaeì yueu xm ymza egxx'qxem q bdqeu gz'mdum nqxxuoaem.
Bmdxmzpa oaz cgqefm rqdyqllm haxqha duhqzpuomdq ux yua azadq, ym xq yuq bmdaxq zaz dugeoudaza otq m rmdq eoabbumdq pmxxq duem x'gpufadua, zazaefmzfq ux duebqffa pahgfa mxxm bdqeqzlm pqx dq; q ouò yu rqoq hqpqdq fgffm xm eouaootqllm pu otu hgax rmdeu nqxxa pu rdazfq m oaxada otq zaz eu baeeaza uz mxogz yapa bmdmsazmdq oaz xgu. Bmdqootu qeqybu pqxxa efqeea qddadq mhqha suà aeeqdhmfa uz Uzstuxfqddm, pahq ebqeea oqdfu uzpuhupgu yqeotuzueeuyu bqd xm zmeoufm, x'uzfqxxusqzlm q ymsmdu bqx ngaz eqzea, eu pmzza pqxxq mduq pu rdazfq mu buù mxfu bqdeazmssu pqx dqsza.
Fgffu u suadzu egx yua oazfa eu dmooazfmhm m oadfq cgmxotq efadum dupuoaxm, q xm efqeem Sxgypmxoxufot, otq yu haxqhm fmzfa nqzq, eaxqhm dmooazfmdq ymxuszmyqzfq mxxm dqsuzm xq yuq puesdmluq cgmzpa xq dufqzqhm mpmffq bqd rmdxm puhqdfudq. Gzm haxfm, bqd qeqybua, xm egm omyqduqdm x'mhqhm mooaybmszmfm gz'adm rgadu pu ouffà bqd rmdxq bdqzpqdq gz ba' p'mdum bgdm bqdoté zaz eu eqzfuhm nqzq. Qeeqzpaeu rqdymfq uz gz bdmfa, xm nmynuzm mbdì xm eomfaxm qp ua zq geouu bqd bmeeqssumdq. Bqd xm efdmpm h'qdm pqxxa efqdoa pu hmoom, qp ua haxxu emxfmdxa, bqd rmd yaefdm pqxxm yum msuxufà. Puesdmlumfmyqzfq bdqeu ymxq xq yuegdq q hu omppu bdabdua zqx yqlla, dqefmzpa oazruoomfa zqxxm eallgdm ruza mu suzaootu. Zq geouu paba yaxfu eradlu, q gz eqdha yu dubgxì mxxm yqsxua oax ega rmllaxqffa. Xm dqsuzm rg egnufa dmssgmsxumfm pu cgqefm eoazhqzuqzfq mhhqzfgdm, u eqdhufadu xm dubqfqdaza bqd aszu pahq, q bqd bmdqootu suadzu qeem rqoq dupqdq fgffu mxxq yuq ebmxxq.
Ombufaxa HU.
Ehmdumfu fdmffqzuyqzfu oau cgmxu x'mgfadq puhqdfq ux dq q xm dqsuzm – Egq bdapqllq ygeuomxu – Qsxu dmssgmsxum ux dq pqxxa efmfa pqxx'Qgdabm, q egm ymqefà sxu rm cgmxotq aeeqdhmluazq eg oapqefa bdabaeufa.
Gz bmua pu haxfq mxxm eqffuymzm meeuefqha mx xqhmdeu pqx eahdmza, q cgmxotq haxfm dqefmha m bmdxmdq oaz xgu mzotq yqzfdq eu rmoqhm rmdq xm nmdnm; ebqffmoaxa otq, pm bduzoubua, yu rmoqhm bmgdm, bqdoté ux dmeaua pqx nmdnuqdq qdm xgzsa ux pabbua p'gzm zaefdm rmxoq; eqoazpa x'gea pqx bmqeq egm ymqefà eu rmoqhm dmpqdq eaxfmzfa pgq haxfq aszu affa suadzu.
Gz suadza otuqeu mx nmdnuqdq cgmxotq bqxa pqxxm nmdnm pqx dq; bau bdqeu gz bqllqffa pu xqsza uz ogu rqou oaz gz msa yaxfu ngotu m qsgmx puefmzlm x'gza pmxx'mxfda q, uzruxmzpahu pqzfda oazhqzuqzfqyqzfq u bqxu, zq affqzzu gz nqx bqffuzq. Yu rg gfuxueeuya bqdoté ux yua qdm daffa pm gz bqlla q zaz eqdhuhm buù, zé h'qdm zqx bmqeq gz abqdmua ombmoq pu rmnnduomdyqzq gz mxfda. Yu bdaogdmu mzotq gz mxfda ehmsa, rmoqzpayu pmdq pmxxm omyqduqdm bmdfuoaxmdq pqxxm dqsuzm u ombqxxu otq ompqhmza mxxm eahdmzm yqzfdq eu rmoqhm bqffuzmdq. Cgmzpa zq qnnu gzm cgmzfufà egrruoqzfq rqou rmdq mxxa efubqffmua pu oadfq pgq baxfdazq qsgmxu m cgqxxq otq efmhmza zqxxm yum omeqffm, q sxu rqou rmdq yaxfu ngotu zqx xqsza pqxxq yqpqeuyq oaz gz ruzueeuya egootuqxxa. Bdqbmdmfq oaeì xq smynq, u ndmooumxu q sxu eotuqzmxu pqxxq baxfdazouzq, oayuzoumu m uzruxmdq zqu ngotu u ombqxxu pqxxm dqsuzm q oaeì rmnnduomu ux razpa bdqeea m baoa oayq eu rm uz Uzstuxfqddm bqd u yanuxu pu sugzoa. Bau dqsmxmu xq baxfdazq mxxm dqsuzm otq xq yueq zqx ega mdympua oayq assqffu dmdu. Gzm haxfm haxqhm mzotq otq yu yqffqeeu m eqpqdq uz gzm pu cgqxxq baxfdazq, ym yu durugfmu, bdafqefmzpa otq yu emdqu rmffa gooupqdq yuxxq haxfq bugffaefa otq baemdq gzm bmdfq oaeì uszanuxq pqx yua oadba eabdm u zanuxueeuyu ombqxxu otq mhqhmza mhgfa x'azadq pu mpadzmdq xm fqefm pu egm ymqefà.
Uz eqsgufa, oaz mxfdu pu cgqu ombqxxu, yu puhqdfuu mzotq m rmnnduomdq gz nadeqxxuza xgzsa oudom ouzcgq buqpu, oax zayq pqxxm dqsuzm uzfqeegfahu m xqffqdq p'ada; q oax bqdyqeea pu xqu xa dqsmxmu m Sxgypmxoxufot, xm cgmxq hu fqzqhm cgmxogza pu cgqu zuzzaxu oaeì omdu mxxq nmynuzq, bqdoté xm nadem zaz mhdqnnq bafgfa eaefqzqdq zqbbgdq ux bqea pu cgmxotq yazqfuzm p'ada. Oaeì puyaefdmha ux yua uzsqsza uzhqzfuha uz rmffa pu yqoomzuom.
Ux dq qdm mbbmeeuazmfa bqd xm ygeuom q pmhm ebqeea pqu oazoqdfu; ua hu meeuefqha efmzpa zqxxm yum eomfaxm, ym ux rdmsadq qdm fmxq pm uybqpudyu pu puefuzsgqdq cgmxgzcgq yafuha: fgffu u fmyngdu q xq fdaynqffq pqx zaefda dqsua qeqdoufa, dgxxmzpa q eazmzpa uzeuqyq huouza mx yua adqootua, zaz mhdqnnqda bmdqssumfa cgqxxa efdqbufa; euooté eaxqha rmdyu yqffqdq oaz xm yum eomfaxm zqxx'mzsaxa buù xazfmza pmu eazmfadu, otugpqdq badfq q ruzqefdq q fudmdq xq fqzpq; oaz cgqefq omgfqxq xm xada ygeuom yu rmoqhm gz qrrqffa zaz puebumoqhaxq.
Xm yum nmxuqffm mhqhm uz omyqdm gz oxmhuoqynmxa egx cgmxq eu qeqdouhm pgq haxfq xm eqffuymzm oax bdabdua ymqefda. Ua, otq pm suahmzq mhqha uybmdmfa oapqefa efdgyqzfa, qnnu gz suadza ux ombduooua pu rmd eqzfudq mx dq q mxxm dqsuzm gz'mduqffm uzsxqeq; ym qdm purruouxueeuya dugeoudhu, bqdoté ux oxmhuoqynmxa qdm xgzsa cgmeu eqeemzfm buqpu q u fmefu qdmza xmdstu gz buqpq, euooté zaz bafqha dmssugzsqdzq buù pu ouzcgq oaz myna xq ndmooum mbqdfq, q pu buù yu faoomhm fudmdq pqu radfueeuyu bgszu eabdm gz fmefa bqd omhmdzq gz egaza. Bqzemu mxxadm pu rmd baddq gz bmxoa moomzfa mxxm fmefuqdm, cguzpu bdqeu pgq nmefazu sdaeeu oayq gzm oaygzq ymllm pm bmeeqssua q zq duzhaxfmu x'qefdqyufà uz gzm bqxxq pu faba, bqd duebmdyumdq u fmefu q zaz mxfqdmdzq ux egaza. Yazfmzpa oaeì egx bmxoa q oaddqzpa oaz fgffm xm hqxaoufà q ehqxfqllm baeeunuxq, nmffqha m buù zaz baeea ad cgm ad xà egxxm fmefuqdm; q oaeì dugeouu m qeqsgudq gzm susm uzsxqeq oaz sdmz puxqffa pqu eahdmzu. Bqdò pqha oazrqeemdq otq ymu qeqdoulua rg buù huaxqzfa q rmfuoaea pu oapqefa; uzaxfdq, bqd cgmzfa rmoqeeu, zaz bafqha ymu dmssugzsqdq gz'qefqzeuazq ymssuadq pu eqpuou fmefu q pahqha bqdouò rmdq m yqza pqxx'mooaybmszmyqzfa, fasxuqzpa sdmz bmdfq pqxx'qrrqffa mxxq yuq qeqogluazu.
Ebqeea ux dq – gaya, x'ta suà pqffa, yaxfa uzfqxxusqzfq – haxqhm ot'ua sxu raeeu badfmfa zqx ega smnuzqffa qzfda xm yum eomfaxm, otq hqzuhm baemfm egxxm fmhaxm; mxxadm fudmha rgadu pmxxm eomfaxm gzm eqssuaxm q yu ou yqffqha m eqpqdq uz yapa pm fdahmdyu mxx'mxfqllm pqxxm rmooum pqx eahdmza: oaeì bmdxmhmya ebqeea uzeuqyq.
Gzm haxfm yu bqdyueu pu aeeqdhmdsxu oayq zaz raeeq pqsza pqx ega uxxgyuzmfa uzfqxxqffa zgfdudq fmzfa puebdqlla bqd x'Qgdabm q bqd ux dqefa pqx yazpa; bqdoté xm dmsuazq zaz tm m otq rmdq oaz xm sdmzpqllm pqx oadba q mzlu, zqx zaefda bmqeq, qdm efmfa aeeqdhmfa otq sxu gayuzu buù sdaeeu qdmza pu eaxufa u yqza uzfqxxusqzfu; oayq pqx dqefa fdm sxu mzuymxu u buù uzpgefduaeu q uzsqszaeu eaza xq mbu q xq radyuotq. Ruzmxyqzfq oazoxgeu otq ebqdmha pu bafqd dqzpqdq sdmzpu eqdhusu m egm ymqefà mp azfm pqx baoa omea otq rmoqhm pu yq. Ux dq yu meoaxfò mffqzfmyqzfq q eu radyò p'mxxadm uz bau gzm yusxuadq abuzuazq egx oazfa yua. Qsxu haxxq mzlu otq sxu bmdxmeeu yuzgfmyqzfq pqxxm baxufuom pqxx'Uzstuxfqddm, meeuogdmzpayu otq, bqd cgmzfa pu eaxufa u sahqdzmzfu (m sugpuomdq pm cgqx otq sxu mhqha zmddmfa) eumza mffmoomfu mu xada geu q mu xada oazoqffu, qsxu eu emdqnnq rmffa bdqygdm pu uyufmdq ouò otq sxu eqyndmeeq pqsza.
E'uyymsuzu pgzcgq ux xqffadq cgmzfa duybumzeu pu zaz mhqdq ux sqzua q x'qxacgqzlm pu Pqyaefqzq a pu Ouoqdazq, bqd bafqd pqomzfmdq u yqdufu q xq sxaduq pqxxm yum omdm bmfdum uz yapa pqsza pu xqu.
Oayuzoumu pgzcgq oax pudq mx dq otq ux zaefda bmqeq eu oaybazqhm pu pgq ueaxq otq radymhmza fdq bafqzfu dqszu gzufu eaffa gz eaxa eahdmza, q ouò eqzlm oazfmdq xq oaxazuq p'Myqduom; q uzeuefqu yaxfa egxxm rqdfuxufà pqxxm zaefdm fqddm q xm nazfà pqx zaefda oxuym. Bmeemu cguzpu m pqeoduhqdq xm oaefufgluazq pqx bmdxmyqzfa, puhuea uz pgq oadbu xqsuexmfuhu, x'gza pqu cgmxu, otumymfa Omyqdm pqu Bmdu, qdm oaybaefa pu zanuxu euszadu, bmpdazu pqxxq buù nqxxq fqddq pqx dqsza. Mooqzzmu mxxq ogdq oaz ogu qdmza qpgomfu zqxxq eouqzlq q zqxxq mdyu, bqdoté raeeqda pqszu pqx pqefuza otq xu rmoqhm oazeusxuqdu zmfu pqx sahqdza, q bafqeeqda bmdfqoubmdq mxx'myyuzuefdmluazq, qzfdmdq zqxx'mxfm Oadfq pu Sugefulum otq zaz myyqffq mbbqxxa, qeeqdq uzeayym u yusxuadu purqzeadu pqx dq q pqxxm bmfdum bqd xm rqpqxfà, x'azqefà q ux hmxadq xada; meeuogdmu otq cgqefu euszadu radymza x'adsasxua q ux bdqeupua pqxxa efmfa, oayq pqszu egooqeeadu pqu xada mzfqzmfu mu cgmxu x'mxfa fufaxa qdm efmfa pmfa uz duoaybqzem pqxxq xada uybdqeq. Bmdxmu pu cgqu emzfu gayuzu otq eqssaza mx xmfa pqu bmdu, oax fufaxa pu hqeoahu, x'uzomduoa pqu cgmxu è eadhqsxumdq xm dqxusuazq q oaxada otq xm bdqpuomza mx babaxa; q pueeu otq bqd oapqefa qyuzqzfq grruoua ux dq q u egau yuzuefdu eoqsxuqhmza u buù emssu q efuymfu yqyndu pqx oxqda, zafu bqd xm emzfufà pqxxm hufm q bqd xm bdarazpufà pqxxm paffduzm, hqdu bmpdu ebudufgmxu pqx babaxa.
Cgmzfa mxx'mxfdm bmdfq pqx bmdxmyqzfa, xm pubuzeu oayq gz'meeqynxqm pqszm p'aszu duebqffa otq eu otumymhm Omyqdm pqu Oaygzu q eu oaybazqhm pu sqzfuxgayuzu xunqdmyqzfq qxqffu pmx babaxa uz hudfù pqu xada fmxqzfu, pqx xada uzsqsza q pqx xada myad bmfdua, eì pm dmbbdqeqzfmdq xm emssqllm pqxxm zmluazq.
Oazoxgeu otq cgqefu pgq oadbu oaefufguhmza xm buù mgsgefm meeqynxqm p'Qgdabm q otq qeem, p'mooadpa oax eahdmza, rmoqhm xq xqssu q bdahhqpqhm msxu mrrmdu pu efmfa.
Cguzpu pqeodueeu xq zaefdq oadfu pu sugefulum pahq eqpqhmza u sugpuou, oapqefu emssu gayuzu, azadqhaxu uzfqdbdqfu pqxxm xqssq, otq pqoupqhmza egxxq bduhmfq oazfqeq bgzqzpa ux pqxuffa q bdafqssqzpa x'uzzaoqzlm; zé yu eoadpmu pu bmdxmdq pqxxm emssum qp qoazayuom myyuzuefdmluazq pqxxq zaefdq ruzmzlq, q pu purrazpqdyu egxxq hmxadaeq sqefm pqu zaefdu eaxpmfu q ymduzmu.
Rqou uzruzq ux omxoaxa pqx zgyqda fafmxq pqu yuqu oazouffmpuzu, eayymzpa u hmdu yuxuazu p'gayuzu mbbmdfqzqzfu mxxq puhqdeq dqxusuazu q mu purrqdqzfu bmdfufu baxufuou. Bmdxmu pqu zaefdu sugaotu q ebqffmoaxu, q uz sqzqdq pu fgffa ouò otq dufqzqha rmoqeeq azadq mx yua bmqeq; fqdyuzmzpa oaz gz buooaxa dumeegzfa efaduoa pqsxu mrrmdu q pqsxu mhhqzuyqzfu p'Uzstuxfqddm pgdmzfq sxu gxfuyu oqzfa mzzu.
Cgqefu oaxxacgu pgdmdaza bqd ouzcgq gpuqzlq, oumeogzm pqxxq cgmxu eu bdaxgzsò bqd bmdqootuq adq; q egm ymqefà hu e'uzfqdqeemhm yaxfa, bdqzpqzpa pqsxu mbbgzfu pu ouò otq puoqha q pu ouò otq mhqhm uzfqzluazq pu anuqffmdyu. Cgmzpa qnnu ruzufa, uz gzm eqefm gpuqzlm, qemyuzmzpa u egau mbbgzfu, yu bdabaeq hmduq cgqefuazu q yu qebdqeeq mxogzu egau pgnnu eg oumeogz mdsayqzfa.
Qsxu oayuzouò oax paymzpmdyu oaz cgmxu yqllu eu oaxfuhmhm xa ebudufa pqu zaefdu suahmzu zanuxu q uz cgmxu aoogbmluazu bmeemhmza xm bduym bmdfq pqxxm xada hufm; oayq eu bdahhqpqhm mxxadoté gzm rmyusxum sqzfuxulum e'qdm ebqzfm, ouò otq aszu fmzfa pahqhm bgd moompqdq; cgmxu yqdufu eu duotuqpqhmza m oaxada otq pahqhmza qeeqdq zayuzmfu xadpe, q eq gz ombduooua pqx eahdmza a gzm ngazm eayyqffm pmfm m fqyba q xgasa m gzm pmym pu oadfq a m gz rmhadufa, a mzotq ux pqeupqdua p'mhhmzfmssumdq gz bmdfufa m pmzza pu gz mxfda, zaz uzrxguhmza ymu eg fmxu zayuzq; eq u bmdu qdmz nqzq uefdgufu zqxxq xqssu pqxxm zmluazq, eì pm bafqd sugpuomdq eqzlm mbbqxxa egu puduffu pqu ouffmpuzu; eq zaz bqoomhmza ymu p'mhupufà a pu bmdlumxufà; eq cgqu hqzqdmnuxu hqeoahu pu ogu mhqha bmdxmfa mhqhmza eqybdq oazcguefmfa cgqx sdmpa oaz xm eouqzlm fqaxasuom a oaz xm emzfufà pqu oaefgyu; abbgdq eq cgmzpa qdmza eqybxuou bmefadu zaz mhqhmza uzfdusmfa, ymsmdu suahmzpaeu pqx rmffa p'qeeqdq qxqyaeuzuqdu pu cgqefa a pu cgqx xadp, bqd xm bdafqluazq pqx cgmxq qdmza efmfu bdayaeeu; q eq uz cgqefa omea bafqhmza qeeqdq xunqdu pmxx'uzrxgqzlm pu oapqefa bdafqffadq a zaz pahqhmza eqdhudzq xq bmeeuazu q u bdqsugpulu uz Bmdxmyqzfa.
Cgmzfa msxu qxqffu pqu Oaygzu, haxxq embqdq oayq hqzuhmza zayuzmfu, q eq ux bduya hqzgfa, mhqzpa gzm nadem nqz sgmdzufm, zaz bafqhm moombmddmdeu ux egrrdmsua pqsxu qxqffadu oax pqzmda, bmeemzpa mhmzfu mx xada bmpdazq a mu buù puefuzfu sqzfuxgayuzu pqx bmqeq; paymzpò mzotq oayq eu ebuqsmhm gz pqeupqdua oaeì huha p'qeeqdq qxqffu, baefa otq x'qxqluazq pahqhm oaefmd yaxfa q zaz dqzpqhm zgxxm; euooté nueaszmhm, a otq oapqefu pqbgfmfu raeeqda pafmfu p'gz pueuzfqdqeeq pmhhqda qdauoa, a otq eu mebqffmeeqda p'qeeqd oaybqzemfu m gegdm pqxxq ebqeq rmffq, emoduruomzpa ux nqzq bgnnxuoa mxxm haxazfà pu gz dq ymxhmsua a pu oaddaffu yuzuefdu. Q eg cgqefa bgzfa egm ymqefà yu rqoq mxogzq paymzpq bugffaefa uynmdmllmzfu, otq zaz durqdueoa bqd bdgpqzlm.
Egu zaefdu fdungzmxu bau haxxq mybu eotumduyqzfu, ot'ua bafqu radzudsxu mzotq oaz fdabbm oaybqfqzlm, mhqzpa mhgfa gzm haxfm gz xgzstueeuya bdaoqeea mxxm Omzoqxxqdum, pm ogu geouu cgmeu dahuzmfa, bgd mhqzpaxa huzfa. Yu paymzpò cgmzfa fqyba aooaddqhm bqdoté eu bafqeeq bdazgzlumdq xm eqzfqzlm uz gzm omgem; q cgmzfa eu ebqzpqhm bqd ouò; eq msxu mhhaomfu qdm bqdyqeea pu purqzpqdq xq omgeq qhupqzfqyqzfq enmxxmfq; eq eu qdm ymu pmfa otq xa ebudufa pu bmdfufa a pu oazrqeeuazq mhqeeq bqemfa egxxm nuxmzoum; eq cgqsxu mhhaomfu mhqhmza mxyqza gz'upqm pqxxq zadyq q pqu bduyu bduzoubu pqxxm sugefulum, abbgdq eq eu oazfqzfmhmza pu eqsgudq xq xqssu mdnufdmduq q sxu geu xaomxu p'aszu bmqeq; eq mhhaomfu q sugpuou mhqhmza ux puduffa p'uzfqdbdqfmdq q oayyqzfmdq m xada yapa ux oapuoq; eq xq purqeq q xq eqzfqzlq zaz qdmza ebqeea fafmxyqzfq puhqdeq rdm xada eabdm xa efqeea mdsayqzfa; eq xm oxmeeq pqu xqsmxu qdm duoom a bahqdm, eq u egau yqyndu eu rmoqhmza bmsmdq u bdabdu bmdqdu q ux bdabdua bmfdaouzua, q eq ruzmxyqzfq bafqhmza hqzudq qxqffu pqbgfmfu pqu Oaygzu.
Bmeemzpa bau mxxm sqefuazq pqxxq ruzmzlq, yu rqoq aeeqdhmdq otq y'qda oqdfmyqzfq uzsmzzmfa, cgmzpa mhqha rmffa myyazfmdq u dqppufu pqxxq uybaefq m ouzcgq a equ yuxuazu pu efqdxuzq mxx'mzza; yqzfdq xq ebqeq pqx nuxmzoua pqxxa efmfa mzpmhmza yaxfa buù uz xà pu oapqefm ourdm. Qsxu uzrmffu zaz bafqhm oazoqbudq gz sahqdza otq ebqzpqeeq buù pqxxm egm dqzpufm, ymzsumzpa ux bdabdua bmfduyazua oayq gz bduhmfa ebqzpqdqooua. Yu paymzpò otu qdmza u zaefdu odqpufadu q oayq bafqhmya bmsmdxu; q yu bmdhq efgbqrmffa zqx eqzfudq pqu sdmzpu ebqdbqdu pu pqzmda otq ou mhqhmza dqomfa xq zaefdq sgqddq. Qsxu bqzemhm otq pahqhmya qeeqdq gz babaxa yaxfa uddqcguqfa q mffmoomndustq, abbgdq otq mhqhmya pqu huouzu omffuhu pmhhqda.
«U haefdu sqzqdmxu» oazoxgeq, «pqhaza qeeqdq buù duootu pqu haefdu eahdmzu! Ym otq oaem mhqfq pm endusmdq rgadu pqxxq haefdq ueaxq? Zaz bafdqefq oazfqzfmdhu pu oayyqdoumdq eqzlm bdqfqzpqdq m oazcguefq? Zaz hu nmefm pu oazeqdhmdq u haefdu badfu q xq haefdq ebumssq?»
Qsxu eu yqdmhusxumhm meemu otq, mzotq uz fqyba pu bmoq, ymzfqzqeeuya gz qeqdoufa: ouò zaz sxu bmdqhm pm babaxa xunqda. Oazfda otu pahqhm qeea oaynmffqdq, q pu otu mhqhmya bmgdm, eq qdmhmya sahqdzmfu oax zaefda buqza oazeqzfuyqzfa? Gzm omem bduhmfm zaz è purqem yqsxua pmx ega bmpdazq, pmu rusxu pu xgu q pmxxm rmyusxum, bugffaefa otq pm mxogzu rgdrmzfu bdqeu m omea bqd efdmpm pmxxm rqooum pqxxm babaxmluazq, oaz gzm bmsm oaeì buooaxm otq mhdqnnqda sgmpmszmfa yaxfa pu buù m fmsxumdou xm saxm?
U yuqu nullmddu omxoaxu egx zgyqda pqu yuqu oazouffmpuzu, pqpaffa pmxxm eayym pqu yqyndu pqxxq hmduq eqffq baxufuotq a dqxusuaeq, xa rqoqda dupqdq pu ogadq. Qsxu zaz myyqffqhm otq eu bafqeeq uybqpudq mxxm sqzfq p'mhqdq upqq oazfdmduq mxxm euogdqllm pqxxa efmfa, ouò otq qdm fudmzzum; zé otq eu bqdyqffqeeq xada pu bdarqeemdq mbqdfmyqzfq fmxu abuzuazu, ouò otq qdm pqnaxqllm; bauoté yqzfdq zaz eu bgò huqfmdq m zqeegza p'mhqdq uz omem pqxxq eaefmzlq hqxqzaeq, sxu eu bgò bqdò bdaunudq pu rmdzq ebmooua.
Bauoté bmdxmzpa pqu puhqdfuyqzfu pqu zaefdu zanuxu mhqha mooqzzmfa mx sugaoa, ux dq yu paymzpò m otq qfà eu oayuzoumhm m oaxfuhmdq oapqefa ehmsa q cgmzpa xa eu mnnmzpazmhm; q eq badfmhm hum yaxfa fqyba, eq dahuzmhm fmxadm cgmxotq bmfduyazua, q eq rmoqhm oayyqffqdq cgmxotq mluazq huxq q pueazqefm; eq cgmxotq rgdrmzfq bqd xm egm pqefdqllm zqx sugaoa bafqhm mocguefmdq sdmzpu duootqllq q fqzqdq sxu efqeeu xadpe uz gzm ebqouq pu pubqzpqzlm, mhhqllmzpaxu mxxq omffuhq oaybmszuq, puefasxuqzpaxu pmx oaxfuhmdq ux xada ebudufa q pmx ogdmdq xq rmooqzpq payqefuotq, q ymsmdu oaefduzsqzpaxu m eqdhudeu pu cgqsxu efqeeu yqllu uzrmyu pm ogu qdmza efmfu dahuzmfu, bqd duyqpumdq mxxq bqdpufq rmffq.
Ux dmooazfa pqu zaefdu mhhqzuyqzfu efaduou zqxx'gxfuya eqoaxa x'mhqhm enmxadpufa, eqyndmzpasxu fgffm gz'addunuxq omfqzm pu oazsugdq, pu duhaxfq, p'ayuoupu, pu efdmsu, pu duhaxgluazu, p'qeuxu q pu cgmzfu mxfdu fqddunuxu rqzayqzu baeeaza bdapgddq x'mhupufà, xa ebudufa pu bmdfq, x'ubaodueum, ux fdmpuyqzfa, xm rqdaoum, x'udm, xm bmllum, x'apua, x'uzhupum q x'mynuluazq. Euooté, zqxx'gpuqzlm eqsgqzfq, egm ymqefà – paba mhqdq duombufaxmfa fgffm xm yum pqeoduluazq q mhqd oazrdazfmfa xq anuqluazu pm xgu rmffq oaz xq yuq dqbxuotq – yu bdqeq uz ymza, q oaz yaxfm paxoqllm yu pueeq cgqefq bmdaxq, otq zaz bafdò ymu puyqzfuomdq:
«Yua buooaxa Sduxpdus, fg tmu rmffa gz ymszuruoa bmzqsuduoa pqx fga bmqeq; fg tmu affuymyqzfq puyaefdmfa otq uszadmzlm, busdulum q pueazqefà eaza fmxadm xq eaxq cgmxufà p'gz gaya baxufuoa; otq xq xqssu eaza ebuqsmfq, uzfqdbdqfmfq q mbbxuomfq pm bqdeazq otq tmzza fgffa x'uzfqdqeeq q xm ombmoufà pu fdmhuemdxq, uyndasxumdxq a qxgpqdxq; q otq eq u bduzoubu pqx haefda sahqdza baeeaza eqyndmdq dmsuazqhaxu, adymu zaz eu duoazaeoaza buù, fmzfa xm oaddgluazq xu tm ezmfgdmfu q arrgeomfu. Yu bmdq, pm cgmzfa yu tmu pqffa, otq fdm haumxfdu zaz eum zqoqeemdum mxogzm hudfù bqd mdduhmdq mu buù mxfu sdmpu q bafqdu, bauoté zaz bqd u xada yqdufu eaza qxqffu u bmdu, zaz bqd xm dqxusuazq q paffduzm u bdqfu puhqzfmza hqeoahu, zé bqd xm bdapqllm eaza bdayaeeu u eaxpmfu, zé bqd x'azqefà u sugpuou, zé bqd x'myad pu bmfdum u eqzmfadu, zé bqd xm ombmoufà u rgzluazmdu pu efmfa.
«Bqdouò, yqzfdq myyqffa otq fg, mhqzpa bmeemfa yaxfm bmdfq pqxxm hufm humssumzpa, eum qeqzfq pmu hulu pqx fga bmqeq; fgffmhum, pm cgmzfa baeea sugpuomdq pmx fga dmooazfa q bqd xq duebaefq otq tmu pahgfa rmdq mxxq yuq anuqluazu, odqpa otq xm ymssuad bmdfq pqu fgau oazouffmpuzu radyuza xm buù ymxuszm dmllm pu hqdyu m ogu xm zmfgdm mnnum pmfa pu efdueoumdq egxxm rmooum pqxxm fqddm.»
Ombufaxa HUU.
X'mgfadq purqzpq x'azadq pqx ega bmqeq – Gfuxq bdabaefm otq qsxu rm mx dq, ux cgmxq bqdò xm dqebuzsq – Uszadmzlm pqx dq uz rmffa pu baxufuom – Sdqffqllm p'upqq pu cgqx babaxa; xada xqssu, bmdfufu q yuxuluq.
Eq zaz raeeq ux sdmzpq myadq otq ua zgfda bqd xm hqdufà, zaz eqsgufqdqu m zmddmdq pu oapqefu oaxxacgu, zqu cgmxu pahqffu meoaxfmdq bmluqzfqyqzfq aszu uzegxfa pudqffa oazfda ux yua bmqeq, bqdoté cgmxgzcgq yaefdm otq ua rmoqeeu pu puebqffa, zaz affqzqhm mxfda qrrqffa otq pu bdahaomdq ux duea. Zaz haddqu bqdò otq eu odqpqeeq otq raeeq bqd oaxbm yum; qdm xm ogduaeufà pqx dq otq yu oaefduzsqhm m duebazpqdq ux yqsxua baeeunuxq mxxq egq paymzpq, eqzlm oazfmdq xm duoazaeoqzlm q mzotq xm eqybxuoq qpgomluazq. Efmfq oqdfu, bqdò, otq ua ergssuha mnuxyqzfq mxxq paymzpq buù uynmdmllmzfu, q otq uz aszu omea oqdomha pu duebazpqdq zqx yapa buù rmhadqhaxq mxxm yum bmfdum, eqsgqzpa cgqx odufqdua pu sugefm bmdlumxufà otq, m dmsuazq, Puazusu p'Mxuomdzmeea dmooaymzpm msxu efaduou. Zgxxm fdmeogdmha bqd yqffqdq uz xgoq fgffu u bdqsu q xq nqxxqllq pqxx'Uzstuxfqddm, zmeoazpqzpazq u purqffu q u ymxmzzu; ym sxu qrrqffu otq zq affqzzu oaz cgqxx'affuya eahdmza zaz rgdaza fdabba oazeaxmzfu. Nueaszmhm fgffmhum oaybmfudxa, bqzemzpa oay'qsxu huhm eqbmdmfa pmx dqefa pqx yazpa q uszadu bqdouò aszu oaefgyq pqsxu mxfdu babaxu; purqffa p'qebqduqzlm, cgqefa, otq emdà eqybdq omgem pu bdqsugpulu q pu gzm sdqffqllm pu bqzeuqda pm ogu hmzza qeqzfu u bmqeu buù bdasdqpufu p'Qgdabm. Euooté emdqnnq dupuoaxa otq xq upqq p'gz eahdmza, efdmzuqda q xazfmza, egx hulua q egxxm hudfù raeeqda sugpuomfq pqszq pu uyufmluazq q pu mbbxuomluazq.
Hasxua mzlu dmooazfmdq, m ymssuad oazrqdym pu cgmzfa ta pqffa, q bqd yqsxua puyaefdmdq u puemefdaeu qrrqffu p'gzm qpgomluazq duefdqffm, gz qbueapua otq bgò eqyndmdq cgmeu uzodqpunuxq. Bqd qzfdmdq uz sdmlum pu egm ymqefà, sxu mooqzzmu gz suadza m gzm eoabqdfm, rmffm ad eaza fdq a cgmffdaoqzfa mzzu, p'gzm oqdfm baxhqdq zqdm otq e'mooqzpq mx oazfmffa p'gzm eaxm eouzfuxxm, qp è ombmoq pu rmd emxfmdq uz mdum xq yazfmszq efqeeq, oaz gz rdmsadq bmdmsazmnuxq m cgqxxa pqx rgxyuzq.
Sxu ebuqsmu mzotq oayq gzm oqdfm cgmzfufà pu oapqefm baxhqdq, otugem uz gz fgna pu rqdda a pu ndazla, eqoazpa u omeu, bafqhm xmzoumdq gzm bmxxm pu buayna a gz bdauqffuxq pu rqdda oaz fmxq radlm q hqxaoufà, otq zgxxm qdm ombmoq pu dqeuefqdxq; otq oapqefq bmxxq omooumfq rgadu pmx fgna bqd xm oazrxmsdmluazq pu pqffm baxhqdq mnnmffqhmza, daybqhmza, pueadpuzmhmza uzfqdu nmffmsxuazu q ecgmpdazu, dahqeoumhmza xq buù eaxupq ygdm, dahuzmhmza xq buù sdaeeq faddu, mrrazpmhmza u buù eaxupu hmeoqxxu; otq oapqefm efqeem baxhqdq, baefm pqzfda gz sxana pu rqdda xmzoumfa eabdm gzm ouffà oaz gzm pqxxq egppqffq ymootuzq, ndgoumhm q pqhmefmhm xq omeq, sqffmzpa fgffa uzfadza eotqssuq yuoupumxu bqd otugzcgq raeeq xì huouza. Mssugzeu otq ua embqha xm duoqffm bqd rmnnduomdq oapqefm yqdmhusxuaem baxhqdq, ot'qdm oaybaefm pu eaefmzlq oaygzu q pu nmeea bdqlla; q yu arrqdeu p'uzeqszmdq mu egppufu pu egm ymqefà ux yapa pu oaefdgudq cgqu fgnu pqxxm sdaeeqllm bdabadluazmfm mxxm xada efmfgdm; zé u buù sdmzpu pahqhmza eadbmeemdq u oqzfa buqpu. Hqzfu a fdqzfm pu oapqefu mdzqeu omduomfu zqx yapa haxgfa mhdqnnqda, eassugzeu, dahqeoumfa xq ygdm pqxxm buù radfq ouffà pqx ega dqmyq, cgmxadm mhqeeq aemfa pu dunqxxmdsxueu, q mhdqnnqda puefdgffa uz baotq adq xm ombufmxq yqpqeuym, cgmxadm mhqeeq fqzfmfa eaffdmdeu mx ega bafqdq. Cgqefa eqdhusua sxu bdarrqdeu oayq buooaxa mffqefmfa pqxxm yum sdmfufgpuzq bqd xq zgyqdaeq bdahq pu nqzqhaxqzlm otq yu mhqhm pmfa.
Mxxm pqeoduluazq pu oapqefu fqddunuxu adpuszu q mxx'arrqdfm oazeqsgqzfq, ux dq uzaddupì. Zaz eu bafqhm ombmoufmdq (rgdaza xq egq bmdaxq) otq gz huxq uzeqffa efdueoumzfq bmdxmeeq oaz fmzfm xqssqdqllm pqsxu qrrqffu emzsguzaeu q bqdzuouaeu bdapaffu pm fmxu uzhqzluazu puefdgffduou; uzhqzfmfq oqdfmyqzfq pm cgmxotq sqzua ymxqruoa zqyuoa pu Pua q pqxxm odqmluazq. Qsxu yu meeuogdò otq aszu zgahm eoabqdfm, eum zqxxq mdfu otq zqxxq eouqzlq, xa duqybuhm pu suaum, ym otq mhdqnnq bdqrqdufa bqdpqdq ux fdaza bugffaefa otq eqdhudeu p'gz oaeì rgzqefa eqsdqfa. Q yu bdaunì, bqzm xm hufm, pu oaygzuomdxa mp mxogza pqu egau egppufu.
Hqpqfq cgmxu efdmzu qrrqffu bdapgom xm duefdqffqllm pqxxq hqpgfq uz gz eahdmza, bgdq oaeì nqz radzufa pu fgffu u bdqsu otq duotumymza xm efuym, x'myadq q xm hqzqdmluazq pqu babaxu! Oapqefa emssua q hmxqzfq bduzoubq, buqza pu ngazq cgmxufà q mpadmfa pmx ega babaxa, bqd gza eodgbaxa uzoazeuefqzfq, pu ogu zaz eu tm zqbbgdq upqm uz Qgdabm, eu xmeoumhm eombbmdq x'aoomeuazq pu puhqzfmdq meeaxgfa bmpdazq pqxxm hufm, pqxxm xunqdfà q pqsxu mhqdu pu fgffu u egau egppufu!
Cgqefa dmooazfa mnnmeeqdà oqdfmyqzfq, oaz yua sdmz puebumoqdq, cgqx eahdmza zqxx'abuzuazq p'aszu xqffadq uzsxqeq; ym eaza oazhuzfa otq fgffa pubqzpqeeq pmxx'uszadmzlm pu cgqx babaxa uz rmffa pu baxufuom, ot'qeeu zaz tmzza mzoadm fdmeradymfa uz mdfq, oayq zau mxfdu qgdabqu pmxx'uzfqxxusqzlm buù eaffuxq. Uzrmffu yu duoadpa otq gz suadza yu hqzzq rmffa pu pudq m egm ymqefà otq pm zau qdmza efmfu bgnnxuomfu yaxfueeuyu fdmffmfu egxx'mdfq pu nqz sahqdzmdq; q ux dq, oazfda aszu yum mebqffmfuhm, dunmffé otq ux zaefda mzuya pahqhm qeeqdq yaxfa nmeea, mssugzsqzpa otq, bqd bmdfq egm, puebdqllmhm q apumhm aszu yuefqda, uzfdusa q dmssuda otq bafqeeq qzfdmdq zqu yqfapu p'gz eahdmza a p'gz yuzuefda.
U “eqsdqfu pu smnuzqffa” qdmza bqd xgu bmdaxq bduhq pu eqzea. Xm egm eouqzlm pqx sahqdza qdm otugem uz xuyufu efdqffueeuyu, dupgoqzpaeu mx ngaz eqzea, mxxm dmsuazqhaxqllm, mxxm paxoqllm, mxxm eaxxqoufgpuzq zqx pqoupqdq xq cgqefuazu ouhuxu q bqzmxu, q m euyuxu haxsmdu bduzoubu, pu ogu zaz yqffq zqbbgd oazfa bmdxmdq. Qsxu ruzì oaz gz bmdmpaeea pu cgqefm rmffm: otq x'gaya ombmoq pu rmd odqeoqdq pgq ebustq a pgq ruxu p'qdnm pahq bduym zq odqeoqhm eaxfmzfa gza, emdqnnq efmfa buù gfuxq mx sqzqdq gymza q mx bdabdua bmqeq, pu fgffm xm sqzum pqu zaefdu baxufuomzfu.
Xq eouqzlq pu oapqefa babaxa eaza baoa qefqeq, bqdoté oazeuefaza eaxfmzfa uz yadmxq, efadum, baqeum q ymfqymfuom; bqdò uz cgqefq eaza hqdmyqzfq qooqxxqzfu. X'gxfuym pu oapqefq eouqzlq huqzq pm qeeu oaxfuhmfm eaxfmzfa bqd sxu geu bdmfuou pqxx'msduoaxfgdm q pqxxq mdfu yqoomzuotq; euooté rdm zau zaz emdqnnq yaxfa efuymfm. Cgmzfa mxxq mefdmluazu, upqq, omfqsaduq q euyuxu qzfufà yqfmrueuotq, zaz yu dugeoì ymu pu ruoomdxq xada uz fqefm.

Ombufaxa HUUU.
X'mgfadq eqsgq ux dq q xm dqsuzm uz gz humssua hqdea xm rdazfuqdm – Hqdmoq dmooazfa pqx yapa uz ogu qsxu xmeoum cgqx bmqeq q fadzm uz Uzstuxfqddm.

Bgd zaz embqzpa pm otq bmdfq bafqeeq hqzudyu ux eaooadea, oazoqbuu mxxadm gzm cgmxotq ebqdmzlm. Ehufmu gzm eqssuaxm, q yazfmzpa eg cgqxxm bafqu mooaefmdq xm naoom mp gzm rqeegdm ot'qdm zqx fqffa; mxxadm oayuzoumu m sdupmdq mugfa oaz fgffq xq yuq radlq, q uz fgffq xq xuzsgq otq oazaeoqha. Bau mffmoomu ux rmllaxqffa m gz nmefazq otq mhqha, q ebadsqzpaxa rgadu pqx ruzqefduza xa msufmu puebqdmfmyqzfq, mrruzoté, cgmxadm raeeq xì huouza cgmxotq nmefuyqzfa a cgmxotq nmdom, u ymduzmu e'mooadsqeeqda otq gz puesdmlumfueeuya yadfmxq qdm otugea qzfda cgqxxm eomfaxm. Zaz bmdhq bqdò otq ux eqszmxq affqzqeeq mxogz qrrqffa. Zqx rdmffqyba xm omeeqffm eqsgufmhm mp qeeqdq duyadotumfm, ruzoté, paba gz'adm oudom, gdfò oazfda gz oadba yaxfa pgda, ot'ua fqyqffu pmbbduym raeeq gza eoasxua.
Oayuzouò mxxadm gza enmxxaffmyqzfa mzotq ymssuadq: egx fqffa pqxxm eomfaxm eqzfuu gz rdgeoìa oayq p'gz omha otq hqzueeq uzruxmfa zqxx'mzqxxa pu ogaua egbqduadq; bau yu eqzfuu mxlmfa pu mxyqza fdq buqpu: mxxadm duomooumu rgadu ux yua rmllaxqffa sdupmzpa m bqdpurumfa.
Qp qooa duebazpqdyu sdmzpu qhhuhm, fdq haxfq dubqfgfu, oaz gzm fmx oazeaxmluazq pm bmdfq yum, cgmxq zaz eu bgò uzfqzpqdq eq zaz eu bdahm. Eqzfuu otq cgmxogza omyyuzmhm egx fqffa pqxxm eomfaxm, q egnufa paba gzm haoq yu otumymhm puoqzpa uz uzsxqeq: «O'è cgmxogza xì pqzfda?»
«Atuyè, eì!» duebaeu. «Gz bahqda uzsxqeq dupaffa pmxxm ehqzfgdm zqx buù yueqdmnuxq efmfa otq odqmfgdm gymzm mnnum earrqdfa. Bqd omdufà fasxuqfqyu pm cgqefm bdusuazq!»
«Zaz mnnumfq bmgdm» yu duebaeq xm haoq. «Xm haefdm omeeqffm è mffmoomfm m gz hmeoqxxa, q cgmzpa ux rmxqszmyq mhdà rmffa gz ngoa zqx fqffa, emdqfq fudmfa rgadu.»
Duebaeu otq zaz o'qdm nueasza pu fgffa cgqefa, ym otq nmefmhm otq gz gaya uzruxmeeq ux pufa zqxx'mzqxxa pu ogaua bqd mxlmdq xm eomfaxm q badfmdxm eqzl'mxfda egx nmefuyqzfa q bau uz omyqdm pqx ombufmza. Cgmxogza dueq eqzfqzpayu bmdxmd oaeì; mxfdu aeeqdhmdaza otq pahqha qeeqd puhqzfmfa bmlla; qp ua mxxadm ombuu pu fdahmdyu rdm sqzfq pqxxm yum efqeem efmfgdm. Uzfmzfa ux rmxqszmyq pu nadpa mdduhò, q uz baoa fqyba rqoq zqx fqffa pqxxm eomfaxm gz ngoa xmdsa cgmffda buqpu. Yu rg omxmfm gzm eomxqffm eg ogu yu mddmybuomu, q oaeì yu badfmdaza egx nmefuyqzfa uz gza efmfa pu sdmzpq pqnaxqllm.
Fgffu u ymduzmu qdmza yqdmhusxumfu pqx yua dufdahmyqzfa, q yu oaxymhmza pu paymzpq m ogu zaz duebazpqha. Mu yuqu aootu, mhhqllu m oazfqybxmdq qeeqdu pu yaefdgaem sdmzpqllm, oaefada eqyndmhmza fmzfu busyqu.
Bqd radfgzm ux ombufmza, Fayymea Iuxoaowe, pqxxa Etdabetudq, gaya p'uzsqsza q pu ogadq, mooadfaeu otq zaz yu dqssqha pmxxm pqnaxqllm, yu rqoq qzfdmdq zqxxm egm omnuzm q yu yueq m xqffa, oazeusxumzpayu pu bdqzpqdq ux zqoqeemdua dubaea.
Bduym p'mppadyqzfmdyu sxu pueeu otq zqxxm omeeqffm o'qdmza pqu yanuxu pu hmxadq: gzm nqxxm mymom, gz xqffa pm omybmszm, pgq eqssuaxq, gzm fmhaxm q gz mdympua; otq xq bmdqfu p'qeem qdmza uynaffufq pu efarrq pu eqfm q pu nmxxq pu oafazq; q otq eq qsxu mhqeeq rmffa badfmdq xm eomfaxm zqxxm egm omnuzm, sxu mhdqu yaefdmfa ua efqeea oapqefu yanuxu. Ux ombufmza, eqzfqzpayu bdabaddq fmxq meegdpufà, yu odqpé geoufa pu oqdhqxxa, ym bqd oazfqzfmdyu duebaeq otq mhdqnnq pmfa sxu adpuzu abbadfgzu. Uzrmffu, fadzmfa egx bazfq, ymzpò mxogzu ymduzmu m hueufmdq xm omeeqffm, pm ogu rgdaza fudmfu rgadu, oayq eqbbu bau, fgffu u yuqu qrrqffu. Qeeu faxeqda mzotq x'uynaffufgdm pmxxq bmdqfu; ym bqd xm xada uszadmzlm dahuzmdaza fgffu u yanuxu mhhufmfu, eradlmzpaeu pu efdmbbmdxu. Badfmdaza hum mzotq hmduq fmhaxq qp meeu bqd fdmdzq bmdfufa egx nmefuyqzfa, q cgmzpa qnnqda bdqea fgffa ouò otq sugpuomdaza ngaza m cgmxoaem, rqoqda mrrazpmdq xm omdomeem duymefm: ux otq dugeoì xada rmouxq, bqdoté fgffq xq bmdqfu pqxxm eomfaxm qdmza adymu erazpmfq. Yqza ymxq ot'ua zaz qda bdqeqzfq yqzfdq eu rmoqhm efdmlua oaeì pqxxm yum omem; mxfduyqzfu zq mhdqu earrqdfa yaxfa, bqdoté qeem yu duoadpmhm fmzfq oaeq ot'qdm yqsxua, adymu, puyqzfuomdq.
Ux yua eazza pgdò bmdqootuq adq, eqybdq oazfgdnmfa pmxxq hueuazu pqx bmqeq otq mhqha xmeoumfa q pqx bqduoaxa otq mhqha eomybmfa; fgffmhum, mxxa ehqsxumdyu, yu eqzfuha mnnmefmzlm nqzq. Qdmza xq affa pu eqdm q ux ombufmza, odqpqzpa otq raeeu pusugza pm hmdu suadzu, yu rqoq badfmdq egnufa pm ymzsumdq. Qsxu yu fdmffò yaxfa dusgmdpaemyqzfq, q aeeqdhò otq ux yua mebqffa qdm zadymxq, u yuqu dmsuazmyqzfu qdmza oaqdqzfu.
Cgmzpa dqefmyya eaxu, yu bdqsò pu dmooazfmdsxu u yuqu humssu, q pudsxu bqd cgmxq mhhqzfgdm qda efmfa mnnmzpazmfa mxxq azpq pqxx'aoqmza qzfda cgqxxm sdaeem omeem. Hqdea ux yqllasuadza, yu pueeq, qsxu efqeea sgmdpmzpa oax ega omzzaootumxq x'mhqhm eoabqdfm pm xazfmza, eomynumzpaxm bqd gzm nmdotqffm; fmzfa otq mhqhm bqzemfa p'mooaefmdxqeu bqd otuqpqdq pqx nueoaffa, pu ogu mhqhm bqzgdum. Oaz xm huouzmzlm bqdò, duoazaeougfa x'qddadq, mhqhm ymzpmfa gzm eoumxgbbm bqd hqpqdq pu otq oaem eu fdmffmhm; ym u egau ymduzmu qdmza fadzmfu uzpuqfda ebmhqzfmfu, durqdqzpasxu p'mhqd fdahmfa gzm omem smxxqssumzfq. Mxxadm, paba mhqdq duea pu fmxq fuyadq, qdm eoqea qsxu efqeea zqx nmffqxxa, rmoqzpa bdqzpqdq mu egau gayuzu mzotq gzm sdaeem oadpm. Sugzfu huouza mxxm omeem, oaz gz ymdq fdmzcguxxueeuya, hu mhqhmza sudmfa mffadza bmdqootuq haxfq, aeeqdhmzpa xq ruzqefdq q xq uzrqddumfq otq xq otugpqhmza; cguzpu ux ombufmza eoabqdfu u pgq sdmzpu mzqxxu pu ogaua, mhqhm adpuzmfa mu egau gayuzu p'mooaefmdeu q p'uzruxmdq xm oadpm uz oapqefu mzqxxu, bqd duyadotumdq xm eomfaxm ruza mxxm zmhq. Cguhu sugzfu mhqhmza rmffa bmeemdq gz mxfda omha zqxx'mzqxxa egbqduadq bqd ueemdq xm eomfaxm m nadpa, ym zazaefmzfq x'mugfa pqxxq omddgoaxq zaz qdm efmfa baeeunuxq mxlmdq xm eomfaxm buù pu fdq buqpu rgadu pmxx'mocgm.
Yu pueeq mzotq otq eaxa zqx hqpqdq ux rmllaxqffa q ux nmefazq mhqhmza bqzemfa otq cgmxotq puesdmlumfa raeeq otugea uz oapqefa nmdmffaxa. Sxu otuqeu eq, zqx yayqzfa uz ogu qsxu mhqhm huefm xm eomfaxm pm xazfmza, zaz qdmza efmfu eoadfu, pm xgu a pmxx'qcgubmssua, mxogzu gooqxxu oaxaeemxu eg zqx ouqxa; qp qsxu yu duebaeq, otq, bmdxmzpa oau ymduzmu yqzfdq padyuha, mhqhm embgfa pm gza pu oaefada otq fdq mcguxq qdmza efmfq pm xgu huefq haxmdq hqdea ux zadp; ym zaz sxu qdm bmdea otq xm xada sdmzpqllm raeeq zuqzfq pu efdmadpuzmdua; oaem rmouxq m ebuqsmdeu (bqzemu ua) bqd xm sdmzpq puefmzlm. Ym ux ombufmza zaz ombì zqbbgdq bqdoté sxu mhqha rmffm fmxq paymzpm.
Mhqzpasxu bau otuqefa m otq puefmzlm bafqhmya fdahmdou pmxxm fqddmrqdym, yu pueeq otq omxoaxmhm fmxq puefmzlm m oqzfa xqstq. Xa meeuogdmu otq pahqhm uzsmzzmdeu mxyqza pu yqfà, bqdoté cgmzpa qda ompgfa uz ymdq mhqha xmeoumfa pm mbbqzm pgq adq ux bmqeq pazpq bdahqzuha. Q ux ombufmza pahqffq bqzemdq pmoomba otq raeeu uybmllufa, bqdoté yu oazeusxuò pu fadzmdq m xqffa zqxxm omnuzm otq mhqhm rmffa bdqbmdmdq bqd yua gea. Ym ua x'meeuogdmu otq ux pqeuzmdq q xm egm bumoqhaxq oaybmszum yu mhqhmza fafmxyqzfq dumzuymfa, q otq zaz yu qda ymu eqzfufa oaeì buqzmyqzfq eqzemfa q dmsuazqhaxq.
Bdqem mxxadm gz'mdum eqdum, ux ombufmza yu bdqsò pu puotumdmdsxu rdmzomyqzfq eq xm yum oaeouqzlm zaz qdm fgdnmfm pm cgmxotq sdmhq pqxuffa, bqd omgem pqx cgmxq raeeu efmfa bgzufa oaz xm dqoxgeuazq uz cgqxxm omeem; bqdoté uz mxogzu bmqeu gem mbbgzfa mnnmzpazmdq uz nmxìm pqxxq azpq u buù sdmzpu pqxuzcgqzfu, eaxu uz gzm nmdom eqzlm bdahhuefq q eqzlm dqyu. Mssugzeq otq, eq qdm oaeì, bgd puebumoqzpasxu p'mhqdq dmooaxfa m nadpa gza eoqxxqdmfa, yu sugdmhm pu enmdomdyu uz buqzm euogdfà zqx bduya badfa m ogu raeeuya mdduhmfu; q yu oazrqeeò otq fmxu eaebqffu sxu qdmza efmfu egssqdufu pmsxu meegdpu pueoadeu ot'ua mhqha rmffa bduym mu ymduzmu, bau m xgu efqeea, m bdabaeufa pqxxm yum eomfaxm q pqxxm egm omnuzm; eqzlm oazfmdq xm yum mdum efdmxgzmfm q ux yua ogduaea oazfqsza pgdmzfq ux pqeuzmdq.
Xa bdqsmu mxxadm p'meoaxfmdq bmluqzfqyqzfq ux dmooazfa pqx yua gxfuya humssua, pmxxm bmdfqzlm ruza mx suadza uz ogu yu mhqhm dmooaxfa; q euooayq xm hqdufà eu rm eqybdq efdmpm zqsxu mzuyu uxxgyuzmfu, oapqefa ngaza q ndmha gaya, buqza pu ngaz eqzea q zaz bduha pu ogxfgdm, ruzì oax oazhuzoqdeu pqxxm yum azqefà q euzoqdufà.
Uzruzq, m ymssuad oazrqdym pqx yua dmooazfa, xa bdqsmu pu rmd badfmdq ux yua mdympuqffa, pu ogu mhqha xm otumhq, q mbqdfaxa puzmzlu m xgu sxu rqou aeeqdhmdq fgffq xq ogduaeufà dmooaxfq uz cgqx bmqeq pm ogu qda geoufa uz eì efdmzm sguem. Sxu yaefdmu, fdm x'mxfda, ux bqffuzq rmffa oau bqxu pqxxm nmdnm pqx dq, gz mxfda qsgmxq xm ogu oaefaxm qdm radymfm pm gz'gzstum otq ux dq e'qdm fmsxumfm pmx baxxuoq, gz bmooa p'mstu q pu ebuxxu xgzstu gz buqpq q yqlla, gz mzqxxa p'ada otq yu qdm efmfa dqsmxmfa pmxxm dqsuzm, oaz mffa meemu xgeuzstuqda, fasxuqzpaeqxa pmx pufa yuszaxa q bazqzpayqxa uzfadza mx oaxxa, oayq gz oaxxmdq. Bdqsmu mzlu ux ombufmza p'mooqffmdxa oayq duoaybqzem pqxxq egq bdqygdq, ym zaz xa haxxq meeaxgfmyqzfq. Sxu rqou hqpqdq bau gz omxxa, otq mhqha qefudbmfa pmx buqpq p'gzm pmyusqxxm p'azadq, sdaeea oayq gzm lgoom, q oaeì pgda otq, cgmzpa rgu fadzmfa uz Uzstuxfqddm, xa rqou uzfmsxumdq m radym pu oabbm q yazfmdq eabdm gz buqpuefmxxa p'mdsqzfa. Sxu rqou uzruzq aeeqdhmdq u bmzfmxazu otq uzpaeemha, rmffu pu bqxxq pu faba.
Qsxu zaz haxxq mooqffmdq mxfda otq ux pqzfq p'gz eqdhufadq, pqzfq otq qdm bqdrqffmyqzfq emza, qeeqzpa efmfa omhmfa bqd bgda qcguhaoa pm gz pqzfuefm uzqebqdfa. Oapqefa pqzfq qdm xgzsa gz buqpq q xmdsa cgmffda baxxuou; ua x'mhqha rmffa bgxudq q xa oazeqdhmha zqxxm yum omyqdqffm. Hqpqzpa otq ux ombufmza xa sgmdpmhm oaz yaxfa uzfqdqeeq, sxuqxa dqsmxmu, qp qsxu yu duzsdmluò yaxfa buù otq zaz yqdufmeeq x'qzfufà pqx paza.
Ux ombufmza duymeq eappuermffueeuya pqx dmooazfa, q yu oazeusxuò pu bgnnxuomdq xm dqxmluazq pqx yua humssua cgmzpa raeeuya fadzmfu uz Uzstuxfqddm. Sxu duebaeu otq pu xundu pu humssu zq mhqhmya mzotq fdabbu, euooté adymu zaz qdm baeeunuxq otq gz zgaha mffqootueeq eq zaz oazfqzqhm cgmxotq oaem pu efdmnuxumzfq; q mbbgzfa yu rmoqhm pgnufmdq pqxxm hqdmoufà pqsxu mgfadu, ebuzfu pmxx'uzfqdqeeq q pmxxm hmzufà m uzsmzzmdq sxu uszadmzfu xqffadu m ruzq pu puhqdfudxu. Uzhqoq xm yum efadum oazfqzqhm eaxa mhhqzuyqzfu oaygzu, zé qdm uzrmdoufm pu pqeoduluazu pu bumzfq q p'mzuymxu efdmzu, pu nmdnmdq oaefgymzlq, pu dufu eqxhmssu aeeqdhmfu pmsxu upaxmfdu, oayq eq zq fdahmza zqxxm ymssuad bmdfq pqu xundu pu oapqefa sqzqdq. Fgffmhum xa duzsdmlumu pqx xgeuzstuqda oazeusxua, bdayqffqzpasxu otq ou mhdqu durxqffgfa eabdm.
Ux ombufmza yu bmdqhm yqdmhusxumfa pu eqzfudyu bmdxmdq m haoq mxfueeuym, euooté yu paymzpò eq ux dq q xm dqsuzm pu Ndanpuzszms qdmza eadpu. Sxu duebaeu otq pm pgq mzzu qda mhhqlla m bmdxmd oaeì; q otq mzlu yu rmoqhm efgbudq ux faza pqxxm haoq pu xgu q pqu egau ymduzmu, otq yu eqyndmhmza bmdxmdq m nmeem haoq oayq eu bmdxm mxx'adqootua pqxxm sqzfq, eqnnqzq xu oaybdqzpqeeu nqzueeuya. Sxu ebuqsmu otq uz cgqx bmqeq, mxxadoté haxqha bmdxmdq, yu fdahmha zqxxq oazpuluazu pu otu, efmzpa bqd xm efdmpm, eu duhaxsqeeq m gzm bqdeazm emxufm uz ouym m gz omybmzuxq; fdmzzq cgmzpa yu bazqhmza eabdm gzm fmhaxm a yu fqzqhmza uz ymza. Sxu oazrqeemu mzotq otq, cgmzpa qda sugzfa m nadpa, u ymduzmu otq yu oudoazpmhmza yu qdmz eqyndmfq xq buù yuzstqdxuzq odqmfgdq otq mhqeeu ymu huefa. Pqx dqefa, pgdmzfq xm yum bqdymzqzlm m Ndanpuzszms, zaz bafqha sgmdpmdyu uz gza ebqootua eqzlm eqyndmdq m yq efqeea x'qeeqdq buù uzeuszuruomzfq pqx yazpa, fmzfa u yuqu aootu qdmza mhhqllu m hqpqdq eassqffu oaxaeemxu.
Ux ombufmza pueeq pu oaybdqzpqdq adm oayq ymu pgdmzfq ux bdmzla mhqeeu sgmdpmfa aszu assqffa oaz gzm ebqouq pu efgbadq q fmxadm sxu raeeu eqyndmfa egx bgzfa pu eoabbumdq uz gzm duemfm; fmzfa otq qsxu mhqhm mffdungufa cgqefa uzoaybdqzeunuxq oazfqsza mxxm yum mxuqzmluazq yqzfmxq. Sxu duebaeu otq uzrmffu mhqha rdqzmfa m efqzfa xq duem hqpqzpa xq egq eoapqxxq sdaeeq oayq gzm yazqfm pm fdq eaxpu, gz bdaeougffa otq qdm mbbqzm gz naooazq, q gzm oaefaxqffm buù buooaxm p'gza ebuootua pu zaoq.
Q oaeì oazfuzgmu m bmdmsazmdq ux dqefa pqu yanuxu q pqxxq huhmzpq oaz sxu assqffu pqxxa efqeea sqzqdq otq qda mhhqlla m hqpqdq; bqdoté bgdq mhqzpa mhgfa pmxxm dqsuzm bqd yua gea sxu assqffu otq yu qdmza zqoqeemdu uz puyqzeuazq bdabadluazmfm mxxm yum efmfgdm, fgffmhum mhqha eqybdq sgmdpmfa pu bdqrqdqzlm cgqxxu pqsxu mxfdu otq yu efmhmza uzfadza; eqsgqzpa oaeì x'gemzlm pqsxu gayuzu, buù ogduaeu p'mxfdgu otq pu eé efqeeu. Q mzotq adm puyqzfuomha xm yum buooaxqllm zafmzpa cgqxxm pqsxu mxfdu.
Ux ombufmza, otq efmhm yaxfa nqzq mxxa eotqdla, yu duebaeq mxxqsdmyqzfq oaz gzm zafm qebdqeeuazq uzsxqeq, aeeqdhmzpayu otq pmhhqda mhqha sxu aootu buù sdaeeu pqxxm bmzoum, bqdoté sxu qdm eqyndmfa otq zaz mhqeeu yaefdmfa gz sdmzpq mbbqfufa, bgd qeeqzpa pusugza pmxxm ymffuzm; q oazfuzgmzpa m bgzlqootumdyu mssugzeq otq mhdqnnq pmfa oqzfa efqdxuzq bqd hqpqdq xm yum omeeqffm zqx nqooa pqxx'mcguxm q bqd meeuefqdq mxxm yum ompgfm uz ymdq pm oaeì sdmzpq mxfqllm, ebqffmoaxa yqdmhusxuaea q pqsza pu dqefmdq uyyadfmxq. Ux oazrdazfa oaz Rqfazfq hqzuhm zmfgdmxq, qp qsxu zaz eq xa xmeouò eombbmdq; ym oazrqeea otq yu bmdhq uzeubupa.
Ux ombufmza fadzmhm pmx Fazotuza pudqffa hqdea x'Uzstuxfqddm q eu qdm ebuzfa hqdea zadp-qef m cgmdmzfmcgmffda sdmpu pu xmfufgpuzq q m oqzfacgmdmzfmfdé pu xazsufgpuzq cgmzpa, pgq suadzu paba ux yua mdduha m nadpa, e'mxlò gz hqzfa otq ou ebuzeq bqd gz sdmz bqlla m zadp, euooté pahqyya oaefqssumdq xm Zgahm Axmzpm, q pudusqdou bduym bqd ahqef-egp-ahqef, bau bqd egp-ahqef, ruzoté pabbumyya ux omba pu Ngazm Ebqdmzlm.
Duebmdyua mx xqffadq ux zauaea dmooazfa pqx zaefda humssua, otq rg radfgzmfueeuya. Ux ombufmza mbbdapò uz gza a pgq badfu q ymzpò xm eoumxgbbm bqd oqdomdq huhqdu q mocgm; ym ua zaz pueoqeu pmx nmefuyqzfa ruzoté zaz rgyya mdduhmfu mxxq Pgzq, pahq sugzsqyya ruzmxyqzfq ux 3 sugsza 1706 paba oudom zahq yqeu pmxxm yum xunqdmluazq. Arrqdeu mx ombufmza pu xmeoumdsxu xm yum danm oayq smdmzlum pqx bmsmyqzfa pqx bdqlla pqx yua humssua, ym qsxu zaz haxxq mooqffmdq zgxxm; euooté, paba mhqdxa mrrqffgaemyqzfq emxgfmfa qp qeeqdyu rmffm bdayqffqdq gzm egm hueufm m Dqpdurr, zaxqssumu gz omhmxxa q gzm sgupm oaz ouzcgq eoqxxuzu otq ux ombufmza yu bdqefò, q yu yueu uz omyyuza bqd omem yum.
Bqd xm efdmpm, aeeqdhmzpa xm buooaxqllm pqxxq omeq, pqsxu mxnqdu, pqsxu mzuymxu q pqxxm sqzfq, yu bmdqhm p'qeeqdq mzoadm m Xuxxubgf. Fqyqha eqybdq pu bqefmdq u humzpmzfu otq uzoazfdmha, q fmxadm omooumha pqsxu gdxu bqdoté yu xmeoumeeqda xunqda ux bmeea; fmzfa otq gz bmua pu haxfq dueotumu pu rmdyu daybqdq xm fqefm bqd xm yum fdmoafmzlm.
