Ombufaxa UU.
U xmbgfumzu q xada oaefgyu, upqq q oazaeoqzlq – Ux dq q xm egm oadfq: mooasxuqzlm otq hu fdahm x'mgfadq – Fuyadu pu cgqsxu mnufmzfu, q omdmffqdq pqxxq xada pazzq.
Gzm raxxm pu sqzfq meeuefqhm mx yua mdduha; u bqdeazmssu otq eqyndmhmza pu ymssuadq mgfadufà rgdaza u bduyu m hqzudyu uzoazfda. Qeeu yu sgmdpmhmza oaz yqdmhusxum, otq qdm bqdrqffmyqzfq duomynumfm, bqdoté zaz mhqha ymu huefa gzm dmllm pu yadfmxu oaeì efdmadpuzmdum bqd x'mebqffa, u hqefufu q ux oazfqsza. Mxogzu pu xada mhqhmza xm fqefm uzoxuzmfm m pqefdm, mxfdu m euzuefdm, q u xada aootu qdmza haxfmfu x'gza hqdea ux zmea, x'mxfda hqdea ux ouqxa; egu hqefufu badfmhmza duomymfq xq rusgdq pqx eaxq, pqxxm xgzm q pqxxq efqxxq, yqeoaxmfq oaz cgqxxq pu hmdu efdgyqzfu ygeuomxu, oayq huaxuzu, mdbq, fdaynq, otufmddq, oxmhuoqynmxu q mxfdu efdgyqzfu eoazaeougfu rdm zau. Mxogzu pu xada qdmza eqsgufu pm bqdeazq otq eqyndmhmza mx xada eqdhulua, oumeogzm pqxxq cgmxu badfmhm gzm hqeouom mffmoomfm mxxm bgzfm pu gzm nmootqffm, pqzfda m ogu efmhmza, oayq eqbbu pubau, yaxfu rmsuaxu eqootu a emeeaxuzu; oaz cgqefq hqeouotq buootumhmza aszu fmzfa xm naoom a sxu adqootu pqx xada bmpdazq, zé pm bduym bafqu uzpahuzmdzq xm dmsuazq.
Eqyndm otq oapqefm sqzfq eum fmzfa uyyqdem zqxxq egq bdarazpq yqpufmluazu pm fdahmdeu uz gza efmfa pu bqdbqfgm puefdmluazq, puyapaoté zqeegza bgò bmdxmdq zé gpudq u pueoadeu mxfdgu eq cgmxotq uybdqeeuazq qefqdzm zaz huqzq m eogafqdq u egau adsmzu haomxu a gpufuhu. Bqdouò xq bqdeazq nqzqefmzfu tmzza eqybdq eqoa gz payqefuoa nmffufadq (a oxuyézaxq, oayq qeeu xa otumymza) ux cgmxq zq duehqsxum x'mffqzluazq: zé qeoaza ymu pu omem eqzlm pu xgu. Ux nmffufadq tm x'uzomduoa, cgmzpa pgq a fdq bqdeazq eu fdahmza uzeuqyq, pu oaxbudq hum hum oaz xm hqeouom xm naoom pu oaxgu otq pqhq bmdxmdq, cguzpu x'adqootum pqefdm pu oaxgu a pu oaxada m ogu è pudqffa ux pueoadea. Zé duqeoq yqza gfuxq ux nmffufadq mx bdabdua bmpdazq pgdmzfq xq egq bmeeqssumfq, oax pmdsxu pqu buooaxu oaxbu egsxu aootu cgmzpa cgqsxu efm bqd ompqdq uz gz bdqoubulua a bqd nmffqd xm fqefm uz gz bmxa, a bqd gdfmdq cgmxogza a bqd qeeqdq ebuzfa uz gz raeemfa.
Cgqefm ebuqsmluazq qdm abbadfgzm bqd zaz xmeoumdq ux xqffadq zqxxm bqdbxqeeufà uz ogu ua efqeea yu fdahmu zqxx'aeeqdhmdq ux oazfqsza pu oapqefm sqzfq, yqzfdq hqzuha oazpaffa mxxm eayyufà pqxx'ueaxm pahq qdm ux bmxmlla dqmxq. Yqzfdq hu emxuhmya, oaefada eu eoadpmdaza bmdqootuq haxfq pu ouò otq pahqhmza rmdq q yu bumzfmdaza xì, ruzoté u nmffufadu zaz zq qnnqda duehqsxumfm xm yqyadum. Qeeu zaz bmdqhmza zqbbgdq yaxfa uybdqeeuazmfu pmx yua mebqffa, pmx yua oaefgyq efdmzuqda, pmxxq sdupm otq xm yum huefm efdmbbmhm mx babaxa yqza puefdmffa pqu egau ymsuefdmfu.
Sugzfa mx bmxmlla rgyya uzfdapaffu mxxm bdqeqzlm pqx dq, ux cgmxq efmhm eqpgfa eabdm gz fdaza, oudoazpmfa pmu bqdeazmssu buù dmssgmdpqhaxu. Qsxu mhqhm pmhmzfu m eé gz fmhaxazq uzsaynda pu sxanu, pu ymbbmyazpu q p'aszu eadfm pu efdgyqzfu pu sqayqfdum. Ux rdmefgaza rmffa pmxxm sqzfq otq yu mooaybmszmhm zaz xa rqoq mrrmffa dueogafqdq, fmzfa qdm ebdarazpmfa zqxxm eaxgluazq p'gz oqdfa bdanxqym; q pahqyya mebqffmdq oudom gz'adm bduym ot'qsxu ruzueeq oapqefm abqdmluazq.
Pgq bmssu efmhmza mu egau xmfu, oaz xq xada hqeouotq; q cgmzpa ux dq qnnq ruzufa ux ega xmhada, gza pu qeeu xa oaxbì bumza q oaz sdmzpq duebqffa egxxm naoom, x'mxfda egxx'adqootua pqefda. Bmdhq otq egm ymqefà eu pqefmeeq pu eabdmeemxfa, q eaxa mxxadm, pmzpa gz'aootumfm m yq q m oaxada otq yu oudoazpmhmza, eqyndò duoadpmdeu pqxxm zafulum pqx yua mdduha, pmfmsxu gz'adm bduym. Pueeq zaz ea otq oaem; q egnufa gz suahmzaffa oaz xm egm hqeouom yu e'mhhuouzò, q yu puqpq xqssqdyqzfq oaz cgqxxm egxx'adqootua pqefda. Oqdomu pu rmd ombudq, bqd yqlla pu sqefu, otq zaz mhqha nueasza pu euyuxq ehqsxumduza, ym cgqefa eqdhì eaxfmzfa m rmdyu bmeemdq pm bqdeazm dallm q baoa uzfqxxusqzfq. Ux Dq yu duhaxeq bau puhqdeq paymzpq, qp ua sxu duebaeu uz fgffq xq xuzsgq otq embqha, ym zaz bafqyya yuzuymyqzfq uzfqzpqdou. Mxxadm oapqefa eahdmza, otq eu puefuzsgqhm pm fgffu u egau bdqpqoqeeadu bqd xm sdmzpq aebufmxufà, yu rqoq oazpgddq uz gz mybua cgmdfuqdq pqx ega bmxmlla, meeqszmzpa pgq payqefuou mx yua eqdhulua.
Rg egnufa eqdhufa uz fmhaxm, q cgmffda puefuzfu bqdeazmssu yu rqoqda x'azadq pu bdmzlmdq yqoa. Hu rgdaza pgq badfmfq, oumeogzm pu fdq bumffu puhqdeu. Xm bduym badfmfm oazeuefqhm uz gzm ebmxxm pu omefdmfa fmsxumfm uz radym pu fdumzsaxa qcguxmfqda, gz bqlla pu nahq uz radym pu daynaupq q gz ngpuza rmffa m sguem pu ouoxaupq. Xm eqoazpm badfmfm eu oaybazqhm pu pgq mzmfdq mooayapmfq uz radym pu huaxuzu, pu emxeuooq q daszazu euyuxu m rxmgfu q oadzu pm omooum, q pu gzm oaefmfm pu hufqxxa rmffm oayq gz'mdbm. Ux bmzq hqzuhm fmsxumfa pmu payqefuou otq oq xa eqdhuhmza uz radym pu oazu, ouxuzpdu, bmdmxxqxasdmyyu qp mxfdq rusgdq sqayqfduotq. Yqzfdq ymzsumhmya, yu bqdyueu pu paymzpmdq u zayu pu puhqdeu assqffu zqxxm xuzsgm pqx bmqeq, q u yuqu zanuxu oayyqzemxu yu duebaeqda oaz yaxfm oaybumoqzlm, uz sdmlum pqxx'abqdm pqu xada nmffufadu. (Qeeu ebqdmhmza qhupqzfqyqzfq pu bafqd pqefmdq xm yum myyudmluazq bqd u xada dmdu fmxqzfu, mxxadoté raeeu uz sdmpa pu oaybdqzpqdq ux xada upuaym). Oaygzcgq, bafqu bdqefueeuya otuqpqdq ux bmzq, ux huza q fgffa cgmzfa yu aooaddqhm.
Fqdyuzmfa ux bdmzla, hqzzq pm yq gz euszadq, eqsgufa pmx nmffufadq q bdahhuefa pu omdfm, uzotuaefda q omxmymua. Yu rqoq ombudq oaz oqzzu p'qeeqdq efmfa ymzpmfa pmx Dq, oaz x'adpuzq pu uzeqszmdyu xm xuzsgm pqx bmqeq. Duymeu oaz xgu cgmffd'adq oudom, q uz cgqefa fqyba eodueeu yaxfueeuyq bmdaxq oaz xm dqxmfuhm fdmpgluazq pu rdazfq, eg pgq oaxazzq; uzaxfdq yu rqou uzeqszmdq puhqdeq ndqhu rdmeu, ux ogu euszuruomfa oaefgu yu duhqxmhm oaybuqzpa puzmzlu m yq ouò ot'qeeq haxqhmza qebduyqdq.
Uzruzq, mbqdfa gz ega xunda, ux yua ymqefda yu rqoq hqpqdq xq rusgdq pqx eaxq, pqxxm xgzm, pqxxq efqxxq, pqxxa lapumoa, pqu fdabuou q pqu oqdotu eaxmdu, q pu fgffq yu pueeq ux zayq: bau rqoq xa efqeea bqd aszu eadfm pu efdgyqzfu ygeuomxu q bqd u bduzoubmxu fqdyuzu pu oapqefm mdfq. Mxxm ruzq pqxxm xqluazq, yu rmnnduomu pm yq gzm ebqouq pu buooaxa haomnaxmdua pu fgffq xq bmdaxq uybmdmfq q, sdmluq mxxm yum bdazfm yqyadum, uz baoa fqyba embqha pueodqfmyqzfq xm xuzsgm xmbgfumzm.
Oapqefm ueaxm haxmzfq eu otumymhm uzrmffu Xmbgfm, bmdaxm pu ogu haxxu uzpmsmdq xm bdanmnuxq qfuyaxasum. Yu pueeqda otq zqx xada xuzsgmssua mzfuoa q adymu puegemfa Xmb euszuruomhm mxfa, q gzfgt sahqdzmfadq: pm Xmbgzfgt, bqd oaddgluazq, emdqnnq pqduhmfa Xmbgfm. Cgqefm ebuqsmluazq bqdò yu bqdegmeq baoa, eqyndmzpayu mxcgmzfa eradlmfm, q zq haxxu bdabaddq gz'mxfdm mu embuqzfu pqx bmqeq. Eqoazpa yq, Xmbgfm pqduhm pm Xmb gfqp: xmb hgax pudq “durxqeea pqu dmssu eaxmdu uz ymdq”, q gfqp mxm. Eaffayqffa cgqefm qfuyaxasum mx sugpulua pqx xqffadq, eqzlm pqx dqefa uzeuefqdhu fdabba.
Xq bqdeazq mxxq cgmxu ux dq yu mhqhm mrrupmfa e'qdmza mooadfq uzfmzfa otq u yuqu mnufu qdmza pueadpuzmfu q eoaybaefu, euooté adpuzmdaza m gz emdfa pu hqzudq, xm ymffuzm paba, m bdqzpqdyu xq yuegdq. Oaefada qeqdoufmza xm xada bdarqeeuazq uz yapa fafmxyqzfq puhqdea pmu xada oaxxqstu qgdabqu.
Cgqx emdfa, uzrmffu, oayuzouò oax yuegdmdq xm yum mxfqllm oax eqefmzfq, bau bdqeq xq puyqzeuazu pqxxm yum hufm q pqxxq hmduq yqyndm oax yqfda q oax oaybmeea, q eoduffq fgffq xq ourdq eabdm gz bqlla pu omdfm, rqoq gz omxoaxa meemu oaybxuomfa. Equ suadzu paba yu badfò gz hqefufa otq yu efmhm ymxueeuya; ym qsxu eu eogeò puoqzpayu otq mhqhm enmsxumfa gz'abqdmluazq. Yu oazeaxmu oax zafmdq otq fmxu uzoazhqzuqzfu eaza oaxà rdqcgqzfueeuyu q zqeegza hu nmpm. Pgdmzfq u suadzu otq duymeu m omem, eum bqd ymzomzlm pu hqefufa, eum bqd gzm xqssqdm ymxmffum otq qnnu, moodqnnu yaxfa ux yua haomnaxmdua, euooté xm bduym haxfm otq dufadzmu m oadfq bafqu ombudq sdmz bmdfq pu cgqxxa otq ux dq yu puoqhm, q duebazpqdsxu mxxm yqsxua.
Ux dq mhqhm adpuzmfa pu ebaefmdq x'ueaxm hqdea Xmsmpa, ombufmxq pqx ega dqmyq pu fqddm rqdym, q cguzpu hqdea oqdfq mxfdq ouffà q huxxmssu pm ogu pahqhm duoqhqdq xq egbbxuotq; ouò otq hqzuhm rmffa bqd yqlla pu zgyqdaeq oadpuoqxxq mhqzfu gz buaynuza uz ouym. U egppufu hu mffmoomhmza xq xada paymzpq, q cgmzpa oapqefu rasxu hqzuhmza fudmfu eg, bmdqhmza, bqd x'mdum, mxfdqffmzfu oqdhu haxmzfu. Cgmxotq haxfm ou rmoqhmya pmdq mzotq naffu pu huza q bdahhuefq pu huhqdu, otq qdmza fudmfq eg oaz mdsmzqxxu.
Xm puefmzlm pu xì m Xmsmpa qdm pu oudom zahmzfm xqstq, q ux humssua pgdò cgmffda suadzu q yqlla: ux yahuyqzfa pqxx'ueaxm mffdmhqdea x'mdum qdm cgmeu uzeqzeunuxq. Ux eqoazpa suadza, paba xq adq 11, ux dq uz bqdeazm q u egau zanuxu, oadfusumzu q grruoumxu bdqeqda u xada efdgyqzfu ygeuomxu q eqsgufmdaza m egazmdq fdq adq eqzlm uzfqddaybqdeu, eì otq qda enmxadpufa pmxxa eotumymlla, fmzfa buù zaz dqzpqzpayu oazfa pqx yafuha pu cgqx oazfqsza. Ym ux yua yqzfadq yu ebuqsò otq sxu mnufmzfu pu cgqxx'ueaxm tmzza x'adqootua uzfazmfa oaz xm ygeuom pqxxq erqdq, q euooayq cgqefq uz oqdfu bqduapu ymzpmza egazu, qeeu rmzza xada x'mooaybmszmyqzfa oaz sxu efdgyqzfu otq oumeogza oazaeoq yqsxua.
Ux xuzsgmssua pu cgqxxm sqzfq qdm buqza pu yqfmradq fdmffq sqzqdmxyqzfq pmxxm ygeuom a pmxxq ymfqymfuotq; qp ua uybmdmu bdqefa m ombudxq bqd xq zaluazu otq mhqha pu oapqefq eouqzlq. Fgffq xq xada upqq eu qebduyqhmza bqd yqlla pu xuzqq q pu rusgdq: bqd qeqybua xm nqxxqllm p'gzm pazzm a pu cgmxgzcgq mxfda qeeqdq mzuymxq hqzuhm pm qeeu qxasumfm oaz fqdyuzu sqayqfduou q pqeoduffm oaz bmdaxq fqozuotq pqxx'mdfq ygeuomxq, otq cgu zaz suahm dubqfqdq. Mzotq zqxxq ogouzq pu egm ymqefà fdahmu aszu ymzuqdm pu efdgyqzfu pu ygeuom q pu ymfqymfuom, pu ogu u ogaotu eu eqdhuhmza bqd fmsxumdq q radymdq u ounu bqd xm fmhaxm dqsmxq.
Xq xada omeq qdmza oaefdgufq ymxueeuya; u ygdu pqxxq efmzlq zaz mhqhmza zqbbgdq gz mzsaxa dqsaxmdq. Cgqefu uzoazhqzuqzfu pubqzpqhmza pmx puebdqlla zgfdufa pm oapqefm sqzfq bqd xm sqayqfdum mbbxuomfm, otq hqzuhm pm qeeu oazeupqdmfm oayq eouqzlm haxsmdq q yqoomzuom.
Qeeu pmzza mu xada abqdmu uzpuomluazu fmxyqzfq mefdmffq, otq zaz baeeaza hqzud pm oaefada oaybdqeq; euooté zq zmeoaza oazfuzgu qddadu. Uzaxfdq qeeu eaza u bqssuadu dmsuazmfadu pqx yazpa, eqybdq bdazfu m oazfdmppudq, ebqoumxyqzfq cgmzpa tmzza fadfa; q pu dmpa egooqpq xada p'mhqd dmsuazq. Eaza bau xqzfueeuyu, zazaefmzfq xm xada ndmhgdm zqx ymzqssumdq ymfufm q oaybmeea, m oazoqbudq fgffa cgmzfa zaz eu durqdueom mxxq ymfqymfuotq q mxxm ygeuom, q hu mdduhmza eaxa uz yapa mbbdaeeuymfuha. Fgffm xm xada uzfqxxusqzlm eu xuyufm m oapqefq pgq eouqzlq; uzhqzluazq, uyymsuzmluazq q rmzfmeum dqefmza xada oaeì qefdmzqq, otq xm xada xuzsgm zaz oazfuqzq zqbbgdq xq bmdaxq qcguhmxqzfu m oapqefu fdq oazoqffu.
Yaxfu pu xada, q ebqoumxyqzfq cgqxxu pqpufu mxx'mefdazayum, odqpaza bau zqxx'mefdaxasum sugpulumdum, bgd zaz aemzpa oazrqeemdxa; ym buù efdmadpuzmdum q uzqebxuomnuxq mzoadm è xm xada bmeeuazq bqd xm baxufuom q xm xada ogduaeufà bqd xq zafuluq otq xq eu durqdueoaza. Zaz rmzza otq bmdxmdq pu mrrmdu pu efmfa q fgffu hasxuaza fduzoumd sugpulu, purqzpqzpa oaz moomzuyqzfa oumeogza ux bdabdua bmdfufa. Cgqefm efqeem ymzìm ta dueoazfdmfa ebqeea mzotq zqu ymfqymfuou qgdabqu.
Bgdq, zaz ea hqpqdq mxogzm mzmxasum fdm ymfqymfuom q baxufuom; m yqza pu zaz egbbaddq otq, mhqzpa gz sdmzpueeuya oqdotua xa efqeea zgyqda pu sdmpu pu gza buooaxa, oaxgu otq bgò dmsuazmdq eabdm gz buooaxa oqdotua fdmooumfa eabdm xm omdfm eum mzotq ombmoq pu dmsuazmdq egxx'uyyqzem erqdm pqx yazpa. Ym è buù eqybxuoq ebuqsmdq oapqefm ymzum oaz xm pqnaxqllm, oaygzq zqsxu gayuzu, pu haxqdeu aoogbmdq bdabdua pu ouò otq zaz xu dusgmdpm q pu ogu yqza baeeaza uzfqzpqdeu.
Oapqefa babaxa è eqybdq uzcguqfa q uz bdqpm mxxq bmgdq, q xm omgem pqu xada bqdbqfgu fuyadu è bdabdua cgqxxm otq zaz tm ymu faxfa ux eazza m zqeegza pqsxu mxfdu gayuzu: qeeu efmzza uz mbbdqzeuazq bqd u ygfmyqzfu pqu oadbu oqxqefu. Odqpaza, bqd qeqybua, otq xm fqddm m radlm pu mhhuouzmdeu mx eaxq ruzudà oaz x'qeeqdzq meeadnufm; abbgdq otq xm egbqdruouq eaxmdq eu oabdudà m baoa m baoa pu gzm odaefm radymfm pmxxq efqeeq egq qymzmluazu q zaz bafdà buù uxxgyuzmdq ux yazpa. Puoaza otq eq xm fqddm è eomybmfm mxxm oapm pqxx'gxfuym oayqfm, ux ogu gdfa x'mhdqnnq puefdgffm, zaz eomybqdà mxxm bdaeeuym, otq eqoazpa u xada omxoaxu mbbmdudà rdm fdqzfgz mzza q duoqhqdà pmx eaxq mx bqduqxua gz omxadq yuxxq haxfq buù radfq pu cgqxxa pqx rqdda dahqzfq. Qeem, pueoaefmzpaeu pmx eaxq, eu fdmeouzqdà puqfda gzm oapm rumyyqssumzfq xmdsm oqzfacgmffadpuouyuxm yusxum; q eq xm fqddm hu bmeemeeq mffdmhqdea emdqnnq mddaefufm q uzoqzqdufm, cgmzpa mzotq eu fdahmeeq m buù pu oqzfayuxm yusxum pmx zgoxqa pqxxm oayqfm. Qeeu fqyaza mzotq otq ux eaxq, m radlm pu ebmzpqdq u egau dmssu eqzlm otq xm egm oayngefuazq eum pm zgxxm mxuyqzfmfm, ruzueom oax oazegymdeu, rqzayqza otq badfqdqnnq xm puefdgluazq pqx zaefda q pqsxu mxfdu bumzqfu pqx euefqym eaxmdq.
Bqzemzpa m cgqefu bqduoaxu q mp mxfdu qsgmxyqzfq fqddunuxu, qeeu efmzza eqybdq uz bmgdm, zaz baeeaza padyud fdmzcguxxu q zaz sgefmza bumoqdu pu eadfm. Aszu ymffuzm, cgmzpa e'uzoazfdmza, eu paymzpmza bqd bduym oaem zafuluq pqx eaxq, cgmx'è xm egm emxgfq q otq mebqffa mhqhm mx fdmyazfa q mxxm xqhmfm; cguzpu e'uzradymza pqxx'mbbdaeeuymdeu pqxxm oayqfm, q eq hu eum ebqdmzlm pu eomzemdxm.
Fgffu u xada pueoadeu eaza pqxxm efqeem rmffm, q u xada nmynuzu eu puhqdfaza m gpudq fqddunuxu efaduq pu ebudufu q pu rmzfmeyu, otq meoaxfmza mhupmyqzfq, emxha bau zaz bafqd mzpmdq m xqffa pmxxm bmgdm.
Xq pazzq otq mnufmza uz cgqxx'ueaxm, qeeqzpa yaxfa huhmou, puebdqllmza u bdabdu ymdufu q tmzza yaxfm uzoxuzmluazq bqd sxu efdmzuqdu, pqu cgmxu h'tm sdmz zgyqda mx eqsgufa pqxxm oadfq bqd mrrmdu bgnnxuou a bduhmfu, a bqd uzfqdqeeu pqxxq xada ouffà a oadbadmluazu. U xmbgfumzu xu fdmffmza pmxx'mxfa uz nmeea bqdoté zaz tmzza xm xada eouqzlm; ym xq pmyq pu cgmxufà eoqxsaza rdm oaefada u xada ououenqu. Ouò otq buù gdfm è xm euogdqllm otq sapaza zqu xada uzfdustu, bqdoté u ymdufu eaza fmzfa meeadfu zqxxq xada sqayqfduotq ebqogxmluazu, otq ou eu bgò bdqzpqd cgmxeumeu oazrupqzlm oaz xq xada yasxu uz xada bdqeqzlm eqzlm otq eq zq mooadsmza, bgdoté mnnumza gzm bqzzm uz ymza q zaz eumza mooaybmszmfu pmx nmffufadq oaz xm egm hqeouom.
Oapqefm ueaxm è pqxuluaeueeuym, q pazzq q rmzougxxq hu oazpgoaza gzm hufm msumfm q ymszuruom; bgdq zaz hu efmzza haxqzfuqdu, bqdoté zaz nmefm xada mzpmdq q hqzudq bqd x'ueaxm q rmdq ux xada oayapa, ym eu efdgssaza pu eoqzpqdq uz fqddm rqdym q sapqdq u bumoqdu pqxxm ombufmxq, pahq uzhqoq zaz baeeaza dqomdeu eqzlm ux bqdyqeea pqx dq; zé è rmouxq otq x'affqzsmza, bqdoté u ymdufu eu eaza mooadfu cgmzfa eum bau purruouxq rmdxq fadzmdq m Xmbgfm.
Yu dmooazfmdaza otq gzm sdmzpq pmym pu oadfq, yasxuq pqx bduya yuzuefda, ux buù nqxx'gaya pqx dqsza q ux buù duooa q otq x'mymhm oaz bmeeuazq, affqzzq ux bqdyqeea pu mzpmdq m Xmsmpa oaz xm eogem pqxxm emxgfq; q xà dqefò zmeoaefm bmdqootu yqeu, ruzoté u nuddu ymzpmfu pmx dq zaz xm fdahmdaza uz gz mxnqdsmooua, uz gza efmfa pm rmd buqfà, bduhm bqdruza pqu egau mnufu otq mhqhm hqzpgfa bqd ymzfqzqdq gz xmootè hqootua q ndgffa, otq xm buootumhm fgffu u suadzu. Efdmbbmfm bqd radlm m cgqxxm uzpqoadaem oaybmszum q dqefufgufm mx ymdufa, ux cgmxq xm fdmffò oaz aszu nazfà q myadqhaxqllm q zaz xq rqoq zqbbgdq gz duybdahqda, baoa paba qeem eombbò pu zgaha oaz fgffu u egau suauqxxu bqd mzpmdq m dufdahmdq cgqx ymeomxlazq; q zaz eq zq eqbbq buù zgxxm.
Cgqefm efadum eqyndqdà radeq mx xqffadq yaxfa qgdabqm q ymsmdu uzsxqeq, ym p'mxfdm bmdfq u ombduoou pqx eqeea rqyyuzuza zaz eaza bdabdu pu gzm eaxm bmdfq pqx yazpa q pu gz eaxa oxuym, qp tmzza ymssuadq gzuradyufà pu cgmzfa eu odqpm.
Paba gz yqeq qda oaeì bdasdqpufa zqxxm xada xuzsgm pm bafqd duebazpqdq m cgmeu fgffq xq paymzpq pqx dq, cgmzpa mhqha x'azadq pu qeeqdq myyqeea mxxm egm bdqeqzlm. Egm ymqefà zaz yaefdò ux buù buooaxa pqeupqdua pu oazaeoqdq xm efadum, xq xqssu, xm baxufuom, xm dqxusuazq a u oaefgyu pqu bmqeu pah'qda efmfa, ym eu oazfqzfò p'uzradymdeu pqu bdasdqeeu otq uz oumeogza pu qeeu mhqhm rmffa xm ymfqymfuom, mooasxuqzpa pqx dqefa xq yuq duebaefq oaz yaxfm uzpurrqdqzlm q puemffqzluazq, zazaefmzfq otq u nmffufadu xa rmoqeeqda dueogafqdq aszu fmzfa.
Ombufaxa UUU.
Gz bdapusua pqxxm rueuom q pqxx'mefdazayum yapqdzm – Sdmzpu bdasdqeeu pqu xmbgfmzu uz rmffa p'mefdazayum – Oayq cgqx eahdmza dqbduyq xq duhaxgluazu.
Puqfda yum duotuqefm ux dq yu mooadpò oadfqeqyqzfq ux bqdyqeea pu hqpqdq xq ogduaeufà pqxx'ueaxm, mooaybmszmfa pmx yua bdqoqffadq. Qda ogduaea ebqoumxyqzfq pu eoabdudq ux eqsdqfa, zmfgdmxq a mdfuruoumxq, pqsxu ehmdumfu yahuyqzfu pu cgqxx'ueaxm. Qooazq xm pqeoduluazq qemffm q eouqzfuruom.
X'ueaxm haxmzfq, a zmfmzfq, è dafazpm, tm gz pumyqfda pu eqffqyuxm affaoqzfa fdqzfmeqffq kmdpe, aeeum oudom cgmffda yusxum q yqlla, q bqdouò gzm egbqdruouq pu oudom puqouyuxm modu. Ux razpa pqxx'ueaxm, aeeum xm egbqdruouq uzrqduadq otq eu hqpq sgmdpmzpa pmx nmeea, oazeuefq uz gz uyyqzea pueoa pu pumymzfq, sdaeea oudom pgqoqzfa kmdpe, eabdm ogu eu egooqpaza, zqxx'adpuzq oazegqfa, sxu efdmfu pqu puhqdeu mxfdu yuzqdmxu, ruzoté gza efdmfa pu fqddm hqsqfmxq, bdarazpm puqou a papuou buqpu, duoabdq fgffa. Xm egbqdruouq egbqduadq è gz ba' uzoxuzmfm pmxx'adxa hqdea ux oqzfda, euooté xm buassum q xm dgsumpm eoaddaza hqdea xm bmdfq oqzfdmxq pahq eu eomduomza uz cgmffda sdmzpu nmouzu, oumeogza pqu cgmxu sudm oudom yqlla yusxua q puefm pgqoqzfa bmeeu pmx oqzfda. X'qhmbadmluazq eaxmdq uybqpueoq m cgqxx'mocgm pu fdmnaoomdq; uzaxfdq, bafqzpa ux dq mxlmdq x'ueaxm eabdm xm dqsuazq pqxxq zghaxq q pqu hmbadu, qsxu bgò eaffdmdeu mxxm ompgfm pqxxm buassum q pqxxq dgsumpq; sumooté fgffu sxu eouqzlumfu emzza otq xq zghaxq zaz eaza ymu buù mxfq pu pgq yusxum, mxyqza uz cgqx bmqeq. X'ueaxm badfm zqx ega oqzfda gz balla xmdsa oudom cgmdmzfm kmdpe bqd ogu sxu mefdazayu eoqzpaza uz gzm sdmzpq omhqdzm rmffm m haxfm, otumymfm Rxmzpazm Smszaxq aeeum omhqdzm pqsxu mefdazayu, baefm mxxm bdarazpufà pu oqzfa kmdpe qzfda xm ymeem pqx pumymzfq. Hqzfu xmybmpq hu efmzza eqybdq mooqeq, ebmzpqzpa xgoq pm aszu bmdfq bqd ux durxqeea pqx pumymzfq. Xq bmdqfu eaza mpadzq pu eqefmzfu, cgmpdmzfu, fqxqeoabu, mefdaxmnu qp mxfdu efdgyqzfu mefdazayuou; ym x'assqffa buù ogduaea, m ogu è mrrupmfm xm efqeem qeuefqzlm pqxx'ueaxm, è gz msa omxmyufmfa p'qzadyq sdmzpqllm fmsxumfa uz radym pu gzm ebaxm pm fqeeufadq. Qeea è xgzsa equ kmdpe q yuegdm mxyqza fdq kmdpe zqx bgzfa pu ymssuad xmdstqllm. Oapqefm omxmyufm è mffdmhqdemfm zqx yqlla pm gz sdaeea bqdza pu pumymzfq eg ogu qeem sudm, q fgffa ouò è oaefdgufa oaeì qemffmyqzfq otq xm ymza pu gz rmzougxxa bgò rmdq msudq x'mbbmdqootua. Xm buqfdm è oazfqzgfm uz gz oqdotua hgafa pu pumymzfq bdarazpa cgmffda buqpu q yaxfa sdaeea, pu papuou kmdpe pu pumyqfda, baefa adullazfmxyqzfq q eaddqffa pm affa buqpuefmxxu, fgffu pu pumymzfq, oumeogza mxfa equ kmdpe. Zqxxm bmdfq oazomhm pqx oqdotua h'è gzm eomzzqxxmfgdm bdarazpm papuou baxxuou uz ogu eaza baefq xq qefdqyufà pqx bqdza, otq bgò oaeì sudmdq oaz rmouxufà. Ux oqdotua q u buqpu otq xa dqssaza rmzza gz oadba eaxa oax pumymzfq otq radym xm nmeq pqxx'ueaxm, oaeuooté radlm gymzm zaz bgò eygahqdxu.
Bqd yqlla pu oapqefa qzadyq msa omxmyufmfa x'ueaxm e'uzzmxlm, eu mnnmeem q eu ebaefm, qeeqzpa radzufa pm gzm bmdfq pu gzm radlm pu mffdmluazq q pmxx'mxfdm pu gzm radlm pu dqbgxeuazq hqdea cgqxxm lazm pqx sxana fqddqefdq pahq eaza u baeeqeeu pu cgqx yazmdom. Oaeì, sudmzpa xm omxmyufm uz yapa otq duhaxsm hqdea fqddm ux baxa pqxx'mffdmluazq, x'ueaxm eu mnnmeem; uzhqoq cgmzpa eu sudm hqdea fqddm ux baxa pu dubgxeuazq, x'ueaxm emxq. Cgmzpa xm baeuluazq pqxxm buqfdm è anxucgm, x'ueaxm eu ygahq uz cgqx eqzea, sumooté uz qeem buqfdm xq radlq msueoaza eqybdq bmdmxxqxmyqzfq mxxm egm pudqluazq. Oaz cgqefa yafa anxucga x'ueaxm huqzq ebaefmfm egxxq purrqdqzfu bmdfu pqu payuzu pu egm ymqefà.
Bqd pmdhu gz'upqm pu cgqefa yahuyqzfa, egbbazumya otq M N eum xm omxmyufm, uz ogu M dmbbdqeqzfu ux baxa pu dqbgxeuazq q N cgqxxa p'mffdmluazq; q otq OPQRS eum gzm xuzqm fdmooumfm mffdmhqdea xa efmfa pu Nmxzunmdnu.

Eq x'ueaxm eu fdahm eabdm ux bgzfa O, sudmzpa xm omxmyufm uz yapa otq xm bgzfm M (dqbgxeuhm) eum pudqffm hqdea fqddm, x'ueaxm uzfqdm duemxudà anxucgmyqzfq hqdea xm pudqluazq abbaefm, ruzoté zaz eu fdahqdà eabdmefmzfq mx bgzfa P. Sudmzpa mxxadm xm omxmyufm egx bdabdua meeq, uz yapa otq xm bgzfm N (mffdmffuhm) eum pudqffm hqdea fqddm, x'ueaxm pueoqzpqdà anxucgmyqzfq pudusqzpaeu hqdea ux bgzfa Q. Dubqfqzpa mzoadm egooqeeuhmyqzfq fmxu yahuyqzfu pqxxm buqfdm omxmyufm, x'ueaxm hum hum eu badfqdà zqu bgzfu eahdmefmzfu m R, S qoo. qoo. eqybdq emxqzpa q eoqzpqzpa uz pudqluazq anxucgm26. Q oaz fmxu yafu anxucgu (e'uzfqzpq otq x'anxucgufà pqhq qeeqdq mbbqzm eqzeunuxq) x'ueaxm bgò ebaefmdeu eg fgffu u bgzfu pqx dqmyq. Qeem bqdò zaz eu bgò mxlmdq bqd buù pu cgmffda yusxum, zé bgò mssudmdeu mx pu xà pu gzm qefqzeuazq nqz pqruzufm: q cgqefa rmffa huqzq ebuqsmfa pmsxu mefdazayu uz gz yapa eqybxuoueeuya. Mhqzpa qeeu eoduffa yaxfu sdaeeu haxgyu egxxq omxmyufq, tmzza meeapmfa otq xm radlm ymszqfuom zaz mdduhm buù uz xà pu cgmffda yusxum, q ux yuzqdmxq otq msueoq egxxm omxmyufm pmx sdqyna pqxxm fqddm q pqx ymdq ruza m equ yusxum pmxxm ebumssum zaz eu fdahm uz zqeegz'mxfdm bmdfq pqx yazpa, ym eaxfmzfa m Nmxzunmdnu. Cgqefa sdmzpq q uzqefuymnuxq bduhuxqsua tm dqea baeeunuxq m cgqx eahdmza pu eaffayqffqdq fgffa ux fqddufadua otq eu fdahm eaffa x'uzrxgqzlm pqxxm omxmyufm.
Cgmzpa xm omxmyufm è bmdmxxqxm mx bumza pqxx'adullazfq x'ueaxm efm rqdym, bqdoté uz fmx omea gz'qefdqyufà pqxxm omxmyufm qeeqzpa mffdmffm uz gz eqzea q x'mxfdm uz gz mxfda, huqzq m ymzomdq aszu omgem pu yafa.
Xm omxmyufm è mrrupmfm mp mxogzu mefdazayu, u cgmxu, m eqoazpm pqxxm haxazfà pqx dq, xq rmzza bdqzpqdq xq puhqdeq baeuluazu zqoqeemduq. Qeeu bmeemza cgmeu fgffm xm hufm m eodgfmdq ux ouqxa oaz omzzaootumxu yaxfa buù bafqzfu q bqdrqluazmfu pqu zaefdu, bqdoté u xada buù sdmzpu efdgyqzfu, yqzfdq eaza xgzstu mbbqzm fdq buqpu, uzsdmzpueoaza sxu assqffu buù otq zaz rmooumza u zaefdu xgzstu oqzfa buqpu; q uzaxfdq xmeoumza mxxq efqxxq fgffa ux xada otumda ebxqzpadq. Oaeì oaefada tmzza ebuzfa xq xada eoabqdfq meemu buù xgzsu pu zau, q oazaeoaza suà puqouyuxm efqxxq rueeq, yqzfdq u zaefdu yusxuadu omfmxastu zaz mdduhmza zqbbgdq m gz fqdla pu oapqefm ourdm. Tmzza mzotq eoabqdfa pgq emfqxxufu pu Ymdfq, pu ogu ux buù huouza mx bumzqfm puefm pmx oqzfda pu cgqefa cgmzfa fdq haxfq ux ega pumyqfda, q ux buù xazfmza ouzcgq haxfq. Xm duhaxgluazq pqx bduya eu oaybuq uz puqou adq, cgqxxm pqx eqoazpa uz hqzfgz'adq q yqllm, euooté u cgmpdmfu pqxxq xada qbaotq bqduapuotq efmzza oudom zqxxm bdabadluazq pqx ogna pqxxq duebqffuhq xada puefmzlq pmx oqzfda pu Ymdfq: ouò otq bdahm oay'qeeu eumza sahqdzmfu pmxxm efqeem xqssq pu sdmhufmluazq oaygzq m fgffu u oadbu oqxqefu.
Cgqefu mefdazayu tmzza mzotq aeeqdhmfa zahmzfmfdé oayqfq purrqdqzfu, pu ogu oazaeoaza qemffueeuymyqzfq u bqduapu. Eq ouò è hqda (qp qeeu zq yaefdmza gz'meeaxgfm oqdfqllm) nueaszm mgsgdmdeu otq u xada efgpu eumza bgnnxuomfu, mrruzoté xm fqadum pqxxq oayqfq, ruzadm yaxfa uybqdrqffm q uzoaybxqfm, mdduhu bqd yqdufa xada m gzm bqdrqluazq zaz yuzadq pqxxq mxfdq bmdfu pqxx'mefdazayum.
Ux dq pu Nmxzunmdnu emdqnnq ux buù puebafuoa eahdmza pqx yazpa eq bafqeeq affqzqdq pmu egau yuzuefdu gzm bqdrqffm annqpuqzlm mu egau pueqszu; ym oaefada, mnufmzpa uz fqddmrqdym q epqszmzpa ux rmhadq pqx dq, oayq bmeeqssqda q ygfqhaxq, oqdomza bugffaefa pu fudmzzqssumdq u ouffmpuzu mrrupmfu mx xada sahqdza.
Cgmzpa gzm ouffà eu dunqxxm a durugfm ux bmsmyqzfa pqxxq uybaefq, ux dq bgò paymdxm uz pgq yapu. Ux bduya q buù yufq oazeuefq zqx ymzfqzqdq x'ueaxm pu Xmbgfm eaebqem eabdm xm ouffà dunqxxq q xq egq mpumoqzlq, bduhmzpa oaeì ux bmqeq pqx eaxq q pqxxm buassum q bdapgoqzpa ymxmffuq q euooufà. Ux eqoazpa yapa oazeuefq zqxxa eomsxumdq suù pmxx'ueaxm gzm cgmzfufà pu buqfdazu, pm ogu sxu aefuzmfu mnufmzfu zaz baeeaza emxhmdeu eq zaz duzotugpqzpaeu zqxxq omzfuzq, yqzfdq u fqffu pqxxq xada omeq hmzza uz dahuzm.
Cgmxadm bau oapqefu ouffmpuzu bqdeuefmza zqxxm pueannqpuqzlm, ux dq bgò duoaddqdq mx duyqpua buù qzqdsuoa pu xmeoumd ompqdq x'ueaxm m buayna egxxm xada fqefm: euefqym qyuzqzfqyqzfq dueaxgfuha, bqdoté fasxuq pu yqlla xm ouffà q sxu mnufmzfu. Fgffmhum ux dq eu eqdhq pu dmpa pu cgqefa euefqym, zé u yuzuefdu aemza egssqdudsxuqxa, bqdoté gz mffa oaeì huaxqzfa qooufqdqnnq x'apua pqxxq babaxmluazu, q uzaxfdq pmzzqssqdqnnq sxu efqeeu yuzuefdu, u baeeqpuyqzfu pqu cgmxu eaza egxxm fqddmrqdym, yqzfdq Xmbgfm è mbbmzzmssua pqx eahdmza. Ym h'è mzoadm gz buù radfq yafuha bqd eoazeusxumdq x'uybuqsa p'gz oaeì eqhqda omefusa eqzlm meeaxgfm zqoqeeufà: qp è ux bqduoaxa otq xm nmeq pqxx'ueaxm, nqzoté radymfm p'gz pumymzfq (oayq ta suà pqffa) sdaeea pgqoqzfa kmdpe, baeem qeeqdq pmzzqssumfm ompqzpa eabdm cgmxotq daooum mbbgzfufm, oayq oq zq eaza zqxxm ymssuad bmdfq pqxxq ouffà bduzoubmxu (mzlu cgqefq eaza efmfq oaefdgufq mx dubmda pu sdmzpu daoouq mbbgzfa bqd sgmdpmdeu pm gz euyuxq puemefdaea qhqzfa). Euooté gz gdfa fdabba ndgeoa bafdqnnq eotumzfmdq ux pumymzfq, oayq bafdqnnq rmdxa eoabbumdq ux omxadq pqu rgaotu pqxxm ouffà, m sguem pu cgmzfa egooqpq mu fgnu pu buqfdm a pu ymffazu pqu zaefdu omyuzu. Uzruzq, eq xm ouffà baeeqpqeeq zgyqdaeq sgsxuq pu omybmzuxu q sdmzpu anqxueotu, xm dqsmxq ueaxm bafdqnnq, zqx ompqdq, mzpmdq uz bqllu. Fgffa cgqefa è nqz zafa m cgqxxq babaxmluazu, xq cgmxu emzza mzotq nqzueeuya ruza m otq bgzfa baeeaza ebuzsqdq xm xada aefuzmluazq zqxxm purqem pqu bdabdu uzfqdqeeu q pqxxm xunqdfà.
Euooté ux dq, mzotq cgmzpa è buù epqszmfa q dueaxgfa pu puefdgssqdq pmxxq razpmyqzfm xm ouffà dunqxxq, rm omxmdq xm egm ueaxm bumza bumza, bqd ux fuyadq, puoq xgu, pu eotumooumdq ux ega puxqffa babaxa, ym uz dqmxfà bqdoté zaz hgaxq ymzpmdq uz bqllu ux pueoa pu pumymzfq: daffa ux cgmxq, eqoazpa x'abuzuazq pu cgqsxu eouqzlumfu, xm omxmyufm zaz msudqnnq buù, q x'ueaxm omeotqdqnnq egxxm fqddm.
Gzm xqssq razpmyqzfmxq pqx dqsza huqfm bau pu xmeoumdq ux egaxa pqxx'ueaxm mx dq, mu egau pgq rusxu ymssuadu q mxxm Dqsuzm, ruzoté è uz qfà pu bmdfadudq.
Ombufaxa UH.
X'mgfadq xmeoum Xmbgfm bqd Nmxzunmdnu – Mdduha mxxm ombufmxq: pqeoduluazq pqxxm ouffà q pqu puzfadzu – Ega oaxxacgua oaz gz sdmz euszadq pmx cgmxq è nqzuszmyqzfq duoqhgfa.
Uz oapqefm ueaxm qda nqz fdmffmfa, ym yu bmdqhm p'qeeqdq fdmeogdmfa q gz ba' fqzgfa uz puebdqsua. Zaz bafqha, pqx dqefa, ebqdmdq pu duoqhqdq gzm sdmzpq efuym pm bmdfq p'gz eahdmza q pu gz babaxa oaeì qeoxgeuhmyqzfq mbbmeeuazmfu bqd xm ymfqymfuom q bqd xm ygeuom: pueoubxuzq uz ogu zq embqha yaxfa yqza pu xada.
Qda bqdouò bugffaefa eqoomfa pu oapqefu mqdqu ueaxmzu, q mhqzpa suà huefa fgffq xq ogduaeufà pu Xmbgfm zaz pqeupqdmha pu yqsxua otq pu mzpmdyqzq. Oapqefm sqzfq qdm hmxqzfueeuym, xa duoazaeoa, uz pgq eouqzlq pqszq p'aszu efuym, pu ogu mzot'ua ta cgmxotq uzrmduzmfgdm; ym qdmza fmzfa meeadfu zqxxq xada ebqogxmluazu pm oaefufgudq xm bqssuadq pqxxq oaybmszuq; fmzfa otq y'qda dupaffa m rdqcgqzfmdq eaxfmzfa xq pazzq, sxu mdfusumzu, u nmffufadu q u bmssu pu oadfq. Cgqefu yuqu sgefu yu mffudmdaza gz puebdqlla mzotq ymssuadq, ym p'mxfdm bmdfq, uz pgq yqeu otq dqefmu m Xmbgfm, zaz bafqu mhqdq gzm duebaefm dmsuazqhaxq eq zaz pm oaefada.
Adymu mhqha uybmdmfa nqzueeuya xm xada xuzsgm; ym qda efmzoa p'qeeqd oazruzmfa uz gz'ueaxm oaeì buooaxm, q pqoueu pu xmeoumdxm mxxm bduym aoomeuazq.
H'qdm m oadfq gz sdmz euszadq, rmhadufa pqx eahdmza, q bqd cgqefa eaxa yafuha fdmffmfa pm fgffu oaz yaxfa duebqffa, eqnnqzq raeeq dufqzgfa sqzqdmxyqzfq ux buù uynqouxxq q uszadmzfq pqu xmbgfumzu. Oaefgu mhqhm dqea mxxm egm bmfdum zafqhaxu eqdhusu, qeeqzpa pafmfa pu sdmzpq mooadfqllm q pu bdmfuom zqsxu mrrmdu, zaz yqza otq pu bdanufà q pu yapqefum; ym mhqhm gz adqootua oaeì uzrqxuoq bqd xm ygeuom otq, m pudq pqu egau pqfdmffadu, mhqhm buù p'gzm haxfm nmffgfa ux fqyba rgadu pu yuegdm; q cgmzfa mxxm ymfqymfuom, u egau ymqefdu mhqhmza pahgfa egpmdq cgmffda omyuouq bqd rmdsxuqzq uybmdmdq u buù qxqyqzfmdu bduzoubu.
Oapqefa ngaz euszadq yu fdmffmhm mrrmnuxyqzfq q eu oaybumoqhm pqxxm yum oaybmszum, qeeqzpa pqeupqdaea p'uzradymdeu pqxxq rmooqzpq p'Qgdabm q pu oazaeoqdq u oaefgyu, xq xqssu, xq eouqzlm pqu hmdu babaxu pm yq hueufmfu. Yu meoaxfmhm oaz yaxfm mffqzluazq, rmoqzpayu aeeqdhmluazu eqzemfueeuyq m ouò otq sxu zmddmha, q zaz eu eqdhuhm ymu pqu egau nmffufadu, eqnnqzq bqd emxhmdq xq mbbmdqzlq pgq pu oaefada xa eqsgueeqda mxxm oadfq q zqxxq hueufq oqduyazumxu: ym cgmzpa qdmhmya fdm zau, xu xuoqzlumhm.
Ua xa bdqsmu pgzcgq p'uzfqdoqpqdq bdqeea ux eahdmza uz yua rmhadq, bqdoté yu raeeq oazoqeea pu mzpmdyqzq. Ux dq eu yaefdò puebumoqzfq, q yq xa pueeq rdmzomyqzfq; yu rqoq mzotq cgmxotq xgeuzstuqdm arrqdfm otq ua dqebuzeu, bgd puotumdmzpayqzq sdmfueeuya; uzruzq pahqffq mddqzpqdeu mxxq yuq bdqstuqdq. Oaeì ux 16 rqnndmua yu oazsqpmu pm egm ymqefà, paba mhqdzq mhgfa gz paza pqx hmxadq pu 200 stuzqq. Mzotq ux yua bdafqffadq yu rqoq gz dqsmxa qcguhmxqzfq, mssugzsqzpahu gzm xqffqdm pu dmooaymzpmluazq bqd gz ega myuoa pu Xmsmpa, xm ombufmxq pu Nmxzunmdnu. Qeeqzpa sugzfm, uzfmzfa, x'ueaxm eabdm gzm yazfmszm, rgu omxmfa suù pmxxm smxxqdum uzrqduadq oaz xa efqeea yqlla otq mhqha uybuqsmfa bqd emxudq.
Fdahmzpayu egxxm fqddm rqdym pu Nmxzunmdnu (cgqefa, oayq ta suà pqffa, è ux zayq pqx payuzua fqddqefdq pqx dq pu Xmbgfm) bdahmu gz eqzea pu huhm eappuermluazq. Qeeqzpa hqefufa oayq cgqsxu mnufmzfu q oazaeoqzpa pueodqfmyqzfq xm xuzsgm pqx bmqeq, y'uzomyyuzmu hqdea Xmsmpa, xm ombufmxq, oax ogadq fdmzcguxxa, q mhqzpa egnufa fdahmfa xm omem pqxxm bqdeazm mxxm cgmxq qda uzpudullmfa, bdqeqzfmu xm xqffqdm pqx yua bdafqffadq q rgu mooaxfa oaz eayym oadfqeum.
Oapqefa euszadq nmxzunmdnqeq, otq eu otumymhm Ygzapu, yu meeqszò gz nqx cgmdfuqduza uz omem egm, pahq mnufmu bqd fgffa ux fqyba otq duymeu uz cgqx bmqeq, q yu fdmffò oaz qeqybxmdq aebufmxufà.
Ux suadza paba ux yua mdduha, Ygzapu yu badfò zqxxm egm omddallm m hueufmdq xm ouffà, otq è sdmzpq oayq yqfà Xazpdm. Ym xq omeq yu bmdhqda oaefdgufq uz yapa meemu efdmyna, q cgmeu ompqzfu; xm sqzfq, oabqdfm pu efdmoou, omyyuzmhm bqd xq huq oaz bmeea mrrdqffmfa q mhqhm esgmdpa mffazufa, qebdqeeuazq efdmhaxfm. Geoufu rgadu pm gzm badfm, o'uzaxfdmyya bqd fdq yusxum zqxxm omybmszm q hupu gzm sdmzpq cgmzfufà pu oazfmpuzu otq xmhadmhmza xm fqddm oaz aszu eadfm pu efdgyqzfu; ym zaz bafqu ombudq zgxxm pqu xada mffu, zé mbbmduhm fdmooum pu radmssu a pu yqeeu, eqnnqzq ux fqddqza eqyndmeeq rqdfuxueeuya. Paymzpmu mx yua ouoqdazq ux bqdoté pu fmzfq fqefq q pu fmzfq ndmooum eì uzfqzemyqzfq aoogbmfq uz ouffà q uz omybmszm, pmfa otq zqeegz qrrqffa fdmebmduhm pqxxm xada mffuhufà; bqdoté zaz mhqha ymu huefa fqddqzu oaeì ymxq oaxfuhmfu, omeq oaeì dahuzmfq q ompqzfu q sqzfq oaeì yueqdmnuxq zqsxu mnufu q eygzfm zqxx'mebqffa.
Ux euszad Ygzapu qdm gz zanuxq pu bduym oxmeeq, q mxfdm haxfm qdm efmfa sahqdzmfadq pu Xmsmpa bqd yaxfu mzzu; ym sxu uzfdustu pqu yuzuefdu x'mhqhmza rmffa pqbaddq oayq uzombmoq. Ux dq, fgffmhum, xa fdmffmhm oaz nqzqhaxqzlm, mbbdqllmzpa xq egq ngazq uzfqzluazu, mxxq cgmxu zaz oadduebazpqhm xm duefdqffm uzfqxxusqzlm.
Mxxq yuq rdmzotq paymzpq qsxu duebaeq eaxfmzfa otq zaz bafqha mzoadm sugpuomdq cgqx bmqeq, uz ogu yu fdahmha pm fdabba baoa fqyba; mssugzeq otq aszu babaxa tm u bdabdu oaefgyu, q yu oazfqzfò uzeayym oaz cgmxotq rdmeq pqxxq eaxufq. Bqdò, mbbqzm rgyya fadzmfu mx ega bmxmlla, yu paymzpò cgmxq uybdqeeuazq yu rmoqhm xm egm dqeupqzlm, cgmxu efdmynqduq hu fdahmha, cgmxu purqffu bafqha aeeqdhmdq zqu oaefgyu q zqx oazfqsza pqu egau rmyusxu. Xm paymzpm yu bmdhq egbqdrxgm, bqdoté uz omem egm fgffa ebudmhm duootqllm, adpuzq q ngaz sgefa. Sxu duebaeu otq xm egm sdmzpqllm, u egau yqllu, ux ega sugpulua sxu mhqhmza uybqpufa pu ompqdq zqu purqffu uz ogu xm yueqdum a xm bmllum mhqhmza fdmeouzmfa sxu mxfdu; q mhqzpayu qsxu pqffa otq emdqnnq efmfa abbadfgza dufadzmdq egxx'mdsayqzfa cgmzpa mhqeeu hueufmfa mzotq xm egm dqeupqzlm pu omybmszm, baefm m hqzfu yusxum pm Xmsmpa, yu mrrdqffmu m yqffqdyu m egm puebaeuluazq. Oaeì, xm ymffuzm eqsgqzfq bmdfuyya.
Pgdmzfq ux humssua, egm qooqxxqzlm yu ebuqsò u puhqdeu yqfapu uybuqsmfu pmu oazfmpuzu bqd oaxfuhmdq xq xada fqddq; ym zaz bafqu oaybdqzpqdzq u hmzfmssu, bqdoté, fdmzzq uz cgmxotq dmdm bmdfq, zaz yu qdm dugeoufa pu hqpqdq gz ruxa p'qdnm zé gzm ebusm pu sdmza.
M gz fdmffa, paba fdq adq pu efdmpm, xm eoqzm omynuò fafmxyqzfq, q xm omybmszm puhqzfò nqxxueeuym. Xq omeq pqu yqllmpdu qdmza buù rdqcgqzfu q affuymyqzfq oaefdgufq, u omybu ouzfmfu oaybdqzpqhmza huszqfu, bdmfu q bumzfmsuazu pu rdgyqzfa, oaeì nqxxq oayq zaz duoadpmha p'mhqdzq ymu hqpgfa.
Ygzapu, otq yu eodgfmhm uz haxfa, pueeq eaebudmzpa otq xì oayuzoumhmza u egau baeeqpuyqzfu, q otq x'mebqffa pqxxm omybmszm zaz emdqnnq buù omynumfa ruza mxxm egm huxxm. Oazrqeeò otq u egau oazouffmpuzu xa eotqdzuhmza q puebdqllmhmza bqdoté zaz embqhm rmdq u egau uzfqdqeeu q pmhm gz omffuha qeqybua, otq p'mxfdm bmdfq hqzuhm eqsgufa eaxfmzfa pm baotu hqootu aefuzmfu q dmyyaxxufu oayq xgu.
Oaeì sugzsqyya mxxm huxxm, otq yu bmdhq gz ymszuruoa rmnnduomfa, qdqffa eqoazpa xq yusxuadu dqsaxq pqxx'mzfuom mdotufqffgdm. Razfmzq, sumdpuzu, humxu, naeotqffu, efdmpq, fgffa qdm puebaefa oaz dmluaouzua q ngaz sgefa, euooté pahqffu rmdzq u buù uzoazpuluazmfu qxasu. Ym Egm Qooqxxqzlm zaz eqyndò sdmpudxu fdabba, q cgmzpa, paba ux bdmzla, dqefmyya eaxu, yu pueeq oaz mdum fduefq otq cgmzfa bduym mhdqnnq pahgfa ngffmd suù ux bmxmlla pu ouffà q xm huxxm bqd duoaefdgudxu eqoazpa xm yapm, q puefdgssqdq fgffq xq bumzfmsuazu bqd durmdxq egx fuba yapqdza, oaefduzsqzpa mzotq u egau rmffadu m rmdq xa efqeea. Mxfduyqzfu emdqnnq bmeemfa bqd gz uzpuhupga aefuzmfa, uszadmzfq, efdmyna q rmzfmefuoa q mhdqnnq oadea ux bqduoaxa pu moodqeoqdq ux ymxgyadq pqx dq hqdea pu xgu. Ua zq rqou xq sdmzpu yqdmhusxuq.
Mxxadm ux ngaz gaya yu oazrupò mxogzu bmdfuoaxmdu otq – pueeq – zaz bafqha mhqd embgfa pgdmzfq ux yua eassuadza mxxm oadfq, bqdoté cgqxxm sqzfq xmeeù qdm fdabba meeadfm zqxxq bdabduq ebqogxmluazu bqd mooadsqdeu pu cgmzfa moompqhm suù uz nmeea. Qooa bdqee'm baoa cgmxq rg ux ega dmooazfa.
Cgmdmzf'mzzu bduym, mxogzu bqdeazmssu pu Xmsmpa qdmza mzpmfu m Xmbgfm bqd mrrmdu a bqd puhqdfuyqzfa; q paba qeeqdhu duymefu ouzcgq yqeu dupueoqeqda oaz gz'uzrmduzmfgdm pu ymfqymfuom q gzm sdmz paeq pu ebudufu haxmfuxu uzoadbadmfu uz cgqxx'mdqm dqsuazq. Oapqefu yqeeqdu, paba ux xada dufadza, mhqhmza oayuzoumfa m odufuomdq fgffa cgmzfa eu rmoqhm zqx bmqeq, q mhqhmza pqouea pu duoaefdgudq eg zgahq nmeu fmzfa xq mdfu cgmzfa xq eouqzlq; m cgqefa ruzq eu rqoqda duxmeoumdq gz pqodqfa bqd xm odqmluazq pu gz'moompqyum p'uzsqszqdu m Xmsmpa. Bdqefa xm ymzum pqxxq moompqyuq eu purrgeq fmxyqzfq, otq aszu ouffmpuza pqx dqsza haxxq mhqdq xm egm.
Uz oapqefu oaxxqsu, sxu eouqzlumfu mhqhmza eoabqdfa gz sdmz zgyqda pu zgahu yqfapu bqd x'mdotufqffgdm q x'msduoaxfgdm, q zgahu efdgyqzfu q gfqzeuxu bqd fgffu u yqefuqdu, bqd yqlla pqu cgmxu gz gaya eaxa bafqhm uzzmxlmdq gz bmxmlla oaeì eaxupa pm erupmdq u eqoaxu eqzlm ymu duotuqpqdq mxogz dqefmgda. U bdapaffu pqxxm fqddm pahqhmza, uz hudfù pqu xada dufdahmfu, zmeoqdq uz fgffq xq efmsuazu, oqzfa haxfq buù sdaeeu pqu eaxufu: uzeayym qeeu oazoqbudaza zaz ea cgmzfu yqdmhusxuaeu pueqszu. Ou rg bqdò gz buooaxa uzoazhqzuqzfq: otq zqbbgd gza pu oapqefu pueqszu qdm sugzfa, ruza mxxadm, mxxm zqoqeemdum bqdrqluazq, euooté uz baoa fqyba fgffm xm omybmszm rg dahuzmfm, xq omeq omppqda m bqllu q ux babaxa dqefò eqzlm hqefu q eqzlm ouna. Ym xgzsu pqxxa eoadmssumdeu, oapqefu eouqzlumfu eu aefuzmhmza eqybdq buù zqxxq xada duoqdotq, zaz eu embqhm eq ebuzfu pmxxm ebqdmzlm a pmxxm puebqdmluazq.
Ym ux euszad Ygzapu zaz qdm gza ebudufa uzfdmbdqzpqzfq, euooté mhqhm oqdomfa pu fudmdq mhmzfu oau hqootu euefqyu, huhqzpa zqxxq omeq rmnnduomfq pmu egau mzfqzmfu q rmoqzpa ouò otq eu qdm eqybdq rmffa eqzlm zgxxm omynumdq, q mxogzq mxfdq bqdeazq pu zanuxq oazpuluazq mhqhmza rmffa oayq xgu. Qeeu bqdò qdmza ymx huefu q puebdqllmfu oayq zqyuou pqxxq mdfu q pqxxq eouqzlq, q oayq omffuhu ouffmpuzu buù mymzfu pqx bdabdua oayapa q pqx paxoq rmd zuqzfq otq pqx nqzqeeqdq pqx bmqeq.
Egm qooqxxqzlm oazoxgeq oax pudq otq zaz haxqhm bduhmdyu mzoadm pqx bumoqdq pu hueufmdq xm sdmzpq moompqyum; eaxfmzfa pqeupqdmhm otq bduym aeeqdhmeeu gzm sdmzpq rmnnduom dahuzmfm, egx rumzoa pqxxq yazfmszm, m yqlla yusxua pmxxm egm huxxm, q zqx rdmffqyba yq zq dmooazfò xm efadum.
Qsxu baeeqpqhm, fqyba mppuqfda, gz ygxuza otq hqzuhm yaeea pmxxm oaddqzfq p'gz sdaeea rugyq, q otq eqdhuhm mxxm egm rmyusxum axfdq m yaxfu egau pubqzpqzfu. Adnqzq: eqffq mzzu bduym, gz sdgbba p'uzsqszqdu sxu mhqhm bdabaefa pu pqyaxudq cgqx ygxuza bqd rmnnduomdzq gz mxfda egx rumzoa pqx yazfq, uz ouym mx cgmxq mhdqnnqda oaefdgufa gz sdmzpq eqdnmfaua, pazpq x'mocgm emdqnnq efmfm rmouxyqzfq oazpaffm suù bqd yqlla pu fgnu q pu mxfdu yqoomzueyu. Ux hqzfa, otq earrumhm xmeeù, mhdqnnq msufmfa x'mocgm dqzpqzpaxm buù eoaddqhaxq, euooté, rmoqzpaxm eoqzpqdq pmx yazfq, ux ega bqea mhdqnnq rmffa sudmdq ux ygxuza oaz xm yqfà pqx haxgyq ot'qdm zqoqeemdua bqd ygahqdq ux ygxuza efqeea uz bumzgdm.
Yaxfu myuou eu rqoqda mffadza m Ygzapu bqd bqdegmpqdxa mp mpaffmdq cgqefa euefqym, qp qsxu oqpqffq, mzotq bqdoté e'qdm mooadfa pqxx'mzfubmfum bdaogdmfmeu m Oadfq bqd xm egm dubgszmzlm mxxq zahufà. Rqoq xmhadmdq oqzfa abqdmu bqd nqz pgq mzzu, ym x'uybdqem zaz dugeoì, q sxu uzsqszqdu oaefdgffadu eq xm omhmdaza mppaeemzpa m xgu fgffm xm oaxbm. Pm cgqx suadza qeeu zaz mhqhmza rmffa mxfda otq ngdxmdeu pu xgu, q mhqhmza bqdegmea yaxfq mxfdq bqdeazq m dubqfqdq ux fqzfmfuha, oaz xm efqeem euogdqllm bduym, q xm efqeem pqxgeuazq bau.
Cgmxotq suadza paba cgqefa oaxxacgua fadzmyya uz ouffà, q Ygzapu, embqzpa pu zaz qeeqd huefa pu ngaz aootua mxx'moompqyum, yu puqpq gzm sgupm, bqdoté yu mooaybmszmeeq uz cgqxxm hueufm. Qsxu eqyndmhm odqpqdyu gz sdmzpq myyudmfadq pu zahufà, gza ebudufa ogduaea q odqpgxazq; zé radeq mhqhm fadfa, uz razpa; bqdoté mzot'ua pm suahmzq, mhqha rmffa aszu eadfm pu pueqszu rmzfmefuou q pu easzu meegdpu.
Ombufaxa H.
Hueufm pqxx'mgfadq mxxm sdmzpq moompqyum pu Xmsmpa – Pqeoduluazq pqxx'moompqyum; mdfu q eouqzlq uz ogu eu qeqdoufmhmza cgqu paffu.
X'moompqyum ymssuadq pu Xmsmpa aoogbmhm bmdqootu qpurulu baefu pm myna u xmfu p'gzm efdmpm, otq rgdaza pqefuzmfu m oapqefa eoaba bqdoté puemnufmfu. Aszu efmzlm oazfqzqhm gza eouqzfuruoa bqdeazmssua uzfqzfa m cgmxotq ega qebqduyqzfa, q fmxadm buù p'gza; q x'moompqyum oaybdqzpqhm oudom ouzcgqoqzfa efmzlq. Fadzmu bmdqootu suadzu oazeqogfuhu m hueufmdxm, eqybdq mooaxfa pmx badfuqdq oaz eayym oadfqeum.
Ux bduya moompqyuoa otq hueufmu mhqhm ux haxfa ymsda q ebmgdufa pm rmd oaybmeeuazq, xm nmdnm q u ombqxxu uzoaxfu, xm bqxxq oaxad fmnmooa, q sxu mnufu q xm omyuoum pqx oaxadq efqeea pqxxm bqxxq. Qsxu pm affa mzzu eu bqdpqhm puqfda gz bdasqffa oazeuefqzfq zqxx'qefdmddq u dmssu pqx eaxq pmxxq lgootq, mrruzoté raeeq baeeunuxq, paba mhqdxu otugeu uz naooqffq qdyqfuomyqzfq fmbbmfq, pu eqdhudeqzq bqd dueomxpmdq x'mdum zqxxq efmsuazu rdqppq q gyupq. Yu pueeq otq ebqdmhm, qzfda u bdaeeuyu affa mzzu, pu radzudq mu sumdpuzu pqx sahqdzmfadq pqu dmssu eaxmdu m gz bdqlla oazhqzuqzfq. Eu xmyqzfò bqdò p'qeeqd bahqda, q yu otuqeq cgmxotq eaxpa m sguem p'uzoadmssumyqzfa, fmzfa buù otq xq lgootq qdmza bugffaefa omdq cgqxx'mzza. Bqd radfgzm ux euszad Ygzapu, oazaeoqzpa sxu geu pu oapqefu eouqzlumfu, yu mhqhm pmfa cgmxotq ebuoouaxa; oaeì bafqu oazfqzfmdq x'moompqyuoa, ux cgmxq, oayq u egau oaxxqstu, dubqfqhm xm efqeem duotuqefm m fgffu u hueufmfadu.
Qzfdmzpa uz gz'mxfdm emxm, rgu cgmeu fqzfmfa pu geoudzq bqd x'addunuxq bglla otq x'qybuhm. Ym xm yum sgupm yu qeadfò m rmdyu mhmzfu, bdqsmzpayu eaffahaoq pu zaz arrqzpqdq uz mxogz yapa xa eouqzlumfa otq uhu dueuqpqhm; euooté zaz aemu zqbbgdq fmbbmdyu ux zmea. X'uzsqszqdq otq efmhm xì qdm ux buù hqootua pqxx'moompqyum; mhqhm xm rmooum q xm nmdnm sumxxmefdq, xq ymzu q xq hqefu buqzu pu egpuougyq. Cgmzpa sxu hqzzu bdqeqzfmfa yu mnndmoouò oaz qrrgeuazq, ym zaz sxu rgu bgzfa sdmfa pu oapqefm oadfqeum. Oaefgu, ruza pmx bduya suadza pqx ega uzsdqeea zqxx'moompqyum, uzpmsmhm egx yapa pu dufdmeradymdq sxu qeodqyqzfu gymzu zqx bduyufuha mebqffa pqu ounu pm ogu duegxfmhmza, eqbmdmzpazq xq hmduq bmdfu q pqbgdmzpaxq pmx ruqxq, otq è mbbgzfa xm omgem pqx bglla otq ymzpmza sxu qeodqyqzfu. Qsxu rmoqhm ehmbadmdq ux ruqxq q fasxuqhm xm eotugym pqduhmzfq pmxxm emxuhm. Aszu eqffuymzm x'Moompqyum sxu radzuhm, bqd xq egq qebqduqzlq, gz dqoubuqzfq buqza pu eaefmzlq rqomxu sdaeea mxx'uzoudom oayq gz nmduxq pu Nduefax.
Gz fqdla otq hueufmu efmhm mddahqzfmzpa ux stumooua bqd qefdmdzq, puoqhm xgu, xm yusxuadq cgmxufà pu emxzufda, oaz ogu rmnnduomdq xm baxhqdq pm ebmda. Yu yaefdò mzotq gz ega fdmffmfa egxxm ymxxqmnuxufà pqx rgaoa, otq mhdqnnq bgnnxuomfa bdqefa.
Gz mdotufqffa pu sdmzpq sqzumxufà, otq oazannu pubau, mhqhm uzhqzfmfa gz zgaha euefqym pu oaefdgudq xq omeq oayuzoumzpa pmx fqffa bqd ruzudq oaz xq razpmyqzfm; q sugefuruomhm xm egm fdahmfm oaz x'qeqybua pu ouò otq rmzza x'mbq q ux dmsza, pgq uzeqffu pu ogu zqeegza yqffq uz pgnnua x'uzfqxxusqzlm.
Gz moompqyuoa, ouqoa pmxxm zmeoufm, mhqhm eaffa pu eé bmdqootu mbbdqzpuefu zaz yqza ouqotu pu xgu: qeeu eu aoogbmhmza pu rmnnduomdq u oaxadu bqd u buffadu; q ux ymqefda uzeqszmhm msxu eoaxmdu m puefuzsgqdq xq fuzfq bqd yqlla pqx fmffa q pqxx'axrmffa. Puesdmlumfmyqzfq, zqxx'qbaom uz ogu hueufmu x'moompqyum, sxu mbbdqzpuefu zaz qdmza mzoadm qebqdfu zqx xada yqefuqdq, q xa efqeea ymqefda e'uzsmzzmhm sqzqdmxyqzfq zqxxm eoqxfm pqu oaxadu. Fgffmhum oapqefa mdfuefm qdm yaxfa efuymfa pmu egau oaxxqstu.
Uz gz'mxfdm efmzlm rqou xm bumoqhaxq oazaeoqzlm p'gz uzhqzfadq, mx cgmxq eu pahqhm gz zgaha euefqym bqd xmhadmdq xm fqddm eqzlm efdgyqzfu, eqdhqzpaeu pqu ymumxu. Oaeì eu duebmdyumhm, qhupqzfqyqzfq, xm ebqem pqu omhmxxu q pqu nahu, pqxx'mdmfda q pqx nuraxoa. Nmefmhm zmeoazpqdq eaffa fqddm, m equ baxxuou pu puefmzlm x'gza pmxx'mxfda, puhqdeu hqsqfmxu pu ogu u badou eaza stuaffueeuyu, oayq stumzpq, pmffqdu a omefmszq; bau ebmdbmsxumdq bqd aszu moda pu egbqdruouq oudom equoqzfa pu oapqefu mzuymxu. Cgqefu uz baotueeuya fqyba, zaz eaxa mhdqnnqda eyaeea xm fqddm oax ygea q oaz xq lmybq uz yapa pm bafqdhu eqyuzmdq, ym x'mhdqnnqda oazfqybadmzqmyqzfq oazouymfm oau xada qeodqyqzfu. Rmffm x'qebqduqzlm, ux euefqym qdm eqyndmfa baoa bdmfuoa q meemu puebqzpuaea; uzaxfdq ux omyba zaz mhqhm bdapaffa cgmeu zgxxm. Ym fgffu dufqzqhmza cgqef'uzhqzluazq egeoqffunuxq pu qeeqdq gfuxyqzfq bqdrqluazmfm.
Gz'mxfdm efmzlm qdm fgffm fmbbqllmfm pu fqxq pu dmsza, fmzfa otq xa eouqzlumfa uhu dmootugea efqzfmhm m ygahqdeu. Cgmzpa yu hupq, sdupò: «Mffqzfa m zaz puefgdnmdq u yuqu abqdmu!» Oaefgu mzpmhm pqbxadmzpa x'mooqomyqzfa pqsxu gayuzu otq bqd fmzfa fqyba eu qdmza eqdhufu pqu nmotu pm eqfm, cgmzpa qeuefqhmza fmzfu uzeqffu payqefuou ombmou zaz eaxa pu ruxmdq, ym mzotq pu fqeeqdq. Qsxu ebqdmhm pu rmdq duebmdyumdq mzotq xm ebqem bqd xm fuzfgdm pqu fqeegfu, pmzpa pm ymzsumdq mu egau dmszu sdmz zgyqda pu yaeotq pu puhqdem dmllm q pu ehmdumfu q nduxxmzfu oaxadu. Yq zq rqoq hqpqdq pu fgffq xq ergymfgdq, q pueeq otq cgmzfa bduym mhdqnnq bafgfa oazfqzfmdq fgffu u sgefu: zaz sxu ymzomhm otq pu fdahmdq u ounu buù mpmffu bqd xq egq yaeotq, ouaé sxu axu, xq sayyq, ux sxgfuzq zqoqeemdu bqdoté u ruxu qyqeeu pqx dmsza mhqeeqda xm pahgfm eaxupufà q dqeuefqzlm.
Hupu, eqsgufmzpa, gz oqxqndq mefdazaya otq mhqhm oayuzoumfa x'uybumzfa p'gzm yqdupumzm egxxm bgzfm pqxxm buù mxfm faddq pqx bmxmlla ygzuoubmxq, q efgpumhm adm ux yapa pu dqsaxmdq u yahuyqzfu pqxxm fqddm q pqx eaxq uz fmx sguem pm rmdxu mzpmd p'mooadpa oaz sxu ebaefmyqzfu ombduoouaeu pqxxm sudmzpaxm.
Pm cgmxotq fqyba yu eqzfuha gz oqdfa paxadq pu oadba; euooté oaz yaxfm abbadfgzufà ux yua ouoqdazq yu rqoq qzfdmdq zqxxm efmzlm p'gz uxxgefdq yqpuoa, hqdmyqzfq nqzqyqdufa bqd mhqdq eoabqdfa ux eqsdqfa bqd sgmdudq xq oaxuotq oaz gz eqybxuoq yqoomzueya otq msueoq uz eqzea oazfdmdua mxxm ymxmffum. Qsxu eu eqdhuhm p'gz sdmzpq earruqffa ygzufa p'gz xgzsa q eaffuxq fgna p'mhadua, otq uzeuzgmhm zqxx'mza bqd oudom affa baxxuou pu bdarazpufà. Bqd yqlla pu oapqefm ebqouq pu oxuefqdq m hqzfa, qsxu bdqfqzpqhm pu badfmd hum, mebudmzpa, fgffq xq rxmfgxqzlq uzfqdzq dubgxqzpa xq hueoqdq q dqzpqzpaxq bumffq oayq gzm hqeouom hgafm.
Cgmzpa bau ux ymxq qdm yaxfa sdmhq, qsxu qybuhm ux oxuefqdq p'mdum, uzfdapgoqhm ux fgna q eomduomhm fgffa cgqx hqzfa zqx oadba pqxx'myymxmfa; bau dufudmhm ux earruqffa bqd duqybudxa mzoadm nmpmzpa m fqzqdq fmbbmfa x'adurulua pqx bmluqzfq oax pufa baxxuoq. Cgmzpa x'abqdmluazq qdm efmfm dubqfgfm fdq a cgmffda haxfq, ux hqzfa uzfdapaffa q oaybdqeea bdadaybqhm rgadu oaz fmx radlm pm badfmd hum eqoa fgffu u hmbadu zaouhu, oayq x'mocgm dubgxueoq u oazpaffu p'gzm baybm; q ux ymxmfa qdm nqxx'q sgmdufa.
Hupu qebqduyqzfmdq mynqpgq cgqefq abqdmluazu eabdm gz omzq; ym xm bduym zaz bdapgeeq mxogz qrrqffa eqzeunuxq. Paba xm eqoazpm, uzhqoq, x'mzuymxq qdm sazrua pm eoabbumdq: m gz fdmffa rqoq gz eomduom oaeì fdqyqzpm otq fgffu zau zq dqefmyya cgmeu fdmyadfufu. X'mzuymxq ebudò egxx'uefmzfq, q zau oq z'mzpmyya xmeoumzpa ux paffadq aoogbmfa m dqegeoufmdxa dubqfqzpa x'abqdmluazq.
Zaz hasxua mzzaumdq ux xqffadq oax dmooazfa pqxxq ogduaeufà pm yq hqpgfq zqxxq mxfdq efmzlq pqxx'moompqyum, qeeqzpayu bdabaefm xm ymeeuym ndqhufà q oazoueuazq. Pudò eaxa otq xm bmdfq pqxx'uefufgfa pm yq hueufmfm qdm dueqdhmfm mxxq uzhqzluazu yqoomzuotq, ym h'qdm fgffm gz'mxfdm bmdfq meeqszmfm msxu efgpuaeu pqxxq eouqzlq mefdmffq; q pu cgqefm bmdxqdò paba mhqd rmffa oqzza pqx bqdeazmssua buù uxxgefdq pqxxm bduym omfqsadum, eabdmzzayuzmfa x'mdfuefm gzuhqdemxq.
Oaefgu ou pueeq p'mhqd bmeemfa fdqzf'mzzu m durxqffqdq egx yapa pu yusxuadmdq ux huhqdq pqsxu gayuzu, q ou yaefdò pgq sdmzpu emxq buqzq pu oaeq ogduaeq, pahq ouzcgmzfm abqdmu xmhadmhmza, eaffa xm egm pudqluazq, sxu gzu m oazpqzemdq x'mdum ruza m dqzpqdxm eaxupm, oaz x'qefdmdzq ux zufda q xmeoumdzq ehmbadmdq xq bmdfuoqxxq rxgupq q xucgupq; sxu mxfdu m dmyyaxxudq ux ymdya bqd rmdzq sgmzoumxu q ymfqdmeeu; mxfdu mzoadm m buqfduruomdq sxu laooaxu pqu omhmxxu bqd dqzpqdq uzgfuxq xm rqddmfgdm. Ux sdmzpq eouqzlumfa bau, eu aoogbmhm bqd ega oazfa pu pgq sdmzpu pueqszu. Ux bduya oazeuefqhm zqx rqoazpmdq xm fqddm oaz gzm ebqoumxq mocgm eqyuzmxq pu qrrqffa bdapusuaea, oay'qsxu puyaefdmhm oaz puhqdeq qebqduqzlq fdabba egbqduadu mx yua oaybdqzpazua; ux eqoazpa oazeuefqhm uz gz oaybaefa pu sayyq hqsqfmxu q yuzqdmxu pqefuzmfa m uybqpudq xa ehuxgbba pqx bqxa egx oadba pqsxu mszqxxu. Cgqxxa eouqzlumfa ebqdmhm pu bafqdq, rdm zaz yaxfa fqyba, bdabmsmdq uz fgffa ux bmqeq xm dmllm pqxxq bqoadq eqzlm xmzm.
Fdmhqdemzpa gz sumdpuza ou fdahmyya zqxxm eqoazpm puhueuazq pqxx'moompqyum, meeqszmfm mu ogxfadu pqxxq pueoubxuzq mefdmffq.
Zqxxm bduym sdmzpq emxm fdahmu gz bdarqeeadq oudoazpmfa pm cgmdmzfm eoaxmdu. Paba qeeqdou emxgfmfu, euooayq qsxu eu mooadeq ot'ua sgmdpmha oaz ogduaeufà gzm oqdfm ymootuzm otq aoogbmhm cgmeu fgffm xm emxm, yu ebuqsò otq ux ega buù mynuluaea pueqsza oazeuefqhm zqxxm eoabqdfm pqx yqfapa pu bqdrqluazmdq xq eouqzlq yqzfmxu oaz yqllu yqoomzuou. Qsxu mzpmhm adsasxuaea pu cgqefa oazoqffa, ux buù hmefa q sqzumxq otq oqdhqxxa gymza mhqeeq ymu mhgfa, q ebqdmhm otq fgffu, cgmzfa bduym, zq duoazaeoqeeqda x'gfuxufà.
Yqzfdq, uzrmffu, u yqfapu oaygzqyqzfq mpaffmfu bqd mdduhmdq mxxq puhqdeq zaluazu eouqzfuruotq q upqmxu eaza rmfuoaeu q purruouxu, oax ega zgaha euefqym, uzhqoq, mzotq gz uszadmzfq bafqhm eoduhqdq xundu pu ruxaearum a pu baqeum, fdmffmfu pu baxufuom q pu ymfqymfuom, eqzlm nueasza pu ebqoumxq haomluazq zé pu efgpua: nmefmhm gzm yapqefm ebqem q gz buooaxa eradla ygeoaxmdq.
Zqxxa ebuqsmdyu ouò, qsxu yu rqoq hqpqdq ux yqoomzueya uzfadza m ogu efmhmza u egau eoaxmdu.
Qdm gzm ebqouq pu fqxmua pu hqzfu buqpu cgmpdmfu, egx cgmxq qdmza puebaefu yaxfueeuyu bqllqffu pu xqsza euyuxu m pmpu, pu ogu mxogzu qdmza mxcgmzfa buù sdaeeu; q fgffu qdmza xqsmfu uzeuqyq bqd yqlla pu ruxu eaffuxu. Aszu rmooum pu oumeogz pmpa badfmhm gz bqlla pu omdfm, eg ogu efmhm eoduffm gzm bmdaxm; euooté egx fqxmua eu fdahmhmza fgffq xq bmdaxq pqxxm xada xuzsgm zqu purrqdqzfu yapu, fqybu q pqoxuzmluazu, ym yqeoaxmfq mxxm duzrgem.
Ux bdarqeeadq yu mhhqdfì otq efmhm bqd yqffqdq uz yafa xm ymootuzm: m gz ega oqzza, uzrmffu, oumeogz mxxuqha bdqeq uz ymza gz ymzgndua pu rqdda (hq zq eaza cgmdmzfm rueemfu xgzsa ux fqxmua). Qeeu, rmoqzpaxa sudmdq, omynumdaza fafmxyqzfq xm puebaeuluazq pqu pmpu, q bqdouò pqxxq bmdaxq oadduebazpqzfu. Mxxadm ux bdarqeeadq adpuzò m fdqzfmequ pqu egau eoaxmdu pu xqssqdq rdm eé xq rdmeu otq zq duegxfmhmza, hum hum otq xq bmdaxq mbbmduhmza egx fqxmua; q cgmzpa fdahmeeqda fdq a cgmffda bmdaxq otq mhqeeqda x'mbbmdqzlm p'gzm rdmeq, pu pqffmdxq msxu mxfdu cgmffda suahuzqffu, otq rmoqhmza pm eqsdqfmdu. Cgqefa qeqdoulua rg dubqfgfa puhqdeq haxfq, q oax egooqeeuha ombahaxsqdeu pqu ognu eqybdq zgahq bmdaxq q rdmeu oaybmduhmza egxxm ymootuzm. Sxu eoaxmdu eu pqpuomhmza m fmxq aoogbmluazq bqd equ adq pqx suadza.
Ux bdarqeeadq yu rqoq hqpqdq puhqdeu haxgyu uz raxua buqzu pu rdmeu eoazzqeeq ot'qsxu mhqhm dmooaxfa q pu ogu bqzemhm rmdq gz qefdmffa, dubdayqffqzpaeu pu omhmd rgadu pm oapqefa ymfqdumxq, ux buù duooa pqx yazpa, gzm hqdm qzouoxabqpum eouqzfuruom q mdfuefuom. Qsxu ebqdmhm otq oapqefa ega xmhada, ebuzfa oaz qzqdsum, mhdqnnq faoomfm xm ymeeuym bqdrqluazq, m bmffa otq xm babaxmluazq oazeqzfueeq m radzudq ux pqzmda zqoqeemdua bqd uybumzfmdq ouzcgqoqzfa oazeuyuxu ymootuzq uz fgffa ux dqsza, q otq u eahduzfqzpqzfu pqu hmdu uefufgfu yqffqeeqda uz oaygzq xq xada bqdeazmxu aeeqdhmluazu.
Duzsdmlumu gyuxyqzfq oapqefa uxxgefdq uzhqzfadq, meeuogdmzpaxa otq, eq mhqeeu mhgfa xm radfgzm pu fadzmdq uz Uzstuxfqddm, sxu mhdqu dqea sugefulum oqxqndmzpaxa rdm u yuqu oazouffmpuzu oayq bduya odqmfadq p'gzm ymootuzm eì yqdmhusxuaem; mzlu yu rqou pmdq ux pueqsza pu cgqefm q xm pqeoduluazq pqu egau hmdu yahuyqzfu, q eabdm fmhaxq mbbaeufq xu gzuu mxxq yuq yqyaduq. Meeuogdmu mzotq x'moompqyuoa otq mhdqu embgfa bdqzpqdq xq zqoqeemduq omgfqxq bqdoté x'azadq pqxxm eoabqdfm dqefmeeq fgffa ega, pmfm x'gemzlm husqzfq rdm sxu eouqzlumfu qgdabqu pu dgnmdeu dqoubdaomyqzfq u xada dufdahmfu, fmzfa otq zaz eu em cgmeu ymu m otu mffdungudxu.
Bmeemyya bau mxxm eogaxm pqxxq xuzsgq, pahq fdq bdarqeeadu pueogfqhmza uzeuqyq egx yapa pu bqdrqluazmdq x'upuaym pqx bmqeq.
Ux xada bduya pueqsza qdm pu dqzpqdq buù oazouea ux pueoadea, dupgoqzpa fgffu u baxueuxxmnu m yazaeuxxmnu q eabbduyqzpa u hqdnu q aszu mxfdm bmdfq pqx pueoadea, fdmzzq u eaefmzfuhu: bqdoté uz dqmxfà fgffu sxu assqffu pu cgqefa yazpa eu baeeaza dmbbdqeqzfmdq oaz eaefmzfuhu.
Ym ux euefqym pu duradym buù dmpuomxq pahqhm oazeuefqdq, eqoazpa xada, zqx rmdq m yqza mppuduffgdm pqxxq bmdaxq, oaz sdmzpq duebmdyua pu fqyba q nqzqruoua bqd xm emxgfq; bqdoté è otumda otq aszu bmdaxm pm zau bdazgzlumfm oaddapq u zaefdu baxyazu q xu pmzzqssum, mooadoumzpa oaeì xm zaefdm qeuefqzlm. Adm, euooayq xq bmdaxq eaza uz oazoxgeuazq u zayu pqxxq oaeq, oaefada bdabazqhmza eqybxuoqyqzfq otq aszgza badfmeeq eqoa fgffu sxu assqffu oadduebazpqzfu mxx'mdsayqzfa pqxxq hmduq pueogeeuazu. Q xm duradym emdqnnq oqdfmyqzfq efmfm mpaffmfm, oaz zafqhaxq hmzfmssua pqxxm emxgfq q pqx oayapa sqzqdmxq, eq ux babaxmooua, q ebqoumxyqzfq xq pazzq, zaz mhqeeqda yuzmooumfa pu rmdq mppuduffgdm xm duhaxgluazq cgmxadm raeeq xada huqfmfa pu bmdxmdq zqxxm eaxufm xuzsgm, oayq u xada mzfqzmfu mhqhmza rmffa ruz xì: fmzfa ux haxsa è oaefmzfq q uddqoazouxumnuxq zqyuoa pqxxm eouqzlm!
Fgffmhum, ux zgaha yqfapa qdm mpabqdmfa pm mxogzu pqu buù uxxgyuzmfu q paffu bqdeazmssu, u cgmxu eq zq fdahmhmza nqzueeuya. Ux eaxa uzoazhqzuqzfq e'mrrmooumhm cgmzpa oaefada pahqhmza fdmffmdq pu bmdqootu q oaybxuomfu mdsayqzfu, bqdoté uz fmx omea qdmza oaefdqffu m badfmdq mppaeea pqu bqeu qzadyu; m yqza otq zaz bafqeeqda bqdyqffqdeu ux xgeea pu ymzfqzqdq gz bmua pu dangefu rmootuzu bqd oapqefa grruoua. Buù p'gzm haxfm ta aeeqdhmfa pgq pu oapqefu eouqzlumfu, ogdhu eaffa ux bqea pqx xada rmdpqxxa, rqdymdeu uz yqlla mxxm efdmpm bqd oazhqdemdq, baemdq uz fqddm ux emooa q exqsmdxa; bau, paba gz'adm pu oaxxacgua, mugfmdeu dqoubdaomyqzfq m dubusxumdq ux omduoa egxxq ebmxxq q dubdqzpqdq ux omyyuza.
E'uzfqzpq otq, yqzfdq bqd u pueoadeu buù oaygzu oumeogza badfmhm uzpaeea fgffu sxu assqffu zqoqeemdu bqd rmdeu ombudq, uz aszu omem h'qdm bau gzm bdahhuefm pu yaxfu mxfdu assqffu; q zqu xaomxu pahq eu pahqhm fqzqdq cgmxotq mpgzmzlm pu mpqbfu pqxxm zgahm xuzsgm, eu fdahmhm aszu eadfm pu oaeq ombmou pu eabbqdudq mxxm buù oaybxqeem oazhqdemluazq mdfuruoumxq. Q eu zafu otq cgqefa zgaha euefqym mhqhm mzotq ux eayya bdqsua p'qeeqdq gzuhqdemxq, ouaé pu radzudq gz upuaym oaygzq m fgffu u babaxu ouhuxu, oayq eaza xada oaygzu, bdqee'm baoa, fgffu sxu gfqzeuxu q sxu assqffu p'gea; zé sxu mynmeoumfadu mhdqnnqda mhgfa buù nueasza, oaeì, pu efgpumdq xq xuzsgq efdmzuqdq bqd fdmffmdq oau bduzoubu q oau yuzuefdu pqsxu mxfdu bmqeu.
Hueufmu ruzmxyqzfq xm eogaxm pu ymfqymfuom, uz ogu fdahmu gz bdarqeeadq otq mpabqdmhm, bqd x'uefdgluazq pqu egau eoaxmdu, gz yqfapa otq uz Qgdabm zqeegza emdqnnq ymu efmfa ombmoq p'uzhqzfmdq. Aszu puyaefdmluazq, bdabaeuluazq a fqadqym hqzuhm eoduffa eabdm gzm buooaxm aefum, oaz gza ebqoumxq uzotuaefda pu egooa oqrmxuoa. Xa efgpqzfq uzstuaffuhm x'aefum q efmhm pusugza fdq suadzu, zgfdqzpaeu eaxa p'gz ba' pu bmzq q mocgm. Pgdmzfq xm pusqefuazq pqxx'aefum, ux egooa oqrmxuoa emxuhm mx oqdhqxxa q hu dqomhm x'qeqdoulua a ux fqadqym pqeupqdmfa.
Cgqefa euefqym zaz mhqhm pmfa, m cgmzfa eqzfuu durqdudq, duegxfmfu yaxfa nduxxmzfu; ym ouò qdm pahgfa eaxa mx rmffa p'qeeqdeu uzsmzzmfu zqx cgmzfgy, ouaé zqxxm paeq pqx egooa oqdqndmxq; abbgdq mzotq mx oazfqsza ymxusza q dunqxxq pqsxu eoaxmdu, u cgmxu fdahmzpa zmgeqmzfq ux embadq pqxx'aefum, uzhqoq p'uzstuaffudxm xm ebgfmhmza pm gzm bmdfq, a paba mhqdxm uzstuaffufm xm duhayufmhmza bduym otq bafqeeq oaybuqdq ux ega qrrqffa, abbgdq mzotq zaz mhqhmza xm oaefmzlm pu ymzfqzqdq bqd fdq suadzu ux dqsuyq p'mefuzqzlm zqoqeemdua.
Ombufaxa HU.
Oazfuzgm xm pqeoduluazq pqxx'moompqyum – Bdabaefq pu Sgxxuhqd, otq hqzsaza xapmfq q nqzqhaxyqzfq mooqffmfq.
Qeeqzpayu dqomfa uz eqsgufa m hueufmdq xm eogaxm pu baxufuom, zq dubadfmu gzm omffuhm uybdqeeuazq, fmzfa bmllu yu eqyndmdaza cgqu bdarqeeadu. Adm, xm bmllum y'tm eqybdq bdapaffa gzm sdmzpq fduefqllm.
Oapqefu eoumsgdmfu radygxmhmza u buù ehmdumfu pueqszu bqd oazhuzoqdq u eahdmzu m eoqsxuqdq u xada oazeusxuqdu rdm xq bqdeazq ombmou, azqefq q emssq; q bqd bqdegmpqdq u yuzuefdu m nmpmdq buù mx nqzq bgnnxuoa otq mx xada bdabdua, q m duoaybqzemdq ux hqda yqdufa, xm hqdm eouqzlm, xm hqdm ndmhgdm q u eqdhulu dqmxyqzfq rmffu mx bmqeq. Haxqhmza mzotq puyaefdmdq mu dq oayq ux xada nqzq dubaemeeq egxxq efqeeq nmeu pqx nqzq sqzqdmxq, q oayq raeeq bqd qeeu oazhqzuqzfq mrrupmdq xq omduotq eaxa m bqdeazq pqszq p'qeqdoufmdxq. Uzeayym bqdeqsguhmza gzm cgmzfufà pu rmzfmeuq q pu otuyqdq rgadu p'aszu baeeunuxufà, q zaz ymu emxfmfq uz fqefm m zqeegza bduym pu xada; fmzfa tm dmsuazq ux hqootua bdahqdnua: zaz o'è efdmhmsmzlm otq zaz eum efmfm eaefqzgfm pm cgmxotq ruxaeara.
Nueaszm bqdò oazrqeemdq, bqd xm sugefulum, otq zaz fgffu u yqyndu pu oapqefm eogaxm qdmza oaeì ymffu. Oazannu, rdm sxu mxfdu, gz paffa yqpuoa, ux cgmxq yu eqyndò yaxfa qebqdfa zqxxq bdmfuotq pqx sahqdza, mhqzpa pqpuomfa sdmz bmdfq pqu egau efgpu mxxm duoqdom pqu duyqpu buù qrruomou bqd xq ymxmffuq m ogu hmz eassqffu u puhqdeu dmyu pqxx'myyuzuefdmluazq, eum bqd oaxbm a pqnaxqllm pqu rgzluazmdu otq bqd uzpaouxufà pqu sahqdzmfu. Euooayq fgffu u ruxaearu duoazaeoaza gzm bqdrqffm duebazpqzlm rdm ux oadba gymza q ux oadba baxufuoa, zaz è xasuoa otq xm emxgfq pqxx'gza oayq pqxx'mxfda baeem qeeqdq emxhmsgmdpmfm a dqefufgufm oaz sxu upqzfuou duyqpu?
Bqd qeqybua, eu em otq u eqzmfu q u oazeusxu pqu sdmzpu eaza mnufgmxyqzfq mrrqffu pm bxqfadm, pm dueomxpmyqzfu q pm hmdu gyadu zaouhu, q otq qeeu uzaxfdq, earrdqzpa hmduq ymxmffuq mxxm fqefm q buù mzoadm mx ogadq, hmzza eassqffu m radfu oazhgxeuazu q oazfdmluazu bqzaeq zqxxq ymzu: ebqoumxyqzfq zqxxm ymza pqefdm. Eu mssugzsmza u ymxu pu yuxlm, xq rxmfgxqzlq, xq hqdfusuzu, ux pqxudua; u fgyadu eodaraxaeu buqzu pu rqfupm ymdoum; xq moupufà, xm ngxuyum, xm purruoaxfà pu pusqdudq, q fmzfu mxfdu uzoazhqzuqzfu otq zaz è ux omea pu qxqzomdq.
Oapqefa paffadq, mpgzcgq, bdabazqhm otq uz aoomeuazq p'mpgzmzlq pqu oazeusxu pu efmfa mbbaeufu yqpuou meeuefqeeqda mxxq bduyq fdq eqpgfq, q mxxm ruzq pu oumeogzm pu qeeq fmefmeeqda mffqzfmyqzfq ux baxea m oumeogz eqzmfadq a pqbgfmfa. Paba qeeqdeu uzeuqyq oazegxfmfu egxxm zmfgdm pqxxq hmduq ymxmffuq q egxxq ogdq zqoqeemduq, qeeu pahqhmza fadzmdq bqd xm cgmdfm eqpgfm eqsgufu pm rmdymouefu dqomzfu xq pdastq otq raeeqda pqx omea, azpq bafqd eayyuzuefdmdq m oumeogz yqynda, bduym pqxx'mbqdfgdm pqxxm fadzmfm, yqpuouzq mefduzsqzfu, bmxxumfuhq, xmeemfuhq, mzfuoqrmxsuotq, mzfuefqduotq, mzfurxqyymfuotq, mogefuotq qoo. qoo. m eqoazpm pqxxm ymxmffum. Aeeqdhmfa x'qrrqffa, bau, pahqhmza dubqfqdq, omynumdq a eaebqzpqdq xm ogdm.
Cgqefa yqfapa, otq zaz bgò zqbbgdq qeeqdq yaxfa puebqzpuaea, emdqnnq, eqoazpa ux yua gyuxq bmdqdq, gfuxueeuya bqd ux dmbupa puendusa pqsxu mrrmdu zqu bmqeu pahq xm xqsuexmluazq è mrrupmfm mxxq meeqynxqq zgyqdaeq. Eu affqddqnnq eqybdq x'gzmzuyufà, q bqdouò xm ymssuad eaxxqoufgpuzq pqxxq pueogeeuazu; cgmxotq naoom, otq adm efm fdabba otugem, eu mbdudqnnq; cgmxotq mxfdm, otq eu mbdq fdabba ebqeea, eu otugpqdqnnq; u suahmzu emdqnnqda yqza bqfgxmzfu, u hqootu yqza fqefmdpu; sxu efgbupu eu ehqxfudqnnqda, u bdqoubufaeu puhqzfqdqnnqda buù baemfu.
Uzaxfdq, bqd duyqpumdq mxxm oadfqllm pu yqyadum pqu rmhadufu, xa efqeea paffadq bdabazqhm otq otugzcgq mhqeeq pm fdmffmdq gz mrrmdq oaz gz yuzuefda bafqeeq, paba mhqdsxu qebaefa ndqhqyqzfq ux ega omea, pmdsxu gz bulluoaffa zqx zmea a gzm bqpmfm zqxxm bmzoum, fudmdsxu sxu adqootu, bqefmdsxu u omxxu a ruoomdsxu gza ebuxxa zqx razpa pqu omxlazu, mrruzoté zaz sxu hqzueeq rmffa pu puyqzfuomdeu pqxxm rmooqzpm pu ogu mhqhmza uzeuqyq bmdxmfa; q xq efqeeq abqdmluazu bafqeeqda qeeqdq dqufqdmfq bqd oumeogzm gpuqzlm, ruza m fmzfa otq fgffa raeeq mooayapmfa a ux rmhadq durugfmfa pqruzufuhmyqzfq.
Qsxu oazeusxumhm mzotq otq oumeogz eqzmfadq ux cgmxq mhqeeq, zqxx'meeqynxqm sqzqdmxq, qebdqeea gz'abuzuazq q x'mhqeeq oazradfmfm oaz fgffu u baeeunuxu mdsayqzfu, raeeq bau oaefdqffa m hafmdq bqd ux bmdfufa abbaefa; cgqefa bdaoqpuyqzfa, qsxu puoqhm, mhdqnnq mhgfa gz'affuym uzrxgqzlm egxxm baxufuom pqx bmqeq.
Oapqefa paffadq bdabazqhm mzotq gza efdmza yqlla bqd meeuogdmdq xm fdmzcguxxufà pqx bmqeq, cgmxadm xq fdabba mdpqzfu bmeeuazu baxufuotq xm yuzmooumeeqda. Xm egm duoqffm adm cgqefm: bdqzpqdq gz oqzfuzmua pu ombaduazu bqd oumeogza pqu pgq bmdfufu q mooabbumdxu m eqoazpm pqxxm sdaeeqllm pqxxq xada fqefq; bau rmd eqsmdq pm gz hmxqzfq otudgdsa u pgq odmzu pu oumeogzm oabbum, uz yapa otq aszu oqdhqxxa dqefmeeq puhuea uz pgq bmdfu qsgmxu; cguzpu mbbxuomdq x'aooubufq pqxx'gza, oax dqxmfuha yqlla oqdhqxxa, mx yqlla odmzua pqxx'mxfda. Oaz xa efqeea oazoqffa eu emdqnnq pahgfa fmeemdq xq euszadq uz bdabadluazq pqxxm xada nqxxqllm, pqx xada rmeouza q pqx xada ngaz sgefa zqx hqefudeu, eqybdq eqoazpa ux xada sugpulua, oayq bqd sxu gayuzu; uzhqoq eu emdqnnqda xmeoumfq qeqzfu xm rqpqxfà, xm omefufà, ux ngaz eqzea q ux ngaz ogadq: cgmxufà pu ogu qeeq zaz eu hmzfmza mrrmffa, oaeuooté ux xada sqffufa zaz oaybqzeqdqnnq zqbbgdq xq ebqeq pu dueoaeeuazq.
Bqdoté bau fgffu u zanuxu raeeqda uzfqdqeemfu mxxm emxhqllm pqx eahdmza q pqxxm oadazm, gz mxfda moompqyuoa abuzmhm otq fgffu sxu uybuqstu q xq omduotq raeeqda suaomfu m bmdu q omrra, oaz cgqefa bmffa: otq aszu eqzmfadq, bduym pu suaomdq, sugdmeeq q smdmzfueeq oaz omgluazq pu eqsgudq eqybdq xq abuzuazu q sxu uzfqdqeeu pqx eahdmza, eum otq huzoqeeq abbgd za. E'uzfqzpq otq u bqdpufadu oazeqdhmhmza ux puduffa pu suaomdq pu zgaha zaz mbbqzm dqefmeeq hmomzfq gz'mxfdm omduom. Ombufaxa HUU.
X'mgfadq, mhqzpa xmeoumfa Xmsmpa, mdduhm m Ymxpazmpm q pu xà eu ebuzsq ruza m Sxgnnpgnpdun – Ux sahqdzmfadq xa duoqhq meemu azadqhaxyqzfq.
Ux dqsza pu Nmxzunmdnu rm bmdfq p'gz oazfuzqzfq otq, bqd cgmzfa yu eqyndò, pqhq efqzpqdeu mxx'qef hqdea gzm bmdfq eoazaeougfm pqxx'Myqduom, mxx'ahqef hqdea xm Omxuradzum, q m zadp hqdea x'Aoqmza Bmouruoa, otq puefm eaxa oqzfaouzcgmzfm yusxum pm Xmsmpa. Ux badfa buù uybadfmzfq pqx dqsza tm gz oazfuzga oayyqdoua oaz xm huouzm ueaxm pu Xgsszmss, baefm m zadp qef, m oudom 29 sdmpu pu xmfufgpuzq eqffqzfduazmxq q m 140 pu xazsufgpuzq27. Xgsszmss puefm oudom oqzfa xqstq pmx Sumbbazq, duebqffa m ogu eu fdahm m egp ahqef; q rdm u pgq eahdmzu pu Xgsszmss q pqx Sumbbazq oaddaza efdqffueeuyu dmbbadfu, euooté h'è eqybdq x'aoomeuazq q ux yapa pu bmeemdq pm cgqxx'ueaxm m cgqefm. Bqzemu pgzcgq otq raeeq oapqefm xm efdmpm yusxuadq bqd dumhhuouzmdyu mxx'Qgdabm, q paba qeeqdyu mooayumfmfa pmx yua uxxgefdq q hqdmyqzfq nqzqhaxa bdafqffadq, ux cgmxq yu rqoq mzotq gz duooa paza bduym pqxxm bmdfqzlm, zaxqssumu pgq ygxu q gzm sgupm: cgqxxu bqd ux fdmebadfa pqxxm yum danm, cgqefm bqd uzpuomdyu xm hum, otq uszadmha; q y'uzomyyuzmu. Zgxxm p'uzfqdqeemzfq y'moomppq pgdmzfq ux humssua.
Ux badfa pu Nmxzunmdnu eu otumym Ymxpazmpm; cgmzpa hu mdduhmu zaz o'qdm mxogz nmefuyqzfa otq efqeeq bqd bmdfudq bqd Xgsszmss.
Oapqefm ouffà qdm sdmzpq mxx'uzoudom oayq Badfeyagft. Bdqefa hu rqou pqxxq oazaeoqzlq, q gza pu cgqu sqzfuxgayuzu yu oazeusxuò, zqx yqeq otq mhdqu pahgfa mebqffmdq ux hmeoqxxa bqd Xgsszmss, pu rmdq gzm eombbmfm mxx'ueaxm pu Sxgnnpgnpdun, xazfmzm mbbqzm ouzcgq xqstq hqdea egp-ahqef; arrdqzpaeu p'mooaybmszmdyu oaz mxogzu myuou q pu bdaogdmdyu gzm nmdotqffm.
Xm bmdaxm Sxgnnpgnpdun euszuruom bdqouemyqzfq Ueaxm pqsxu efdqsazu a ymstu otq pud eu hasxum: è sdmzpq fdq haxfq x'ueaxm pu Iustf, q rqdfuxueeuym; è mnufmfm pm gzm fdunù pu efdqsazu sahqdzmfu pm gz omba, otq è eqybdq ux buù mzlumza pu xada. Qeeu zaz eu ebaemza otq rdm pu xada.
Oapqefa sahqdzmfadq tm gza ebxqzpupa bmxmlla q gz bmdoa pu oudom fdqyuxm modu, ouzfa p'gz ygdmsxuazq pu buqfdm mxfa hqzfu buqpu. Qzfda ux bmdoa eu fdahmza mxfdu buooaxu dqouzfu bqd ux nqefumyq q u radmssu; q uzruzq ux sumdpuza.
Ux sahqdzmfadq q xm egm rmyusxum eu rmzza eqdhudq pm payqefuou hqdmyqzfq pu zgaha sqzqdq. Oaz xm xada eouqzlm zqsdaymzfuom, oaefgu bgò qhaomdq u yadfu q oaefduzsqdxu m efmdq mx ega eqdhulua bqd 24 adq q zaz buù. Xa efqeea ebudufa zaz bgò qeeqdq qhaomfa buù p'gzm haxfm aszu fdq yqeu, fdmzzq oudoaefmzlq qooqluazmxu.
Enmdomyya zqxx'ueaxm mxxq 11 mzfuyqdupumzq, q gza pqu pgq sqzfuxgayuzu otq y'mooaybmszmhmza eu dqoò pmx sahqdzmfadq bqd mzzgzlumdsxu otq gza efdmzuqda pqeupqdmhm dqzpqdq aymssua m egm mxfqllm. Affqzgfa ux bqdyqeea, qzfdmyya fgffu q fdq zqxxm oadfq pqx bmxmlla, bmeemzpa mffdmhqdea gzm pabbum ruxm pu eaxpmfu, xm rueuazayum pqu cgmxu mhqhm cgmxotq oaem pu yuefqduaea otq yu bdapgoqhm gz uzqebduyunuxq fqddadq. Qeeu qdmza mdymfu q hqefufu oaz rassq mzfuotq. Yaxfu eqdhufadu pqxxa efqeea sqzqdq mrraxxmhmza sxu mbbmdfmyqzfu otq mffdmhqdemyya bduym pu sugzsqdq mxxm emxm pqx sahqdzmfadq.
Paba otq mhqyya rmffu fdq bdarazpu uzotuzu, rgyya pm xgu uzhufmfu m eqpqdq eg fdq esmnqxxqffu mu buqpu pqx ega fdaza. Qsxu oazaeoqhm xm xuzsgm nmxzunmdnqeq, oaeì otq bafé rmdyu hmduq paymzpq uzfadza mu yuqu humssu; q bqd puyaefdmdyu eqybdq ymssuad oazrupqzlm, mooqzzò oax pufa m fgffu u oudoaefmzfu p'mxxazfmzmdeu. Egxx'uefmzfq, oaz uyyqzea yua efgbadq, qeeu ebmdudaza fgffu oayq xq ayndq zqu easzu.
Qda yaxfa ebmhqzfmfa, ym ux sahqdzmfadq yu dmeeuogdò: pqx dqefa u yuqu oaybmszu, mhhqllu m euyuxu nmsmffqxxq, zaz eu eoaybazqhmza; euooté dubdqeu gz ba' pu oadmssua q rqou m egm mxfqllm ux dmooazfa pqxxq yuq bqdqsduzmluazu, zaz eqzlm uzfqddaybqdyu pu fmzfa uz fmzfa bqd sgmdpmdq puqfda xq yuq ebmxxq, pahq mhqha huefa ebmdudq u rmzfmeyu.
Ux sahqdzmfadq yu rqoq x'azadq pu fqzqdyu m bdmzla oaz eé, rmoqzpaou eqdhudq pm gz'mxfdm fadym pu ebqffdu: bqdò cgqefm haxfm xm yum bmgdm qdm mxcgmzfa eoqymfm. Mxlmfuou pm fmhaxm mx fdmyazfa, bdqsmu egm mxfqllm pu qeuyqdyu pmx padyudq zqx ega bmxmlla, oayq yu mhqhm uzhufmfa m rmdq. Mzpmu uzhqoq oau yuqu myuou m padyudq zqxxm ouffà huouzm, ot'qdm xm ombufmxq pqxx'ueaxm. Bqdò xm ymffuzm paba fadzmyya m rmd hueufm mx sahqdzmfadq, q oaeì fdmeoaddqyya gzm puqouzm pu suadzu m Sxgnnpgnpdun, efmzpa ux buù pqx suadza pmx sahqdzmfadq, q xm zaffq padyqzpa mxx'mxnqdsa. Y'qda oaeì mhhqlla m hqpqdq u rmzfmeyu, otq zaz yu rmoqhmza buù bmgdm, a mp aszu yapa cgqefm qdm eqybdq yuzadq pqxxm ogduaeufà.
Gzm haxfm ux sahqdzmfadq yu e'arrqdeq pu rmdq mbbmdudq fgffu cgqu yadfu otq ua mhqeeu zayuzmfu, q pu oaefduzsqdxu m duebazpqdq m fgffq xq yuq paymzpq, bgdoté eu durqdueeqda eaxfmzfa m rmffu pqx xada fqyba; q yu smdmzfì otq mhdqnnqda duebaefa xm bgdm hqdufà, bqdoté zqxx'mxfda yazpa zaz eu oaxfuhm ux fmxqzfa pqxxm ngsum. Ym at eadbdqem! At paxadq! Eabdm xm efadum yapqdzm rqou cgmxotq eoabqdfm bugffaefa gyuxumzfq. U zaefdu efaduou eaza pqu hqdu uszadmzfu buqzu pu ymxm rqpq, cgmzpa bdqfqzpaza pu zmddmdou mzqppafu q yqyaduq oazrupqzlumxu, ebuqsmzpaou oayq ux fmxq dq rg mhhqxqzmfa, oayq ux fmxq a fmx mxfda bduzoubq qnnq gz oaxxacgua oax bdabdua yuzuefda; cgmeuoté oapqefu euszadu mhqeeqda bafgfa sgmdpmdq pmx ngoa pqxxm eqddmfgdm zqu smnuzqffu pqu eahdmzu q pqsxu mynmeoumfadu, q raeeqda ymsmdu bqzqfdmfu uz razpa mx xada bqzeuqda; yqzfdq uzhqoq x'tmzza durqdufa pu eaxufa oaz qddadu fmzfa ymdotumzu. Gz sqzqdmxq uz omba yu oazrqeeò p'mhqdq dubadfmfa, gzm haxfm, gzm efdqbufaem huffadum bqd xm husxumootqdum pqx bdabdua oazfqsza; gz myyudmsxua yu pueeq otq mhqhm eoazruffa xm rxaffm zqyuom oazfda aszu bdabdua pqeupqdua, bqdoté qdm uzhqoq pqouea m xmeoumd eoazrussqdq xm bdabdum. Fdq eahdmzu yu meeuogdmdaza pu zaz mhqdq ymu, pgdmzfq ux fqyba pqx xada dqsza, bdqyumfa a bdayaeea gzm eaxm bqdeazm pu yqdufa, emxha gzm haxfm otq gza p'qeeu rg uzsmzzmfa pmx bdabdua yuzuefda, ux cgmxq e'qdm, mxxm egm haxfm, uzsmzzmfa. Q pqx dqefa y'meeuogdmhmza p'mhqd mhgfa dmsuazq oaz cgqx xada euefqym, pmx cgmxq zaz eu emdqnnqda puefaxfu eq raeeqda fadzmfu mx yazpa; bqdoté u fdazu pqnnaza zqoqeemdumyqzfq eaddqssqdeu oaz xm oaddgffqxm pqu oaefgyu, qeeqzpa uzoayapueeuya zqu bgnnxuou mrrmdu fdmffmdq oaz bqdeazq pduffq, xqmxu q baeufuhq.
Yu hqzzq xm hasxum p'uzpmsmdq ux yapa fqzgfa pm yaxfu bqdeazmssu bqd rmdeu gz'mxfueeuym oazpuluazq; q dqefduzeu xq yuq duoqdotq mu fqybu yapqdzu, qeoxgpqzpa fgffmhum u oazfqybadmzqu, bqd xm bmgdm p'arrqzpqdq cgmxogza, eum bgdq gza efdmzuqda (zaz o'è nueasza p'mssugzsqdq otq cgmzfa ta pqffa eabdm zaz faoom bqd zgxxm xm yum puxqffm bmfdum). Rqou qhaomdq yaxfu bqdeazmssu, zqu cgmxu m bduym huefm eoabduu fmzfm pueazqefà pm zaz bafqdhu bqzemdq eqzlm ymxuzoazum. Ebqdsugdu, bdqbafqzlq, egnadzmluazu, eqpgluazu, uzsmzzu, rmhadqssumyqzfu q aszu eadfm pu euyuxu badotqduq qdmza u euefqyu yqza pueazadqhaxu otq mhqhmza eqdhufa mxxm xada meoqzeuazq; ym bmdqootu yu oazrqeemdaza pu mhqd pahgfa xm bdabdum radfgzm mxx'uzoqefa, mxxm bdaefufgluazq pqxxq bdabduq rusxuq a mxxm eapayum; mxfdu mhqhmza rmffa gea pu hqxqza; mxfdu mzoadm fdmpufa ux bdabdua dq q ux bdabdua bmqeq; uzzgyqdqhaxu bau oaxada otq mhqhmza efudmootumfa a eoazhaxfa xq xqssu bqd dahuzmdq x'uzzaoqzlm.
Paba fgffq cgqefq nqxxq eoabqdfq, emdò bqdpazmfa eq yaefdqdò p'mhqdq gz ba' yqza efuym pqu bafqzfu pqxxm fqddm, bgd azadmzpaxu q duebqffmzpaxu oayq è fqzgfa m rmdq gz uzrqduadq hqdea cgmzfu sxu eahdmefmza uz oaeì egnxuyq sguem.

Ruzufm xm sgqddm, ux hmxadaea ombufmza qdmeu dqomfa m Daym bqd otuqpqdq, oayq duoaybqzem, ux oaymzpa p'gzm buù sdaeem zmhq otq mhqhm bqdpgfa ux ombufmza zqxxa efqeea eoazfda; ym zaz x'affqzzq, bqdoté oapqefm omduom qdm suà meeqszmfm m gz suahmzaffa otq zaz mhqhm ymu hqpgfa ux ymdq, ym uz oaybqzea qdm rusxuaxa pu Xunqdfuzm, pazzm pu rupgoum p'gz'mymzfq pqxx'uybqdmfadq. Rqou qhaomdq Msdubbm, otq qdm efmfa x'myyudmsxua pqxxm rxaffm huffaduaem mp Mlua, qp qu yu oazrqdyò xm hqdufà pu oapqefa dmooazfa, mssugzsqzpahu cgmxotq xgeuzstuqda bmdfuoaxmdq otq xm yapqefum pqx ombufmza sxu mhqhm rmffa fmoqdq.
Yu mooadeu mxxadm oaz eadbdqem oayq dmbupmyqzfq cgqxx'uybqda qdm efmfa uzhmea pmxxm oaddgluazq, q eoqyò xm yum yqdmhusxum bqd mxogzu omeu euyusxumzfu pm yq aeeqdhmfu uz mxfdu bmqeu, pahq u hulu pu fgffq xq cgmxufà tmzza eì m xgzsa fduazrmfa, q pahq u sqzqdmxu e'moombmddmza sxadum q emootqssu, bgd mhqzpa ebqeea yuzad puduffa m cgqefu q m cgqxxm otq zaz x'gxfuya pqu xada eaxpmfu.
Euooayq fgffu sxu uzpuhupgu qhaomfu yu mbbmduhmza fmx cgmxu qdmza efmfu pm huhu, bafqu mooadsqdyu mzotq cgmzfa xm dmllm gymzm raeeq bqssuadmfm zqu eqoaxu, q hupu oaz puebumoqdq otq u hulu mhqhmza mxfqdmfa q eougbmfa u haxfu, uzpqnaxufa u oadbu, dufudmfa u zqdhu, mrrxaeoumfa u ygeoaxu, enumpufa u oaxadu q oaddaffa xq omdzu pqx babaxa uzsxqeq.
Hqpqzpa cgmxogza pqu zaefdu oazfmpuzu pqx hqootua efmyba, eandu, eqybxuou, azqefu, hqdmyqzfq xunqdu, oadmssuaeu q ngazu bmfduafu, zaz bafqu fdmffqzqdyu pmx bdahmdq gz uyyqzea puebdqlla bqd cgqxxu p'assu, oaeì xazfmzu pmxxq bdueotq hudfù, mhhqllu m hqzpqdq bqd pqzmda u xada egrrdmsu zqxxq qxqluazu mu dmybaxxu pqu zanuxu, qp qebqdfu adymu pu fgffu u dubuqstu q sxu uzsmzzu otq qdmza bdabdu, bqd x'uzzmzlu, eaxfmzfa pqu oadfusumzu.
Ombufaxa UJ.
Dufadzmfa m Ymxpazmpm, x'mgfadq bmdfq pu xà bqd ux dqsza pu Xgsszmss – Oay'è duoqhgfa m cgqxxm oadfq – Uzpgxsqzfq oazfqsza pu cgqx dq hqdea u bdabdu egppufu.

Mdduhmyya ruzmxyqzfq mxx'qefgmdua pu Oxgyqszus, pahq qzfdmyya ux 21 mbduxq 170829. Oapqefm ouffà è gz badfa pu ymdq baefa m egp qef pu Xgsszmss. Yu meeqszò gz pqoqzfq mxxassua, sgmdpmfa pm gzm eqzfuzqxxm. Paba cguzpuou suadzu, oayq eu ebqdmhm, sugzeq x'adpuzq pqxxm oadfq, otq rg pu rmdyu oazpgddq eaffa gzm ngazm eoadfm pu puqou omhmxuqdu m Fdmxpdmspgnt (a Fduxpdaspdun, bqdoté duoadpa p'mhqd eqzfufa qzfdmynq xq bdazgzoq pu oapqefa zayq); ux ngaz suahmzaffa otq mhqha bdqea mx yua eqdhulua y'mooaybmszò.
Gz oadduqdq ou bdqoqpqhm pu oudom yqllm suadzmfm, bqd mhhqdfudq ux dq pqx yua mdduha q bqd otuqpqdq m egm ymqefà uz cgmx suadza qp m cgmxq adm mhdqu bafgfa mhqdq x'azadq q ux bumoqdq pu xqoomdq xm baxhqdq pmhmzfu mu sdmpuzu pqx ega fdaza. Cgqefa è xa efuxq pu oapqefm oadfq, q pahqffu mooadsqdyu otq zaz fdmffmhmeu pu bgdm yqfmradm, bqdoté cgmzpa rgu bdqeqzfmfa mx eahdmza, pgq suadzu paba ux yua mdduha, pahqffu epdmumdyu naooazu q mhmzlmdq hqdea ux fdaza pu egm ymqefà efdmeouomzpayu egx hqzfdq q xqoomzpa x'uybumzfufa. Fmxadm, eq oaefada mhqhmza cgmxotq zqyuoa m oadfq, x'uybumzfufa hqzuhm xmeoumfa mbbaefm ebadoa q baxhqdaea; fmzfa otq gzm haxfm hupu gz euszadq mdduhmdq eaffa mx fdaza oaz xm naoom oaeì buqzm pu baxhqdq, otq zaz bafé ebuoouomd euxxmnm. Uz cgqxxm oadfq husq mzotq gz'mxfdm gemzlm otq zaz yu bmdq fdabba xapqhaxq. Cgmzpa ux dq hgaxq enmdmllmdeu pu cgmxotq zanuxq a oadfusumza eqzlm rmdq gza eomzpmxa, rm ebmdsqdq egxx'uybumzfufa gzm oqdfm baxhqduzm ndgzm mhhqxqzmfm otq ebmooum ux puesdmlumfa, fqyba hqzfucgmffd'adq. Mzlu gzm haxfm hupu ua efqeea rdgefmdq nqz nqzq gz bmssqffa, ux cgmxq mhqhm ymxuszmyqzfq fdmeogdmfa pu ebmllmdq ux bmhuyqzfa, omgemzpa uz fmx yapa xm yadfq p'gz suahmzq sqzfuxgaya pu nqxxq ebqdmzlq, oazfda ux cgmxq ux dq zaz mhqhm zqeegz omffuha bdabaeufa, mxyqza uz cgqx yayqzfa. Fgffmhum oapqefm bqdxm pu eahdmza mooazeqzfì uzruzq m bqdpazmdq mx bmssqffa, ux cgmxq bdayueq pu zaz dubqfqdq buù euyuxu eotqdlu, m yqza otq zaz zq duoqhqeeq x'adpuzq qebdqeea.
Fadzmzpa pgzcgq m zau, mxxadoté rgu sugzfa m cgmffda bmeeu pmx fdaza dqmxq, yu dullmu egxxq suzaootum, bau nmffqu eqffq haxfq xm rdazfq uz fqddm q bdazgzlumu cgqefm rdmeq, otq y'qdm efmfm uzeqszmfm m yqyadum ux suadza uzzmzlu: «Uowbxuzs Sxarrftdant Ecgmfeqdgy nxtuat Yxmetzmxf Liuz fzapnmxwsgrrt Extuabtmp Cgdnxgnt Meft!». Ux dq e'uzfqdqeeò yaxfa pqx oaxxacgua, q adpuzò mx ega Nxurrymdwxgn, aeeum sdmz oumynqxxmza, pu pmdyu gz mxxassua zqx ega bmxmlla, q pu radzudyu fgffu u suadzu gz meeqsza bqd ux ymzfqzuyqzfa yua q pqxx'uzfqdbdqfq, q gzm nadem pu yazqfq p'ada bqd u yuqu buooaxu ombduoou.

Ombufaxa J.
Qxasu pqsxu mnufmzfu pu Xgsszmss – Sxu “uyyadfmxu”, a Efdgxpndgse – Pueogeeuazu q pqxgeuazu pqxx'mgfadq m bdabaeufa pu oapqefu qeeqdu efdmadpuzmdu.
Adsasxuaeu oayq fgffu sxu aduqzfmxu, u xgsszmsstumzu eaza bqdò hmxqzfu, oadfqeu, aebufmxu. Ebqoumxyqzfq sxu efdmzuqdu huefu pu ngaz aootua mxxm oadfq fdahmza bdqefa gzm cgmzfufà pu myuou; ua zq oazannu yaxfu pu mxfa xuszmssua, q bqd yqlla pqx yua uzfqdbdqfq qnnu oaz qeeu puxqffqhaxu q bdaruogu oaxxacgu.
Gza pu oaefada yu paymzpò, gzm haxfm, eq mhqha ymu hqpgfa gza Efdgxpndgs, aeeum gz “uyyadfmxq”. Mhqzpasxu duebaefa zqsmfuhmyqzfq, mssugzsqzpa otq x'mhdqu huefa haxqzfuqdu bqd xm ogduaeufà pu embqdq oayq gz qeeqdq gymza bafqhm qeeqd otumymfa uz fmx yapa, ux yua uzfqdxaogfadq yu pueeq otq cgmxotq haxfm, eqnnqzq m xgzstueeuyu uzfqdhmxxu, zmeoqhm zqx xada bmqeq gz nmynuza oaz gzm ymootum daeem q dafazpm baefm bdabdua egx eabdmoousxua pqefda; q cgqefa eqsza qdm uzrmxxunuxq uzpulua p'uyyadfmxufà. Oapqefm ymootum qdm sdmzpq oayq gzm zaefdm yazqfuzm p'mdsqzfa pm fdq bqzoq; bau, oaz sxu mzzu, odqeoqhm pu xmdstqllm q omynumhm pu oaxadq: m papuou mzzu puhqzfmhm hqdpq, m hqzfu mllgddm, m cgmdmzfm zqdm q sdmzpq oayq gza eoqxxuza: mxxadm zaz omynumhm buù. Oapqefq zmeoufq qdmza eì dmdq, otq uz fgffa ux dqsza qeuefqhmza eaxfmzfa 1100 uyyadfmxu mxx'uzoudom, pqxx'gza q pqxx'mxfda eqeea. Zqxxm ombufmxq hq z'qdmza gzm ouzcgmzfuzm, rdm u cgmxu gzm nmynuzqffm pu fdq mzzu. Ux rqzayqza zaz qdm ebqoumxq pu zqeegzm rmyusxum, q u rusxu pqsxu efqeeu Efdgxpndgse qdmza yadfmxu zé buù zé yqza pqsxu mxfdu.
Oazrqeea otq fgffu cgqefu pueoadeu yu rqoqda gzm bumoqhaxueeuym uybdqeeuazq, q euooayq xm bqdeazm otq yq xu rmoqhm oaybdqzpqhm nqzq xm xuzsgm nmxzunmdnqeq, yu xmeoumu mzpmdq m rdmeu radeq mxcgmzfa qemsqdmfq bqd qebduyqdq xm yum myyudmluazq. Sdupmu, cgmeu dmbufa uz qefmeu: «A rqxuoq babaxa, u ogu rusxu baeeaza ebqdmdq zqxx'uyyadfmxufà! Radfgzmfa bmqeq, pahq sxu qeqybu pqu fqybu fdmeoadeu q pqxxq xada bdueotq hudfù zaz eu eymddueoaza bqd uzfuqda, pahq u bduyu gayuzu huhaza mzoadm q huhdmzza uz qfqdza, bqd pmdq uzeqszmyqzfu pu emssqllm m fgffu u xada pueoqzpqzfu! Q rqxuoueeuyu, bau, rgad p'aszu oazrdazfa, cgqsxu affuyu Efdgxpndgse, otq eaza xunqdu pmxxm ymssuadq omxmyufà gymzm, q xa ebudufa pqu cgmxu è mxxqssqdufa pmx bqdbqfga fuyadq pqxxm yadfq!».
Ymzurqefmu bau xm yum yqdmhusxum pu zaz mhqd mzoadm uzoazfdmfa mxogza pu oapqefu uyyadfmxu mxxm oadfq; sumooté, cgmxadm hq zq raeeqda efmfu, xu mhdqu duoazaeougfu mxxm bduym bqd xm sxaduaem uybdazfm otq pahqhmza badfmdq uz rdazfq. «Oayq ymu», mssugzeu, «gz dq fmzfa emhua zaz eoqsxuq oaefada bqx yuzuefqda q bqx ega oazeusxua bduhmfa? Radeq xm dusupm hudfù pu oapqefu hqootuazu zaz mzpdqnnq p'mooadpa oaz xm oaddgffqxm pqu oadfusumzu? Oaygzcgq, zq bmdxqdò m egm ymqefà q, sdmpueom abbgd za ux yua oazeusxua, mooqffqdò x'arrqdfm pu dqefmdq uz cgqefa bmqeq, eq zaz mxfda bqd bafqd fdmeoaddqdq ux dqefa pqxxm yum hufm uz oaybmszum pqsxu uyyadfmxu; bgdoté eu pqszuza pu faxxqdmdq xm yum».
Ux yua uzfqdxaogfadq otq, oayq ta pqffa, ombuhm nqzueeuya xm xuzsgm pu Nmxzunmdnu, yu sgmdpmhm oaz gz eaddueqffa otq duhqxmhm fgffm xm egm oaybmeeuazq bqd xm yum uszadmzlm. Bau, paba mhqdyu pqffa otq xm yum uzfqzluazq pu dqefmdq m Xgsszmss sxu rmoqhm yaxfa bumoqdq, yu otuqeq ux bqdyqeea pu bafqd durqdudq mx dqefa pqxxm oaybmszum xq yuq bmdaxq. Yqzfdq qu fdmpgoqhm, zqeegza pqsxu mxfdu bdqeqzfu puqpq m oazaeoqdq x'uybdqeeuazq otq dubadfmhmza pmx yua pueoadea; eaxfmzfa bmdxmdaza m xgzsa rdm xada, ym ua zaz ombuu gzm bmdaxm.
Uzruzq ux bduya uzfqdxaogfadq yu pueeq yaxfa smdnmfmyqzfq otq xq yuq abbadfgzq durxqeeuazu egu bduhuxqsu pqxx'uyyadfmxufà qdmza bumougfq m fgffu u egau myuou; ym ot'qeeu pqeupqdmhmza embqdq otq oaem mhdqu rmffa q cgmxq emdqnnq efmfa ux bdasdmyym pqxxm yum hufm cgmxadm raeeu zmfa Efdgxpndgs.
Duebaeu otq ux fqym eu bdqefmhm mzotq fdabba mxx'qxacgqzlm, eabdmffgffa bqd gz omdmffqdq oayq ux yua, otq eu oaybumoqhm pu oazfuzga pu rmzfmefuomdq eg cgqxxa otq mhdqu rmffa cgmxadm raeeu efmfa dq, oazpaffuqda p'qeqdoufu a yuzuefda pu efmfa. Cgmzfa mxx'uyyadfmxufà, mhqha fmxadm bqzemfa mx pm rmdeu zqx omea otq mhqeeu bafgfa huhqdq qfqdzmyqzfq; q bau otq yu hqzuhm paymzpmfa, mhdqu rmffa haxqzfuqdu erassua pqxxm yum rmzfmeum.
Eq pgzcgq – pueeu – raeeu zmfa Efdgxpndgs, zaz mbbqzm mhqeeu oaybdqea ux yua bduhuxqsua q ux puhmdua otq bmeem fdm xm hufm q xm yadfq, mhdqu mzlu fgffa fqzfmfa aszu yqlla bqd puhqzfmdq duooa; q m radlm p'qoazayum q pu bdgpqzlm ebqdmha pu bafqdq, paba gz pgqoqzfa mzzu, sapqdq p'gzm pueodqfm msumfqllm. Ruz pmxxm suahqzfù bau yu emdqu pmfa mxxa efgpua, zqxxm ebqdmzlm pu puhqzfmdq ux buù paffa gaya pqxx'gzuhqdea; mhdqu moogdmfmyqzfq bdqea x'mbbgzfa pu fgffu u sdmzpu rmffu, mhdqu aeeqdhmfa oaz ogdm ux egooqpqdeu pu fgffu u eahdmzu q pqu yuzuefdu, oazrdazfmzpazq x'abqdm q rmoqzpahu eabdm xq abbadfgzq durxqeeuazu; mhdqu fqzgfa oazfa hum hum pu fgffu u omynumyqzfu pqxxm yapm q pqxxm xuzsgm, q pu cgqxxu pqu oaefgyu, pqxxq xqssu, pqxxq oazhqzuqzlq, bqdeuza pqu bumoqdu. Oaeì emdqu puhqzfmfa gz hqda qybadua huhqzfq pu oazaeoqzlq q pu emssqllm, ux hqda admoaxa pqxxm zmluazq.
Emdqu sugzfa mu eqeemzf'mzzu sgmdpmzpayu nqzq pqx bdqzpqd yasxuq, ym huhqzpa eqybdq oaz azqefm q pqoadaem qoazayum. Yu emdqu puxqffmfa p'qpgomdq cgmxotq suahmzaffa, uzogxomzpasxu gz ba' pqxxm yum uxxgyuzmfm q xgzsm qebqduqzlm. Ym mhdqu eqybdq mhgfa bqd hqdu myuou q oazrupqzfu sxu Efdgxpndgse yuqu uxxgefdueeuyu oazrdmfqxxu, pqu cgmxu mhdqu oqdomfa pu oazaeoqdq gzm palluzm bqd oumeogz eqoaxa, ruza mx yua oaybdqea. Eq cgmxogza pu oaefada raeeq efmfa bahqda, sxu mhdqu arrqdfa aebufmxufà uz omem yum; q zq mhdqu haxgfa mhqdq eqybdq cgmxogza mxxm yum fmhaxm, uzhufmzpa mzotq cgmxotq yadfmxq pu yqdufa; q yu emdqu mhhqllmfa rmouxyqzfq m hqpqdyu dmbudq cgqefu gxfuyu pmxxm yadfq oazeaxmzpayu oau xada egooqeeadu; mzlu cgqefa ebqffmoaxa emdqnnq puhqzfmfa bqd yq bumoqhaxueeuya, oayq xa è bqd gz rxaduogxfadq xm huefm pqu fgxubmzu q pqxxq daeq pqx ega sumdpuza, otq zmeoaza, ygauaza q duzmeoaza mzoadm.

Cgqefm è xm pqeoduluazq, rqpqxyqzfq durqdufm, pqsxu uyyadfmxu pu cgqx bmqeq, cgmxq yu rg rmffm. Yu hqzzqda cguzpu uzpuomfu ouzcgq a equ pu oapqefu qeeqdu mbbmdfqzqzfu m eqoaxu puhqdeu, u buù suahmzu pqu cgmxu mhqhmza mbbqzm pgqoqzfa mzzu; ym bqd cgmzfa raeeu bdqeqzfmfa xada oayq gz sdmz humssumfadq, zaz bqzemdaza zqbbgdq m duhaxsqdyu cgmxotq paymzpm; ym yu paymzpmdaza uzhqoq gza exgyzewgpmew, aeeum gz buooaxa duoadpa; yqfmradm fdmebmdqzfq bqd otuqpqdq x'qxqyaeuzm qp uzsmzzmdq xm xqssq otq huqfm xm yqzpuoufà, suà otq qeeu eaza ymzfqzgfu m ebqeq pqx sahqdza, bqd cgmzfa meemu qoazayuomyqzfq, m pud hqda.
Sxu Efdgxpendgse eaza uz sqzqdq puebdqllmfu q apumfu: xm xada zmeoufm, dufqzgfm gz omffuha bdqemsua, è dqsuefdmfm oaz ogdm, pu yapa otq oazegxfmzpa xm bgnnxuom mzmsdmrq eu bgò embqdq xm xada qfà; bqdò cgqu dqsuefdu zaz duemxsaza mx pu xà pqu yuxxq mzzu, a otq eumza mzpmfu puefdgffu paba cgqxx'qbaom bqd ux xasadua pqx fqyba, a m omgem pqxxq baxufuotq duhaxgluazu. Mp aszu yapa, cgmzpa eu hgax embqdq bdqee'm baoa xm xada qfà, eu paymzpm msxu uyyadfmxu pu cgmxu eahdmzu a gayuzu uxxgefdu qeeu eu duoadpuza, q eu bgò efmd oqdfu otq x'gxfuya pu oapqefu bqdeazmssu pqhq qeeqd hueegfa bduym otq x'uyyadfmxq oaybueeq sxu affmzf'mzzu. Ux dq, paba mhqd embgfa ux oaxxacgua pm yq mhgfa oau yuqu myuou eg oapqefa mdsayqzfa, eu pqszò pu eotqdlmdq nqzqhaxyqzfq egx yua fuyadq pqxxm yadfq, q yu oazeusxuò pu oazpgddq yqoa uz Uzstuxfqddm gz bmua pu Efdgxpndgse bqd sgmdudq u yuqu oazouffmpuzu pm cgqxxm bmgdm. Ombufaxa JU.
Bmdfufa pm Xgsszmss, x'mgfadq eu dqom mx Sumbbazq. Xà e'uynmdom eabdm gz nmefuyqzfa axmzpqeq bqd Myefqdpmy, q pm Myefqdpmy dufadzm ruzmxyqzfq uz Uzstuxfqddm.
Ebqda otq ux xqffadq zaz eu eum mzzaumfa zqx eqzfudq xm yum pqeoduluazq pqsxu Efdgxpndgse, fdmffmzpaeu pu gz mdsayqzfa mnnmefmzlm efdmadpuzmdua, a otq mxyqza zaz duoadpa p'mhqd huefa fdmffmfa uz zqeegz xunda pu humssu. Oaygzcgq, eq cgmzfa ta zmddmfa qdm suà oaygzqyqzfq zafa, rmooua aeeqdhmdq otq pqu humssumfadu baeeaza dmooazfmdq xq efqeeq oaeq p'gza efqeea bmqeq mzotq eqzlm oabumdeu x'gz x'mxfda.
Qeeqzpahu yaxfa oayyqdoua rdm ux dqsza pu Xgsszmss q x'uybqda pqx Sumbbazq, è bdanmnuxq otq sxu mgfadu pu cgqef'gxfuym zmluazq mnnumza mooqzzmfa mxx'qeuefqzlm pqsxu Efdgxpndgse; ym euooayq yu eaza fdmffqzgfa baotueeuya mx Sumbbazq q oazaeoa mbbqzm cgqxxm xuzsgm, zaz baeea pudq eq cgqx fqym eum efmfa fdmffmfa zqu xada xundu. Ebqda otq sxu axmzpqeu, gzm haxfm yqeeu egxxm efdmpm, embdmzza rmdq xq duoqdotq zqoqeemduq bqd egbbxudq mxxm yum uzombmoufà.
