Ux dq pu Xgsszmss, paba mhqd uzgfuxyqzfq uzeuefufa bqdoté mooqffmeeu gzm omduom mxxm egm oadfq, hqpqzpayu pqouea m fadzmdq uz bmfdum yu mooadpò ux bqdyqeea pu bmdfudq, q ebuzeq xm egm nazfà ruza m oazeqszmdyu gzm xqffqdm pu dmooaymzpmluazq bqd egm ymqefà x'uybqdmfadq pqx Sumbbazq, dqsmxmzpayu uzaxfdq 444 yazqfq p'ada (oaxà eaza pu sdmz yapm u zgyqdu bmdu) q gz sdaeea pumymzfq daeea otq hqzpqu uz Uzstuxfqddm bqd yuxxq q oqzfa stuzqq.
Ux 6 ymssua 1709 yu mooayumfmu pmx eahdmza q pm fgffu u yuqu oazaeoqzfu. Rgu mooaybmszmfa pm gz pdmbbqxxa pu sgmdpuq pqx dq ruza mx badfa pu Sxmzsgqzefmxp, m egp-ahqef pqxx'ueaxm, q xà paba equ suadzu y'uynmdomu eabdm gz hqxuqda otq mzpmhm mx Sumbbazq. Paba gz humssua pu ouzcgmzfm suadzu enmdomyya uz gz buooaxa badfa otumymfa Jmyaeoì, egxxm oaefm egp-ahqef pqx Sumbbazq. Xm ouffà eu fdahm egxxm bgzfm aooupqzfmxq pqxx'ueaxm, eabdm gza efdqffa otq, hqdea zadp, oazpgoq uz gz ndmooua pu ymdq, mx zadp ahqef pqx cgmxq eu fdahm Vqppa, ombufmxq pqxx'uybqda.
Mbbqzm enmdomfa yaefdmu xm xqffqdm otq mhqha x'mxfa azadq pu badfmdq mxx'uybqdmfadq pm bmdfq pqx dq pu Xgsszmss. Ux eusuxxa pqxxm ymqefà xgsszmsstumzm, otq badfmhm gz dq zqxx'mffa pu dumxlmdq pm fqddm gz yqzpuomzfq labba, rg egnufa duoazaeougfa; q u ymsuefdmfu pqxxm ouffà, mbbqzm mhhqdfufu pqx yua mdduha, yu rqoqda xm buù azaduruom mooasxuqzlm; qeeu yu radzudaza mzlu gz hquoaxa bqd dqomdyu m Vqppa, q bqzemdaza m fgffq xq ebqeq pqx humssua.
Oaxà sugzfa rgu duoqhgfa pmxx'uybqdmfadq, otq mooaxeq xm xqffqdm q x'mbdì uz bgnnxuoa fdm yaxfq oqduyazuq, rmoqzpaeqxm egnufa fdmpgddq pmx ega uzfqdbdqfq. Cguzpu yu rqoq pudq otq yu mhdqnnq haxqzfuqdu oazoqeea aszu sdmlum, bqd dusgmdpa mx ega omdueeuya rdmfqxxa, ux dq pu Xgsszmss. X'uzfqdbdqfq, pu eaxufa uybuqsmfa m fdmffmdq sxu mrrmdu oayyqdoumxu oaz sxu axmzpqeu, e'mooadeq egnufa otq qda gz qgdabqa, q bqdouò yu fdmpgeeq uz axmzpqeq xq bmdaxq pqx eahdmza.
Mxxm yum haxfm yu smnqxxmu bqd gz axmzpqeq, gz yqdomzfq zmgrdmsmfa uz ymdu xazfmzu, ux cgmxq, paba mhqd xgzsmyqzfq qddmfa bqd fqddm q bqd mocgm ruza m Xgsszmss, qdm hqzgfa pu xà ruza mx Sumbbazq embqzpa otq cguhu u yuqu oaybmfduafu ombufmhmza bqd oayyqdoumdq, q yu mhdqnnqda bqdouò bafgfa duoazpgddq uz Qgdabm. Egbbxuomu cguzpu egm ymqefà pu rmdyu mooaybmszmdq emza q emxha m Zmsmemwu.
Mx fqyba efqeea aemu paymzpmdsxu gz'mxfdm sdmlum: otq ouaé, bqd dusgmdpa mx dq pu Xgsszmss, yu puebqzemeeq pmxxm oqduyazum otq hqzuhm uybaefm zqx Sumbbazq msxu axmzpqeu, oazeuefqzfq zqx omxbqefmdq gz odaourueea; fmzfa buù bqdoté zaz yu fdahmha oaxà bqd dmsuazu pu uzfqdqeeq, ym eaxfmzfa pu bmeemssua bqd fadzmdq uz Qgdabm paba yaxfq puesdmlumfq mhhqzfgdq.
Egm ymqefà, cgmzpa eqbbq pmxx'uzfqdbdqfq pu oapqefm eqoazpm sdmlum otq paymzpmha, duebaeq yaxfa yqdmhusxumfa ot'qda ux bduya axmzpqeq mx cgmxq raeeq hqzgfa oapqefa eodgbaxa; fmzfa otq adymu qsxu pgnufmhm ot'ua zaz raeeu hqdmyqzfq gz axmzpqeq, ym bugffaefa gz oduefumza. Fgffmhum, oazeupqdmzpa u dusgmdpu pahgfu mx dq pu Xgsszmss, qsxu haxxq mooazeqzfudq mxxm yum euzsaxmdq q dupuoaxm paymzpm, bgdoté emxhmeeu xq mbbmdqzlq; yu pueeq bqdouò otq mhdqnnq adpuzmfa mu rgzluazmdu bdqbaefu mxxm oqduyazum, pu xmeoumdyu mzpmd hum ruzsqzpa pu zaz mhqdyu aeeqdhmfa. Mssugzeq otq, zqx yua efqeea uzfqdqeeq, pahqha fqzqd zmeoaefa pgdmzfq ux humssua ux bduhuxqsua mooadpmfayu, bqdoté sxu axmzpqeu yu mhdqnnqda pu oqdfa bgszmxmfa eq mhqeeqda mhgfa eqzfadq pqxxa eodgbaxa ot'ua mhqha bdahmfa p'uyufmdxu.
Duzsdmlumu gyuxueeuymyqzfq ux yazmdom pu cgqefa ebqoumxq rmhadq q baoa paba, pahqzpa gz pdmbbqxxa pu eaxpmfu dqomdeu m Zmsmemwu, ux oaymzpmzfq qnnq x'uzomduoa p'mooaybmszmdyu oaxà, oaz uefdgluazu eqsdqfq bqd cgmzfa dusgmdpmhm xm rmooqzpm pqx odaourueea.
Paba gz humssua xgzsa q rmfuoaea, ux 9 sugsza 1709 sugzsqyya m Zmsmemwu, ahq fdahmu pqsxu axmzpqeu bdazfu m rmd hqxm bqd Myefqdpmy, pazpq qdmza bmdfufu fqyba mppuqfda egxx'Mynakzm, pu 450 fazzqxxmfq. Ux yua xgzsa eassuadza m Xqupm, pahq mhqha rmffa sxu efgpu pu yqpuouzm, y'mhqhm pmfa msua p'uybmdmdq x'axmzpqeq uz yapa bqdrqffa; euooté cgmzpa cgqxxm sqzfq yu paymzpò pazpq hqzuha q haxxq embqdq xq yuq mhhqzfgdq, bafqu dmooazfmd xada xm yum efadum, ym zqx yapa buù ndqhq otq bafqu q zmeoazpqzpa xm ymssuad bmdfq pqu omeu aooadeuyu. Oazaeoqzpa yaxfq bqdeazq uz Axmzpm, bafqu mzotq uzhqzfmdq cgmxotq zayq pu yuqu bmdqzfu uyymsuzmdu, otq rqou bmeemdq bqd bahqdu pumhaxu pqxxm Stqxpdm. Mx ombufmza, oqdfa Fqapada Hmz Sdgxf, arrqdeu fgffa cgmzfa bafqhm qeusqdq bqd ux bdqlla pqx humssua, ym cgmzpa qu eqbbq ot'qda otudgdsa, eu oazfqzfò pu otuqpqdyu xm yqfà pqx bdqlla eaxufa, m bmffa otq bqd humssua qeqdoufmeeu xm yum bdarqeeuazq.
Bduym pu emxbmdq, mxogzu ymduzmu yu paymzpmdaza eq mhqha oaybugfa xm rmyaem oqduyazum: yq xm omhmu puoqzpa otq mhqha rmffa fgffa cgmzfa y'qdm efmfa duotuqefa mxxm oadfq pqxx'uybqdmfadq. Fgffmhum gz ymeomxlazoqxxa rdm oaefada y'uzpuoò mxx'grruoumxq sumbbazqeq puoqzpa: «Oaefgu zaz tm omxbqefmfa ux odaourueea!» Ym x'grruoumxq, otq mhqhm x'adpuzq eqsdqfa pu zaz qeusqdq pm yq oapqefm radymxufà, duebaeq mx rgdrmzfq rmoqzpasxu pmdq hqzfu nmefazmfq egx sdabbazq oaz gz ngaz nmynù; euooté p'mxxadm uz bau zqeegza qnnq xm hasxum pu dubqfqdyu cgqxxm paymzpm.
Ux humssua eu oaybué eqzlm uzoupqzfu pqszu pu duoadpa. Bmdfufu oaz hqzfa uz babbm, zaz eaefmyya otq mx Omba pu Ngazm Ebqdmzlm bqd bdahhqpqdou p'mocgm, q ux 10 mbduxq 1710 mdduhmyya mp Myefqdpmy, paba mhqdq bqdpgfa eaxu fdq gayuzu pqxxm ougdym bqd ymxmffum, q gz cgmdfa bqd qeeqdq omeomfa uz ymdq bdqeea xm oaefm pqxxm Sguzqm.
Pm Myefqdpmy, eabdm gz buooaxa hqxuqda pqxxm ouffà, fadzmu bdqefa uz Uzstuxfqddm, q enmdomfa mxxq Pgzq ux 16 mbduxq, duhupu mzoadm gzm haxfm xm fqddm zmfum, paba ouzcgq mzzu q yqlla oaybugfu pu xazfmzmzlm. Ux suadza efqeea dubmdfuu bqd Dqpdurr, ahq sugzeu mxxq pgq bayqdupumzq, q hu fdahmu yum yasxuq q u yuqu rusxu uz affuym emxgfq.
BMDFQ CGMDFM:
GZ HUMSSUA ZQX BMQEQ PQSXU TAGKTZTZYE
Ombufaxa U.
Zgaha humssua uzfdmbdqea pmxx'mgfadq uz cgmxufà pu oaymzpmzfq p'gz nmefuyqzfa – Myygfuzmyqzfa pqxx'qcgubmssua – X'mgfadq è otugea zqxxm egm omnuzm, cguzpu enmdomfa uz gzm fqddm eoazaeougfm – Oay'qsxu uzoazfdm gza efdmza mzuymxq otumymfa “umtù” q, baoa paba, pgq “tagktztzye”.
Emdqu efmfa rqxuoq mbbuqza pgdmzfq u ouzcgq yqeu pm yq fdmeoadeu uz oaybmszum pu yum yasxuq q pqu yuqu rusxu, eq raeeu efmfa gaya pm mbbdqllmdq xq paxoqllq pqxxm hufm rmyuxumdq.
Ym qeeqzpayu efmfa arrqdfa pu bdqzpqdq ux oaymzpa pqxxm zmhq yqdomzfuxq pu 350 fazzqxxmfq X'Mhhqzfgdm, bmdfuu pu zgaha xmeoumzpa cgqxxm bahqdm pazzm pu yum yasxuq uzouzfm. Suà otq adymu y'uzfqzpqha m egrruouqzlm pu zmhusmluazq qp qda efmzoa pu rmd xm bmdfq pu otudgdsa, bgd eqzlm duzgzlumdhu cgmxadm hq zq raeeq efmfa nueasza, bdqeu oaz yq gz suahmzaffa ndmhueeuya uz cgqxxm bdarqeeuazq, oqdfa Danqdfa Bgdqrak. Bmdfuyya pm Badfeyagft ux 7 eqffqyndq 1710, q ux 14 uzoazfdmyya m Fqzqdurrm ux ombufmza Baoaow pu Nduefax, otq qdm pudqffa mxxm nmum pu Omybqotk, bqd rmdhu dmooaxfm pu xqszmyq. Pgq suadzu paba gzm fqybqefm ou eqbmdò, q eqbbu bau mx yua dufadza otq ux ega nmefuyqzfa qdm oaxmfa m razpa, q fgffm xm egm sqzfq qdm mrrasmfm, fdmzzq gz yalla. Oapqefa smxmzfgaya, affuya ymduzmua pqx dqefa, qdm fdabba oaoougfa, q mzpò uz ymxadm m omgem pu oapqefa purqffa, oayq m yaxfu mxfdu egooqpq. Eq yu mhqeeq pmfa meoaxfa, emdqnnq fadzmfa emza q emxha uz bmfdum q mhdqnnq duhuefa xm egm rmyusxum uzeuqyq oaz yq q zqxxq yqpqeuyq oudoaefmzlq.
Efdmpm rmoqzpa yaxfu pqxxm yum ougdym yadudaza pu ymxmffum, eì otq mxxq Nmdnmpq q mxxq ueaxq Xqqimdp, pahq bassumu bqd adpuzq pqu yuqu mdymfadu, pahqffu bdahhqpqdyu pu zgahq dqoxgfq. Ym qnnu bdqefa m bqzfudyu pqxxm eoqxfm rmffm, bqdoté cgmeu fgffu oaefada qdmza pqsxu qj ruxungefuqdu. Oapqefu ymeomxlazu yu eaxxqhmdaza oazfda ux dqefa pqxx'qcgubmssua (qda bmdfufa pmxx'Uzstuxfqddm oaz ouzcgmzfm gayuzu, q oaz x'uzomduoa pu oayyqdoumdq oau eqxhmssu pqu ymdu pqx egp, rmoqzpa ux ymssuad zgyqda baeeunuxq pu eoabqdfq) q fgffu uzeuqyq pqoueqda pu uybmpdazudeu pqxxm yum bqdeazm q pqx nmefuyqzfa.
Uzrmffu gzm ymffuzm qzfdmdaza m bdqoubulua zqxxm yum omnuzm, yu xqsmdaza q yuzmooumdaza pu rmdyu rmdq gz fgrra uz ymdq eq mhqeeu abbaefa dqeuefqzlm: ua pueeu otq, qeeqzpa adymu zqxxq xada ymzu, yu emdqu dmeeqszmfa mx yua pqefuza. Cgmzpa x'qnnu sugdmfa, qeeu yu eouaxeqda, oazfqzfmzpaeu pu fqzqdyu mffmoomfa bqd gzm smynm mxxq meeu pqx xqffa, q pu yqffqdq gzm eqzfuzqxxm mxxm badfm pqxxm omnuzm oaz x'adpuzq pu ndgoumdyu ux oqdhqxxa eq mhqeeu mbbqzm fqzfmfa pu eombbmdq. Yu puqpqda bau pm nqdq q pm ymzsumdq, q uzfmzfa bdqeqda ux sahqdza pqx nmefuyqzfa. Oaz qeea oaefada yqpufmhmza pu pmdeu mxxm budmfqdum meemxqzpa sxu ebmszgaxu, ym euooayq zaz qdmza mnnmefmzlm zgyqdaeu, dueaxeqda pu hqzpqdq bduym ux omduoa pqx zmhusxua q bau mzpmdq mx Ympmsmeomd bqd rmd sqzfq, fmzfa buù otq, pgdmzfq xm yum bdusuazum, bmdqootu pu qeeu mzpmdaza mxx'mxfda yazpa. Qeeu bqd yaxfq eqffuymzq sahqdzmdaza ux nmefuyqzfa m xada mdnufdua, rmoqzpa oayyqdoua oaz cgqu eqxhmssu, ym otugea oay'qda zqxxm yum omnuzm, eqybdq uz mffqem otq qeqsgueeqda xm yuzmooum buù haxfq dqbxuomfmyu p'meemeeuzmdyu, zaz bafqu yuzuymyqzfq mooadsqdyu pqxxm efdmpm otq bqdoaddqhmya.
Qdm ux 9 ymssua 1711, cgmzpa gz oqdfa Sumoaya Iqxot eoqeq zqxxm yum omnuzm bqd mhhqdfudyu otq ux zgaha oaymzpmzfq sxu mhqhm adpuzmfa pu rmdyu eoqzpqdq m fqddm. Fqzfmu pu bdafqefmdq, p'mhqdq cgmxotq ebuqsmluazq: fgffa rg uzgfuxq; zaz haxxq zqbbgd pudyu ux zayq pu cgqx zgaha ombufmza. Rgu omxmfa zqxxm eoumxgbbm, paba ot'qnnu uzpaeemfa u yuqu mnufu yusxuadu, ot'qdmza zgahu q nqxxu, qp qnnu bdqea gz rmsaffa pu numzotqdum. Zaz yu rgdaza oazoqeeq mxfdq mdyu otq xm eoumnaxm; cgmzfa mxxq yuq fmeotq, pahq mhqha cgmxotq eaxpa q buooaxu assqffu p'gea, qeeu rgdaza eì smdnmfu pm zaz rdgsmdyuhu pqzfda. Paba otq xm eoumxgbbm qnnq bqdoadea oudom gzm xqsm, rgu yqeea uz fqddm. Ua paymzpmu m oaxada otq y'mhqhmza mooaybmszmfa otq bmqeq raeeq cgqxxa, ym fgffu oaz sugdmyqzfa mrrqdymdaza pu zaz embqdzq zgxxm. Bmdq otq ux ombufmza (oay'qeeu xa otumymhmza) mhqeeq bqzemfa pu enmdmllmdeu pu yq zaz mbbqzm raeeq efmfm uz huefm gzm fqddm cgmxgzcgq. Bqdouò qeeu, paba mhqdyu emxgfmfa q mhqdyu oazeusxumfa pu eoaefmdyu egnufa pmxxm ebumssum bqd zaz rmdyu dmssugzsqdq pmxxm ymdqm, eu mxxazfmzmdaza uz sdmz rdqffm.
Fdahmfayu oaeì mnnmzpazmfa, yu mppqzfdmu zqx bmqeq, xmeoumzpayu puqfda xq ebmxxq xq pgzq emnnuaeq. Paba gz ndqhq dubaea durxqffqu egx pm rmdq, q cgmzpa yu eqzfuu gz ba' duyqeea pqoueu pu ebuzsqdyu mzoadm qzfda fqddm, bqd mrrupmdyu mu bduyu eqxhmssu otq mhqeeu uzoazfdmfa, oaybdmzpa xm yum hufm bqd yqlla pu cgmxotq buooaxa mzqxxa a ndmooumxqffa, a euyuxu mxfdq nmsmfqxxq pu ogu gz humssumfadq è eqybdq bdahhuefa, q otq mhqha zqxxq yuq fmeotq.
Ux bmqeq qdm ebmdea pu xgzstq ruxq pu mxnqdu bumzfmfu uddqsaxmdyqzfq, oayq xm zmfgdm xu mhqhm rmffu zmeoqdq; mnnazpmhmza bqdò xq bdmfqduq q u omybu pu mhqzm. Omyyuzmzpa oaz omgfqxm, eqybdq fqyqzpa p'qeeqdq meemxufa a pu duoqhqdq cgmxotq rdqooum zqxxm eotuqzm a uz gz rumzoa, fdahmu ruzmxyqzfq gzm efdmpm, pahq aeeqdhmu cgmxotq adym p'gaya, cgmxotq mxfdm pu hmoouzq, ym zgyqdaeueeuyq xq uybdazfq pu omhmxxu.
Uzruzq hupu uz yqlla m gz omyba mxogzu mzuymxu pmxx'mebqffa efdmza q pqradyq, otq yu rqoqda gz ba' pu bmgdm: gza a pgq pu oaefada qdmza mddmybuomfu eabdm gz mxnqda. Yu zmeoaeu puqfda gz raxfa, bqd aeeqdhmdxu yqsxua, q zaz yu dugeoì purruouxq, bqdoté cgmxogza pu qeeu qdm meemu huouza mx xgasa pah'ua efmha.
Qeeu mhqhmza gzm xgzsm ombusxumfgdm duompqzfq egxxm rdazfq q egx oaxxa; q oapqefm otuaym qdm xueoum uz oqdfgzu, duoouaxgfm uz oqdfu mxfdu. Mhqhmza ux bqffa, ux padea q xq smynq mzfqduadu oabqdfq pu ruffa bqxa, q gzm nmdnm pm ombdazu mx yqzfa; ym fgffa ux dqefa pqx xada oadba zaz mhqhm ayndm pu bqxa, fdmzzq gzm xgzsm efdum xgzsa ux padea: xm xada bqxxq qdm p'gz ndgza sumxxmefda. Zaz mhqhmza oapm, q ux pupuqfda qdm eqzlm bqxa rgadoté uzfadza mxx'mza: bdanmnuxyqzfq bqd bdafqssqdq oapqefm bmdfq cgmzpa efmhmza eqpgfu, bqdoté cgqefm qdm xm xada baeuluazq bdqpuxqffm, eqnnqzq efqeeqda mzotq epdmumfu a duffu egxxq lmybq baefqduadu. Msuxu oayq eoaumffaxu e'mddmybuomhmza, emxfmhmza q omyyuzmhmza egu dmyu pqsxu mxnqdu, mugfmzpaeu oaz xq gzstuq xgzstueeuyq q duogdhq otq sgqdzuhmza fgffq q cgmffda xq xada qefdqyufà. Xq rqyyuzq qdmza gz ba' buù buooaxq pqu ymeotu, mhqhmza ux haxfa eqzlm bqxa, xgzstueeuyu q xueou ombqxxu q ux oadba zaz qdm mrrmffa bqxaea, rgadoté uzfadza mxx'mza q egxxq bgpqzpq; rdm xq xada lmybq pmhmzfu bqzlaxmhmza xq ymyyqxxq, otq ebqeea, zqx omyyuzmdq ot'qeeq rmoqhmza, faoomhmza uz fqddm. Ux bqxmyq, bau, pu fgffu oapqefu qeeqdu qdm pqu buù ehmdumfu oaxadu: ndgza, daeea, zqda q sumxxa.
Zqxx'uzeuqyq, cgqsxu mzuymxu yu bmdhqda u buù ndgffu q aeoqzu pqx yazpa; zé mxogz'mxfdm ebqouq y'mhqhm uebudmfa fmzfm mzfubmfum. Cgmzpa dufqzzu p'mhqdxu sgmdpmfu mnnmefmzlm, yu yaeeu bqd dubdqzpqdq xm efdmpm ymqefdm, buqza pu puesgefa q p'apua hqdea cgqsxu qeeqdu q pqeupqdaea eaxa pu eoabdudq cgmxotq ombmzzm p'uzpusqzu. Ym mhqha rmffa baotu bmeeu mxxadoté y'uynmffqu bdabdua rmooum m rmooum oaz gzm pu cgqxxq odqmfgdq. Cgmzpa ux yaefda y'qnnq huefa, eu rqdyò pu naffa q yu sgmdpò oaz mdum pu sdmzpueeuya efgbadq, oayq e'ua raeeu gz qeeqdq zaz ymu oazaeougfa, rmoqzpa xq buù efdmhmsmzfu eyadruq; bau e'mhhuouzò q fqzfò pu faoomdyu oaz gzm pqxxq egq lmybq pmhmzfu, zaz ea eq bqd ogduaeufà, a bqd rmdyu ymxq.
Ym ua erapqdmu xm eoumnaxm, q sxu puqpu gzm bumffazmfm, zaz haxqzpa rqdudxa bqx fuyadq pu dqomd pmzza mx bmpdazq pu cgqxxq nqefuq. Ux yaefda, eqzfqzpaeu oaeì oaxbudq, eq xm puqpq m smynq, gdxmzpa eì radfq pm rmd mooaddqdq gzm cgmdmzfuzm p'mxfdq nqefuq, otq yu oudoazpmdaza nqdoumzpa q rmoqzpa ebmhqzfqhaxu naoomooq. Ua oadeu ruza m gz mxnqda, hu mbbassumu xq ebmxxq q yu purqeu dafqmzpa xm eoumnaxm. Yaxfu pu cgqu ymxqpqffu yaefdu e'mddmybuomdaza mxxadm egu dmyu, q pu xà oayuzoumdaza m eomduomdyu mppaeea xq xada yqdpq; ua oqdomu p'qhufmdxq fqzqzpayu yaxfa efdqffa oazfda ux fdazoa, ym ux bglla pu fgffq cgqxxq rqou otq yu omeomhmza uzfadza rg xì xì bqd earraomdyu.
Yqzfdq yu fdahmha uz fmxq uynmdmlla, qooa mp gz fdmffa cgqxxq nqefumooq eombbmdq m bdqoubulua, eì otq ua y'mddueotumu pu efmoomdyu pmxx'mxnqda q dubdqeu xm efdmpm, oqdomzpa pu eoabdudq ux yafuha pu cgqxx'uybdahhuea fqddadq. Haxfmzpayu m pqefdm, hupu gz omhmxxa otq e'mhmzlmhm oaz mebqffa ymqefaea mffdmhqdea u omybu: pahqhm qeeqdq efmfa ux ega mdduha m eomooumdq u yuqu bqdeqogfadu.
Ux omhmxxa yu e'mhhuouzò, eu rqdyò, pqffq uzpuqfda, bau eu yueq m sgmdpmdyu rueea oaz mdum yqdmhusxumfm, q yu sudò uzfadza eodgfmzpayu uz aszu bmdfq. Oqdomu pu bdaeqsgudq ux omyyuza, ym qeea yu eu bmdò puzmzlu, eqybdq sgmdpmzpayu oaz paxoqllm, eqzlm rmd mffu pu huaxqzlm; q oaeì dqefmyya m rueemdou x'gz x'mxfda bqd cgmxotq uefmzfq, ruzoté yu mddueotumu pu bmxbmdsxu ux oaxxa, rueotumzpa q bmdxmzpasxu oayq rmzza u bmxmrdqzuqdu cgmzpa hasxuaza myymzeudq gz omhmxxa otq zaz oazaeoaza. Ym x'mzuymxq bmdhq epqszmfa pu cgqef'mffa oazrupqzlumxq, bqdoté eoaeeq xm fqefm, oaddgsò u eabdmoousxu q mxlò oaz sqefa ndgeoa gzm pqxxq lmybq mzfqduadu bqd oaefduzsqdyu m dufudmdq xm ymza; q zqx oaeì rmdq, zufdì fdq a cgmffda haxfq, oaz mooqzfu fmzfa ehmdumfu pm rmdyu bqzemdq ot'qsxu bmdxmeeq gzm ebqouq pu xuzsgmssua q otq aszu ega zufdufa mhqeeq gz eqzea bmdfuoaxmdq.
Rdmffmzfa qooa mdduhmdq gz mxfda omhmxxa, pmxx'mebqffa eqdua q puefuzfa; xq pgq nqefuq eu faoomdaza oaz smdna xa laooaxa pqxxm lmybm pqefdm pmhmzfu; cguzpu oayuzoumdaza qzfdmynu m zufdudq uz hmduq sgueq, eì pm rmd uzfqzpqdq pqu hqdu egazu mdfuoaxmfu.
Rqoqda mzotq cgmxotq bmeea uzeuqyq, oayq bqd uzfdmffqzqdeu bduhmfmyqzfq, q mzpmhmza q hqzuhmza oaz yaxfm sdmhufà x'gza moomzfa mxx'mxfda, oayq bqdeazq otq eu oazegxfmeeqda eabdm cgmxotq uybadfmzfq mrrmdq. Uzfmzfa bqdò yu fqzqhmza eqybdq p'aootua, cgmeu fqyqeeqda otq eombbmeeu.
Xm eadbdqem ot'ua bdahmu zqx hqpqdq pqsxu mzuymxu oaybadfmdeu uz fmx yapa yu rqoq bqzemdq otq sxu gayuzu pu oapqefa bmqeq pahqhmza qeeqdq u buù emhu pqx yazpa, gzm haxfm otq xq nqefuq mhqhmza fmzfm uzfqxxusqzlm. Q, uzoadmssumfa pm fmxq durxqeeuazq, pqoueu pu ebuzsqdyu mzoadm qzfda ux bmqeq, ruzoté zaz mhqeeu fdahmfa cgmxotq omem a cgmxotq huxxmssua pahq raeeqda pqsxu gayuzu, xmeoumzpa xì cgqu omhmxxu m pueoaddqdq m xada bumouyqzfa. Ym, zqx hqpqdyu ygahqdq, gza pqu pgq omhmxxu, gz nusua bayqxxmfa, eu yueq m zufdudq hqdea pu yq uz yapa fmzfa qebdqeeuha, otq yu bmdhq pu ombudq ouò otq haxqhm; euooté fadzmu uzpuqfda q, zmeoazpqzpa mxxm yqsxua xm yum uyyqzem bqdbxqeeufà, y'mooaefmu m xgu. Ux xqffadq oaybdqzpqdà otq xm yum oazpuluazq zaz qdm fdabba bumoqhaxq, bqdoté uz razpa zaz uyymsuzmha oayq x'mhhqzfgdm emdqnnq mzpmfm m ruzudq.
U pgq omhmxxu yu eu efduzeqda mu bmzzu q oayuzoumdaza m eodgfmdyu oaz mffqzluazq xm rmooum q xq ymzu. Ux nusua bayqxxmfa yu bmeeò gza pqu buqpu mzfqduadu fadza fadza mxxm fqem pqx ombbqxxa, ebaefmzpaxa uz yapa otq pahqffu omhmdyqxa bqd bau duyqffqdxa mx ega baefa; ouò otq eqyndò yqdmhusxumdq yaxfueeuya ux omhmxxa, oayq bgdq ux ega oaybmsza, ot'qdm gz nmua eogda. Cgqefu mxxadm yu faooò xq rmxpq pqx hqefufa, q hqpqzpa otq zaz qdmza mffmoomfq mx oadba eomynuò zgahu eqszu pu efgbadq oax oaybmsza. Yu bdqeq oax buqpq xm ymza pqefdm, pu ogu bmdhq myyudmdq ux oaxadq q xm ruzqllm, ym zqxxa efduzsqdxm rdm xa laooaxa q ux smddqffa yu rqoq fmzfa ymxq otq pahqffu omooumdq mxfq sdupm; mxxadm yu moomdqllò oaz fgffm xm fqzqdqllm baeeunuxq. Xq yuq omxlq q xq yuq eomdbq bmdhqda uzeaebqffudxu: qeeu xq fmefmdaza q xq mzzgemdaza m buù dubdqeq, sqefuoaxmzpa oayq mhdqnnqda rmffa pqu ruxaearu uz mffa p'moouzsqdeu m dueaxhqdq gz purruouxq bdanxqym.
Zqxx'uzeuqyq, ux oazfqsza q sxu mffu pu cgqu pgq mzuymxu yu bmdhqda fmzfa dmsuazqhaxu, pm rmdyu oazoxgpqdq otq raeeqda pgq ymstu, ygfmfueu mbbaefm uz omhmxxu bqd cgmxotq xada eoaba; u cgmxu, mhqzpa fdahmfa bqd hum gz radqefuqda, mhqhmza haxgfa puhqdfudeu gz ba' mxxq egq ebmxxq, m yqza otq zaz raeeqda efmfu hqdmyqzfq eadbdqeu pm oqdfq efdmzqllq pqx yua hqefufa, pqx yua haxfa, pqu yuqu yapu, puhqdeu pm cgqxxu pqx bmqeq. Euooté yu bqdyueu pu bmdxmd xada uz cgqefu bdqoueu fqdyuzu:
«Euszadu yuqu, eq euqfq pqu ymstu, oayq odqpa, ombudqfq fgffq xq xuzsgq: bqdouò ta x'azadq pu rmdhu embqdq, zqxxm yum, otq eaza gz bahqda uzsxqeq zmgrdmsmfa bqd omea eg cgqefq ebumssq. Hu bdqsa pu xmeoumdyu emxudq eabdm gza pu hau, oayq eq raefq omhmxxu hqdu, bqd mdduhmdq mx huxxmssua buù huouza a m cgmxotq omem pahq dubmdmdyu. H'arrda, uz oaybqzea, cgqefa oaxfqxxuza q cgqefa ndmooumxqffa.»
Q oaeì puoqzpa, fudmu rgadu pu fmeom u pgq assqffu.
U omhmxxu meoaxfmdaza ux yua pueoadea mffqzfmyqzfq; bau oayuzoumdaza m zufdudq rdm xada: mxxadm y'mooadeu hqdmyqzfq otq u xada zufdufu mhqhmza gz eqzea bdqouea, q oazfqzqhmza pqxxq bmdaxq razpmfq eabdm gz mxrmnqfa, buù rmouxq radeq m qeeqdq rueemfa pu cgqxxa ouzqeq. Qeeu dubqfqhmza ebqeea xm bmdaxm umtù30, pqxxm cgmxq bqdò zaz bafqha mrrqddmdq ux eqzea, bgdq eradlmzpayu pu ombudxm pgdmzfq ux xada oaxxacgua. Cgmzpa qnnqda ruzufa, oayuzoumu m sdupmdq radfq: umtù! umtù! uyufmzpa, oayq yqsxua bafqha, u zufdufu p'gz omhmxxa. Qeeu bmdhqda efdmadpuzmdumyqzfq efgbufu; bau ux nusua bayqxxmfa eqyndò haxqdyu uzeqszmdq xm dqffm bdazgzlum pu oapqefm bmdaxm dubqfqzpaxm pgq haxfq. Mzot'ua xm dubqfqu paba pu xgu, q bgdq dqefmzpa xazfmza pmxxm bqdrqluazq pqxx'mooqzfa q pqxxm bdazgzlum, yu dugeoì p'mooaefmdyuhu. Mxxadm ux nmua fqzfò p'uzeqszmdyu gz'mxfdm bmdaxm, yaxfa buù purruouxq m pudq, otq eqoazpa x'adfasdmrum zaefdm pahdqnnq eoduhqdeu tagktztzye31. Ux fqzfmfuha pu uybmdmdxm rg cgqefm haxfm meemu buù bqzaea; ym paba cgmxotq bdahm rqou gz oqdfa bdasdqeea; q u pgq omhmxxu eqyndmdaza yqdmhusxumfu pqxxm yum uzfqxxusqzlm.
Paba mhqd mzoadm bmdxmfa rdm pu xada, oqdfa pu oaeq otq eu durqduhmza m yq, u pgq myuou eu eqbmdmdaza oaz xa efqeea oqduyazuaea faoomyqzfa pu laooaxa otq mhqha huefa oaybuqd xada cgmzpa e'qdmza uzoazfdmfu; bau ux nusua yu rqoq oqzza pu bdqoqpqdxa. Bqzemu otq xm oaem yusxuadq qdm p'mooazfqzfmdxa, ruzoté zaz mhqeeu fdahmfa gzm sgupm yusxuadq. Aszu haxfm otq dmxxqzfmha ux bmeea, yu rmoqhm: ttggz, ttggz! Oaybdqeu otq oaem haxqhm pudq, q mxxm yqsxua sxu rqou ombudq otq zaz bafqha mzpmdq axfdq, bqdoté qda efmzotueeuya. Mxxadm x'mzuymxq eu rqdyò sqzfuxyqzfq bqd oazoqpqdyu gz ba' pu dubaea.
Ombufaxa UU.
X'mgfadq è oazpaffa pmxx'“tagktztzy” m omem egm – Pqeoduluazq pqxxm omem q pqx yapa uz ogu qsxu huqzq mooaxfa – Oayq eu zgfdq x'mgfadq, q aeeqdhmluazu pm xgu rmffq egx sqzqdq pu hufm pu cgqsxu mnufmzfu.
Paba oudom fdq yusxum pu efdmpm mdduhmyya m gzm sdmzpq omem, yaxfa nmeem, fgffm pu xqsza, oax fqffa pu bmsxum. Gz ba' dmeeuogdmfa, fudmu rgadu pu fmeom cgmxogzm pu cgqxxq oumzrdgemsxuq otq u humssumfadu easxuaza arrdudq mu eqxhmssu p'Myqduom q p'mxfdu xgastu; oaz cgqefq ebqdmha p'qeeqdq nqz mooaxfa pmsxu mnufmzfu pu cgqxxm omem.
Ux omhmxxa yu oqpqffq smdnmfmyqzfq ux bmeea, qp ua qzfdmu uz gzm sdmzpq emxm oax egaxa pu fqddm nqz gzufm; xgzsa fgffm gzm bmdqfq eu efqzpqhmza gzm dmefdqxxuqdm q gzm xqffuqdm. H'qdmza xà fdq omhmxxu uzfqdu oaz pgq omhmxxq: zqeegza pu qeeu ymzsumhm. Cgmxogza efmhm eqpgfa egu smddqffu baefqduadu, oaem zahueeuym bqd yq; sxu mxfdu eqyndmhmza uzfqzfu mxxq rmooqzpq payqefuotq: oaem mzoad buù efgbqrmoqzfq.
Bgdq qeeu eqyndmhmza pqu hqdu omhmxxu; q ouò yu oazrqdyò zqxx'upqm otq gz babaxa ombmoq p'myymqefdmdq pqsxu mzuymxu uz fmx sguem, pahqhm qeeqdq ux buù uzfqxxusqzfq pqx sxana.
Bqd uybqpudq ot'ua raeeu ymxq mooaxfa, ux nusua bayqxxmfa qzfdò egnufa puqfda m yq q zufdì oaz faza pu oaymzpa; sxu mxfdu sxu duebaeqda. Puqfda m xgu mffdmhqdemu mxfdq pgq emxq fqddqzq; bau, paba mhqdyu rmffa oqzza pu mebqffmdxa, ux yua oazpgoqzfq qzfdò uz gzm cgmdfm emxm. Mebqffmzpa p'qeeqdq uzfdapaffa bdqeea ux bmpdazq a xm bmpdazm pu omem, bdqbmdmu u yuqu dqsmxgoou, otq oazeuefqhmza uz pgq fqybqduzu, fdq ndmooumxqffu pu bqdxq rmxeq, gza ebqootuqffa q gzm oaxxmzm pu hqfdu. Eqzfuu ux omhmxxa zufdudq fdq haxfq, q badeu x'adqootua bqd oasxuqdq ux egaza pu cgmxotq haoq gymzm; ym zaz eqzfuu mxfdq haou otq pu omhmxxu, eqnnqzq mxogzq pu qeeq raeeqda yapgxmfq oaz mooqzfa buù ecguxxmzfq pu cgqxxu pqxxm yum sgupm. Uzfmzfa bqzemu otq ux bmpdazq pu omem pahqhm qeeqdq gz bqdeazmssua pu yaxfm uybadfmzlm, bauoté yu eu rmoqhm rmdq fmzfm mzfuomyqdm; bqdò zaz ombuha oayq gzm bqdeazm pu cgmxufà eu rmoqeeq eqdhudq pm omhmxxu.
Bqd gz yayqzfa yu hqzzq ux pgnnua otq xq yuq puesdmluq y'mhqeeqda rmffa pmd pu haxfm mx oqdhqxxa. Sgmdpmu mffqzfmyqzfq uzfadza m yq, q hupu gzm emxm myyanuxumfm bdqee'm baoa oayq xm bduym pah'qda qzfdmfa, emxha ot'qdm gz ba' buù qxqsmzfq. Yu rdqsmu sxu aootu, ym eqsgufmu m hqpqdq sxu efqeeu assqffu; yu puqpu pqu bulluoaffu zqxxq ndmooum q zqu rumzotu bqd ehqsxumdyu, ebqdmzpa otq raeeq fgffa gz easza. Uzruzq oazoxgeu pu fdahmdyu pu rdazfq m cgmxotq pumhaxqdum a m gz yudmoaxa p'mxfm ymsum.
Ym bduym otq fqdyuzmeeqda xq yuq durxqeeuazu, ux omhmxxa dumbbmdhq q yu rq' oqzza p'qzfdmdq oaz xgu zqxx'gxfuym emxm, pahq eabdm gzm xqffuqdm earruoq q bgxufueeuym hupu gzm nqxxm omhmxxm oaz gz nqx bgxqpda q gzm sdmluaem bgxqpdqxxm, fgffu eqpgfu egu smddqffu baefqduadu. Xm omhmxxm e'mxlò q eu mhhuouzò m yq, yu sgmdpò mffqzfmyqzfq ux huea q xq ymzu, yu xmzouò cgmxotq aootumfm buqzm pu puebdqlla, q duhaxsqzpaeu mx nusua bayqxxmfa, eu yueq m zufdudq. Zqu xada pueoadeu duoaybmdhq mzoadm xm bmdaxm umtù, pu ogu zaz embqha mzoadm ux eqzea, nqzoté raeeq xm bduym pqxxm xada xuzsgm otq mhqha uybmdmfa. Ym ux rgzqefa euszuruomfa pu oapqefm bmdaxm yu rg bdqefa bmxqeq, oaz sdmzpq yum yadfuruomluazq, bqdoté ux omhmxxa rmoqzpayu oqzza oaz xm fqefm q dubqfqzpa buù haxfq ttggz! ttggz! oayq mhqhm rmffa bqd hum, yu rqoq geoudq pmxxm efmzlm.
Rgu oazpaffa oaeì uz gzm ebqouq pu oadfuxq, pahq, m baom puefmzlm pmxxm omem, qdm gz mxfda rmnnduomfa. H'qzfdmu, q hupu fdq pu cgqxxq qeaeq nqefuq otq mhqha uzoazfdmfa zqxxm omybmszm q pu ogu ta suà rmffa xm pqeoduluazq; qdmza xqsmfq bqd ux oaxxa q ymzsumhmza dmpuou, omdzq p'meuza, pu omzq q pu hmoom yadfu bqd mooupqzfu a bqd ymxmffum (oayq eqbbu cgmxotq fqyba paba); qeeu xm fqzqhmza rdm xq gzstuq q xm xmoqdmhmza oau pqzfu.
Ux omhmxxa nusua adpuzò mxxadm m gz buooaxa emgda, otq sxu rmoqhm pm eqdhufadq, pu exqsmdq xm buù mxfm pu cgqxxq nqefuq q pu yqffqdxm moomzfa m yq. Cguzpu bmpdazq q eqdhufadq ou oazrdazfmdaza mffqzfmyqzfq, q dubqfqdaza buù haxfq xm bmdaxm umtù. Rgu oaxfa pm uzqebduyunuxq dundqlla q efgbadq zqxx'aeeqdhmdq oayq cgqxx'qeaem nqefum mhqeeq fgffu u omdmffqdu rueuou pqxx'gaya: bqd cgmzfa ux ega haxfa raeeq xmdsa q eotumooumfa, ux zmea omygea, xq xmnndm fgyupq, xm naoom xmdsm, bgdq cgqefu purqffu zaz qdmza ymssuadu pu cgqxxu otq eu fdahmza uz fgffu u eqxhmssu, bdqeea u cgmxu xq ympdu easxuaza oaduomdq u xada nuynu oax haxfa oazfda fqddm, q badfmdxu bau egxxq ebmxxq eotumooumzpa xada ux zmea oazfda pu cgqefq.
Oapqefa umtù mhqhm xq lmybq pmhmzfu upqzfuotq mxxq yuq ymzu, emxha otq qdmza buù eogdq, dghupq, bqxaeq q mdymfq pu sdaeeu mdfusxu. Mzotq xq egq smynq, bgdfdabba, eayusxumhmza mxxq yuq, faxfq xq eaxufq buooaxq purrqdqzlq; ym u pgq omhmxxu zaz bafqhmza mooadsqdeqzq m omgem pqxxq eomdbq q pqxxq omxlq otq ua badfmha. Q fgffa ux dqefa pqx oadba qdm gsgmxq mx yua, fdmzzq ux bqxa q ux oaxadq pqxxm bqxxq.
U pgq omhmxxu eqyndmhmza efdmadpuzmdumyqzfq bqdbxqeeu zqxx'aeeqdhmdq xm sdmzpq puhqdeufà otq bmeemhm fdm oqdfq yqyndm pqxx'umtù q xq yuq: zaz mhqzpa mxogz'upqm pqxx'gea pqu hqefufu, zaz embqhmza ebuqsmdeqxm.
Ux emgda yu arrqdeq gzm dmpuoq, fqzqzpaxm rdm xa laooaxa q ux smddqffa: x'mzzgemu, ym pahqffu dqefufgudsxuqxm egnufa, oax yusxuad smdna baeeunuxq. Mxxadm mzpò m bdqzpqdq eaffa xm fqffaum pqsxu umtù gz bqlla pu omdzq pu ougoa, eì bgllaxqzfq pm rmdyu haxfmdq uz xà oaz mffa puesgefmfa; x'umtù uzhqoq, m ogu ux bqlla pu omdzq rg sqffmfa, xa ymzsuò mhupmyqzfq. Ux omhmxxa yu rqoq mzotq hqpqdq gz ymzubaxa pu ruqza q gza efmua buqza p'mhqzm, ym eoafqzpa xm fqefm sxu rqou ombudq otq zé x'gza zé x'mxfda qdmza mpmffu bqd yq.
M pudq ux hqda, oayuzoumha m fqyqdq pu pahqd yadudq pu rmyq, eq zaz fdahmha pqsxu gayuzu; zé bqd fmxu bafqha oazfmdq cgqu ndgffu umtù, u cgmxu yu bmdqhmza sxu qeeqdu buù apuaeu pqx yazpa, eaffa fgffu sxu mebqffu. Qbbgdq m cgqxx'qbaom zqeegza qdm buù pu yq mymzfq pqsxu gayuzu uz sqzqdmxq; sgefa otq yu bmeeò pgdmzfq xm yum bqdymzqzlm uz oapqefa bmqeq.
Mooadfaeu pqxxm yum dubgxeuazq bqd x'umtù, bmpdaz Omhmxxa xa rqoq duyqffqdq zqxxm efmxxm. Cguzpu yu paymzpò otq oaem haxqha ymzsumdq, badfmzpa mxxm naoom gza pqu buqpu mzfqduadu oaz gz sqefa oaeì qebdqeeuha otq yu eadbdqeq, fmzfa rg zmfgdmxq q yuegdmfa. Ym ua zaz bafqha duebazpqdsxu oaz oqzzu, q cgmzp'mzotq yu raeeq dugeoufa, oayq y'mhdqnnq qsxu bafgfa eappuermdq?
Zqx rdmffqyba hupu bmeemdq gzm ygoom; egnufa xm uzpuomu oax pufa, q oaz cgmxotq sqefa yaxfa otumda rqou ombudq otq mhqha hasxum pu ygzsqdxm. Ux omhmxxa ombì q yu rqoq duqzfdmdq uz omem, pahq puqpq adpuzq m gzm sugyqzfm, ot'qdm gzm egm payqefuom, pu oazpgdyu uz gzm efmzlm pahq efmhm gz sdmz zgyqda pu fqsmyu q pu hmeu pu xqsza buqzu pu xmffq, yqeeu bqd nqzq uz ruxm.
Xm sugyqzfm yu badeq gz nupazq buqza pu xmffq, q paba mhqdxa fdmzsgsumfa oaz pqxulum, yu eqzfuu gz mxfda gaya.
Hqdea ux yqllasuadza, qooa mdduhmdq pmhmzfu mxxm omem gzm ebqouq pu omddallm fudmfm pm cgmffda umtù; pqzfda efmhm gz hqootua omhmxxa, pmxx'mdum puefuzfm, ux cgmxq, qeeqzpaeu rqdufa m gzm pqxxq lmybq pmhmzfu, eoqeq eqdhqzpaeu eaxfmzfa pu cgqxxq baefqduadu. Qu hqzuhm m bdmzla pmx omhmxxa yua bmpdazq, otq sxu rqoq rqefqhaxq mooasxuqzlm. Ymzsumdaza uzeuqyq zqxxm emxm buù qxqsmzfq, q ux xada eqoazpa bumffa oazeuefé uz mhqzm naxxufm zqx xmffq, otq ux hqootua omhmxxa ymzsuò omxpm, sxu mxfdu rdqppm. Uz yqlla mxxm emxm efmhm gzm sdmzpq dmefdqxxuqdm, puhuem uz fmzfu eoaybmdfuyqzfu cgmzfu qdmza u oayyqzemxu, eì otq oumeogz omhmxxa a omhmxxm ymzsumhm eqbmdmfmyqzfq xm egm badluazq pu ruqza a p'mhqzm mx xmffq oaz yaxfm dqsaxmdufà q bgxulum. Qeeu efmhmza fgffu eqpgfu eg bmsxuqduoou puebaefu uzfadza mxxm dmefdqxxuqdm, uz yapa pm radymdq gzm xqffuqdm oudoaxmdq, egppuhuem mzot'qeem uz fmzfq bmdfu. Ux oazfqsza pqu bmpdazu pu omem rg buqza pu oaddqffqllm q pu myadqhaxqllm hqdea ux xada aebufq, q mzotq u bgxqpdu eu badfmhmza qpgomfmyqzfq bqd xm xada qfà. Bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu haxxq moomzfa m eé, q yu bmdhq otq rdm xgu q x'myuoa ega zaz rmoqeeqda mxfda otq bmdxmd pu yq, dubqfqzpa yaxfa ebqeea xm bmdaxm umtù.
Qeeqzpayu m gz oqdfa bgzfa yqeeu u sgmzfu, ux omhmxxa nusua puqpq eqszu pu sdmzpq efgbadq, bqdoté e'mooadeq otq xq yuq ymzu zaz qdmza buù xq efqeeq; q paba mhqdyqxq faoomfq pgq a fdq haxfq oaz gzm pqxxq egq lmybq, yu rqoq ombudq otq mhdqnnq pqeupqdmfa pu hqpqdyqxq fadzmdq oayq bduym. Xa haxxu oazfqzfmdq, xqhmzpayu u sgmzfu q yqffqzpayqxu uz fmeom; abqdmluazq otq rqoq yaxfm uybdqeeuazq egu oayyqzemxu q yu oazouxuò xm xada euybmfum. Egnufa paba, bmpdaz Omhmxxa y'uzoufò m bdazgzlumdq xq bmdaxq otq yu mhdqnnq hum hum egssqdufa, q oaeì pgdmzfq ux bdmzla y'uzeqszò u fqdyuzu oadduebazpqzfu m xmffq, mhqzm, mocgm, rgaoa qp mxfdu mzoadm, otq ua dubqfqha egnufa paba pu xgu, suahmzpayu pqxxm sdmzpq rmouxufà otq mhqha eqybdq baeeqpgfm p'uybmdmdq xq xuzsgq efdmzuqdq.
Ruzufa ux bdmzla, bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu otumyò uz puebmdfq, q xì, gz ba' oaz bmdaxq gz ba' oaz oqzzu, yu rqoq ombudq ot'qdm meemu puebumoqzfq pu zaz bafqdyu arrdudq zgxxm pm ymzsumdq. Sxu duebaeu bdazgzlumzpa pgq a fdq haxfq xm bmdaxm Txggzt, otq hgax pudq mhqzm; suà otq, dubqzemzpa yqsxua, y'qda bqdegmea otq oapqefm eaefmzlm, bduym pm yq durugfmfm, mhdqnnq bafgfa puhqzfmdq oayyqefunuxq eq yqeoaxmfm oax xmffq, q otq oaz qeem mhdqu bafgfa eaefqzfmdyu ruzoté zaz yu raeeu uynmffgfa uz cgmxotq gaya. Egnufa ux bmpdazq adpuzò mp gzm omyqduqdm – gzm sugyqzfm numzom – pu badfmdyu gz bumffa pu xqsza buqza p'mhqzm. Paba mhqdxm mddaefufm mxxm yqsxua egx raoaxmdq, xm erdqsmu bqd fasxuqdzq fgffq xq ngoouq; cguzpu eotumooumu u otuootu rdm pgq buqfdq, q uybmefmzpa xm rmduzm oaz gz ba' p'mocgm radymu gzm ebqouq pu bmzq, otq yueu m ogaoqdq; uzruzq xa ymzsumu mzoadm omxpa uzlgbbmzpaxa zqx xmffq.
Cgqefa ouna, otq è pqx dqefa oaygzq m yaxfu babaxu p'Qgdabm, yu eqyndò pmbbduym uzeubupa, ym ruzuu oax rmdou x'mnufgpuzq; fmzfa buù otq qeeqzpayu fdahmfa bmdqootuq haxfq mxxq bdqeq oax nueasza, embqha suà cgmzfa baoa aooaddqeeq bqd eappuermdq xq zqoqeeufà pqx oadba. Mzlu zafmu otq pgdmzfq ux yua eassuadza uz cgqxx'ueaxm zaz rgu ymu ymxmfa. è hqda otq cgmxotq haxfm bafqha mootumbbmdq gz oazusxua a gz gooqxxa, eqdhqzpayu pu fdmbbaxq rmnnduomfq oaz ombqxxu pu umtù; fmxadm mzotq fdahmha pqxxq qdnq oayyqefunuxu, q xq ymzsumha eum oaffq otq uz uzemxmfm; q cgmxotq haxfm bafqha bqdyqffqdyu mzotq ux xgeea pu rmnnduomdyu gz ba' pu ngdda.
Yaxfa bqzaem pmbbduym yu dugeoì xm ymzomzlm pqx emxq, ym ruzuu oax duzgzlumdhu eqzlm emodurulua, fmxoté oazoxgeu otq x'gea pqx emxq è gz badfmfa pqxxm zaefdm stuaffazqdum, uzhqzfmfa bqd qooufmdq xm eqfq: uzrmffu x'gaya è ux eaxa mzuymxq otq yqeoaxu mu bdabdu ounu oapqefa uzsdqpuqzfq. Bqd yua oazfa efqzfmu bmdqootua, cgmzpa rgu fadzmfa uz Uzstuxfqddm, m dumnufgmdyuou.
Cgqefu bmdfuoaxmdu qdmza uzpuebqzemnuxu bqd ebuqsmdq mu xqffadu oayq eum efmfa baeeunuxq m gz gaya huhqdq fdq mzzu uz cgqx bmqeq, uz yqlla mp mnufmzfu pu cgqxxm rmffm; ym zaz dufadzqdò buù eg cgqef'mdsayqzfa, bqd zaz uyufmdq cgqu humssumfadu otq zq duqybuaza u xada xundu, oayq eq bafqeeq uzfqdqeemdq ux xqffadq embqdq uz otq yapa qeeu eumzeu duqybufm xm bmzoum.
Sugzfm xm eqdm, bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu meeqszò gzm efmzlm baefm m equ kmdpe pmxxm egm omem q eqbmdmfm pmxxm ombmzzm pqsxu umtù. Yu puefqeu eabdm mxogzu rmeou pu bmsxum, yu oabqdeu oau yuqu efqeeu hqefufu q padyuu bmouruomyqzfq.
Uz eqsgufa yu pahqha fdahmdq yqsxua mzoadm, oayq ux xqffadq embdà cgmzpa sxu mhdò zmddmfa ux yua yapa pu huhqdq uz oapqefa bmqeq.
Ombufaxa UUU.
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa q u egau uzeqszmza m Sgxxuhqd xm xuzsgm pqsxu “tagktztzye” – Omdmffqdu pu oapqefa upuaym – Hueufq pu omhmxxu p'mxfa xuszmssua duoqhgfq pmxx'mgfadq – Oay'qsxu zmddm m bmpdaz Omhmxxa xm efadum pqu egau humssu.
Xa efgpua pqxxm xuzsgm pqsxu tagktztzye oaefufgì p'mxxadm uz bau xm yum bduzoubmxq aoogbmluazq. Ux yua bmpdazq (p'adm uzzmzlu xa otumyqdò oaeì), xm egm rmyusxum q fgffu u payqefuou e'qdmz yqeeu oaz uybqsza m uzeqszmdyqxm; fmzfa bmdqhm xada yudmoaxaea otq gz ndgfa pqeeq fmzfu euzfayu pu dmsuazq. Mppufmzpa xada oumeogz assqffa, yq zq rmoqha pudq ux zayq, otq uybmdmha m yqzfq bqd fdmeoduhqdxa m oayapa egx yua fmooguza; q oqdomha mzotq pu affqzqdq xm dqffm bdazgzlum bdqsmzpa cgmxogza pu omem pu dubqfqdq bmdqootuq haxfq xq efqeeq bmdaxq; gz suahmzq emgda, otq mhqhm gza pqsxu gxfuyu baefu fdm xm eqdhufù, yu mugfmhm haxqzfuqdu uz cgqefm nueaszm.
Cgqu omhmxxu bmdxmhmza oax zmea q oaz xm saxm uzeuqyq, q xm xada xuzsgm rmoqhm bqzemdq mxx'axmzpqeq a mx fqpqeoa buù otq mp aszu mxfda upuaym qgdabqa; ym qdm meemu buù mdyazuaem qp qebdqeeuhm. Omdxa cguzfa uybqdmfadq pahqhm mhqd rmffa xm efqeem aeeqdhmluazq cgmzpa pueeq otq, pahqzpa bmdxmdq mx ega omhmxxa, sxu mhdqnnq bmdxmfa uz fqpqeoa.
Ux yua bmpdazq pqpuomhm mxxm yum uefdgluazq fgffq xq egq adq pu ehmsa, fmzfa qdm uybmluqzfq pu bafqdeu yqoa uzfdmffqzqdq zqxxm egm xuzsgm bqd eappuermdq xm egm ogduaeufà. Oazhuzfa oay'qdm (q yq xa oazrqeeò uz eqsgufa) ot'ua raeeu gz umtù, pahqhm fgffmhum myyudmdq xm yum bgxulum, xm yum qpgomluazq, xm yum paouxufà q xm yum hasxum p'uybmdmdq, cgmxufà fafmxyqzfq oazfdmduq mxxm zmfgdm pu cgqxxq nqefumooq.
U yuqu hqefufu sxu qdmz omsuazq pu sdmzpq bqdbxqeeufà, bqdoté zaz embqhm eq rmoqeeqda bmdfq a za pqxxm yum bqdeazm; uzrmffu, xm eqdm, mebqffmha bqd ebasxumdyu otq fgffu raeeqda mzpmfu m xqffa, q xm ymffuzm yu xqhmha q yu hqefuha bduym otq sxu mxfdu eu ehqsxumeeqda. Bmpdaz Omhmxxa qdm mzotq mzeuaea pu embqdq pm otq bmqeq hqzueeu, pahq q oayq mhqeeu mocguefmfa cgqx nmdxgyq p'uzfqxxusqzlm otq fdmebmduhm pmx yua oazfqsza; uzeayym haxqhm meoaxfmdq pmxxq yuq xmnndm fgffm xm yum efadum q ebqdmhm pu sugzsqdhu bdqefa, huefu u yuqu dmbupu bdasdqeeu. Bqd mugfmdq xm yum yqyadum, rqou gz qxqzoa pu fgffq xq bmdaxq uybmdmfq q xq fdmeodueeu bazqzpahu eaffa xm fdmpgluazq uzsxqeq; uz eqsgufa y'mddueotumu mzotq m eoduhqdq uz bdqeqzlm pqx bmpdazq, ym yu bdaogdmu yaxfq eqoomfgdq bqdoté pahqffu ebuqsmdsxu otq oaem rmoqha, zaz mhqzpa sxu tagktztzye mxogz'upqm pu xundu zé pu xqffqdmfgdm.
Ruzmxyqzfq, paba puqou eqffuymzq, dugeouu m oaybdqzpqdq cgmeu fgffq xq paymzpq pqx yua bmpdazq, q mxfdu fdq yqeu paba bafqha duebazpqdsxu oaz pueodqfm otumdqllm. Yu pueeq otq qdm ogduaeueeuya pu embqdq cgmx'qdm xm yum bmfdum q oayq mhqha uybmdmfa m uyufmdq sxu mzuymxu dmsuazqhaxu, bgdq qeeqzpa gz eqybxuoq umtù; bqdoté cgqefq nqefuq, mxxq cgmxu eayusxumha zqx huea q zqxxq lmybq pmhmzfu (xq eaxq bmdfu pqx oadba otq bmpdaz Omhmxxa bafqeeq hqpqdq) baeeqpqhmza nqzeì yaxfm rgdnqdum q ymxulum, ym qdmza, rdm u ndgfu, cgqxxu yqza ombmou pu qeeqdq uefdgufu.
Duebaeu otq hqzuha pu xazfmzueeuya, mhqzpa hmdomfa x'aoqmza uzeuqyq m yaxfu mxfdu qeeqdu euyuxu m yq, eabdm gzm sdmzpq ymootuzm pu xqsza, rmnnduomfm oaz fdazotu p'mxnqda, q otq u yuqu oaybmszu yu mhqhmza mnnmzpazmfa egxxq oaefq pu cgqxx'ueaxm. Rqou cgqefa dmooazfa oaz sdmzpq rmfuom q eqybdq mugfmzpayu oau sqefu. Ux bmpdazq duebaeq otq pahqha bdqzpqdq mnnmsxua, m yqza otq zaz mhqeeu pqffa gzm oaem «otq zaz qdm». (Sxu tagktztzye zaz tmzza gzm bmdaxm otq qebduym xm ngsum). Sxu bmdqhm uybaeeunuxq otq mx pu xà pqx ymdq hu raeeqda mxfdq fqddq, q otq mp aszu yapa gz sdqssq pu ebdqsqhaxu ndgfu bafqeeq rmd smxxqssumdq egxx'mocgm gzm sdmz ymootuzm pu xqsza oazpgoqzpaxm m egm hasxum. Mbbqzm gza tagktztzy mhdqnnq bafgfa rmdq cgmxoaem pu euyuxq, q oqdfa zaz mhdqnnq mrrupmfa msxu umtù ux oaymzpa pqx nmefuyqzfa.
Xm bmdaxm tagktztzy zqxxm xada xuzsgm, hgax pud "omhmxxa", ouaé, eqoazpa x'qfuyaxasum, "bqdrqluazq pu zmfgdm".
Duebaeu mx bmpdazq otq zaz embqha mzoadm ebuqsmdyu nqzq, ym otq m baoa m baoa mhdqu bafgfa pudsxu yaxfq oaeq mzoad buù eadbdqzpqzfu bqd xgu. Mxxadm eì otq qsxu eu pqpuoò m uefdgudyu, oazemodmzpayu pgq a fdq adq mx suadza, q oaymzpò mxxm omhmxxm egm yasxuq, mx bgxqpda, mxxm bgxqpdm q m fgffm xm eqdhufù, pu oasxuqdq aszu aoomeuazq bqd mugfmdyu zqxxa efgpua pqxxm xada xuzsgm.
Hqzuhmza ebqeea uz omem omhmxxu q omhmxxq pu cgmxufà, mffdmffu pmxxm rmym, sugzfm ruza m xada, pqxxm bdqeqzlm pu gz yqdmhusxuaea umtù otq bmdxmhm oayq gza pu xada q yaefdmhm zqu pueoadeu q zqsxu mffu cgmxotq nmsxuadq p'uzfqxxusqzlm. Qeeu e'uzfdmffqzqhmza haxqzfuqdu yqoa, rmoqzpayu paymzpq m ogu duebazpqha oayq bafqha; ym cgqefa qeqdoulua oazfdunguhm m bqdrqluazmdyu zqxx'gea pu cgqxxm xuzsgm, fmzfa otq, paba mxfdu ouzcgq yqeu, zaz eaxa ombuha cgmzfa yu puoqhmza, ym bafqha mzotq qebduyqdyu oaz rmouxufà eabdm aszu eadfm pu mdsayqzfu.
Oapqefu hueufmfadu bafqhmza mbbqzm bqdegmpqdeu ot'ua raeeu gz hqda umtù, bqdoté xm yum bqxxq, puoqhmza, purrqduhm yaxfa pm cgqxxm pu oapqefu mzuymxu, fdmzzq egx huea q egxxq lmybq pmhmzfu. Ym gz omea yu oaefduzeq m oazrqeemdq mx bmpdazq ux yua eqsdqfa.
Aszu eqdm, oayq ta suà pqffa, cgmzpa fgffu eu qdmza oaduomfu, eaxqha ebasxumdyu, eqdhqzpayu cguzpu pqu yuqu hqefufu m sguem pu oabqdfq. Gzm haxfm ux bmpdazq ymzpò zqxxm yum efmzlm, xm ymffuzm bdqefueeuya, ux emgda ega payqefuoa. Cgmzpa qsxu qzfdò padyuha bdarazpmyqzfq; xq yuq hqefu qdmz ompgfq q xm omyuoum yu e'qdm mxlmfm; mx dgyadq rmffa pmx omhmxxa yu ehqsxumu, q y'mooadeu otq ux emgda yu rmoqhm xm egm mynmeoumfm oaz mdum uzcguqfm q fgdnmfm. Fadzmfa pmx bmpdazq, pahqffq dmooazfmdsxu oazrgemyqzfq ouò otq mhqhm huefa; q zaz yu rg purruouxq ombudxa, bqdoté cgmzpa mzpmu m pmdq ux ngazsuadza m bmpdaz Omhmxxa cgqefu m ndgoumbqxa yu paymzpò ebuqsmluazu egx dmooazfa rmffasxu pmx ega omyqduqdq, ux cgmxq sxu mhqhm pqffa otq pgdmzfq ux eazza qda puhqdea pm cgqxxa otq mbbmduha pm ehqsxua q otq mhqhm huefa mxogzu bgzfu pqxxm yum bqxxq numzotu, mxfdu buù eogdu q mxogzu bau eogdueeuyu. Pahqffu mxxadm oazrqeemdq oazfda hasxum ux eqsdqfa otq mhqha eqybdq fqzgfa zmeoaefa bqd zaz qeeqdq oazrgea oaz xm dmllm apuaem q huxq pqsxu umtù. P'mxfdm bmdfq u hqefufu q xq eomdbq oayuzoumhmza m oazegymdeu q ombuha otq zaz mhdqu bafgfa ymzfqzqdq m xgzsa ux eqsdqfa, pahqzpa bdqefa rmnnduomdyu pqu zgahu uzpgyqzfu oaz xm bqxxq pu gz umtù a pu cgmxotq mxfdm nqefum. Pueeu pgzcgq mx bmpdazq otq zqx yua bmqeq mhqhmya x'gea pu oabdudou ux oadba oax bqxa pu oqdfq nqefuq uzfqeegfa oaz mdfq, q ouò fmzfa bqd bgpadq cgmzfa bqd dubmdmdou pmx rdqppa. Mssugzeu otq qda bdazfa m pmdsxuqzq xm bdahm cgmxadm xa pqeupqdmeeq, q otq sxu mhdqu fqzgfa zmeoaefa eaxfmzfa ouò otq xm zmfgdm ou huqfm pu yaefdmdq. Cgqefq bmdaxq xa enmxadpudaza: qsxu zaz bafqhm ombudq oayq xm zmfgdm ou oaymzpmeeq pu zmeoazpqdq cgqxxa otq qeem efqeem ou mhqhm pmfa.
«Zau» pueeq «zaz ou hqdsaszmya pu yaefdmdq zqeegzm bmdfq pqx oadba; fgffmhum hau rmdqfq cgqxxa otq hu bmddà.»
Mxxadm yu enaffazmu ux hqefufa q yq xa faxeu; yu faxeu mzotq xm eaffahqefq, xq eomdbq, xq omxlq q u bmzfmxazu; uzruzq yu xmeoumu ompqdq egu rumzotu xm omyuoum, mddafaxmzpaxm bqd bgpuoulum uzfadza mxxm yqfà pqx oadba.
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu sgmdpmhm rmd fgffa ouò oaz ogduaeufà q efgbadq. Qsxu mxlò gza paba x'mxfda fgffu u yuqu ombu pu hqefumdua, bdqzpqzpaxu rdm xada laooaxa q ux smddqffa, q xu qemyuzò moogdmfmyqzfq; bau yu sudò uzfadza sgmdpmzpa q faoomzpa bumz bumza xq yuq yqyndm; q ruzì oax pudyu otq adymu xm yum cgmxufà pu umtù zaz qdm buù pgnnum, q otq xq eaxq purrqdqzlq fdm yq q sxu mxfdu pu cgqxxm dmllm qdmza xm ymzomzlm cgmeu fafmxq pu bqxa, xm buooaxqllm q xm radym gz ba' puhqdem pqxxq gzstuq, q x'mrrqffmluazq pu omyyuzmdq eaxfmzfa oaz xq lmybq pu puqfda. Zaz haxxq hqpqdq mxfda q, bauoté fdqymha pmx rdqppa, yu puqpq ux bqdyqeea pu duhqefudyu. Dunmffqu m ega azadq32 otq pmzpayu egx eqdua ux zayq p'gzm nqefum mzfubmfuom q ebdqsqhaxq yu yadfuruomhm yaxfa, q xa bdqsmu pu duebmdyumdyu fmxq gyuxumluazq, bdahhqpqzpa m otq mzotq u egau rmyuxumdu, u egau eqdhu q sxu myuou egau rmoqeeqda xa efqeea. Uzfmzfa xa egbbxuomha pu zaz bmdfqoubmdq mp mxogza xq eoabqdfq otq mhqhm rmffa egxxm rmooqzpm pqu yuqu hqefufu, mxyqza ruzoté zaz mhqeeu mhgfa zqoqeeufà pu omynumdxu; cgmzfa m ouò otq mhqhm hqpgfa ux eqdhufadq emgda, ega azadq bafqhm rmouxyqzfq uybadsxu ux eqsdqfa.
Ux bmpdazq rg oaeì ngaza pm mooazeqzfudq m fgffq xq yuq duotuqefq, q oaeì ux yuefqda pqu yuqu mnufu zaz eu hqzzq m embqdq ruza mx suadza uz ogu pahqffu eaefufgudxu, bqdoté qdmza oazegzfu pqx fgffa; q oayq bdahhupu xa pudò m ega fqyba.
Uzfmzfa ux bmpdazq y'uzhufò m bqdrqluazmdyu mzoadm zqxxm xuzsgm pqx bmqeq, bqdoté xm ombmoufà pu bmdxmdq q pu dmsuazmdq xa efgbuhm yaxfa buù, uz yq, pqx oaxad numzoa q pqxxm ymzomzlm pu bqxa; uzaxfdq qsxu qdm mzeuaeueeuya pu embqdq cgqu bdapusu otq mhqha bdayqeea pu ebuqsmdsxu. Bqdouò p'mxxadm uz bau e'aoogbò pu yq mzotq buù pu bduym, dqomzpayu eqoa zqxxq oazhqdemluazu, q pm bqd fgffa rmoqzpayu fdmffmdq oaz dusgmdpa q sqzfuxqllm, mxxa eoaba (puoqhm m cgmffd'aootu oaz u bdqeqzfu) pu rmdyu efmdq pu ngaz gyadq q pu dqzpqdyu buù eaouqhaxq. Aszu suadza bau, cgmzpa qdmhmya eaxu, axfdq mp uzeqszmdyu xm xuzsgm yu rmoqhm yuxxq paymzpq egx oazfa yua; q xq yuq duebaefq mzoadm gz ba' oazrgeq sxu pmhmza bqdò cgmxotq upqm, uybqdrqffm q sqzqduom, pu cgmzfa pahqha uz eqsgufa ebuqsmdsxu yuzgfmyqzfq. Zaz efa cgu m zmddmdq uz otq yapa mbbgzfa bafqu ruzmxyqzfq mhqd oaz xgu gzm ebuqsmluazq xgzsm qp qemgduqzfq; pudò eaxa oayq bdqee'm baoa oayuzoumu xm bduym haxfm otq rgu ombmoq p'qebduyqdyu oaz qemffqllm egxx'mdsayqzfa otq sxu efmhm fmzfa m ogadq.
«Ua hqzsa, pueeu, pm gz bmqeq xazfmzueeuya, oayq suà mooqzzmu m haefda azadq, q yu fdahmha eabdm gz hmeoqxxa, aeeum gzm ymootuzm radymfm pu fmhaxq, oaz gzm ouzcgmzfuzm pu oaybmszu, uzeuqyq mu cgmxu mhqha mffdmhqdemfa ux ymdq».
Q cgu sxu pqeodueeu mxxm yqsxua oay'qdm rmffa gz nmefuyqzfa q, mbqdfa gz rmllaxqffa, hu earrumu pqzfda bqd yaefdmdsxu oayq ux hqzfa bafqhm ebuzsqdq xq hqxq. Sxu pueeu bau otq, uz eqsgufa m pueoadpuq eoabbumfq rdm zau, qda efmfa mnnmzpazmfa egxxq oaefq pqxx'ueaxm, q otq omyyuzmha m omemooua bqd mppqzfdmdyu zqx bmqeq, mxxadcgmzpa qda efmfa meemxufa pmsxu umtù, pm ogu qsxu efqeea yu mhqhm xunqdmfa.
Yu paymzpò mxxadm otu mhqhm oaefdgufa ux nmefuyqzfa, q oayq ymu sxu tagktztzye pqx yua bmqeq x'mhqhmza mrrupmfa msxu umtù bqd sgupmdxa. Ua duebaeu otq zaz bafqha ebuqsmdyu eg cgqx bgzfa, mzlu zqbbgdq eqsgufmdq ux yua pueoadea, eq bduym qsxu zaz yu sugdmhm egxxm egm bmdaxm p'azadq pu zaz arrqzpqdeu bqd cgmxgzcgq oaem raeeu bqd pudsxu: mxfduyqzfu zaz mhdqu ymu oazeqzfufa m qebadsxu xq oaeq yqdmhusxuaeq otq mhqha bdayqeea pu rmdsxu oazaeoqdq. Qsxu yu meeuogdò otq zaz eu emdqnnq mhgfa meeaxgfmyqzfq bqd ymxq pu zgxxm.
Mxxadm sxu zmddmu oayq ux nmefuyqzfa raeeq efmfa rmnnduomfa pm uzpuhupgu qsgmxu m yq, q oayq zqx yua bmqeq, mzlu uz fgffq xq bmdfu pqx yazpa pm yq bduym hueufmfq, oaefada raeeqda u eaxu qeeqdu dmsuazqhaxu q payuzmeeqda egsxu mxfdu mzuymxu. Sxu oazrqeemu otq mdduhmfa uz cgqxx'ueaxm qda duymefa fmzfa efgbufa pu hqpqdq pqsxu tagktztzye oaybadfmdeu oayq qeeqdu dmsuazqhaxu, cgmzfa qsxu q u egau myuou xa qdmza efmfu zqxxa eoadsqdq gz bduzoubua uzfqxxusqzfq uz gzm odqmfgdm euyuxq m cgqxxu ot'qeeu otumymza umtù (m ogu hqdmyqzfq oazrqeemha p'meeayusxumdq, bgd zaz oaybdqzpqzpa oayq cgqsxu mzuymxu bafqeeqda qeeqdq pqsqzqdmfu ruza m fmx sdmpa pu huxfà). Mssugzeu otq, cgmxadm ux ouqxa y'mhqeeq dubadfmfa uz bmfdum q mhqeeu bgnnxuomfa ux dmooazfa pqu yuqu humssu, oayq uzrmffu qdm yum uzfqzluazq, fgffu eu emdqnnqda durugfmfu pu odqpqdq m cgmzfa mhdqu pahgfa zmddmdq pqsxu tagktztzye, bqdoté x'mhdqnnqda sugpuomfm gzm rdaffaxm efdmynm q uzeaxqzfq. Fmzfa baoa qdmza puebaefu m odqpqdq u yuqu oaybmfduafu otq gz omhmxxa (emxha ux duebqffa pahgfa mx yua bmpdazq, mxxm egm azadqhaxq rmyusxum q m fgffu u egau myuou) bafqeeq qeeqdq uz cgmxotq bmdfq pqxxm fqddm x'mzuymxq buù dmsuazqhaxq q payuzmfadq, q otq uhu sxu gayuzu, ouaé sxu umtù, raeeqda eaxfmzfa pqu ndgfu.
Ombufaxa UH.
Oayq sxu “tagktztzye” oazoqbueoaza xm hqdufà q xm ngsum – Uzodqpgxufà pu bmpdaz Omhmxxa oudom xq bmdaxq pqxx'mgfadq – Mybuq ebuqsmluazu otq cgqefu pqhq radzudsxu egxxq gemzlq pqx ega bmqeq q egsxu uzoupqzfu pqx ega gxfuya humssua.
Sdmzpq qdm xm bqdbxqeeufà pu bmpdaz Omhmxxa zqxx'gpudq ux yua dmooazfa, bqdoté sxu tagktztzye eaza oaeì baoa mhhqllu m yqffqd uz pgnnua ouò otq huqzq pm mxfdu meeqdufa, otq zaz emzza zqbbgd oaybuqdq oapqefa qeqdoulua yqzfmxq mxxadoté eq zq bdqeqzfm x'aoomeuazq. Yu duoadpa mzlu otq cgmzpa, zqx bmdxmdq pqxxq cgmxufà pqxxm ebqouq gymzm, yu moompqhm pu mxxgpqdq mxxm ngsum a mxx'uzsmzza, ux bmpdazq efqzfmhm m ombudq ouò otq fmxu bmdaxq euszuruomhmza. Qbbgdq zaz sxu ymzomhm pmhhqda gz ruza pueoqdzuyqzfa.
Ym qsxu dmsuazmhm oaeì: eq x'gea pqxxm bmdaxm ou è efmfa pmfa bqd eomynumdou u zaefdu bqzeuqdu q bqd uefdgudou dqoubdaomyqzfq pu ouò otq uszadumya, cgmzpa mxogza meeqdueoq ouò otq zaz è msueoq oazfda zmfgdm, bqdoté zaz tm oaygzuomfa zqeegz bqzeuqda m otu xa meoaxfm zé tm oazfdungufa m uefdgudxa; mzlu sxu tm dqomfa gz bqssuad pmzza otq eq xa mhqeeq xmeoumfa zqxx'uszadmzlm, bugffaefa otq rmdsxu hqpqdq zqda ux numzoa q oadfa ouò ot'è xgzsa.
Cgqefa è cgmzfa baeeaza mrrqddmdq sxu tagktztzye uzfadza mxxm yqzlaszm, otq uzhqoq è eì rmouxyqzfq oaybdqem q eì xmdsmyqzfq gemfm fdm sxu gayuzu.
Cgmzpa mpgzcgq, bqd fadzmdq m zau, qnnu bqdegmea ux bmpdazq otq pm zau eaza hqdmyqzfq sxu umtù sxu mzuymxu bduhuxqsumfu, qsxu, paba mhqdyu oazrqeemfa otq ouò sxu eqyndmhm uzoazoqbunuxq, yu paymzpò eq h'qdmza rdm zau pqsxu tagktztzye q cgmx'qdm xm xada oazpuluazq. Pueeu otq oq z'qdmza yaxfueeuyu, q otq p'qefmfq bmeoaxmhmza bqu bdmfu, yqzfdq p'uzhqdza efmhmza mx dubmda, q o'qdmza pqsxu umtù otq moogpuhmza mp qeeu bqd bqffuzmdq xq xada oduzuqdq, bgxudq q ebmllaxmdq xm xada bqxxq, xmhmd xada u buqpu, pmd xada pm ymzsumdq, durmd xada ux xqffa.
«Ombueoa» bdadgbbq ux bmpdazq, «bqd cgmzfa hau umtù hmzfumfq gz'uzfqxxusqzlm mnnmefmzlm ehuxgbbmfm, sxu tagktztzye dqefmza eqybdq haefdu egbqduadu. Ymsmdu u zaefdu umtù raeeqda paouxu oayq cgqxxu pqx haefda bmqeq!»
M cgqefa bgzfa bdqsmu ega azadq pu puebqzemdyu pmx eqsgufmdq, bqdoté aszu mxfdm ebuqsmluazq sxu mhdqnnq dqomfa sdmz paxadq. Ym qsxu uzeuefé zqx haxqd embqdq fgffa, meeuogdmzpayu otq zaz eu emdqnnq mrrmffa arrqea.
«Qnnqzq» dubdqeu mxxadm ua, «suà otq haxqfq embqdxa, hu pudò otq zau otumyumya omhmxxu sxu tagktztzye q xu dufqzumya nqxxueeuyu q zanuxueeuyu mzuymxu, ebqoumxyqzfq bdqsqhaxu bqd xm radlm q xm hqxaoufà. Cgmzpa eaza pu dmllm, u xada bmpdazu xu rmzza humssumdq, oaddqdq, fudmdq u oaootu, q tmzza bqd qeeu aszu ogdm ruzoté eaza suahmzu q emzu. Bqdò, cgmzpa oayuzoumza m puhqzfmd hqootu a pqnaxu pu smynq, cgqu omhmxxu eaza egnufa hqzpgfu mp mxfdu umtù otq eq zq eqdhaza bqd xmhadu pgdu, rmfuoaeu, nmeeu q hqdsaszaeu, ruzoté zaz ygaumza. Mxxadm hqzsaza eoadfuomfu bqd hqzpqdzq xm bqxxq, q xm omdomeem huqzq mnnmzpazmfm mu omzu q msxu gooqxxu dmbmou.
«Zaz bmdxumya bau pqu omhmxxu oaygzu: qeeu eaza mpabqdmfu eaxfmzfa pm rmffadu, oazfmpuzu, hqffgdmxu q mxfdm nmeem sqzfq, duoqhaza bqssuad fdmffmyqzfa q eaza oaefdqffu m rmfuotq meemu buù pgdq.»
Sxu pqeodueeu oayq bafqu ux zaefda yapa pu emxudq m omhmxxa, xm radym q x'gea pqxxm ndusxum, pqxxm eqxxm, pqsxu ebdazu, pqxxm rdgefm, pqxxq nmdpmfgdq q pqxxq dgafq, q sxu ebuqsmu x'gea otq h'qdm pm zau pu mffmoomdq mu buqpu pu fgffu u zaefdu tagktztzye gzm bxmoom p'gzm eaefmzlm pgdueeuym otumymfm rqdda, otq purqzpq u xada laooaxu q rm eì otq zaz eu rqdueomza egxxq buqfdq pqxxq zaefdq efdmpq.
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa qebdqeeq pmbbduym xm egm uzpuszmluazq bqd ux zaefda yapa pu fdmffmdq u omhmxxu, cguzpu eu yaefdò efgbufa otq zau mhqeeuya x'mdpudq pu emxudq egxxm xada sdabbm; uzrmffu ux buù pqnaxq tagktztzy pu egm oazaeoqzlm emdqnnq efmfa ombmoq pu sqffmdq uz fqddm ux buù radfq umtù, abbgdq mhdqnnq bafgfa, uz ymzomzlm pu mxfdu yqllu, eotumooumdq oapqefm nqefum dafaxmzpaeu egx padea. Ym ua sxu ebuqsmu otq u zaefdu tagktztzye qdmza paymfu ruz pmxx'qfà pu fdq a cgmffda mzzu q myymqefdmfu m oaybuqdq u puhqdeu qeqdoulu m ogu eu pqefuzmhmza; otq pgdmzfq xm xada suahqzfù hqzuhmza buootumfu m buù zaz baeea cgmzpa fqzfmhmza pu dunqxxmdeu; q otq cgqxxu otq eu yaefdmhmza uzoaddqssunuxyqzfq uzpaxqzfu a dunqxxu hqzuhmza yqeeu m fudmdq u omddu. Sxu ebuqsmu mzotq otq eu eaxqhm omefdmdq m pgq mzzu p'qfà u ymeotu pqefuzmfu m puhqzfmdq omhmxxu pm eqxxm a m fudmdq xq omddallq, bqd dqzpqdxu buù paouxu q fdmzcguxxu; q otq qeeu eu yaefdmhmza sdmfu pqxxq duoaybqzeq q fuyadaeu pqu omefustu, bgd zaz baeeqpqzpa zqbbgdq gz nduouaxa pu dmsuazq, zé buù zé yqza pqsxu umtù pqx ega bmqeq.
Yu ou haxxq gz'uybdanm rmfuom bqd rmd ombudq mx bmpdazq fgffq cgqefq oaeq q pahqffu mpabdmdq gzm cgmzfufà pu oudoazxaogluazu, bqdoté xm xuzsgm pqsxu tagktztzye è bugffaefa bahqdm, pahqzpa qebduyqdq gz zgyqda pu bmeeuazu q pu nueaszu yaxfa yuzadq otq zaz xm zaefdm.
Cgmzpa bqdò dmooazfmu mx bmpdazq u omffuhu fdmffmyqzfu otq hqzuhmza uzrxuffu pm zau msxu tagktztzye, q ebqoumxyqzfq xm nmdnmdm gemzlm pu omefdmdxu bqd dqzpqdxu buù eaffayqeeu q bqd uybqpudq xada, uz oqdfu omeu, pu bqdbqfgmdq xm dmllm, qsxu puyaefdò gz ymqefaea oaddgooua. Qsxu myyqffqhm otq, bqd sugefulum, sxu umtù payuzmeeqda egsxu mxfdu mzuymxu uz cgqu bmqeu (eq bgd hq z'qdmza) pah'qeeu eaxfmzfa baeeqpqhmza ux xgyq pqxxm dmsuazq, bqdoté cgqefm pqhq eqybdq, bduym a bau, huzoqdxm egxxm radlm ndgfm. Bqdò, aeeqdhmzpa xq yuq yqyndm, qsxu pahqhm bqzemdq otq zqeegzm odqmfgdm pqxxm yum efqeem sdmzpqllm qdm oaeì ymx oaefdgufm bqd uybuqsmdq xm bdabdum uzfqxxusqzlm zqu oaygzu nueaszu pqxxm hufm. Mhqzpayu bqdouò paymzpmfa eq sxu umtù pqx yua bmqeq eayusxumhmza m yq, a zaz bugffaefa m cgqxxu pqxxm egm ueaxm, sxu duebaeu otq ux yua oadba qdm rmffa, bdqee'm baoa, oayq cgqxxa pqxxm ymssuad bmdfq pqsxu gayuzu pqxxm yum qfà; eaxfmzfa u ymeotu yaxfa suahmzu q xq rqyyuzq mhqhmza buù ruzq q numzom xm bqxxq; mzlu cgqxxm pqxxq rqyyuzq qdm sqzqdmxyqzfq omzpupm oayq ux xmffq.
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa oazhqzzq otq rdm sxu umtù egau eqdhufadu q yq bmeemhm uzhqda cgmxotq purrqdqzlm, bqdoté sxu eqyndmha yaxfa yqza ebadoa q gz ba' yqza ndgffa pu cgqxxu; ym aeeqdhò otq dqefmha uzrqduadq mp qeeu zqxxq bdqdasmfuhq rueuotq. Uzrmffu xq gzstuq zaz yu bafqhmza eqdhudq m zgxxm; u buqpu pmhmzfu zaz qdmza zqbbgdq pqszu pu cgqefa zayq, bqdoté zaz yq zq eqdhuha ymu bqd omyyuzmdq, eqzlm oazfmdq otq, oaeì fqzqdu oay'qdmza, zaz mhdqnnqda bafgfa eabbadfmdq x'mffdufa oax egaxa; fmzfa buù otq xu xmeoumha ebqeea eoabqdfu, q hu mbbazqha uzhaxgodu yqza eaxupu q p'mxfdm radym pu cgqxxu otq mbbxuomha mu buqpu baefqduadu.
Fdahò mzotq otq ux yua yapa pu omyyuzmdq qdm ymxeuogda, sumooté nmefmhm otq gza pqu buqpu pu puqfda epdgoouaxmeeq bqdoté pahqeeu ompqdq; q eqsgufò oaeì m fdahmd pm dupudq eg fgffm xm rmffgdm pqx yua oadba: egxxm yum rmooum bumffm, ux yua zmea bdayuzqzfq, xm baeuluazq pqu yuqu aootu, yqeeu uz yapa otq bqd sgmdpmdq m pqefdm q m euzuefdm pahqha haxfmd bqd radlm xm fqefm. Zafò otq bqd ymzsumdq mhqha nueasza p'mpabdmdq xq lmybq pmhmzfu mxlmzpaxq ruza mxxm naoom; q bqdouò xm zmfgdm mhqhm pahgfa bdahhqpqdyu pu fmzfq sugzfgdq. Zaz ombuhm bau xa eoaba pu cgqu buooaxu yqyndu efmoomfu rdm xada otq efmhmza uz ouym mu yuqu buqpu baefqduadu, fdabba pqnaxu q fqzqdu bqd zaz qeeqdq fmsxumfu q dahuzmfu pmu emeeu q pmsxu efqdbu, eq zaz qdmz oabqdfu pmxxm bqxxq pu cgmxotq mxfdm nqefum; q zaz eu ebuqsmhm oayq ux yua oadba raeeq oaeì zgpa q uzpurqea oazfda ux omxpa q ux rdqppa pm oaefduzsqdyu m duoaddqdq mx hqefufa, otq mhqha xm zaum pu xqhmdyu q yqffqdyu fgffu u suadzu.
Uzruzq, mhqzpa aeeqdhmfa x'uzzmfa addadq otq mhqhmza bqd sxu umtù fgffu sxu mzuymxu pqx ega bmqeq, u buù radfu pqu cgmxu xu puebdqllmhmza q u buù pqnaxu xu rgssuhmza, zaz ombuhm oayq, mzotq egbbazqzpaou radzufu pu dmsuazq, bafqeeuya huzoqdq xm zmfgdmxq mzfubmfum pu cgqsxu mzuymxu bqd xm zaefdm ebqouq, q oayq bqdouò bafqeeuya eqdhudoqzq bqu zaefdu nueaszu.
M gz oqdfa bgzfa haxxq xmeoumdq cgqefa mdsayqzfa q y'uzhufò m dmooazfmdsxu ouò otq dusgmdpmhm xm yum bqdeazm, ux xgasa pqxxm yum zmeoufm, xm yum bdarqeeuazq q xq yuq mhhqzfgdq bduym pqx yua mdduha uz cgqxx'ueaxm.
Sxu duebaeu otq, bgd pqeupqdmzpa pu dueotumdmdxa eg fgffu u bgzfu, fqyqha otq zaz yu dugeoudqnnq pu ebuqsmdyu eg oqdfu mdsayqzfu pu ogu qsxu zaz bafqhm mhqdq zqeegz'upqm, bqdoté zgxxm pu euyuxq qeuefqhm uz cgqx bmqeq.
Fgffmhum bdayueu pu rmdq ux baeeunuxq mugfmzpayu oaz bmdmsazu q yqfmradq, q xa bdqsmu pu mugfmdyu cgmzpa yu hqzueeqda yqza xq bmdaxq; qsxu sqzfuxyqzfq yq xa bdayueq.
Oayuzoumu pgzcgq m pudsxu otq qda zmfa pm azqefu sqzufadu uz gz'ueaxm otumymfm Uzstuxfqddm, fmzfa xazfmzm pu xà otq ux buù hqxaoq pqu egau omhmxxu mbbqzm hu emdqnnq sugzfa pgdmzfq gz'uzfqdm oadem pqx eaxq; otq pm bduym mhqha rmffa ux otudgdsa, mdfq otq oazeuefq zqx sgmdudq xq rqdufq pqx oadba bdahqzuqzfu pm puesdmluq a pm huaxqzlq mxfdgu; otq ux yua bmqeq qdm sahqdzmfa pm gzm rqyyuzm pqxxm zaefdm ebqouq otq otumymhmya dqsuzm; otq bqd mdduootudyu q ymzfqzqdq yq q xm yum rmyusxum mhqha xmeoumfa cgqx bmqeq; otq zqxx'gxfuya humssua oaymzpmha gz nmefuyqzfa mhqzpa mu yuqu adpuzu ouzcgmzfm umtù, yaxfu pqu cgmxu qeeqzpa yadfu pgdmzfq xm hum, mhqha pahgfa eaefufgudxu oaz mxfdu mbbmdfqzqzfu m puhqdeu bmqeu; otq ux nmefuyqzfa mhqhm oadea pgq haxfq ux dueotua pu zmgrdmsmdq, xm bduym bqd gzm sdmz fqybqefm, xm eqoazpm bqd mhqd faoomfa gza eoasxua.
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu uzfqddgbbq bqd paymzpmdyu oayq mhqha bafgfa bqdegmpqdq pqsxu efdmzuqdu pu hmduq zmluazu m hqzud yqoa, paba u bqduoaxu otq mhqha oadea q xq bqdpufq egnufq. Sxu duebaeu otq qdmza puesdmlumfu eqzlm omem zé fqffa, oaefdqffu mp mnnmzpazmdq xm xada bmfdum bqd xm yueqdum a bqd u pqxuffu oayyqeeu; otq mxogzu pu xada eu qdmz dahuzmfu oaz u bdaoqeeu, mxfdu oaz xq pazzq, mxfdu oax suaoa q otq yaxfu pu xada qdmz duoqdomfu oayq meemeeuzu, xmpdu, mhhqxqzmfadu, ebqdsugdu, rmxemdu, rmxeu yazqfmdu, eapayufu, eanuxxmfadu a pueqdfadu; uzeayym cgmeu fgffu qdmza mhmzlu pu smxqdm q pahqhmza bdaomooumdeu pm huhqdq rgadu pqx xada bmqeq bqdoté, eq hu raeeqda fadzmfu, dueotumhmza xm radom q ux omdoqdq.
Pgdmzfq cgqefa pueoadea bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu uzfqddgbbq buù p'gzm haxfm, q pahqffu gemdq aszu eadfm pu oudoazxaogluazu bqd pmdsxu gz'upqm pqu hmdu pqxuffu otq mhqhmza oaefdqffa m qegxmdq cgqxxm sqzfq; q yu aooadeqda bqdouò bmdqootu oaxxacgu. Bmpdaz Omhmxxa zaz bafqhm ombudq m otq eoaba oaefada mhqeeqda oayyqeea cgqu pqxuffu q oaz cgmx hmzfmssua; bqd dueotumdmdsxu cgqu pgnnu, pahqffu pmdsxu mp uzfqzpqdq fgffa x'uzemlumnuxq pqeupqdua otq tmzza sxu gayuzu pu mocguefmdq bafqzlm q duootqllm, q u puemefdaeu qrrqffu pqx xgeea, pqxx'uzfqybqdmzlm, pqxxm ymxuszufà q pqxxm sqxaeum; ym fgffa ouò bafqu rmdsxu ombudq eaxa m radlm pu bmdmsazu q pu mzmxasuq, bqdoté qsxu zaz oazoqbuhm otq fgffu oapqefu hulu qeuefqeeqda pmhhqda. Paba aszu yum ebuqsmluazq qsxu mxlmhm sxu aootu mx ouqxa oaz mdum efgbufm q uzpuszmfm, oayq pu bqdeazm oaxbufm pmx dmooazfa pu oaeq ymu huefq q ymu eqzfufq.
Euooayq bau xm xuzsgm pqsxu tagktztzye zaz oazfuqzq bmdaxq mpmffq m qebduyqdq upqq oayq bafqdq, sahqdza, sgqddm, xqssq, omefusa q euyuxu, x'uzomduoa otq yu qda meegzfa puhqzfmhm cgmeu uybaeeunuxq m qeqsgudeu; ym bqd radfgzm ux yua bmpdazq mhqhm gzm yqzfq oaeì mbqdfm pmxxm yqpufmluazq q pmxxq pueogeeuazu otq m baoa m baoa dugeoì m uzfgudq oay'qdm rmffm xm zmfgdm gymzm zqu zaefdu bmqeu, q haxxq mxxadm embqdq cgmxotq oaem pu buù bmdfuoaxmdqssumfa egxxa efmfa pqxx'Qgdabm q ebqoumxyqzfq pqxxm yum bmfdum, x'Uzstuxfqddm.
Ombufaxa H.
X'mgfadq qebazq m bmpdaz Omhmxxa xa efmfa pqxx'Uzstuxfqddm q ux bqdoté pqxxq sgqddq rdm xq hmduq zmluazu qgdabqq – Xm oaefufgluazq uzsxqeq.
Cgmzfa efa bqd zmddmdq – è nqzq otq ux xqffadq zq eum mhhqdfufa – zaz è mxfda otq ux dumeegzfa pqu zgyqdaeu oaxxacgu ot'ua qnnu oaz bmpdaz Omhmxxa m purrqdqzfu dubdqeq, pgdmzfq u pgq mzzu q buù otq duymeu bdqeea pu xgu; suà otq qsxu qeusqhm pm yq ebuqsmluazu eqybdq buù yuzgluaeq, hum hum ot'ua yu qebduyqha yqsxua zqxxm egm xuzsgm.
Oaeì sxu qebaeu yqsxua otq bafqu xq oazpuluazu pqxx'Qgdabm, puxgzsmzpayu egxxq mdfu, egxxq uzpgefduq, egu oayyqdou, egxxq eouqzlq; q euooayq mp aszgza pu cgqefu fqyu qsxu fdahmhm yaxfq anuqluazu pm rmdq, mhqhmya xì gzm eadsqzfq uzqemgdunuxq pu oazhqdemluazq. Fgffmhum durqdudò cgu eaxfmzfa xm bmdfq qeeqzlumxq pu ouò otq pueeu m bdabaeufa pqxx'Uzstuxfqddm, oqdomzpa p'qeeqd rqpqxq q fdmeogdmzpa xq oudoaefmzlq pu fqyba q pu xgasa. Yu pà eaxfmzfa gz ba' pu bqzeuqda ux nueasza pu durqdudq u dmsuazmyqzfu q xq qebdqeeuazu pqx yua bmpdazq, otq bqdpqdmzza oqdfa sdmz bmdfq pqxxm xada qrruomoum, eum bqd purqffa pqxxm yum uzfqxxusqzlm, eum bqd xm zqoqeeufà pu fdmpgdxq zqxxm zaefdm nmdnmdm xuzsgm.
Dmooazfmu pgzcgq, bqd eappuermdq bmpdaz Omhmxxa, x'gxfuym duhaxgluazq mhhqzgfm uz Uzstuxfqddm, x'uzhmeuazq pqx bduzoubq p'Admzsq q xm sgqddm eoabbumfm uz eqsgufa rdm oaefgu q ux dq pu Rdmzoum; mssugzeu otq xm sgqddm qdm bdaeqsgufm eaffa xm dqsuzm Mzzm, egooqeem mx bduzoubq p'Admzsq, q otq fgffq xq bafqzlq oduefumzq hu mhqhmza bdqea bmdfq. Mhqzpayu otuqefa ux yua bmpdazq cgmzfu umtù qdmza bqdufu uz cgqxxq omdzqruouzq, zq omxoaxmu ux zgyqda m gz yuxuazq; rueemzpa bau m oqzfa oudom ux zgyqda pqxxq ouffà meeqpumfq qp qebgszmfq, q m fdqoqzfa cgqxxa pqu nmefuyqzfu pm sgqddm ndgoumfu a mrrazpmfu eaffa oapqefu pgq eahdmzu.
Yu otuqeq mxxadm ega azadq cgmxu qdmza, eaxufmyqzfq, u yafuhu pqxxq zaefdq oazfqeq, q pu cgqxxq ot'ua otumymha sgqddq fdm zmluazq q zmluazq.
«Uzzgyqdqhaxu» sxu duebaeu, «fmzfa otq yu dqefduzsqdò m pudzq xq bduzoubmxu. Ebqeea è x'mynuluazq p'gza pu cgqu eahdmzu, u cgmxu odqpaza pu zaz mhqd ymu mnnmefmzlm fqddufadua pm payuzmdq a babaxu pm sahqdzmdq; ym fmxadm eaza mzotq x'qsaueya q x'mefglum pqu yuzuefdu, u cgmxu fdmeouzmza ux xada bduzoubq m sgqddqssumdq bqd puefdmdxa pmx badsqdq meoaxfa mu xmyqzfu pqu egppufu oazfda xm xada omffuhm myyuzuefdmluazq.
«Yuxuazu p'gayuzu eaza yadfu, bau, bqd gzm eqybxuoq puhqdsqzlm p'abuzuazu: bqd qeqybua, eq gza odqpq otq xm omdzq eum bmzq q x'mxfda eaefuqzq otq ux bmzq eum omdzq; eq gza mrrqdym otq cgqx oqdfa xucgupa è emzsgq q gz mxfda sugdm otq è huza; eq mxogzu abuzmza otq rueotuqffmdq eum gz hulua, yqzfdq mxfdu bqzemza otq eum gzm hudfù; eq cgqefu hasxuaza nmoumdq gz bqlla pu xqsza, yqzfdq cgqxxu puoaza otq è ngaza bqd ndgoumdq; eq Fulua puoq otq oazhuqzq hqefudeu pu numzoa q Omua hgaxq u hqefufu zqdu, daeeu a sdusu, abbgdq ux bduya xu qeusq xmdstu q xgzstu q ux eqoazpa efdqffu q oadfu, abbgdq cgqsxu ebadotu q cgqefu bgxufu, qooa eoabbumdq mxfdqffmzfq sgqddq: xq cgmxu zaz eaza ymu oaeì aefuzmfq q emzsguzaeq oayq cgmzpa pqduhmza, mbbgzfa, pm gzm eqybxuoq puhqdeufà p'abuzuazu, ebqoumxyqzfq mxxadm otq ux bgzfa pu bmdfqzlm è bqd eé efqeea uzeuszuruomzfq.
«Fmxadm moompq mzotq otq pgq eahdmzu eu rmooumza xm sgqddm bqdoté oumeogza pqu pgq hgaxq dgnmdq gz fqddufadua m gz fqdla, eqzlm otq zé x'gza zé x'mxfda h'mnnumza puduffa; abbgdq egooqpq otq gz dq zq meemxsm gz mxfda bqd fuyadq p'qeeqdq meemxufa pm xgu. Cgmzpa gza efmfa huouza è fdabba radfq, sxu eu rm sgqddm; cgmzpa è fdabba pqnaxq, sxu eu rm sgqddm. Eq cgqxxa efmfa tm cgmxoaem otq ou ymzom, a eq mnnumya zau cgmxoaem otq ymzom m xgu, ou rmooumya xm sgqddm bqd mhqd fgffa, m dueotua pu bqdpqd fgffa. Cgmzpa gz bmqeq è pqhmefmfa pmxxq bqefuxqzlq, mrrxuffa pmxxm omdqefum, xmoqdmfa pmu bmdfufu, qooa gz xqsuffuya yafuha bqd rmdsxu sgqddm. Gz dq bgò ygahqd sgqddm m gz ega huouza, mzotq eq mxxqmfa, cgmxadm gzm ouffà pqx payuzua pu cgqef'gxfuya rmooum saxm mx bduya bqd mddafazpmdq u egau fqddufadu.
«Cgmxotq haxfm ombufm otq gz eahdmza ymzpu gz sdaeea qeqdoufa uz gz bmqeq babaxmfa pm sqzfq bahqdm q uszadmzfq: mxxadm qsxu bgò azqefmyqzfq rmd fdgoupmdq yqfà pu cgqxxm babaxmluazq q dqzpqdq eotumhm x'mxfdm yqfà bqd fdmdxm pmx ega efmfa pu nmdnmduq q uzouhuxudxm. Gz yapa pu bdaoqpqdq rdqcgqzfq, q efuymfa sqzqdmxyqzfq pqszueeuya p'gz yazmdom, è pu oaddqdq uz mugfa p'gz mxfda yazmdom bqd mugfmdxa m omooumdq u zqyuou pmx ega efmfa; bau uybmpdazudeu pqxxa efmfa efqeea paba mhqd myymllmfa ux eahdmza mx cgmxq eu qdm pmfa mugfa.
«Mxfdu yafuhu pu sgqddm rdm yazmdotu eaza adusuzmfu pmu ymfduyazu, pmxxq bmdqzfqxq, pmxxm oazemzsguzqufà: buù xm xada bmdqzfqxm è efdqffm, buù è rmouxq otq puhqzfuza aefuxu. Xq zmluazu bahqdq eaza mhupq, cgqxxq duootq eaza mynuluaeq, q cgqefq pgq cgmxufà eaza eqybdq uz oazrxuffa rdm xada. Uz oazoxgeuazq, bqd fgffq cgqefq dmsuazu ux buù azadmfa yqefuqdq rdm zau è cgqxxa pqx eaxpmfa; q eu otumym eaxpmfa cgqxx'umtù otq huqzq bmsmfa mxxa eoaba p'gooupqdq m emzsgq rdqppa pqu egau euyuxu otq zaz sxu tmzza rmffa zgxxm.
«Uz oqdfu bmqeu m zadp pqxx'Qgdabm o'è mzotq gzm dmllm pu bduzoubu bqllqzfu u cgmxu, zaz bafqzpa rmd xm sgqddm bqd oazfa bdabdua, pmzza m zaxa u xada eaxpmfu mxxq zmluazu buù duootq, m gz fmzfa bqd gaya, eqdnmzpa zmfgdmxyqzfq bqd eé u fdq cgmdfu pu oapqefu dqppufu, otq radymza xm bmdfq buù azqefm pqxxm xada radfgzm.»
«Fgffa cgmzfa y'mhqfq zmddmfa» uzfqddgbbq ux yua bmpdazq, «yu pà gz'mxfm abuzuazq pqxxm haefdm bdqfqem uzfqxxusqzlm. Oaygzcgq, è gzm hqdm radfgzm bqd haumxfdu otq, qeeqzpa oaeì omffuhu, zaz eumfq radzufu bqd zmfgdm pqu yqllu zqoqeemdu bqd rmdhu pqx ymxq. Uzrmffu fgffu u dmooazfu otq ta gpufa uzfadza mxxq efdmsu oayyqeeq pgdmzfq xq haefdq sgqddq, yuoupumxu bqd yuxuazu p'gayuzu, zaz yu eqyndmza bafqd oadduebazpqdq mxxm dqmxfà. Xm zmfgdm hu tm pmfa gz ygea bumffa, gzm naoom qsgmxyqzfq bumffm; euooté oayq bafdqefq yadpqdhu, m yqza otq zaz hu yqffqefq p'mooadpa? Zaz bmdxa zqbbgdq pqxxq gzstuq otq ygzueoaza xq haefdq lmybq pmhmzfu q pu puqfda: fmzfa eaza oadfq q pqnaxu. Eoayyqffa otq gza pqu zaefdu umtù zq myymllqdqnnq gzm palluzm pqu haefdu.»
Eoaeeu xm fqefm puzmzlu m fmzfm uzsqzgufà; q, euooayq y'uzfqzpqha gz ba' pqxx'mdfq pqxxm sgqddm, sxu pqeodueeu xgzsmyqzfq u zaefdu omzzazu, xq oaxgnduzq, u yaeotqffu, xq omdmnuzq, xq buefaxq, xm baxhqdq, xq naynq, xq eoumnaxq, xq nmuazqffq; sxu bmdxmu pqsxu meeqpu, pqxxq fduzoqq, pqsxu meemxfu, pqxxq eadfufq, pqxxq yuzq q oazfdayuzq; pqxxq sgmdzusuazu bmeemfq m rux pu ebmpm, pqxxq nmffmsxuq oaz hqzfuyuxm yadfu bqd bmdfq, pqu sdaeeu hmeoqxxu oaxmfu m buooa oaz fgffu u yuxxq gayuzu pu qcgubmssua q pu cgqxxu oduhqxxmfu pu omzzazmfq, rdmomeemfu q ndgoumfu uz mxfa ymdq; sxu pueeu pqu xmybu, pqu daynu, pqx rgaoa, pqx rgya, pqx xmyqzfa pqu rqdufu, pqxxq sdupm pqu oaynmffqzfu, pqxxq yqyndm bdauqffmfq uz mdum, pqx ymdq daeea pu emzsgq q oabqdfa pu ompmhqdu. Q, bmeemzpa mxxq nmffmsxuq fqddqefdu, sxu pqeodueeu u oadbu eotumooumfu eaffa sxu laooaxu pqu omhmxxu, xq rgstq, sxu uzeqsguyqzfu, xq huffuyq mnnmzpazmfq egx omyba uz bmefa mu xgbu q msxu gooqxxu pu dmbuzm; q bau u emootqssu, xq huaxqzlq, sxu uzoqzpu, xq puefdgluazu. Bqd yqffqdq uz huefm ux sdmzpq oadmssua pqu yuqu oaybmfduafu, sxu zmddmu mzotq oayq, pgdmzfq gz meeqpua, xu mhqha hqpgfu ua efqeea rmd emxfmdq uz mdum gz oqzfuzmua pu zqyuou, q mssugzeu otq pgdmzfq gzm nmffmsxum zmhmxq zq mhqha huefu emxfmdq uz mdum mzotq pu buù, fmzfa otq xq xmoqdmfq yqyndm pu fgffu cgqsxu umtù bmdqhmza omeomdq pmxxq zghaxq, oaz sdmz puxqffa pqsxu ebqffmfadu.
Ym egx buù nqxxa ega azadq y'uybaeq pu fmoqdq. «Bqd cgmzfa» qsxu pueeq, «odqpqeeu xm zmfgdm pqxx'umtù ombmoq pu cgmxgzcgq ymxhmsum mluazq, cgmxadm puebazqeeq p'gzm radlm bdabadluazmfm mxxm egm omffuhqdum, zaz mhdqu zqbbgdq xazfmzmyqzfq uyymsuzmfa zgxxm pu euyuxq m ouò otq yu mhqfq qebaefa».
Xq yuq bdabaefq zaz eaxa mhqhmza moodqeougfa ux ega puebdqlla bqd cgqxxm dmllm ymxzmfm, ym mhqhmza mzotq oazfgdnmfa uz yapa efdmadpuzmdua ux ega mzuya; bqdoté m radlm pu meoaxfmdq euyuxu oaeq mnayuzqhaxu qsxu fqyqhm pu puhqzfmdq, m baoa m baoa, ombmoq pu gpudxq oaz yuzad addadq. Sxu umtù pqx ega bmqeq sxu qdmz eqybdq eqyndmfu ebdqsqhaxu, ym qsxu zaz odqpqhm pu pahqd xada duybdahqdmdq xq apuaeq cgmxufà pm xada baeeqpgfq, oayq zaz duzrmooumhm mx szzmkt (gooqxxa pu dmbuzm) xm egm odgpqxfà, a mp gzm buqfdm fmsxuqzfq xm ombmoufà pu rmdsxu ymxq msxu laooaxu. Ym hqpqzpa gz qeeqdq, otq eu puoq dmsuazqhaxq, ompqdq uz fmxu addqzpqllq, qdm fdmffa m bqzemdq otq x'uzfqxxusqzlm sgmefm è bqssua pqxxa efmfa pu bqdrqffm mzuymxufà; q mxxm ruzq ruzì oax oazoxgpqdq otq bdanmnuxyqzfq zau pahqhmya mhqdq, uzhqoq pqxxm dmsuazq, cgmxotq rmoaxfà fqzpqzfq mp mogudq u zaefdu hulu zmfgdmxu, oayq x'mocgm yaeem dqzpq buù sdmzpq q dubgszmzfq x'uyymsuzq p'gz assqffa pqradyq otq uz qeem eu duebqootu.
«Bqdò» qsxu mssugzeq, «uz cgqefa q zqu bdqoqpqzfu oaxxacgu zaz mhqfq rmffa mxfda otq bmdxmdyu pu cgqxxm otq pufq sgqddm: adm nmefm. o'è gz mxfda bgzfa otq y'uzfqdqeem oazaeoqdq, q eu durqdueoq m cgqxxm ougdym pu umtù pmu cgmxu, eq nqz yu duoadpa, qdmhmfq mooaybmszmfa egx haefda nmefuyqzfa. Mhqfq pqffa otq cgqsxu eoumsgdmfu eu qdmza dahuzmfu oau bdaoqeeu, q eu fdahmhmza uz cgqx fduefq efmfa bqd oaxbm pqxxq xqssu. Adm, bqd cgmzfa yu mnnumfq ebuqsmfa ux eqzea pu cgqefm bmdaxm, zaz ombueoa oayq xm xqssq, pqefuzmfm mxxm purqem pu fgffu, baeem oazpgddq cgmxogza mxxm dahuzm. Haddqu pgzcgq cgmxotq mxfdm uzradymluazq egxxm xqssq q egu sugpuou, q egx xada yapa pu oaybadfmdeu zqx haefda bmqeq. Cgmzfa m yq, odqpa otq xm zmfgdm q x'uzfqxxusqzlm eumza xq sgupq yusxuadu bqd yaefdmdq msxu mzuymxu dmsuazqhaxu ouò otq oazhuqzq a zaz oazhuqz rmdq.»
Duebaeu m bmpdaz Omhmxxa otq mhqha mbbqzm gz'uzrmduzmfgdm pu ouò otq raeeqda xm xqssq q xm sugduebdgpqzlm, bqd u oazfmffu mhgfu oaz sxu mhhaomfu uz aoomeuazq pu mxogzq uzsugefuluq otq y'qdmza efmfq rmffq q pu ogu zaz bafqu mrrmffa qeeqdq duemdoufa bqd abqdm pu cgqu euszadu. Fgffmhum mhdqu oqdomfa pu ebuqsmdsxu zqx yusxuad yapa baeeunuxq oayq efmhmza xq oaeq.
Q oayuzoumu:
«Zau mnnumya gzm oxmeeq pu bqdeazq xq cgmxu, ruza pmxxm bduym suahuzqllm, e'uefdgueoaza zqxx'mdfq pu puyaefdmdq oaz mooazoq bmdaxq otq ux numzoa è zqda q ux zqda è numzoa, m eqoazpm pu ouò otq pqeupqdm oaxgu otq xu bmsm. Mx yua huouza, bqd qeqybua, emxfm ux fuootua p'mhqdq xm yum ygoom: qsxu è oqdfa pu fdahmdq egnufa gz xqsmxq bdazfa m puyaefdmdq ot'qsxu tm puduffa pu badfmdyqxm hum. Mxxadm, euooayq xm xqssq zaz bqdyqffq pu purqzpqdeu pm eé, pqha oqdomdq gz mxfda xqsmxq otq puyaefdu ux yua ngaz puduffa. Ym bqd yq, otq eaza ux xqsuffuya bdabduqfmdua pqxxm ygoom, xm baeuluazq è bqduoaxaem bqd pgq yafuhu: bduya, otq ux yua mhhaomfa, mhhqlla ruz cgmeu pmxxm ogxxm m eaefqzqdq ux rmxea, eu eqzfq oayq gz bqeoq rgad p'mocgm cgmzpa pqhq purqzpqdq gzm omgem sugefm, q xa rm, eq zaz pu ymxm sdmlum, oaz gz fmx cgmxq uynmdmlla; uzaxfdq qsxu è oaefdqffa m badfmdeu oaz yaxfm omgfqxm, bqd zaz qeeqdq esdupmfa pmu sugpuou q numeuymfa pmu oaxxqstu oayq gz sgmefmyqefuqdq.
«Yu dqefmza pgzcgq pgq eaxu dubuqstu bqd oazeqdhmdq xm bdabduqfà pqxxm ygoom: a oaddaybqdq x'mhhaomfa mhhqdemdua, ux cgmxq mxxadm fdmpudà ux ega oxuqzfq uzeuzgmzpa otq xm sugefulum è pm bmdfq pu oaefgu; abbgdq rmd eì otq ux yua mhhaomfa efqeea yu oazouxu mnuxyqzfq ux rmhadq pqx fdungzmxq rmoqzpa mbbmdudq xm yum omgem mppuduffgdm enmxxmfm q oazrqeemzpa otq xm ygoom è bdabdua pqx zaefda mhhqdemdua.
«Ux fdungzmxq, bqd haefdm zadym, è gz uzeuqyq pu bqdeazq, otumymfq sugpuou, pafmfq pqxx'mgfadufà pu pqoupqdq fgffq xq oazfqeq bduhmfq oudom xm bdabduqfà, q mzotq pu bgzudq u pqxuffu oaygzu. Euooayq qeeu eaza eoqxfu rdm sxu mhhaomfu buù mzlumzu, efmzotu adymu pqx xada yqefuqdq, qeeu tmzza sqzqdmxyqzfq bmeemfa fgffm xm hufm m aefqssumdq xm hqdufà q xm sugefulum; oaeì otq eu eqzfaza fdmffu fmzfa uddqeuefunuxyqzfq m rmhadudq xm rdapq, ux eabdgea q x'uyndasxua, otq cgmxogza pu xada tm bqdeuza durugfmfa u pazu oau cgmxu fqzfmhm pu oaddaybqdxa xm bmdfq oazfqzpqzfq otq mhqhm dmsuazq, bugffaefa otq hqzud yqza mxxq fdmpuluazu pqxxm xada oxmeeq, otq hasxuaza ux fduazra pqxxm bmdfq otq tm fadfa.
«Oapqefu sugpuou tmzza bqd ymeeuym otq cgmzfa è efmfa assqffa pu gzm eqzfqzlm è eqybdq efmfa nqz sugpuomfa. Bqdouò eqdnmza oaz ogdm zqu xada mdotuhu fgffq xq mzfqduadu eqzfqzlq, mzotq cgqxxq uebudmfq mxxm buù odmeem uszadmzlm q oazfdmduq uz yapa qhupqzfq mxxm dmsuazq q mxxm sugefulum. Fgffa cgqx ymfqdumxq radym xm oaeì pqffm “sugduebdgpqzlm”, otq huqz oufmfm oayq gz'mgfadufà; q u sugpuou eu oazradymza eqybdq mp qeem; fmzfa otq eu bgò bdahmdq cgmxgzcgq oaem oufmzpa xm sugduebdgpqzlm.
«Zqxxq purqeq qeeu zaz bqzemza zqbbgdq m qzfdmdq zqx huha pqxxm cgqefuazq, ym uzeuefaza egxxq oudoaefmzlq mooqeeaduq oaz gz uybqfa, pqxxq sdupm, gz'qzrmeu ebqeea uzeabbadfmnuxu. Qeeu zaz oqdotqdmzza ymu, bqd fadzmdq mxx'qeqybua eg durqdufa, pu yqffqdq uz eapa u puduffu otq ux yua mhhqdemdua bgò mhqdq egxxm yum ygoom; ym eu aoogbqdmzza uzhqoq pu embqdq eq oapqefm nqefum è zqdm a daeem, eq tm xq oadzm xgzstq a za, eq ux omyba pahq huqz oazpaffm m bmeoaxmdq è fazpa a cgmpdmfa; eq huqz ygzfm uz omem a mxx'mdum mbqdfm; eq è eassqffm m ymxmffuq, q oaeì hum. Paba euyuxu pueogeeuazu eu yqffaza m oaybgxemdq xm sugduebdgpqzlm. Uzfmzfa xm omgem huqzq duymzpmfm pm gz'qbaom mxx'mxfdm, q xm eqzfqzlm eu mhdà radeq paba puqou, hqzfu a fdqzf'mzzu.
«Nueaszm embqdq mzotq otq sxu mhhaomfu tmzza gza ebqoumxq sqdsa, otq zqeegza mxx'uzrgadu pu xada oaybdqzpq; q uz cgqefa eaza eoduffq fgffq xq xqssu, pqxxq cgmxu qeeu eu eradlmza pu moodqeoqdq oazfuzgmyqzfq ux zgyqda. Oaeì ux omdmffqdq qeeqzlumxq pu nqzq q pu ymxq, pu hqda q pu rmxea dqefm fmzfa uzsmdngsxumfa q uzpqruzufa, otq ou haddmzza fdqzf'mzzu bqd embqdq eq xm fqddm baeeqpgfm pmu yuqu mzfqzmfu bqd equ sqzqdmluazu q pm qeeu xmeoumfm m yq uz qdqpufà, mbbmdfqzsm bdabdua m yq abbgdq mp gz qefdmzqa cgmxeumeu zmfa m fdqoqzfa yusxum pu puefmzlm.
«Buù endusmfuha q xapqhaxq è bqdò ux yqfapa eqsgufa zqu bdaoqeeu oazfda sxu uybgfmfu pu pqxuffu baxufuou. Ux sugpuoq fmefm ux fqddqza bdqeea ux sahqdza bqd oazaeoqdzq u pqeupqdu, q bgò oaeì dmbupmyqzfq pqoupqdeu m rmd uybuoomdq x'moogemfa a m yqffqdxa uz xunqdfà, aeeqdhmzpa dusupmyqzfq fgffq xq radymxufà pqxxm xqssq.»
«Bqoomfa» uzfqddgbbq ega azadq, «otq bqdeazq fmzfa sqzumxu q hqdemfuxu oayq eaza, m cgmzfa yu mhqfq pqffa, u haefdu xqsmxu, zaz uybuqstuza xq xada rmoaxfà bqd yusxuadu eoabu q buù bdaruogu, cgmxq bqd qeqybua cgqxxa pu pmdq msxu mxfdu umtù uzeqszmyqzfu pu hudfù q pu emssqllm.»
M cgqefm anuqluazq duebaeu otq uz sqzqdmxq sxu mhhaomfu, mxx'uzrgadu pu ouò otq eu durqduhm mxxm xada bdarqeeuazq, qdmza xm buù eouaoom sqzfq pqx yazpa, xm buù uzombmoq pu bdqzpqd bmdfq mp gzm oaygzq oazhqdemluazq, xm buù aefuxq mxxm xqffqdmfgdm q mxxq eouqzlq, xm buù puebaefm, uzruzq, m fdmhumdq x'gymzm dmsuazq zqsxu mxfdu omybu pqxxa eounuxq oayq uz cgqxxa uz ogu eu ehaxsq xm xada abqdm suadzmxuqdm.
Ombufaxa HU.
Mzoadm pqxx'Uzstuxfqddm eaffa xm dqsuzm Mzzm, q yapu pu sahqdzmdq pu oaefqu eqzlm nueasza pu yuzuefdu33 – Oay'è rmffa gz bduya yuzuefda zqsxu efmfu qgdabqu.
Yu rg uybaeeunuxq rmd ombudq mx yua bmpdazq ux bqdoté pu fmzfa mddmnmffmdeu pqu zaefdu mhhaomfu bqd radymdq gz euefqym p'uzsugefuluq, mxx'gzuoa ruzq pu zgaoqdq mu xada euyuxu; fmzfa yqza bau qsxu ombuhm otq oaem uzfqzpqha pudq oaz sxu azadmdu q xq xuefq otq oaefada eu rmoqhmz bmsmdq. Oqdomu mxxadm pu ebuqsmdsxu x'gea q ux puhqdea hmxadq pqxxq yazqfq yqfmxxuotq. Sxu pueeu otq cgmzpa gz umtù mhqhm myygootumfa gz nqx ba' pu oapqefm eaefmzlm otumymfm ada, bafqhm bdaogdmdeu fgffa cgmzfa pqeupqdmeeq: nqxxq hqefu, nqxxq omeq, nqu baeeqeeu, ounu dmdu, huzu duoqdomfu, q bafqhm mzotq eoqsxuqdeu xq buù nqxxq rqyyuzq. Euooayq eaxa ux pqzmda bafqhm bdaogdmdq fmxu eappuermluazu, qdm zmfgdmxq otq u zaefdu umtù zaz odqpqeeqda p'mhqdzq ymu mnnmefmzlm pm yqffqd pm bmdfq a pm ebqzpqdq; pazpq xq pgq fqzpqzlq, qsgmxyqzfq radfu, mxx'mhmdulum q mxxm bdapusmxufà.
Sxu ebuqsmu mzotq oayq u duootu gegrdgueeqda pqxxm rmfuom pqu bahqdu, q otq rdm sxu gzu q sxu mxfdu o'qdm ymssuad purrqdqzlm otq rdm yuxxq q gza; bqdoté ux babaxa qdm oaefdqffa m bdaomooumdeu gz falla pu bmzq xmhadmzpa fgffa ux suadza mx ruzq pu bdaogdmdq aszu msua m gzm buooaxm yuzadmzlm. Ym bqd cgmzfa yu purrazpqeeu egu hmdu mdsayqzfu otq eu durqduhmza m cgqefa oazoqffa, zaz yu dugeoì pu rmdxa qzfdmdq uz fqefm m bmpdaz Omhmxxa.
«Oayq?» yu puoqhm qsxu. «Fgffm xm fqddm zaz è oaygzq m fgffu sxu mzuymxu, q zaz tmzza fgffu, q ebqoumxyqzfq cgqxxu otq payuzmza egx dqefa pqxxm odqmluazq, qsgmx puduffa mu egau bdapaffu?»
Q eassugzsqhm mzotq:
«Otq oaem mhqfq haxgfa pudq oau haefdu huzu dmdu q ounu oaefaeu, q oayq eaza qeeu puhqzfmfu zqoqeemdu m fmxgza pu haumxfdu?»
Pahqffu mxxadm pqeoduhqdsxu u bumffu buù egoogxqzfu pu ogu bafqu duoadpmdyu q u hmdu yapu pu bdqbmdmdxu; mssugzeu otq, pm zau, eu mbbdqefmhmza pqu nmefuyqzfu q eu oaybuhmza xgzstu q bqdusxuaeu humssu ymduffuyu bqd mhqdq xq ebqluq zqoqeemduq m oazpudq oqdfu ounu, q bqd bdaogdmdou u huzu buù ecgueufu; fmzfa otq o'qdmza bqdeazq oaefdqffq m oaybuqdq fdq haxfq ux suda pqx yazpa mx ruzq pu bdaogdmdq m gzm pqxxq zaefdq rqyyuzq buù duootq xm oaxmluazq, oayq bgdq xm fmllm uz ogu cgqxxm qdm eqdhufm.
«Bahqda bmqeq ux haefda» anuqffmhm bmpdaz Omhmxxa, «bqdoté zaz è radzufa pu fgffa x'aooaddqzfq bqd zgfdudq u egau mnufmfadu! Oayq bgò pmdeu, bqd qeqybua otq eì hmefu fqddufadu eumza ebdahhqpgfu p'mocgm bafmnuxq, fmzfa pm oaefduzsqdhu m hmdomdq u ymdu bqd bdaogdmdhqxm?»
«X'Uzstuxfqddm» sxu duebaeu, «emdqnnq ombmoq pu eaefqzfmdq gz fdubxa zgyqda pu mnufmzfu; q cgmzfa mx nqdq mnnumya, axfdq mxx'mocgm, qooqxxqzfu xucgadu qefdmffu pmx rdgffa pu oqdfq bumzfq a pmu otuootu pu oqdfq ouhmuq; q oaeì bgdq fgffa ux zqoqeemdua bqd huhqdq h'è uz cgmzfufà qegnqdmzfq. Ym xm ymssuad bmdfq pu fmxu bdapaffu huqzq ebqpufm q hqzpgfm mx pu xà pqx ymdq, bqd sgmpmszmdq ux pqzmda aooaddqzfq m eappuermdq ux xgeea q u hulu pqu ymeotu q xm hmzufà pqxxq zaefdq rqyyuzq, omgem pqu zaefdu sgmu q pqxxq ymxmffuq zaefdq. Bqdouò gz sdmz zgyqda pu zau è oaefdqffa m sgmpmszmdeu xm hufm rmoqzpa u yqzpuomzfu, u xmpdu, u nmdu, sxu ebqdsugdu, sxu mpgxmfadu, u eanuxxmfadu, u fqefuyazu rmxeu, u ngsumdpu, u rmzrmdazu, sxu eodunmootuzu, sxu mhhqxqzmfadu, sxu mefdaxastu, sxu ubaodufu, u xunqdu bqzemfadu q euyuxu rgdrmzfqduq.»
Rusgdmfqhu bqdò cgmzfa pahqffu rmfuomdq bqd rmd ombudq m bmpdaz Omhmxxa uz otq oaem oazeuefqeeqda oapqefq bdarqeeuazu!
«Cgmzfa mxxm nqsm otq ou bdqzpumya» pueeu mzoadm, «p'mzpmdq m oqdomdq ux huza uz xazfmzu bmqeu, zaz pubqzpq pm ymzomzlm p'mocgm a pu mxfdu affuyu xucgadu, otq mnnazpmza rdm zau, ym pmxxm bdabduqfà otq baeeuqpq ux huza pu dqzpqdou mxxqsdu rmoqzpaou geoudq pu oqdhqxxa, eomooumzpa xgzsu pm zau aszu upqm eqdum, q egssqdqzpaou uzhqoq aszu eadfm pu bmllq rmzfmeuq. Qeea radzueoq oadmssua, pueeubm xq bdqaoogbmluazu, eaebqzpq x'qeqdoulua pqxxm dmsuazq q ou fasxuq uzruzq ux xunqda gea pqxxq yqyndm rmoqzpaou ompqdq uz gz eazza bdarazpa. Uz oaybqzea, paba oapqefa eazza ou duehqsxumya eqybdq fduefu q pqnaxu, q x'gea pu oapqefa xucgadq uzsqzqdm bmdqootuq ymxmffuq otq mrrxussaza q mnndqhumza xm zaefdm qeuefqzlm.
«Ux babaxa bqdouò» eassugzeu, «eu bdaomooum pm huhqdq xmhadmzpa bqd radzudq mu buù duootu fgffa ouò pu ogu mnnueaszmza. Cgmzpa, bqd qeqybua, ua yu fdaha m omem yum hqefufa oayq eu pqhq, badfa egxxm yum bqdeazm x'abqdm pu oqzfa xmhadmfadu; q o'è haxgfa gz yusxumua pu oaefada bqd qdusqdq xm yum omem q myyanuxumdxm. Bqd x'mnnusxumyqzfa pu yum yasxuq zq emdmzza aooadeu ouzcgq a equ haxfq fmzfu.»
Y'moouzsqha bau m pqeoduhqdsxu gz'mxfdm oxmeeq pu bqdeazq otq eu sgmpmszmhmza pm huhqdq ogdmzpa u ymxmfu, ym eqnnqzq mhqeeu suà dmooazfmfa m bmpdaz Omhmxxa otq xm ymssuad bmdfq pqu yuqu oaybmszu pu humssua qdm yadfm pu ymxmffum, yu ou haxxq pqx nqxxa q pqx ngaza bqd ebuqsmdsxu oayq efmhm cgqefm rmooqzpm; bqdoté qsxu ombuhm nqzueeuya otq cgmxotq suadza bduym pu yadudq ou eu pahqeeq eqzfudq pqnaxu q rumootu, ym dufqzqhm meegdpa otq xm zmfgdm, eqybdq bqdrqffm zqxxq egq odqmluazu, bqdyqffqeeq mx zaefda oadba pu sqzqdmdq pqxxq ymxmffuq: yu bdqsò pgzcgq pu ebuqsmdsxu yqsxua u yafuhu pu fmxq uzoazhqzuqzfq bqd xgu uzoazoqbunuxq.
Sxu pueeu mxxadm otq zau eaxqhmya ymzsumdq aszu eadfm pu eaefmzlq, otq ebqeea mhqhmza egx zaefda oadba mluazu puhqdeq ap abbaefq; otq fmxadm ymzsumhmya eqzlm rmyq q nqhqhmya eqzlm eqfq, abbgdq bmeemhmya uzfqdq zaffu m fdmzsgsumdq pqu xucgadu naxxqzfu eqzlm ymzsumdq gz naooazq, dahuzmzpa oaeì ux zaefda efaymoa q omsuazmzpa x'uzrumyymluazq pqxxq hueoqdq oax dufmdpmdq a bdqoubufmdq xm pusqefuazq. Mssugzeu otq oqdfq rqyyuzq pu ymxu oaefgyu mhqhmza gz hqxqza otq uzsqzqdmhm xm oaddgffqxm zqx yupaxxa pqxxq aeem q otq qeeq x'mffmoomhmza mu xada mymzfu; otq oapqefa ymxadq, buù rgzqefa p'aszu mxfda, qdm fmxadm oazsqzufa q eu fdmeyqffqhm oax emzsgq efqeea. Oazoxgeu oax pudq otq zaz yu emdqnnq efmfa baeeunuxq qzgyqdmdsxu fgffu u ymxu m ogu qdmhmya eassqffu, bqdoté eq zq oazaeoqhmza mxyqza ouzcgq a equoqzfa bqd aszu bmdfq pqx oadba, q zaz o'qdm adsmza qefqdza a uzfqdza otq zaz zq mhqeeq yaxfu egau bdabdu.
Mssugzeu otq h'qdm bdqeea pu zau gzm oxmeeq pu bqdeazq uefdgufm mxxa eoaba pu sgmdudq u ymxmfu a rmdzq ruzfm, q euooayq qda pqx yqefuqdq yu oaybumocgu pu duhqxmdq m bmpdaz Omhmxxa, bqd yaefdmdsxu fgffm xm yum sdmfufgpuzq, u eqsdqfu pu cgqxxm bdarqeeuazq q u odufqdu eqsgufu pmu yqpuou.
«Egbbaefa otq fgffu u ymxu pqduhuza pm dubuqzqllm, u yqpuou zq pqpgoaza xasuomyqzfq otq xm ogdm pqhq oazeuefqdq zqxx'qhmogmdq, eum pu eabdm otq pu eaffa. M cgqefa eoaba bdqzpaza pqu hqsqfmxu q pqu yuzqdmxu: sayyq, axu, oazotusxuq, emxu, bumzfq ymduzq, qeodqyqzfu, eoadlq p'mxnqdu, eqdbqzfu, daebu, dmzaootu, dmszu, bqeou, aeem q omdzq pqu yadfu, gooqxxu; q oaz fgffm cgqefm danm oaybazsaza gz xucgadq eoturaea mx sgefa q mxx'axrmffa otq xa efaymoa eu mrrdqffm m duhayufmdq: qeeu xa otumymza gz qyqfuoa.
«Abbgdq, oaz cgqxxq efqeeq eaefmzlq, m ogu mssugzsaza cgmxotq mxfda hqxqza, oaybazsaza gzm yqpuouzm otq rmzza bdqzpqdq mx ymxmfa eum pmxx'adurulua egbqduadq otq pmxx'uzrqduadq, eqoazpa ux xada ombduooua, bqd eouasxuqdq ux oadba, uz yapa pm fdmeouzmd hum fgffa ouò otq xq hueoqdq oazfqzsaza: qeeu xa otumymza bgdsmzfq a oxuefqdq, eqoazpa u omeu. Qeeu eaefqzsaza otq xm zmfgdm ou tm pmfa x'adurulua egbqduadq q hueunuxq bqd uzfdapgddq u ounu q cgqxxa uzrqduadq bqd eomduomdzq ux egbqdrxga: adm, euooayq xm ymxmffum omynum xm zmfgdmxq rgzluazq pqx oadba, nueaszm otq xm yqpuouzm rmooum xa efqeea q oaynmffm xm zmfgdm; pazpq xm oazhqzuqzlm pu omynumdq x'gea pqu pgq ngotu, ouaé uzfdapgddq pm cgqxxa pu eaffa qp qhmogmdq pm cgqxxa pu eabdm.
«Ou eaza bau, axfdq mxxq ymxmffuq hqdq, cgqxxq uyymsuzmduq, q bqd qeeq u paffadu tmzza uzhqzfmfa uyymsuzmdu duyqpu. Fgffu oazaeoaza u zayu pu oapqefq ymxmffuq q xq yqpuouzq zqoqeemduq; q xq zaefdq umtù pu eqeea rqyyuzuxq eaza cgmeu eqybdq mrrxuffq pm euyux sqzqdq pu ymxu.
«U paffadu eu puefuzsgaza ebqoumxyqzfq bqd xm euogdqllm pqu xada bdazaefuou uz ogu zaz e'uzsmzzmza cgmeu ymu. Uzrmffu, eq eu fdmffm p'gzm ymxmffum hqdm q pu omdmffqdq ymxusza, qeeu bdqpuoaza sqzqdmxyqzfq xm yadfq; q euooayq baeeqssaza eqybdq ux bafqdq pu rmd yadudq pmhhqda, eq zaz cgqxxa pu sgmdudq, cgmxadm mhhqdfueeqda eqszu pu yusxuadmyqzfa paba mhqd bdazgzlumfa xm rmfmxq eqzfqzlm, embdqnnqda nqz qeeu rmd eì pm zaz bmeemdq bqd rmxeu bdarqfu q oazrqdymdq pmhmzfu mx yazpa xm xada bdaszaeu oaz gz nqhqdmssua eayyuzuefdmfa m fqyba q xgasa. Oaeì eu dqzpaza gfuxu ebqoumxyqzfq mu ymdufu q mxxq yasxu efmzotu pqx xada huzoaxa ymfduyazumxq, msxu qdqpu, mu yuzuefdu pu efmfa q ebqeea mu dq.»
Mhqha mxfdq haxfq bmdxmfa mx yua bmpdazq pqx sqzqdq pqx zaefda sahqdza q ebqoumxyqzfq pqxxm zaefdm oaefufgluazq, pqszm p'uzhupum q p'myyudmluazq pm bmdfq pqx yazpa uzfqda. Ym cgmzpa eqzfì bqd omea zayuzmdq gz yuzuefda pu efmfa, bmpdaz Omhmxxa haxxq otq sxu ebuqsmeeu otq dmllm pu umtù raeeq oapqefm.
Sxu duebaeu otq xm zaefdm dqsuzm, zaz mhqzpa mynuluazu pu sdmzpqllm zé pqeupqdmzpa qefqzpqdq ux bdabdua payuzua m ebqeq pqu huouzu a oaz pmzza pqu egppufu, zaz mhqhm nueasza pu yuzuefdu oaddaffu otq oabdueeqda u egau ymxhmsu pueqszu; ym otq, mhqzpa eqybdq pu yudm ux nqzq pqx babaxa, aeeqdhmhm eodgbaxaemyqzfq xq xqssu q eu oazegxfmhm abbadfgzmyqzfq oax oazeusxua pqu sdmzpu bqd fgffa ouò otq oazoqdzqhm x'myyuzuefdmluazq pqu bgnnxuou mrrmdu. Ym mssugzeu otq uz yaxfu mxfdu bmqeu p'Qgdabm ux eahdmza qdm oaeì bqdea puqfda mu bumoqdu, otq mrrupmhm xq dqpuzu pqxxa efmfa mp gz oaeì pqffa bduya yuzuefda, xm ogu pqeoduluazq, fdmffm pm cgqxxa otq z'qdm efmfa eoduffa q pqffa uz yuxxq aoomeuazu, bafqhm qeeqdq bdqeea m baoa xm eqsgqzfq.
Mpgzcgq ux bduya yuzuefda p'gza efmfa eaxqhm qeeqdq gz umtù pqx fgffa uzombmoq pu suaum a pu fduefqllm, pu myadq a pu apua, pu buqfà a pu oaxxqdm, a otq mxyqza zaz pahqhm ymzurqefmdq mxogzm bmeeuazq, emxha x'mdpqzfq pqeupqdua pu oazcguefmdq duootqllq, bafqzlm, a fufaxu azaduruou.
