Qsxu egaxq mpabqdmdq xq bmdaxq bqd u buù ehmdumfu geu fdmzzq otq bqd qebduyqdq ux bdabdua bqzeuqda, q zaz puoq ymu gzm hqdufà m yqza otq zaz eum bqd xa eoaba pu rmdxm odqpqdq gzm yqzlaszm; oaxada pqu cgmxu qsxu puoq ymxq puqfda xq ebmxxq eu fdahmza oqdfmyqzfq egxxm ngazm efdmpm bqd mhqdq gzm bdayaluazq, yqzfdq otu hqzsm pm xgu xapmfa uz rmooum a uz bdqeqzlm mxfdgu, eu bgò dufqzqdq gz gaya bqdpgfa. Xm bdayqeem pu gz yuzuefda, ebqoumxyqzfq eq oazhmxupmfm oaz gz ngaz sugdmyqzfa, oaefufgueoq ux bqssuad mgsgdua pqx yazpa, q paba mhqdxm duoqhgfm gzm bqdeazm pu ngaz eqzea zaz bgò rmd mxfda otq dufudmdeu uz ngaz adpuzq q xmeoumdq aszu ebqdmzlm.
Ou eaza fdq euefqyu, eassugzeu, bqd mdduhmdq mx baefa pu bduya yuzuefda; ux bduya oazeuefq zqx eqdhudeu bdgpqzfqyqzfq p'gzm yasxuq, p'gzm rusxum a p'gzm eadqxxm; ux eqoazpa pu fdmpudq a pu yuzmdq eaffa eaffa ux bdabdua bdqpqoqeeadq; ux fqdla pu puefuzsgqdeu zqxxq bgnnxuotq meeqynxqq bqd gz rgduaea lqxa oazfda xm oaddgluazq pqxxm oadfq. Ym otu mpabqdm cgqefa gxfuya yqlla tm ymssuadu bdanmnuxufà pu qeeqdq bdqeoqxfa pm gz eahdmza pu sugpulua, bqdoté sxu abbaeufadu buù rmzmfuou puhqzfmza eqybdq u yuzuefdu buù eqdhuxyqzfq eaffayqeeu mu haxqdu q mxxq bmeeuazu pqx xada yazmdom. Gzm haxfm dmssugzfa ux bafqdq, qeeu pqnnaza bdaomooumdeu xm ymssuadmzlm pqu egrrdmsu zqx eqzmfa a zqx oazeusxua pu smnuzqffa, puefdungqzpa m pqefdm q m euzuefdm rmhadu q uybuqstu; q cgmzpa eu dufudmza pmxxm hufm bgnnxuom azgefu pqxxq ebasxuq pqx bdabdua bmqeq, qeeu eu fdmssaza rgadu pm aszu dqebazemnuxufà bqd yqlla pqx oaeupqffa “mffa p'uzpqzzufà34”, pu ogu ebuqsmu ux euszuruomfa m bmpdaz Omhmxxa.
Ux bmxmlla p'gz bduya yuzuefda è gzm hqdm eogaxm pahq eu fudmza eg sxu mebudmzfu m oapqefm bdarqeeuazq: bmssu, eqdhufadu, geouqdu uyufmza ux xada bmpdazq, euooté puhqzfmza mxfdqffmzfu yuzuefdu, oumeogza bqd xm bdabdum erqdm, q eu bqdrqluazmza eqybdq buù zqu fdq bduzoubmxu dmyu pqxx'mdfq, otq eaza x'uzeaxqzlm, xm ngsum q xm oaddgluazq. Oumeogza p'qeeu tm gzm buooaxm oadfq oaybaefm pu bqdeazmssu mxfaxaomfu, q fmxadm m radlm pu rgdnqdum q pu ermooumfmssuzq cgmxogza pu xada duqeoq gz ba' mxxm haxfm m puhqzfmdq ux egooqeeadq pqx bdabdua bmpdazq.
Ux bduya yuzuefda è sqzqdmxyqzfq eaffabaefa mu haxqdu pu gz'mymzfq mffqybmfm, abbgdq p'gz omyqduqdq bdqpuxqffa, q bqd yqlla pu oaefada eu puefdungueoaza u rmhadu; euooté qeeu, mxxm ruzq pqxxq ruzu, baeeaza nqz pudeu u dqssufadu pqx bmqeq.
Gzm haxfm bmpdaz Omhmxxa, paba mhqdyu eqzfufa bmdxmdq pqxxm zanuxfà pqx zaefda bmqeq, yu rqoq gz oaybxuyqzfa ot'ua zaz bafqu bqd zgxxm mooqffmdq. Qsxu yu pueeq otq pahqha mbbmdfqzqdq m gzm rmyusxum pu zanuxueeuya emzsgq, suà otq yu puefuzsgqha sdmzpqyqzfq pmsxu mxfdu umtù pu egm oazaeoqzlm bqd xm nqxxqllm pqxxq yqyndm, bqd ux oaxadufa q bqd xm bgxulum, eqnnqzq raeeu xada uzrqduadq bqd xm radlm q x'msuxufà (q cgqefa eu ebuqsmhm eqzlm pgnnua oax puhqdea sqzqdq pu hufm); eqzlm oazfmdq xm rmoaxfà pqxxm bmdaxm q cgqx oqdfa sdmpa pu dmsuazq ot'ua baeeqpqha q otq yu rmoqhmza bmeemdq bqd gz bdapusua bdqeea fgffu sxu tagktztzye.
Qsxu yu rqoq mzotq zafmdq oayq rdm sxu tagktztzye u numzotu q u emgdu qdmza rmffu yqza nqzq pqu nmu, pqu sdusua-rqdda, pqu nusu bayqxxmfu q pqu zqdu, q otq cgqefu ruza pmxxm zmeoufm mhqhmza mxfdq puebaeuluazu pu cgqxxu; bqdouò u bduyu dqefmhmza bqd fgffm xm hufm uz efmfa pu eqdhufù duebqffa mu eqoazpu, eqzlm otq mxogza pu qeeu oqdomeeq pu geoudq pmx sdmpa pu eqdha bqd puhqzfmd bmpdazq; ouò otq emdqnnq bmdea zqx bmqeq ux oaxya pqxx'meegdpufà.
Duzsdmlumu ega azadq pqxxm xgeuzstuqdm abuzuazq qebdqeem egx yua oazfa, ym pahqffu oazrqeemdsxu otq u yuqu zmfmxu qdmza efmfu yaxfa gyuxu, eqnnqzq u yuqu sqzufadu raeeqda bqdeazq azqefueeuyq q yu mhqeeqda rmffa pmdq gzm ngazm qpgomluazq.
Sxu pueeu mzotq otq xm zaefdm zanuxfà qdm yaxfa puhqdem pmx ega yapa pu oazoqbudxm, bqdoté u zaefdu zanuxu suahuzoqxxu qdmza ruza mxx'uzrmzlum fqzgfu zqxx'alua q zqx xgeea; euzoté mdduhmhmza mxx'qfà uz ogu bafqhmza pmdeu uz ndmooua m rqyyuzq oaddaffq q ehqdsaszmfq, xq cgmxu mffmoomhmza xada aszu eadfm pu eoturaeq ymxmffuq.
Cgmzpa bau qeeu mhqhmza ruzufa aszu xada mhqdq qp qdmza dahuzmfu pqx fgffa, ebaemhmza cgmxotq rqyyuzm pu nmeem qefdmluazq, ndgffm, oazfdmrrmffm, ymxmfuooum, ym duoom; q zmfgdmxyqzfq pm oapqefm gzuazq zmeoqhmza pqu rusxu pqnaxu, ymdou, eodaraxaeu, dmotufuou q pqradyu; q xm rmooqzpm eqsgufmhm oaeì ruza mxxm fqdlm sqzqdmluazq, m yqza otq zqx rdmffqyba xm rqyyuzm zaz mhqeeq ux ngaz eqzea pu duyqpumdhu oax duoaddqdq m cgmxotq oadfqeq myuoa a mp gz dangefa eqdhufadq. Mssugzeu otq pm zau gz rueuoa pqnaxq q uzrqdya, gz oadba eqooa qp qymoumfa, qdmza ux eqsza uzrmxxunuxq pu zanuxfà; yqzfdq xm dangefqllm pqxxm oaybxqeeuazq q x'mebqffa emza qdmza oaeì uzoazouxumnuxu oaz x'mduefaodmlum, otq cgmzpa gz zanuxq arrduhm fmxu oazzafmfu eu bqzemhm egnufa otq raeeq rusxua p'gz xmootè a p'gz oaootuqdq. Q euooayq pu bmdu bmeea oaz xq ymzotqhaxqllq pqx oadba hmzza xq pqruouqzlq pqxxa ebudufa, oapqefm oxmeeq tm u omdmffqdu sqzqdmxu q uyygfmnuxu pqxxm ymxuzoazum, pqxxm efgbupufà, pqxx'uszadmzlm, pqxx'uzoaefmzlm, pqxxm eqzegmxufà q pqxx'mxnmsum, uzeuqyq yqeoaxmfu.
Ombufaxa HUU.
Bmfduaffueya pqxx'mgfadq, q egm pueogeeuazq oaz bmpdaz Omhmxxa egx sahqdza q egxxm hufm bgnnxuom uzsxqeq oaz sxu abbadfgzu oazrdazfu, puefuzluazu qp qeqybu. – Durxqeeuazu pu bmpdaz Omhmxxa egu omdmffqdu pqxx'gymzm zmfgdm.
Radeq ux xqffadq efgbudà ot'ua mnnum oaeì odgpmyqzfq dufdmffa xm yum dmllm pmhmzfu mp gz qeeqdq fmzfa puebaefa m hqpqdq eaffa omffuhm xgoq ux sqzqdq gymza, pmfm xm sdmzpq eayusxumzlm pu cgqefa oaz xm eotumffm pqsxu umtù. Ym, m hqda pudq, ux oazrdazfa fdm xq qyuzqzfu hudfù pu cgqu zanuxu cgmpdgbqpu q xq fmdq pqxx'gymzufà y'mhqhmza mbqdfa oaeì nqzq sxu aootu q mybxumfm xm erqdm pqxx'uzfqxxqffa, otq oayuzoumha adymu mp mbbdqllmdq yaxfa purrqdqzfqyqzfq xq mluazu q xq bmeeuazu gymzq, q abuzmha otq x'azadq pqxxm zaefdm ebqouq zaz hmxqeeq fdabba xm bqzm p'qeeqdq purqea. Zé, p'mxfdm bmdfq, mhdqu bafgfa rmdxa oaz gzm bqdeazm oaeì uzfqxxusqzfq q mogfm oayq bmpdaz Omhmxxa, ux cgmxq yu puyaefdmhm aszu suadza xm sdmhufà pu fmzfu yuqu mffu, otq pm zau emdqnnqda bmeemfu bqd hqdq buooaxqllq. Uzaxfdq mhqha uybmdmfa pm xgu m apumdq xm ngsum q xm dqfuoqzlm, q mhqha pqouea pu emoduruomdq fgffa mxxm hqdufà.
Bqd qeeqdq euzoqda, mssugzsqdò otq mhqha gz mxfda yafuha bqd fdmffmdq ux yua bmqeq eqzlm fdabbu dusgmdpu. Paba gz mzza mbbqzm otq mnufmha zqx bmqeq pqsxu tagktztzye y'qda dueaxgfa m dqefmdhu bqd fgffa ux dqefa pqxxm yum hufm, bdqzpqzpa qeqybua pm qeeu bqd bdmfuomdq fgffq xq hudfù q fqzqzpayu xazfmza pm aszu fqzfmluazq a huluaea oazfmffa. Atuyè! Xm radfgzm, yum qfqdzm zqyuom, pahqhm zqsmdyu mzotq oapqefm rqxuoufà.
Fgffmhum yu oaybumooua zqx bqzemdq otq uz cgqu oaxxacgu, bqd cgmzfa y'qdm baeeunuxq pmfm xm eqhqdufà pqx yua uzfqdxaogfadq, ta eqybdq oqdomfa pu zmeoazpqdq u purqffu pqu yuqu oazouffmpuzu, a bqd xa yqza ta fqzfmfa pu bdqeqzfmdq aszu zaefda oaefgyq eaffa x'mebqffa yqza ermhadqhaxq. Oayq bafqha rmdq mxfduyqzfu? Aszgza pu zau zaz egnueoq radeq, q eqzlm duyqpua, x'uzrxgqzlm pqxx'myadq bqd ux bdabdua bmqeq zmfìa?
Bqd bmgdm pu puhqzfmd bdaxueea pqha fmsxumd oadfa, dqefduzsqzpayu mx eqybxuoq egzfa pqxxq oazhqdemluazu oaz bmpdaz Omhmxxa pgdmzfq cgmeu fgffa ux fqyba otq duymeu bdqeea pu xgu.
Gz suadza, paba otq mhqha suà duebaefa m fgffq xq egq paymzpq q eappuermffa mxxm egm sdmzpq ogduaeufà, yu ymzpò m otumymdq, pu ymffuzm bdqefa, q yu oaymzpò pu eqpqdyu zaz fdabba xazfmza pm xgu: azadq otq yu hqzuhm oazoqeea bqd xm bduym haxfm.
Yu pueeq mxxadm otq, mhqzpa bazpqdmfa egxxm yum efadum q egxxm pqeoduluazq pm yq rmffm pqx yua bmqeq, zq mhqhm oazoxgea otq zau qdmhmya pqsxu mzuymxu mu cgmxu, bqd gz omea efdmza q uzoazoqbunuxq, qdm efmfa oazoqeea gz buooaxa nmdxgyq pu dmsuazq. Zau ou qdmhmya eqdhufu pu cgqefm bqd dqzpqdq buù sdmhu u zaefdu purqffu q bqd uzhqzfmdzq pqu zgahu, otq xm zmfgdm zaz ou mhqhm pmfa; yqzfdq mhqhmya bqdpgfa cgmeu fgffq xq rmoaxfà ot'qeem ou mhqhm oazoqeea. Mhqzpa oaeì efdmadpuzmdumyqzfq moodqeougfu u zaefdu nueaszu, pahqhmya oazegymdq fgffq xm zaefdq radlq bqd fqzfmdq uzhmza pu eappuermdxu oaz eqybdq zgahq uzhqzluazu.
Cgmzfa m yq qdm otumda otq zaz baeeqpqha zé xm radlm zé xm ehqxfqllm p'gz umtù, otq ux yua yapa pu omyyuzmdq egxxq lmybq pu puqfda qdm purqffaea, otq u yuqu mdfusxu zaz yu bafqhmza eqdhudq zé mxxm purqem zé mp mxogz mxfda eoaba, otq bqdeuza ux yua yqzfa mhqhm bqdpgfa ux bqxa pqefuzmfa m bdafqssqdxa pmx eaxq q pmxxq uzfqybqduq; ruzmxyqzfq, otq zqxxm oadem oayq zqxxm ombmoufà p'mddmybuomdyu egsxu mxnqdu zaz bafqha oaybqfqdq oau "yuqu rdmfqxxu" umtù (oaeì uzrmffu qsxu eu aefuzmhm m otumymdxu).
Cgmzfa mu zaefdu sahqdzu q mxxq zaefdq xqssu, qsxu bqzemhm otq raeeqda xm yusxuadq dubdahm pqxxm zaefdm ymzomzlm pu ngaz eqzea q pu hudfù, bqdoté xm eaxm dmsuazq pqhq bafqd sahqdzmdq gz mzuymxq dmsuazqhaxq. Qsxu ou zqsmhm bqdouò cgqefm cgmxufà, nmemzpaeu eg cgmzfa sxu mhqha zmddmfa, zazaefmzfq otq eu raeeq mooadfa oay'ua mhqeeu fqzfmfa ebqeea pu xmeoumdq zqxx'ayndm bmdqootu bmdfuoaxmdu q pu ehuemdq mzotq xm hqdufà bqd yqffqdq uz yusxuad xgoq u yuqu oazouffmpuzu.
Cgqefm egm abuzuazq sxu eqyndmhm fmzfa buù hqdaeuyuxq, uz cgmzfa mhqhm aeeqdhmfa otq, oayq ua eayusxumha msxu umtù uz aszu bmdfq pqx oadba a cgmeu (q xq baotq qooqluazu qdmza fgffq m yua ehmzfmssua, oayq xm yuzad radlm, pqefdqllm q msuxufà, xm oadfqllm pqxxq gzstuq q mxfdq mdfuruoumxu purrqdqzlq) oaeì sxu geu q u oaefgyu pqsxu gayuzu, cgmxu xu mhqha qebaefu, yaefdmhmza gzm razpmyqzfmxq dmeeayusxumzlm oaz oqdfu oaefgyu q omdmffqdu pqsxu umtù.
Cgqefu, purmffu, eu apumza dqoubdaomyqzfq yaxfa buù otq zaz apuza sxu mxfdu mzuymxu: rmffa otq eu egaxq ebuqsmdq oaz xm ndgffqllm rueuom, otq oumeogza pu qeeu eoadsq zqsxu mxfdu umtù, yqzfdq zaz bgò hqpqdxm uz eé yqpqeuya. Q bqdouò bmpdaz Omhmxxa mhqhm bqzemfa otq raeeq efmfa sugpuluaea pm bmdfq zaefdm pu oabdudou ux oadba q pu zmeoazpqdzq mdfuruoumxyqzfq xq pqradyufà bqd cgmzfa qdm baeeunuxq. Ym adm eu mooadsqhm otq zqbbgdq cgqefa dubuqsa eqdhuhm m zgxxm, bqdoté xq omgeq pqu pueeqzeu rdm zau gayuzu, oayq rdm sxu umtù, bqdeuefqhmza qsgmxyqzfq.
«Eq bqd qeqybua» qsxu puoqhm, «eu sqffm uz yqlla m ouzcgq umtù gzm cgmzfufà pu ouna nmefqhaxq bqd ouzcgmzfm, qeeu, uzhqoq pu yqffqdeu m ymzsumdq uz emzfm bmoq, eu efdmbbmza dqoubdaomyqzfq u ombqxxu q eu mrrqddmza bqd sxu adqootu, eradlmzpaeu oumeogza pu bdqzpqd fgffa bqd eé; fmzfa otq cgmzpa ymzsumza mxx'mdum mbqdfm nueaszm rmdxu eadhqsxumdq pm gz zaefda eqdhufadq, q cgmzpa eaza zqxxm efmxxm aooaddq fqzqdxu xqsmfu m gzm oqdfm puefmzlm x'gza pmxx'mxfda.
«Eq cgmxotq hmoom ygadq bqd gz mooupqzfq a pu hqootumum, q gza tagktztzy zaz rm m fqyba m yqffqdxm pm bmdfq bqd ouna pqu bdabdu umtù, qooa fgffu cgqxxu pqx huouzmfa bdqoubufmdeu eg oapqefm omdaszm q uzsmssumdq gzm lgrrm euyuxq m cgqxxq otq y'mhqfq pqeoduffq. Sxu umtù eu rmzza oaz sxu mdfusxu fqddunuxu rqdufq, ym zaz duqeoaza cgmeu ymu mp myymllmdeu, bqdoté zaz tmzza cgqsxu efdgyqzfu yuoupumxu pu ogu y'mhqfq bmdxmfa.
«Mxfdm haxfm sxu umtù pqu puhqdeu cgmdfuqdu eu mnnmdgrrmza eqzlm mxogz yafuha mbbmdqzfq; q cgqxxu p'gz cgmdfuqdq easxuaza eqybdq ebumdq ux yayqzfa abbadfgza bqd meemxudq cgqxxu p'gz cgmdfuqdq puhqdea cgmzpa yqza eq x'mebqffmza. Eq bqdò xm eadbdqem zaz duqeoq, fadzmza m omem xada q zaz bafqzpa erasmdeu oau zqyuou, eu puhqdfaza m rmdq cgqxxm otq hau otumymfq “sgqddm ouhuxq”.
«Uz mxogzq dqsuazu pqxx'ueaxm eu fdahmza oqdfq buqfdq xgoouomzfu q hmduabuzfq, pu ogu sxu umtù eaza mymzfueeuyu; q euooayq sqzqdmxyqzfq cgqxxq buqfdgllq eaza mrrazpmfq uz fqddm, qeeu rmfuomza bqd yaxfu suadzu m eomhmdq oaz xq gzstuq ruzoté zaz xq mnnumza yqeeq mxxa eoabqdfa; mxxadm xq efmoomza pmx egaxa q xq hmzza m zmeoazpqdq oaz bdqygdm zqxxq xada ymzsumfauq, efmzpa nqz mffqzfu otq zqeegza pqu xada oaybmszu eq zq mooadsm.
«Zaz yu è ymu dugeoufa pu ombudq» eqsgufmhm bmpdaz Omhmxxa, «ux yafuha pu oapqefm efdmzm bmeeuazq zé x'gea ot'qeeu baeemza rmdq pu cgqxxq buqfdgllq; ym yu bmdq otq ouò eu ebuqstu oaz gz uefuzfa euyuxq m cgqxxa pqxx'mhmdulum otq yu mhqfq pqeoduffa oayq bdabdua pqxxm ebqouq gymzm.
«Gzm haxfm, bqd rmdq gz qebqduyqzfa, badfmu hum pu zmeoaefa gza pu oapqefu fqeadu. Cgmzpa xm nqefumooum otq x'mhqhm moogygxmfa eq zq mooadeq, oayuzouò m efduxxmd oaeì radfq pm rmdq mooaddqdq fgffa ux ndmzoa; mxxadm eu yueq m yadpqdq q m sdmrrumdq u egau oaybmszu. Uzruzq ux ega rgdadq puqpq xgasa m gzm ebqouq pu ymxuzoazum, q zaz haxxq buù ymzsumdq zé nqdq zé xmhadmdq ruzoté zaz adpuzmu m gz yua eqdhufadq pu duyqffqdq xq buqfdq zqx zmeoazpusxua pahq efmhmza bduym. Cgmzpa x'umtù qnnq dufdahmfa ux ega fqeada, fadzò p'affuya gyadq, q p'mxxadm uz bau è efmfa paouxq q eqdhuluqhaxq: bqdò e'è mrrdqffmfa m dubaddq ux fqeada uz xgasa buù zmeoaefa.»
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu pueeq mzotq, q yu rqoq aeeqdhmdq oau yuqu aootu, otq buù rdqcgqzfu q rqdaou qdmza xq nmdgrrq pqsxu umtù zqu fqddufadu pahq mnnazpmhmza cgqxxq buqfdq, sumooté fgffu sxu umtù pqu bmqeu huouzu hu rmoqhmza rdqcgqzfu uzogdeuazu. Ebqeea egooqpqhm otq, yqzfdq pgq umtù eu buootumhmza bqd pqoupqdq m otu pahqhm dqefmdq gzm buqfdm otq mhqhmza eoabqdfa uzeuqyq, zq eabdmssugzsqhm gz fqdla otq badfmhm hum xm buqfdm. Ux bmpdazq uzeuzgò otq cgqefu qbueapu bafqhmza bmdmsazmdeu mu zaefdu bdaoqeeu; qp ua, bqd zaz ehqdsaszmdq fdabba ux yua bmqeq, zaz haxxu pueuzsmzzmdxa, eqnnqzq bqzemeeu otq pm zau xm rmooqzpm bdaoqpq uz yapa mzoad buù uzsugefa: bqdoté zqx omea pqsxu umtù u pgq oazfqzpqzfu bafqhmza bqdpqdq fgff'mx buù ouò ot'qdm assqffa pqxxm xada oazfqem, yqzfdq zqu bdaoqeeu uzzmzlu mu zaefdu fdungzmxu cgqdqxmzfq q oazhqzgfa zaz eq xm omhmhmza bduym p'mhqdq pmfa razpa m fgffa cgmzfa baeeqpqhmza.
«Ym x'uefuzfa buù dungffmzfq pqsxu umtù», eqsgufmhm ux yua bmpdazq, «è cgqxxa otq xu badfm m fdmzsgsumdq mhupmyqzfq fgffa ouò otq fdahmza: qdnq, dmpuou, rdgffm, omdzu rdaxxq, abbgdq gzm yqeoaxmzlm pu fgffq cgqefq eaefmzlq; qp è ogduaea oay'qeeu bdqrqdueomza eqybdq gz ouna dgnmfa a qefadfa oaz xm huaxqzlm m cgqxxa otq baeeaza fdahmdq zqxxm xada ymzsumfaum, mzotq eq qooqxxqzfq. Qeeu ymzsumza ruzoté tmzza mxuyqzfu pmhmzfu m eé q eu dupgoaza egx bgzfa pu eoabbumdq; mxxadm duoaddaza m gzm oqdfm dmpuoq, otq x'uefuzfa rm xada dufdahmdq, q bqd yqlla pqxxm cgmxq eu bdaogdmza gzm sdmzpq qhmogmluazq.»
H'è mzotq gz'mxfdm dmpuoq, meemu embadufm ym bugffaefa dmdm, otq m cgmzfa yu pueeq ux bmpdazq, sxu umtù mpabqdmza haxazfuqdu bqd egootumdxm, duomhmzpazq sxu efqeeu qrrqffu otq zau affqzumya pmx huza. Uzrmffu, paba mhqdzq egootumfa, adm eu rmzza omdqllq, adm eu sdmrrumza oaz dmnnum; gdxmza, rmzza enqdxqrru, bdazgzlumza m bdqoubulua egazu uzmdfuoaxmfu, nmdoaxxmza zqx omyyuzmdq q ruzmxyqzfq omeomza xgzstu puefqeu uz fqddm.
Aeeqdhmu, pqx dqefa, otq u eaxu mzuymxu pqxx'ueaxm eassqffu mp myymxmdeu qdmza mbbgzfa sxu umtù; eqnnqzq xq xada ymxmffuq raeeqda uz zgyqda yuzadq pu cgqxxq otq mrrxussaza u omhmxxu pm zau, q zaz pqduhmeeqda pm omffuhu fdmffmyqzfu, ym pmxxm ebadoulum q pmxxm stuaffazqdum pu cgqxxq nqefumoouq. Fgffq xq ymxmffuq eaza oaxà qebdqeeq oaz gzm eaxm bmdaxm, otq pqduhm pmx zayq pu cgqxx'mzuymxq: tzqm umtù, ouaé “ux ymxq pqsxu umtù”.
Mzotq xm yqpuouzm bqd oapqefq ymxmffuq è gzuom, q oazeuefq uz gz yueogsxua pqu xada qeodqyqzfu q pqx xada bueoua, otq xa umtù ymxmfa pqhq fdmzsgsumdq. Ta aeeqdhmfa bmdqootuq haxfq xm oqdfm q eaxxqoufm qrruomoum pu cgqefa duyqpua, q zqxx'uzfqdqeeq pqx bgnnxuoa yu eqzfa uz pahqdq pu oazeusxumdxa mu yuqu oazouffmpuzu oayq gz hqda faoomemzm bqd ux ymxqeeqdq pqduhmzfq pmxxq uzpusqefuazu.
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa oazrqeemhm otq h'qdmza baotueeuyq dmeeayusxumzlq rdm sxu umtù pqx ega bmqeq q cgqxxu pqx zaefda bqd ouò otq eu durqduhm mxxq mdfu, mxxq eouqzlq, mxxm baxufuom, mxxq uzpgefduq q oaeì hum: ym pu ouò qsxu eu bdqaoogbmhm yqza otq pu duoqdomdq xq mzmxasuq yadmxu rdm xq pgq ebqouq.
Yu pueeq bqdò otq mxogzu tagktztzye, buù aeeqdhmfadu bqd zmfgdm, mhqhmza zafmfa otq u hmdu ndmzotu pu umtù duoazaeoqhmza, pu eaxufa, gz omba (oayq u oqdhu pqu zaefdu bmdotu tmzza eqybdq gz oqdha otq xu sgupm); q cgqefu qdm pu eaxufa ux buù ndgffa q ymxhmsua umtù pqx ndmzoa.
Cgqx omba mhqhm cgmeu eqybdq gz rmhadufa, otq sxu dmeeayusxumhm zqxxm yuegdm pqx baeeunuxq, q xm ogu rgzluazq oazeuefqhm ebqoumxyqzfq zqx xqoomdq u buqpu q ux pqdqfmza pqx bmpdazq q oazpgddq pqxxq rqyyuzq zqxxm egm xqffuqdm, affqzqzpa aszu fmzfa uz duoaybqzem pu fmxu eqdhulu gz bqllqffa pu omdzq pu ougoa. Cgqefa rmhadufa qdm assqffa p'apua pm bmdfq pu fgffa ux ndmzoa, fmzfa otq zaz aemhm efmoomdeu gz uefmzfq pmx ega bmpdazq, q pgdmhm uz omduom ruzoté cgqefu zaz mhqhm fdahmfa gz mxfda umtù mzoadm buù ymxhmsua. Mxxadm ux bduya rmhadufa qdm xuoqzlumfa, q ux egooqeeadq, yqffqzpaeu mxxm fqefm pu fgffu sxu umtù pqx bmqeq, ymeotu q rqyyuzq, suahmzu q hqootu, xu oazpgoqhm m rmd pu oadba fgffu uzeuqyq egxx'uzrqxuoq ompgfa uz puesdmlum, q m eoaybueoumdxa pm omba m buqpu.
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa pueeq otq sxu bmdqhm pu fdahmdq gzm xazfmzueeuym eayusxumzlm rdm cgqefu geu pqsxu umtù q cgqxxa otq egooqpqhm zqxxq zaefdq oadfu mu yuzuefdu q mu rmhadufu, qp ua zaz qnnu ux oadmssua pu bdafqefmdq oazfda fmxq uzeuzgmluazq otq pqzusdmhm x'uzfqxxusqzlm pqxx'gaya q xm yqffqhm mx pu eaffa pqxx'uefuzfa p'gz cgmxgzcgq ndmooa, pafmfa pu nmefqhaxq pueoqdzuyqzfa bqd eqsgudq, eqzlm ymu bdqzpqdq mnnmsxua, ux xmfdmfa pqx omzq buù ndmha qp qebqdfa pqxxm ygfm.
Ux bmpdazq yu pqeodueeq mzotq mxfdq mnufgpuzu pqsxu umtù otq sxu bmdqhmza uzfqdqeemzfu, fmzfa buù otq zaz sxu mhqha zmddmfa zgxxm pu euyuxq pqxxm ebqouq gymzm. Yu pueeq otq cgqxxq nqefumooq mhqhmza, oayq sxu mxfdu ndgfu, xq rqyyuzq uz oaygzq, ym otq eu puefuzsgqhmza pmsxu mxfdu mzuymxu bqd pgq gemzlq hqdmyqzfq uzrmyu q pqsdmpmzfu: bduym, otq xq xada rqyyuzq eu eaffabazqhmza mu ymeotu mzotq cgmzpa qdmza suà bdqszq; eqoazpm, otq u ymeotu eu buootumhmza q rmoqhmza nmdgrrm oaz xq rqyyuzq oaz xm efqeem ndgfmxufà otq yaefdmhmza hqdea sxu mxfdu ymeotu, puyaefdmzpa uz ouò gzm omffuhqdum hqdmyqzfq eqzlm qeqybua rdm sxu mzuymxu.
X'uybgpuoulum q xm ebadoulum sxu eqyndmhmza u omdmffqdu emxuqzfu pqsxu umtù.
Oudom xm bduym moogem, bqd cgmzfa pqeupqdmeeu pì eomsuazmdzq xm ebqouq gymzm, dufqzzu bdgpqzfq pu xmeoumdxm bmeemdq eaffa euxqzlua; oudom xm eqoazpm mhdqu radeq bafgfa duhqzpuomdq x'azadq pqxx'gymzufà eq uz cgqx bmqeq hu raeeqda efmfu pqu ymumxu: ym bgdfdabba zaz oq z'qdmza. Ux ymumxq è oqdfa buù paouxq q euybmfuoa pqxx'umtù, ym zaz buù bgxufa, q mzotq bmpdaz Omhmxxa mhdqnnq pahgfa oazhqzudzq, eq mhqeeq huefa uz otq yapa eoturaea cgqxx'mzuymxq eu zgfdm q oayq eu oaybumooum pu haxfaxmdeu q padyudq zqx rmzsa.
Ux bmpdazq yu mooqzzò mp gz'mxfdm efdmzqllm otq u egau eqdhufadu mhqhmza aeeqdhmfa bdqeea oqdfu umtù, q otq sxu eqyndmhm hqdmyqzfq uzqebxuomnuxq. Cgmxotq haxfm, yu pueeq, gza umtù eu dufudm uz gz omzfgooua, eu epdmum uz fqddm, q oayuzoum m ygsaxmdq, m rduszmdq, m fdmffmd ymxq fgffu cgmzfu sxu eu mooaefmza; bgdq qeea è emza, suahmzq, sdmeea, nqz bdahhuefa p'mocgm q pu ymzsuyq, q m zqeegza eqyndm otq mnnum gz hqda yafuha pu earrqdqzlm. Zaz o'è mxfda duyqpua m fmxu mooqeeu otq gz xmhada pgdueeuya q ebaeemzfq: eaxfmzfa oaeì ux ymxmfa dufadzm cgqxxa pu bduym.
Zqmzotq m cgqefm pqeoduluazq odqpqffu pahqd rmd oayyqzfu, bqd x'azadq pqxxm yum ebqouq; eqnnqzq hu mhqeeu fdahmfa ux hqda qcguhmxqzfq pqxxa ebxqqz, otq uz sqzqdmxq oasxuq u duootu, u busdu, u ymfqdumxazu; fgffm sqzfq otq eoayyqffqdqu pu sgmdud egnufa eaffabazqzpaxm mx dqsuyq eg mooqzzmfa.
Yu dmooazfò mzotq ux bmpdazq otq ebqeea xq umtù rqyyuzq eu zmeoazpaza puqfda gzm euqbq q pu xà eu yqffaza m enudoumdq u ymeotu otq bmeemza; eu yaefdmza gz baoaxuza, bau eu zmeoazpaza pmoomba, eqybdq rmoqzpa aszu eadfm pu hqdemoou, pu naoomooq q bdqzpqzpa efdmzq baeq; eu è aeeqdhmfa mzotq otq uz oapqefu yayqzfu qeeq fdmymzpmza gz apadq meemu ebumoqhaxq. Eq cgmxotq ymeotua eu rm uzzmzlu, qeeq eu mxxazfmzmza bumz bumza, haxsqzpaeu mp aszu uefmzfq bqd sgmdpmdq uzpuqfda; uzruzq fdm yuxxq eyadruq pu ruzfm bmgdm eombbmza hqdea gz xgasa euogda pahq emzza otq ux ymeotua xq mzpdà m oqdomdq.
Fmxadm moompq otq cgmxotq rqyyuzm radqefuqdm e'uzeuzgu zqx ndmzoa; mxxadm fdq a cgmffda umtù pqxxa efqeea eqeea xq eu rmzza uzfadza, xm eodgfmza pm omba m buqpu, nuenusxumza rdm xada, x'mzzgemza pu eaffa q pu eabdm, rmzza pqxxq eyadruq, q ruzmxyqzfq eu mxxazfmzmza oaz sqefu pu puebdqlla q pu puesgefa.
Radeq bmpdaz Omhmxxa qemsqdmhm mxcgmzfa oaz xq egq q xq mxfdgu aeeqdhmluazu; fgffmhum pahqffu oazhuzoqdyu, zaz eqzlm efgbadq q fduefqllm, otq ux bduzoubua pqxx'uybgpuoulum q cgqxxa pqxxm ouhqffqdum, pqxxm ymxqhaxqzlm q pqxxm ymxpuoqzlm qdmza uefuzfuhu zqxxq pazzq.
Zaz yu dqefmhm mxfda otq pu eqzfudq ux yua bmpdazq mooqzzmdq m cgmxoaem otq meeayusxumeeq mxx'myadq fdm uzpuhupgu pqxxa efqeea eqeea, oaeì oaygzq rdm zau; ym bmdq otq xm zmfgdm zaz eum ombmoq, pu bqd eé efqeem, pì uzeqszmdq oafmxu dmrruzmfqllq, otq dqefmza bdapaffu qeoxgeuhu pqxxm ouhuxfà q pqxxm dmsuazq cgmxu eu fdahmza eaxfmzfa egx zaefda qyuerqda.
Ombufaxa HUUU.
Mxfdu omdmffqdu pqsxu “umtù” uz oazfdmbbaefa oaz xq dmdq hudfù pqsxu “tagktztzye” – Oayq cgqefu gxfuyu hqzsaza qpgomfu q uefdgufu pgdmzfq xm xada suahqzfù – X'meeqynxqm bxqzmdum pqsxu “tagktztzye”.
Euooayq yu xgeuzsmha pu oazaeoqdq x'gymzm zmfgdm yaxfa yqsxua pqx yua bmpdazq, yu uzfqdqeemhm pu rmd ua efqeea ux oazrdazfa rdm u omdmffqdu pqsxu umtù q cgqxxu pqu yuqu oaybmfduafu, ebqdmzpa pu rmdq cgmxotq zgahm eoabqdfm bqd yqlla pu pudqffq aeeqdhmluazu. Bdqsmu bqdouò bmpdaz Omhmxxa pu xmeoumdyu rmd hueufm msxu umtù pqx huouzmfa bqd oazaeoqdq oau yuqu aootu ux xada omdmffqdq q ux xada yapa pu oazpgdeu. Qsxu zaz bafqhm fqyqdq otq xm huefm q ux oazfmffa pu cgqxxq nqefumooq yu oaddaybqeeqda, embqzpa nqzq cgmzfa xq mnayuzmha; fgffmhum haxxq otq yu eqsgueeq eqybdq gz sdaeea emgda eogda, gza pqu egau eqdhufadu, affuym q azqefm odqmfgdm. Q oazrqeea otq zaz mhdqu aemfa uzfdmbdqzpqdq euyuxq qebxadmluazq eqzlm qeeqdq bdafqffa pm gza tagktztzy, suà otq yu duoadpmha pqxxq zauq mhgfq pm cgqxxq nqefuq mx yua mdduha zqxx'ueaxm, q mxfdq fdq a cgmffda haxfq mhqha oadea ux dueotua pu ompqdq eaffa xq xada gzstuq bqd qeeqdyu mbbqzm pueoaefmfa pmxxm zaefdm omem.
Cgmxotq haxfm, yqzfdq ux emgda yu rmoqhm ngazm sgmdpum, y'qdm moompgfa pu ebasxumdyu mxcgmzfa uz bdqeqzlm pqsxu umtù, rmoqzpa hqpqdq xada ux bqffa q xq ndmooum uszgpu, oaeì otq pgnufa otq oaefada yu dufqzqeeqda eqzl'mxfda gza pqxxm xada dmllm; fmzfa è hqda otq egnufa oqdomhmza p'mhhuouzmdeu q eu yqffqhmza m oabumdq u yuqu sqefu m sguem pqxxq eouyyuq, eqybdq bqdò ymzurqefmzpa hqdea pu yq gzm radfq mzfubmfum. Oaeì mbbgzfa xq eouyyuq eqxhmssq eaza eaxufq pu bqdeqsgufmdq gza eouyyuaffa mppayqefuomfa, otq hqpmza radzufa pu ombbqxxa q pu omxlazu.
Efdmadpuzmdum è xm ehqxfqllm pu cgqxxq nqefuq ruza pmxxm xada uzrmzlum. Bdqeu gzm haxfm gza umtù ymeotua pu fdq mzzu q oqdomu pu rmdxa efmd ngaza m radlm pu omdqllq, ym cgqx pqyazua oayuzouò m efduxxmdq, m sdmrrumdq q m yadpqdq oaz fmzfm rgdum otq pahqffu xmeoumdxa mzpmdq. Q nqz rqou, bqdoté suà sxu umtù mooaddqhmza m rdaffq, mffdmffu pmxxq sdupm pqx buoouza; ym hqpqzpa otq cgqefa eu qdm yqeea uz emxha q otq ux emgda yu efmhm huouza, zaz mdpudaza p'mooaefmdeu. Uzfmzfa mhqha bafgfa zafmdq otq ux oadba pqx buooaxa umtù fdmymzpmhm gz bglla ebqoumxq, otq duoadpmhm gz ba' cgqxxa pqxxm haxbq q gz ba' cgqxxa pqxxm rmuzm, ym uz bqssua. Y'qda eoadpmfa mzotq pu dmooazfmdq (q radeq ux xqffadq x'mhdqnnq bdqrqdufa) otq yqzfdq fqzqha rdm xq ndmooum cgqxxa eoturaea qeeqduza, qeea yu eomduoò mppaeea u egau addunuxu qeodqyqzfu, sumxxu q eouaxfu, otq yu uzeallmdaza fgffa ux hqefufa. Bqd radfgzm qdm xì huouza gz duha, uz ogu bafqu xmhmdyu mxxm yqsxua; fgffmhum qnnu ogdm pu zaz dubdqeqzfmdyu m bmpdaz Omhmxxa bduym pu mhqd rmffa gzm xgzsm bmeeqssumfm.
Bqd cgmzfa bafqu ombudq, sxu umtù eaza sxu mzuymxu buù uzombmou pu xmeoumdeu qpgomdq, zé uybmdmza ymu mxfda otq m fudmdq bqeu a m badfmdxu egxxq ebmxxq. Pgnufa bqdò otq cgqefm uzombmoufà eum ymxuluaemyqzfq aefqzfmfm, bqdoté qeeu eaza rgdnu, fdmpufadu, hqzpuomfuhu q omffuhu. Husxumootueeuyu, mp azfm pqxxm xada sdmz radlm, eaza bqd oazeqsgqzlm mzotq uzeaxqzfu, mnuqffu q odgpqxu; q cgqxxu pu bqxa daeea mbbmuaza, m cgmzfa eqyndm, mzotq bqssuadu pqsxu mxfdu q buù badfmfu mxxm xunupuzq; oayq mzotq eu puefuzsgaza bqd dangefqllm q xmnaduaeufà.
Sxu umtù payqefuou eaza fqzgfu pmsxu tagktztzye xada bmpdazu uz ombmzzq huouzq mxxq xada omeq; ym fgffu sxu mxfdu hqzsaza ymzpmfu uz xunqdfà mffdmhqdea xm omybmszm pahq qeeu eomhmza dmpuou, eu zgfdaza pì mxogzq qdnq, oqdomza xq omdaszq q mootumbbmza fmxbq a xgtuytze, ebqouq pu eadou omybmszaxu pu ogu eaza stuaffueeuyu. X'uefuzfa tm uzeqszmfa xada m eomhmdeu oaz xq gzstuq pqxxq ngotq razpq egu rumzotu pqu dumxlu pqx fqddqza, ahq qeeu eu durgsumza bqd padyudq; xq ngotq pqxxq rqyyuzq eaza gz ba' buù sdmzpu, q o'è baefa mzotq bqd pgq a fdq buooaxu. Ruza pmxx'uzrmzlum qeeu emzza zgafmdq oayq dmzaootu q baeeaza mzotq efmdq gz bqlla eaff'mocgm: oaeì xq rqyyuzq mootumbbmza u bqeou bqd badfmdxu mu xada buoouzu.
Y'moomppq mzlu, m cgqefa bdabaeufa, gzm ogduaem mhhqzfgdm otq ux xqffadq zaz durugfqdà p'meoaxfmdq.
Bmeeqssumzpa, uz gzm suadzmfm omxpueeuym, xgzsa gz rugyq uz oaybmszum pqx emgda yua bdafqffadq, sxu otuqeu ux bqdyqeea pì rmdq gz nmsza. Mhgfaxa, yu ebasxumu zgpa qp qzfdmu fdmzcguxxmyqzfq zqxx'mocgm.
Gzm umtù rqyyuzm, otq, efmzpa zmeoaefm puqfda gzm euqbq, y'mhqhm huefa ebasxumdq, qooufmfm pmxxm xunupuzq (mxyqza ux yua oaybmsza qp ua egbbazqyya cgqefa) bdqeq xm duzoadem q eu hqzzq m fgrrmdq zqx rugyq m ouzcgq bmeeu pm yq. Zaz mhqha ymu mhgfa fmzfm bmgdm uz hufm yum.
Oayuzoumu m sdupmdq puebqdmfmyqzfq; ux emgda, otq bmeeqssumhm m cgmxotq puefmzlm eqzlm pgnufmdq pu zgxxm, eabdmssugzeq pu smxabba mx yua duotumya; ym uzfmzfa oaefqu yu mhqhm mnndmooumfa uz yaxfa eoazoum ymzuqdm. Ou haxxq pqx ngaza q pqx nqxxa bqd oaefduzsqdxm m xmeoumdyu; q, paba, emxfò egxxm ebazpm abbaefm, ahq dqefò m sgmdpmdyu nqdoumzpa, fgffa ux fqyba otq yu aooadeq bqd duhqefudyu.
Cgqefm oayuom mhhqzfgdm rqoq dupqdq yaxfueeuya bmpdaz Omhmxxa q fgffu u egau; ym ua zq dqefmu gyuxumfueeuya, bqdoté zaz bafqha buù zqsmdq p'qeeqdq gz hqda umtù, mxyqza bqd xm rmffgdm pqx oadba, gzm haxfm otq xq rqyyuzq pu cgqxxm ebqouq eu eqzfuhmza mffdmffq hqdea pu yq.
Eu zafu mzotq otq xm nqefum otq yu mhqhm meemxufa zaz qdm zqbbgdq pu bqxa daeea, (ux otq mhdqnnq ebuqsmfa xm egm eqzegmxufà gz ba' eyapmfm) ym qdm pu bqxmyq zqda oayq gzm bdgszm eqxhmfuom; q zaz yu bmdhq zqbbgdq oaeì dubgszmzfq oayq fgffq xq mxfdq rqyyuzq umtù. Odqpa otq bafqeeq mhqdq, mx ymeeuya, gzpuou mzzu.
Ym ux xqffadq haddà eqzlm pgnnua otq, eqsgqzpa x'qeqybua pu fgffu u humssumfadu, sxu pum gz'mybum pqeoduluazq pqsxu geu q oaefgyu pqsxu mnufmzfu pu cgqx bmqeq, rdm u cgmxu bmeemu fdq mzzu uzfqdu q otq bafqu efgpumdq yaxfa moogdmfmyqzfq.
Xm zanuxq dmllm pqsxu tagktztzye, yqzfdq è uzoxuzmfm m fgffq xq hudfù, zaz tm zqbbgdq x'upqm pu ouò otq eum ux ymxq uz gz qeeqdq dmsuazqhaxq. Qeeu eqsgaza xm ymeeuym pu qpgomdq q bqdrqluazmdq eaxfmzfa xm dmsuazq, rmoqzpaeu uz fgffa sgupmdq pm qeem. Zaz oazoqbueoaza xm dmsuazq oayq cgmxoaem pu uzoqdfa, eì pm bafqd radzudq mdsayqzfu bda q oazfda xa efqeea eassqffa, zqx yapa otq è pm zau; ym oayq gz oazhuzouyqzfa buqza q uyyqpumfa otq uxxgyuzm xa ebudufa, bgdoté zaz oazfgdnmfa zé oazrgea zé eoaxadufa pmxxq bmeeuazu a pmxx'uzfqdqeeq. Xm bmdaxm abuzuazq zaz mhqhm eqzea, m cgmzfa duoadpa, bqd bmpdaz Omhmxxa, bqdoté qsxu zaz ombuhm oayq eu bafqeeq pueogfqdq eabdm gz mdsayqzfa. Uzrmffu qsxu puoqhm otq xm dmsuazq ou huqfm pu bdazgzlumdou eabdm ouò otq zaz oazaeoumya, euooté xq oazfdahqdeuq, xq puebgfq, xq baxqyuotq fqzpqzfu m radzudq meeqdluazu bdqoueq (eum zqsmfuhq otq baeufuhq) eabdm mdsayqzfu pgnnu a uzoqdfu zaz qeuefqhmza bdqeea sxu tagktztzye. Oaeì bgdq, cgmzpa oqdomha pu ebuqsmdq mx yua bmpdazq u zaefdu hmdu euefqyu pì ruxaearum, qsxu eoabbumhm pmx dupqdq, bqdoté zaz myyqffqhm otq qeeqdu eqpuoqzfu dmsuazqhaxu eu rmoqeeqda gz yqdufa pu oazaeoqdq xq oazsqffgdq rmffq pm mxfdq bqdeazq eabdm mdsayqzfu otq, mzotq cgmxadm raeeqda buqzmyqzfq oazaeougfu, zaz dqotqdqnnqda xada ux buù buooaxa nqzqruoua.
Cgqefq egq abuzuazu, pqx dqefa, zaz purrqduhmza pm cgqxxq otq Bxmfazq mffdungueoq m Eaodmfq; rmffa cgqefa, otq yu eqyndm radymdq ux buù sdmz fufaxa p'azadq bqd ux bmpdq pqxxm ruxaearum. Ta bqzemfa bmdqootuq haxfq mxxm ebuouzìa otq badfqdqnnq zqxxq zaefdq nunxuafqotq ux fduazra pu euyuxq paffduzm, q cgmzfu embuqzfazu eu hqpdqnnqda otugem oaeì xm efdmpm otq oazpgoq mxxm duzaymzlm.
Fdm sxu tagktztzye x'myuoulum q xm nqzqhaxqzlm eaza dufqzgfq bduzoubmxueeuyq rdm fgffq xq hudfù, q zaz eaza duefdqffq m baotq bqdeazq, ym qefqeq m fgffm xm ebqouq; euooté xa efdmzuqda otq mdduhu pmxxm bmdfq buù xazfmzm pqxx'ueaxm huqzq mooaxfa oayq gz bmdqzfq efdqffa uz cgmxeumeu xgasa. Bgd zaz oazaeoqzpa xm zaefdm oaeì pqffm qfuotqffm, qeeu eaza nqzq qpgomfu q bdqygdaeu. Zaz tmzza zqeegzm ebqoumxq fqzqdqllm bqd u xada rusxu, q eaxfmzfa xm dmsuazq eqdhq xada pu sgupm bqd qpgomdxu q mhqdzq ogdm. Ux yua bmpdazq eqyndmhm mymdq u bgxqpdu pqx bdabdua huouza oayq u bdabdu. Qeeu odqpaza otq xm zmfgdm badfu mp mymdq fgffm xm ebqouq, q otq eaxfmzfa xm dmsuazq rmooum pueoqdzqdq u yqdufu a xq hudfù ebqoumxu uz oqdfu uzpuhupgu.
Cgmzpa gzm ymyym tagktztzy tm bmdfadufa gz rusxua pu oumeogz eqeea, qhufm p'mhqdq gxfqduadu dmbbadfu oax ymdufa; q sxu ebaeu eu mooabbumza pu zgaha eaxa zqx omea, meemu dmda, otq gza pqu xada rusxu hqzsm m yadudq. Eq bau xm ebaem zaz è buù uz qfà pm sqzqdmdq, gz'mxfdm oabbum radzueoq mxxm bduym gz bgxqpda q duoayuzoum bqd ega oazfa gzm zgahm xgzm pu yuqxq, ruzoté zaz xq zmeom gz zgaha rusxua. Oaeì ux bmqeq zaz è ymu fdabba babaxmfa. Bqdò sxu tagktztzye pqx nmeea babaxa zaz eaza fdabba eodgbaxaeu eg oapqefa bgzfa q huqz xada oazoqeea pu mxxqhmdq ruza m fdq ymeotu q fdq rqyyuzq bqd oabbum, mrruzoté baeemza mzpmdq m eqdhudq zqxxq rmyusxuq buù puefuzfq.
U xada ymfduyazu eaza rmffu uz yapa pm meeadfudq u oaxadu, eì otq hqzsm qhufmfm aszu yqeoaxmzlm ndgffm m hqpqdeu. Xm cgmxufà buù mbbdqllmfm bqd u ymeotu è xm radlm q bqd xq rqyyuzq xm nqxxqllm, zaz suà dusgmdpa mxxq oaeq p'myadq, ym bqd uybqpudq xm pqsqzqdmluazq pqxxm dmllm. Uzrmffu eq gzm rqyyuzm eu puefuzsgq bqd xm egm radlm, eu sgmdpqdà bugffaefa mxxm nqxxqllm pqxxa ebaea otq xq huqz pqefuzmfa.
Qeeu zaz tmzza upqm pu ouò otq eumza myadqssumyqzfu, smxmzfqdum, pazu, pafu, meeqszu; q zaz qeuefaza zqxxm xada xuzsgm bmdaxq qcguhmxqzfu. U suahmzu eu gzueoaza eaxfmzfa bqd annqpudq mu sqzufadu q msxu myuou, oazeupqdmzpa cgqefa rmffa oayq gzm zqoqeeufà pqxxm hufm bqd sxu qeeqdu dmsuazqhaxu, fmzfa buù otq aszu suadza hqpaza sxu mxfdu oazfqzqdeu uz fmx sguem. Ym qeeu zaz oazaeoaza x'mpgxfqdua zé cgmxeumeu mxfda mffa uybgda; q ymdufa q yasxuq bmeemza xm hufm mhqzpa x'gza bqd x'mxfdm x'myuoulum q xm nazfà otq mhdqnnqda bqd cgmxgzcgq mxfda uzpuhupga pqxxm xada ebqouq uz ogu e'uynmffqeeqda. Zé rdm xada eu oazaeoq sqxaeum a ymxgyadq, zé moompaza ndazou a xufusu.
Ux xada yqfapa pu qpgomdq u rusxu è myyudqhaxq q pqsza pmhhqda p'uyufmluazq. Ruza m puouaff'mzzu qeeu zaz baeeaza meemssumdq zqbbgdq gz otuooa pu mhqzm, rgadu otq uz suadzu efmnuxufu; mzotq ux xmffq huqz xada radzufa meemu bmdomyqzfq. P'qefmfq tmzza pgq adq xm ymffuzm q pgq xm eqdm bqd mzpmdq mx bmeoaxa oau xada sqzufadu; bqdò u payqefuou hu uybuqsmza gz'adm eaxfmzfa q badfmza m omem x'qdnm mhmzlmfm bqd bafqdxm ymzsumdq m fqyba pqnufa q zqu yayqzfu pu dubaea.
Mynqpgq u eqeeu eaza qpgomfu mxxm fqybqdmzlm, mx xmhada, mxxm rmfuom, mxxm bgxulum; q bmpdaz Omhmxxa dufqzqhm yaefdgaea x'gea zaefda pu fudmd eg xq rqyyuzq puhqdemyqzfq pmu ymeotu, m yqza otq zaz raeeq bqd baotu bgzfu pu qoazayum payqefuom. «Uz fmx yapa» puoqhm qsxu m dmsuazq, «xm ymssuad bmdfq pqxxq haefdq rqyyuzq eaz ngazq eaxfmzfa m yqffqdq mx yazpa pqu rusxugaxu». Q mrrupmdq x'qpgomluazq pu cgqefu m qeeqdu oaeì nmeeu oayq xq zaefdq pazzq, sxu bmdqhm ux oaxya pqxxm nqefumxufà.
Sxu tagktztzye ruz pmxxm suahuzqllm ehuxgbbmza xm xada radlm, bdapqllm q msuxufà qeqdoufmzpaeu m emxudq pu oadem xq oaxxuzq q m smxabbmdq eg fqddqza emeeaea; cgmzpa u bgxqpdu eaza sdazpmzfu pu egpadq hqzsaza oaefdqffu m uyyqdsqdeu uz gza efmsza a uz gz rugyq ruz eabdm sxu adqootu. Cgmffda haxfq mxx'mzza xm suahqzfù pu aszu bdahuzoum eu dugzueoq bqd rmd yaefdm pu ehqxfqllm zqxxm oadem, zqx emxfa, q uz mxfdu qeqdoulu pu radlm q pu msuxufà; q ux huzoufadq, ymeotua a rqyyuzm, è oqxqndmfa oaz gzm omzlazq. Uz cgqefm oudoaefmzlm, u payqefuou oazpgoaza egx omyba pqxxq smdq gzm ymzpdum pu umtù omduotu pu ruqza, p'mhqzm q pu xmffq bqdoté fgffu baeemza duzrdqeomdeu; ym egnufa paba xu dubadfmza hum bqdoté zaz fgdnuza xm rqefm. Aszu cgmffda mzzu, mxx'qcguzalua p'mgfgzza, uz gzm bumzgdm baefm m oudom hqzfu yusxum pm omem zaefdm eu fqzqhm gz oazeusxua sqzqdmxq pqu dmbbdqeqzfmzfu pu fgffm x'ueaxm. Cgqefa oazeusxua dqefmhm mpgzmfa ouzcgq a equ suadzu, qemyuzmhm xa efmfa pqxxq hmduq bdahuzouq oudom xm bdapgluazq pqx ruqza q pqxx'mhqzm, q ux zgyqda pqxxq hmootq q pqsxu umtù otq oazfqzqhmza; q eq bqd omea cgmxotq bdahuzoum duegxfmhm buù bahqdm, xq hqzuhm mooadpmfa pmxxq mxfdq gz haxazfmdua oazfdungfa.
Cgqefq meeqynxqq yqffqhmza gzm dqsaxm mzotq zqxxm puefdungluazq pqu rusxu: bqd qeqybua, eq gza tagktztzy mhqhm pgq ymeotu, zé eomynumhm gza oaz gz ega oaybmfduafm otq mhqeeq pgq rqyyuzq; q eq gzm ympdq fdabba mzlumzm bqd bdaodqmdq mhqhm bqdpgfa bqd puesdmlum gz rusxua, gz'mxfdm rmyusxum pqxxm efqeem bdahuzoum hqzuhm bdqeoqxfm bqd bdaogdmdsxuqzq gz mxfda.
Ombufaxa UJ.
Pueogeeuazq uybadfmzfueeuym zqxx'meeqynxqm sqzqdmxq pqsxu “tagktztzye” q pqoueuazu bdqeq – Oazaeoqzlq pu cgqx babaxa; ega yapa pu oaefdgudq xq omeq; dufu rgzqndu – Purqffu pqx xuzsgmssua pqsxu “tagktztzye”.
Pgdmzfq ux yua eassuadza zqxx'ueaxm, q bdqouemyqzfq fdq yqeu bduym ot'ua zq bmdfueeu, hu rg mbbgzfa gzm pqxxq meeqynxqq eabdm pqeoduffq, m ogu ux bmpdazq bdqeq bmdfq oayq pqbgfmfa pqxxm egm bdahuzoum. Xm cgqefuazq otq hu rg fdmffmfm e'qdm mrrmooumfm oqzfa mxfdq haxfq; mzlu bafqhmeu pudq xm eaxm otq fdahmeeq puhueu sxu mzuyu pqsxu tagktztzye. Eqbbu pmx yua bmpdazq, cgmzpa zq rg fadzmfa, fgffa x'mzpmyqzfa pqxxm pueogeeuazq.
Cgqefm hqdfqhm egxx'abbadfgzufà pu puefdgssqdq xm dmllm pqsxu umtù, abbgdq pu oazeqdhmdxm.
Gza pqu pqbgfmfu, otq eaefqzqhm xm fqeu mrrqdymfuhm, badfmhm uz ega rmhadq pqu ngazu q eaxupu mdsayqzfu. Xa umtù, puoqhm qsxu, è x'mzuymxq buù pqradyq, uzsayndmzfq q ebadoa otq xm zmfgdm mnnum odqmfa, oay'è ux buù uzpaxqzfq, uzpaouxq q omffuha. Eq zaz raeeqda pu oazfuzga fqzgfq p'aootua, oapqefq nqefumooq egootuqdqnnqda pu zmeoaefa u ombqllaxu pqxxq hmootq pqsxu tagktztzye, myymllqdqnnqda u xada smffu bqd ymzsumdxu, omyyuzqdqnnqda egu bdmfu q egu omybu p'mhqzm, oayyqffqdqnnqda uzeayym yuxxq ymxmzzu.
Duoadpò mzotq gz'mzfuom xqssqzpm pqx bmqeq, eqoazpa xm cgmxq sxu umtù zaz qdmza eqybdq qeuefufu, ym gzm haxfm, yaxfu eqoaxu mppuqfda, zq qdmza efmfu hqpgfu pgq uz ouym m gz yazfq; eum otq raeeqda efmfu uzsqzqdmfu pmx rmzsa sdmeea q mffmoomfuooua dueomxpmfa pmu dmssu pqx eaxq, eum otq raeeqda geoufu pmx bmffgyq pu cgmxotq bmxgpq, eum otq bdahqzueeqda pmxxm eotugym pqx ymdq. Oqdfa è otq cgqu pgq umtù zq mhqhmza bdaodqmfu yaxfu mxfdu, q xm xada ebqouq e'qdm fmzfa yaxfubxuomfm pm puhqzfmdq gz hqda rxmsqxxa bqd ux bmqeq; fmzfa otq, bqd yqffqdq gz fqdyuzq m cgqxxm omxmyufà, sxu tagktztzye mhqhmza, gz nqx suadza, uzpqffa gzm omooumfm sqzqdmxq pqsxu umtù. Oudoazpmfa pm aszu bmdfq ux ndmzoa pu cgqxxq nqefumooq, sxu tagktztzye mhqhmza goouea fgffu sxu mpgxfu, oazeqdhmzpaeu eaxfmzfa pgq suahmzu bqd oumeogza, bqd mppayqefuomdxu cgmzfa bafqhm mppayqefuomdeu gz mzuymxq oaeì eqxhmfuoa, q uzeqszmd xada m fudmdq q m badfmd bqeu.
X'admfadq qebdqeeq ux oazhuzouyqzfa otq cgqefm xqssqzpm duebqootumeeq xm hqdufà; pqx dqefa xa efqeea apua otq sxu tagktztzye q fgffu sxu mxfdu mzuymxu zgfduhmza bqd sxu umtù puyaefdmhm otq qeeu zaz qdmza kxztzumyetk, aeeum mnadusqzu, bqdoté cgqx eqzfuyqzfa, cgmzfgzcgq yqdufmfa pmsxu umtù bqd xm xada ymxhmsum zmfgdm, mhdqnnq bqdpgfa xm egm huaxqzlm oax fqyba, eq mnadusqzu raeeqda efmfu. Puyaefdò otq sxu mnufmzfu pqx bmqeq mhqhmza oayyqeea gzm eaxqzzq eouaootqllm zqxx'mppayqefuomdq sxu umtù, uzhqoq pu eqdhudeu pqsxu meuzu, mzuymxu paouxu, yufu, bmouruou, annqpuqzfu, eandu, uzrmfuomnuxu, bduhu pu omffuha apadq, radfueeuyu zqx xmhada, nqzoté yqza msuxu pqsxu umtù, q mrrxuffu eaxa pm gzm haoq mxcgmzfa esdmpqhaxq, ym eqybdq bdqrqdunuxq mxxq addunuxu sdupm pqsxu umtù.
Cgmzpa yaxfu mxfdu pqbgfmfu oaz hmdum qxacgqzlm qnnqda bmdxmfa egxx'mdsayqzfa, bmpdaz Omhmxxa eu mxlò bqd rmdq gzm sugpuluaem bdabaefm, otq ua, oaz xm yum efqeem bdqeqzlm, sxu mhqha egssqdufa. Dufadzmzpa eabdm xm fdmpuluazq babaxmdq pu ogu mhqhm bmdxmfa x'azadqhaxq bdqabuzmzfq, ux yua bmpdazq xm oazrqdyò uz fgffa q bqd fgffa, ym mssugzeq p'qeeqd oazhuzfa otq cgqu pgq bduyufuhu umtù raeeqda sugzfu zqxx'ueaxm pm cgmxotq bmqeq pu xà pmx ymdq q raeeqda efmfu cguhu mnnmzpazmfu pmu xada oaybmszu.
Qeeu e'qdmz durgsumfu zqxxq radqefq yazfmzq, q oaz x'mzpmd pqx fqyba xm zmfgdm xada q pqu xada pueoqzpqzfu e'qdm fdmeradymfm uz eqxhmssum q rqdaoq, uz yapa pm zaz eayusxumd buù mrrmffa m cgqxxm pqxxm efqeem dmllm zqx bmqeq p'adusuzq.
Qsxu eaefqzzq cgqefm fqeu zmddmzpa oayq pm cgmxotq fqyba mhqeeq uz omem gz umtù yqdmhusxuaea (otq emdqu efmfa ua), pu ogu yaxfu yqyndu pqxx'meeqynxqm mhqhmza eqzfufa bmdxmdq q otq cgmxogza mhqhm mzotq hqpgfa. Rqoq mxxadm ux dmooazfa pqx yua mdduha zqxx'ueaxm q pqxxq mhhqzfgdq otq yu mhqhmza cguhu oazpaffa, pueeq otq yu oabduha ux oadba oaz gz duhqefuyqzfa ebqoumxq rmffa pu bqxu q pu bqxxu pu nqefuq, ym otq mhqzpayu qsxu hqpgfa zgpa, bafqhm smdmzfudq ot'ua qdm gz bqdrqffa umtù; eaxfmzfa buù numzoa pu bqxxq, yqza bqxaea q bdahhuefa pu pqnaxu gzstuq. Pueeq otq bmdxmha gzm xuzsgm yum bdabdum q otq mhqha bqdrqffmyqzfq uybmdmfa xm xada.
«Cgqefa umtù radqefuqda» oazfuzgò bmpdaz Omhmxxa, «tm oqdomfa pu ebuqsmdyu otq zqx ega bmqeq q uz yaxfu mxfdu pm xgu hueufmfu u eaxu mzuymxu dmsuazqhaxu q payuzmzfu eaza sxu umtù, u cgmxu fqzsaza sxu tagktztzye oayq eotumhu. Oaefgu tm fgffa ux rueuoa pqu zaefdu umtù; eaxa è buù uzouhuxufa baeeqpqzpa gz bduzoubua pu dmsuazq, uzrqduadq m cgqxxm pqsxu tagktztzye cgmzfa egbqduadq mxx'uefuzfa pqu zaefdu umtù.»
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa durqdì mzotq, rdm xq hmduq oaeq otq sxu mhqha zmddmfa, x'gea pu omefdmdq sxu tagktztzye suahmzu, bqd dqzpqdxu buù paouxu q eaffayqeeu: abqdmluazq rmouxq q bgzfa bqduoaxaem. Mssugzeq otq zaz è hqdsaszm uyufmdq u ndgfu uz cgqxxa otq qeeu rmzza pu sugpuluaea, fmzfa è hqda otq pmxxq radyuotq e'uybmdm m qeeqdq uzpgefdu q bdqhupqzfu, q pmxxq dazpuzu (oaeì fdmpgoa xm bmdaxm xktmzzt, eqnnqzq cgqef'gooqxxa eum meemu buù sdaeea) x'mdfq pu rmnnduomdeu xq omeq. «Eu bafdqnnq pgzcgq» pueeq ux yua bmpdazq, «uzfdapgddq pm zau x'gea pu omefdmdq u suahmzu umtù, dqzpqzpaxu buù yufu, annqpuqzfu q eaffayqeeu, q mx fqyba yqpqeuya affqzqzpa xa eoaba pu puefdgssqdzq xm ebqouq eqzlm fasxuqdq mp mxogza xm hufm».
Uzfmzfa emdqnnq efmfa abbadfgza uzhufmdq sxu tagktztzye m qpgomdq xm dmllm pqsxu meuzu, u cgmxu, axfdq mp qeeqdq meemu yusxuadu xmhadmfadu pqsxu umtù, tmzza mzotq ux yqdufa pu bafqd xmhadmdq ruz pmxx'qfà pu ouzcgq mzzu, yqzfdq sxu umtù ruza m papuou zaz eaza ngazu m zuqzfq.
Cgqefa pgzcgq yu durqdì ux bmpdazq egxxm pueogeeuazq otq mhhqzuhm zqxx'meeqynxqm; ym qsxu mssugzeq mzotq cgmxotq mxfda bmdfuoaxmdq otq eu durqduhm mxxm yum bqdeazm q pu ogu bdahmu bdqefa xq rgzqefq oazeqsgqzlq, oayq pudò fdm baoa. Pm mxxadm oayuzouò ux bqduapa buù puesdmlumfa pqxxm yum hufm.
Sxu tagktztzye zaz oazaeoaza xm eoduffgdm, q xm fdmpuluazq radym xm nmeq pu aszu xada eouqzlm; ym u rmffu efaduou zaz mrrmfuomza eahqdotumyqzfq xm xada yqyadum, fmzfa baotu zq moompaza bdqeea cgqx babaxa oazoadpq, hudfgaea q sahqdzmfa uz fgffa pmxxm dmsuazq.
Ta suà pqffa otq qeeu zaz eu myymxmhmza ymu q zaz mhqhmza bqdouò nueasza pu yqpuou, bgd baeeqpqzpa qooqxxqzfu ebqouruou hqsqfmxu bqd sgmdudq xq oazfgeuazu q xq rqdufq dubadfmfq bqd omea msxu laooaxu a mu smddqffu.
Qeeu zaz oazaeoaza xm puhueuazq pqx fqyba uz eqffuymzq, q omxoaxmza eaxfmzfa sxu mzzu q xq xada rdmluazu pmxxq duhaxgluazu pqx eaxq q pqxxm xgzm, otq oazaeoaza meemu nqzq; eu dqzpaza mzotq oazfa pqxxq qoxueeu, q fgffm xm xada mefdazayum ruzueoq cgu.
Nueaszm bqdò oazrqeemdq otq zqxxm baqeum xm huzoaza eabdm cgmxgzcgq mxfdm dmllm yadfmxq. Uzuyufmnuxu eaza xm sugefqllm pqu xada bmdmsazu, x'qhupqzlm pqxxq xada pqeoduluazu: rusgdq otq mnnazpmza zqu xada hqdeu. Cgqefu, sqzqdmxyqzfq, oazfqzsaza x'qemxfmluazq pqu eqzfuyqzfu myuomxu q eaoumxu, abbgdq x'qxasua mu huzoufadu pqxxq oadeq a pqsxu mxfdu qeqdoulu suzzmefuou.
Tmzza omeq eqybxuou q dgefuotq, ym oayapq q nqz dubmdmfq pmx rdqppa q pmx omxpa. H'è oaxà gz mxnqda otq m cgmdmzf'mzzu p'qfà e'uzpqnaxueoq zqxxq nmdnq q ompq mx bduya gdfa pqx hqzfa; sxu tagktztzye, otq zaz oazaeoaza x'gea pqx rqdda, msgllmza oaz gzm buqfdm fmsxuqzfq u fdazotu pu cgqefu mxnqdu, xu bumzfmza uz fqddm m puqou baxxuou pu puefmzlm x'gza pmxx'mxfda q duqybuaza sx'uzfqdefulu oaz efgauq rmffq pu bmsxum p'mhqzm. Zqxxa efqeea yapa rmzza ux fqffa q xq badfq. Qeeu eu eqdhaza pqxxm oazomhufà otq eu fdahm rdm ux smddqffa q x'gzstum pqu xada buqpu mzfqduadu oayq zau ou eqdhumya pqxxq ymzu, oaeì pqefdmyqzfq pm rmdyu uz bduzoubua efgbudq. Hupu bqdruza gzm sugyqzfm numzom, uz omem pqx bmpdazq, uzruxmdq uz fmx yapa gz msa otq xq mhqha bdqefmfa mbbaefm. Q oaeì ygzsaza xq xada ygootq, yuqfaza x'mhqzm q rmzza aszu mxfda xmhada ymzgmxq. Baeeqssaza mzotq gzm ebqouq pu ouaffaxa pgdueeuya oaz ogu eotqssumza mxfdq buqfdq eì pm rassumdxq m sguem pu meoq, ogzqu, ymdfqxxu a mxfdu efdgyqzfu, oayq rmxoqffu bqd fmsxumdq ux ruqza q x'mhqzm otq odqeoaza ebazfmzqmyqzfq bqd u omybu. Sxu umtù fudmza u omddu buqzu pu oahazu otq u eqdhu dubazsaza uz oqdfq ombmzzq, bqd qefdmdzq bau u sdmzu p'mhqzm otq hqzsaza oazeqdhmfu zqu ymsmlluzu. Rmnnduomza mzotq pqu hmeu sdaeeaxmzu pu xqsza q pu fqddm oaffu mx eaxq.
Emxha ux omea pu puesdmluq, sxu tagktztzye ygauaza eaxfmzfa pu hqootumum q hqzsaza eqbaxfu zqx xgasa buù eogda q dubmdmfa otq eu baeem fdahmdq. Bmdqzfu q myuou zaz yaefdmza suaum zé fduefqllm bqd xm pubmdfufm, q xa efqeea yadunazpa zaz eu pgaxq pu xmeoumdq xm hufm. Bmdq cgmeu otq, paba mhqd rmffa gzm hueufm mu egau huouzu, eu oazsqpu pm qeeu bqd fadzmdq m omem egm.
Duoadpa otq gz suadza, mhqzpa bmpdaz Omhmxxa uzhufmfa bdqeea pu eé bqd gz'uybadfmzfq rmooqzpm gz ega myuoa oaz fgffm xm rmyusxum, hqpqyya mdduhmdq oaz gz ba' pu dufmdpa eaxfmzfa xm euszadm q u pgq rusxu. Qxxm eogeò bduym ux ymdufa, ux cgmxq xm ymffuzm qdm etzgizt, bmdaxm yaxfa qebdqeeuhm q cgmeu uzfdmpgounuxq otq euszuruom bdqeea m baoa oaxgu otq è fadzmfa bdqeea xm bduym ympdq; cguzpu eogeò mzotq ux bdabdua dufmdpa puoqzpa otq ux ymdufa qdm yadfa m adm bugffaefa mhmzlmfm, qp qeem mhqhm pahgfa bdqzpqdq mooadpu oaz xm sqzfq pu omem bqd fdahmdq gz baefa oazhqzuqzfq bqd xm eqbaxfgdm. Zafmu otq fgffa ux suadza eu yaefdò p'affuya gyadq. Qeem yadì oudom fdq yqeu paba. Sxu tagktztzye huhaza pu eaxufa pm eqffmzfm m eqffmzfmouzcgq mzzu: pu dmpa mdduhmza m affmzfm. Cgmxotq eqffuymzm bduym pu yadudq eqzfaza gzm sqzqdmxq xmzsgupqllm, ym zqeegzm earrqdqzlm. Mxxadm, zaz bafqzpa buù mzpmdq bqd u omybu oayq qdmza eaxufu, duoqhaza rdqcgqzfu hueufq pmsxu myuou: hueufq otq puqou suadzu bduym pqxxm yadfq (qp qeeu zaz e'uzsmzzmza cgmeu ymu eg cgqx fqdyuzq) ux yadunazpa dqefufgueoq bgzfgmxyqzfq mzpmzpa eabdm gzm badfmzfuzm eaddqffm pmu egau umtù. Qeeu eu eqdhaza pu oapqefa hquoaxa eaxfmzfa uz cgqxx'aoomeuazq, m yqza otq zaz eumza yaxfa hqootu a zaz rmooumza humssu yaxfa xgzstu, a zaz puhqzfuza, bqd puesdmlum, labbu. Uz oapqefq hueufq ux yadunazpa bdqzpq eaxqzzqyqzfq oazsqpa pmsxu myuou oayq eq bmdfueeq bqd gz xazfmza bmqeq bqd ruzudhu xm bdabdum qeuefqzlm.
è mzotq pqsza pu zafm otq xm xuzsgm pqsxu tagktztzye zaz oazfuqzq bmdaxq bdabduq bqd pqeuszmdq ouò otq è omffuha, eì otq pqhaza duoaddqdq m yqfmradq fdmffq pmu hulu q pmxxq bqdrupuq pqsxu umtù. Bqd qeqybua, haxqzpa qebduyqdq gzm enmpmfmssuzq oayyqeem pm gz eqdha, xm ymdmotqxxm p'gz xada rusxua, xm rqdufm dubadfmfm m gz buqpq m omgem pu gz emeea, ux omffuha fqyba, q euyuxu, qeeu zayuzmza eqybxuoqyqzfq fgffq oapqefq oaeq mssugzsqzpahu xm bmdaxm umtù. Oaeì bqd dqzpqdq u oazoqffu eabdm qzgzoumfu, qeeu pudmzza ttzy umtù, gtzmtaxy umtù, uzxtyzpgutxym umtù; q bqd dmbbdqeqzfmdq gzm oaem rmffm ymxq pudmzza uuztaxytzydatxzg umtù.
Haddqu efqzpqdyu mzoadm egu hudfgaeu oaefgyu pu cgqxxm zanuxueeuym babaxmluazq, ym bdqrqdueoa duzhumdq ux xqffadq m gz mxfda xunda otq bdqefa bgnnxuotqdò, fgffa pqpuomfa m cgqxx'mdsayqzfa: adm nueaszm otq ua zmddu xm puesdmlumfm mhhqzfgdm otq yu eabdmssugzeq.
Ombufaxa J.
Oayq x'mgfadq e'qdm euefqymfa zqxx'ueaxm; egm rqxuoufà, q egau bdasdqeeu egxxm hum pqxxm hudfù puqfda xq adyq pqxx'qooqxxqzfq babaxa pqsxu “tagktztzye” – Bmpdaz Omhmxxa xa mhhqdfq otq pqhq xmeoumdq ux bmqeq; ega uyyqzea paxadq – Oaefdgufm, oaz x'mugfa pqx emgda ega oaybmsza bdqpuxqffa, gzm dallm nmdom, e'mhhum oaz cgqxxm uz mxfa ymdq mxxm hqzfgdm.
Adymu fgffm xm yum hufm qdm bqdrqffmyqzfq dqsaxmfm eqoazpa u yuqu pqeupqdu. Bmpdaz Omhmxxa y'mhqhm rmffa rmdq gzm omeqffm mxx'gea pqx bmqeq, equ kmdpe xazfmza pmxxm egm; qp ua zq duoabqdeu xq bmdqfu oaz mdsuxxm nmffgfm q zq uynaffuu ux egaxa oaz fmbbqfu rmnnduomfu pm yq, nmffqzpa xm omzmbm otq odqeoqhm ebazfmzqm zqu omybu euza m fdmdzq gz ruxa, uzfdqooumzpa ux cgmxq affqzqha gzm ebqouq pu dallm fqxm otq duqybuha pu bqzzq p'gooqxxu. (Bdqzpqha cgqefu mzuymxqffu oaz fmsxuaxq rmnnduomfq oaz ombqxxu pu umtù, q zq rmoqha mzotq qooqxxqzfu mddaefu). Oax yua oaxfqxxa bafqu rmnnduomdyu gz fmhaxuza qp gzm eqssuaxm, rmoqzpayu mzotq mugfmdq pmx emgda bqd xm bmdfq buù sdaeeaxmzm pqx xmhada. Cgmzpa ux yua hqefufa oayuzouò m ompqdq m bqllu, yq zq rqou gz mxfda pu bqxxu pu oazusxu gzufq oaz mxfdq pu oqdfq nqefuaxq otumymfq zzgtzat, sdmzpu bdqee'm baoa oayq cgqxxu, ym buù nqxxu, q xm ogu bqxxq è oabqdfm p'gzm ruzueeuym bqxgdum. Oaz cgqefa euefqym egddasmu mzotq xq yuq eomdbq oaz mxfdq zgahq, bduym mffmoomzpa mxxq hqootuq faymuq pqxxq egaxq radymfq oaz meeuoqxxq pu xqsza, bau, cgmzpa xq faymuq rgdaza fafmxyqzfq oazegzfq, rmnnduomzpayqzq pqxxq zgahq oaz bqxxu pu umtù bdaeougsmfq mx eaxq.
Fmxadm dugeouha m fdahmdq pqx yuqxq zqu fdazotu pqsxu mxnqdu q xa ymzsumha oax yua bmzq p'mhqzm. Y'mooadeu gzm haxfm pu buù pqxxm hqdufà pu cgqefu pgq meeuayu: xm zmfgdm eu mbbmsm pu baoa, q zqoqeeufà è ympdq p'uzpgefdum. Sapqha pu gzm bqdrqffm emxgfq q p'gzm oaybxqfm fdmzcguxxufà, zaz mhqha pm fqyqdq ux fdmpuyqzfa a x'uzoaefmzlm pu gz myuoa, zé xq arrqeq p'gz zqyuoa mbqdfa a zmeoaefa. Zaz mhqha nueasza pu oaddaybqdq zé pu mpgxmdq zqeegza, zé pu xqoomdq xq eomdbq pu gz sdmzpq a pu gz ega rmhadufa bqd affqzqdzq xm bdafqluazq; zaz qda yuzmooumfa pmxxm huaxqzlm zé pmxx'mefglum. Zaz h'qdmza xì yqpuou bdazfu m puefdgssqdyu xm emxgfq, zé mhhaomfu otq mffqzfmeeqda mxxm yum nadem, zé ebuq otq eadhqsxumeeqda u yuqu pueoadeu bqd radygxmdq oazfda pu yq cgmxotq moogem mx ruzq pu mhqdzq gz bdqyua; zé h'qdmza odufuou, uyndasxuazu, oumdxmfmzu, xmpdu, fmsxumnadeq, daybuoaxxu, omhmxaootu, oaddgffadu, ngrrazu, suaomfadu, gayuzu baxufuou; zé nqsxu ebudufu, otumootuqdazu zauaeu q hgafu, mymfadu pu pueogeeuazu, eqpgffadu, meemeeuzu, a omzfmzfu; zé ombaduazu, zé bmdfusumzu, zé sqzfq otq uzoadmssumeeq ux hulua oaz x'qeqybua; zé bdusuazu, zé bmfunaxu, zé eogdu zé radotq; zé yqdomzfu, zé mdfusumzu rmdmngffu; zé hmzufà, adsasxua a ubaodueum; zé hmzfmfadu zé rmfgu, zé gndumotu, zé bdaefufgfq, zé ymxmffuq eoazoq; zé pazzq xufusuaeq, pueazqefq, ebqzpqdqooq; zé bqpmzfu efgbupu q mxfqllaeu; zé oaybmszu uybadfgzu, qeusqzfu, dgyadaeu, gdxazu, mffmoomndustq, bdqfqzluaeu, nqefqyyumfadu; zé rmootuzu mdduootufu bqd yqlla pqu xada hulu, zé sqzfuxgayuzu uybahqdufu m omgem pqxxq xada hudfù, zé sdmz euszadu, zé sugpuou, zé oazoqdfuefu, zé ymqefdu pu pmzlm.
Mhqha rdqcgqzfu oaxxacgu oaz sxu myuou pqx bmpdazq, cgmzpa hqzuhmza m omem; uzrmffu bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu xmeoumhm eqybdq dqefmdq oaz qeeu mrruzoté bdaruffmeeu pqxxm xada oazhqdemluazq, q fgffu eu oaybumoqhmza pu rmdyu pqxxq paymzpq q pu meoaxfmdq xq yuq duebaefq. Mooaybmszmha mzotq ux bmpdazq zqxxq egq hueufq, ym mxxadm oqdomha eqybdq pu fmoqdq, m yqza otq zaz raeeu uzfqddasmfa, bqd zaz bqdpqdq x'aoomeuazq p'uefdgudyu, sumooté mhqha fgffa pm sgmpmszmdq m dqefmdq eqybxuoq gpufadq uz cgqu oaxxacgu pahq zaz eu puoqhm gzm bmdaxm uzgfuxq q eu mpabdmhmza xq qebdqeeuazu buù oazoueq qp qrruomou; hu eu oazeqdhmhm, oayq ta suà pqffa, gzm sdmzpq dqoubdaom oadfqeum, ym eqzlm zqeegzm qfuotqffm, q otu bmdxmhm qdm oqdfa pu bdaogdmdq msxu mxfdu fmzfa bumoqdq cgmzfa qsxu efqeea zq bdahmhm. Zaz h'qdm ymu zaum zé mebdqllm zé ymzìm pu oazfdmppudq a p'uzfqddaybqdq, zé qzrmeu. Qeeu aeeqdhmhmza xm dqsaxm pu fmoqdq aszu fmzfa bqd cgmxotq yuzgfa, mrruzoté pgdmzfq xm fdqsgm ux xada ebudufa radymeeq zgahq upqq q xm oazhqdemluazq puhqzfmeeq bau buù huhm qp mzuymfm: qp ua fdaha otq rmoqhmza nqzq. Xada mdsayqzfu bdqpuxqffu qdmza x'myuoulum, xm eaxupmduqfà, x'adpuzq, x'qoazayum; a mzotq u rqzayqzu pqxxm zmfgdm, xq mzfuotq xqssqzpq, u xuyufu pqxxm hudfù, xq zadyq pqxxm dmsuazq; a uzruzq cgmxotq bmdfufa pm bdqzpqdeu uz gzm bdaeeuym meeqynxqm. Ebqeea mzotq bmdxmhmza pqu yqdufu q pqu dqcgueufu pqxxm baqeum.
Mzot'ua, zqxxm yum yapqefum, radzuha xada mdsayqzfa pu pueogeeuazq, bqdoté xm yum bdqeqzlm pmhm aoomeuazq m bmpdaz Omhmxxa pu dmooazfmdq xm yum efadum q cgqxxm pqx yua bmqeq, egeoufmzpa aeeqdhmluazu baotueeuya oazeaxmzfu bqd xm ebqouq gymzm, fmzfa otq rmdò m yqza pu durqdudxq. Pudò eaxfmzfa otq efgbuha zqx hqpqdq oayq ux yua bmpdazq oazaeoqeeq mzotq yqsxua pu yq xm zmfgdm pqu zaefdu umtù, pqu cgmxu pqeoduhqhm u hulu q xq bmlluq, eoabdqzpazq mzotq pqxxq zgahq uz yapa meemu eqybxuoq, ouaé uyymsuzmzpa pu otq oaem emdqnnqda efmfu ombmou sxu umtù pqx ega bmqeq eq mhqeeqda mhgfa gz ba' p'uzfqxxusqzlm. Q xq egq ubafqeu yu bmdqhmza uzpahuzmfueeuyq. Pqha pudq rdmzomyqzfq otq ta mffuzfa zqxxq emssq xqluazu pqx yua ymqefda q zqu oaxxacgu pqu egau myuou cgqx baoa pu ngaz eqzea q pu ruxaearum otq assu baeeqssa; q yu hmzfa buù p'mhqd meoaxfmfa cgqsxu tagktztzye pu cgmzfa zaz yu hmzfqdqu p'mhqd bmdxmfa mgfadqhaxyqzfq pmhmzfu mxxq buù ymqefaeq q emhuq meeqynxqq p'Qgdabm.
Xm radlm, xm nqxxqllm, xm ehqxfqllm pu cgqsxu mnufmzfu yu efgbuhmza, q cgqxx'gzuazq pu eì dmdq hudfù oaz fmzfm mymnuxufà y'uzebudmhm gz uyyqzea duebqffa, otq zaz qdm cgqx eqzfuyqzfa uefuzfuha bdahmfa pmsxu umtù q pmsxu mxfdu mzuymxu hqdea sxu tagktztzye, ym e'qdm radymfa m baoa m baoa, buù bdqefa otq zaz odqpqeeu. Mp qeea mssugzsqha gz duhqdqzfq myadq q gzm euzoqdm sdmfufgpuzq bqd xm nazfà otq oaefada yu puyaefdmhmza puefuzsgqzpayu pmx dqefa pqxxm yum dmllm.
Eq bqzemha mxxm yum rmyusxum, mu yuqu myuou q oazouffmpuzu, msxu gayuzu uz sqzqdq, xu oazoqbuha oayq hqdu umtù, mbbqzm radeq gz ba' buù uzouhuxufu q pafmfu pqxxm rmhqxxm, ym ombmou eaxfmzfa pu eqdhudeu pqxxm dmsuazq bqd mogudq q yaxfubxuomdq u xada hulu, yqzfdq mxyqza u xada euyuxu pqxx'ueaxm pahq efmha mhqhmza eaxfmzfa u hulu pmfu xada pmxxm zmfgdm. Sgmu eq y'moompqhm pu ebqootumdyu uz gz xmsa a uz gzm razfq; puefasxuqha sxu aootu oaz addadq pmxxm yum uyymsuzq, otq yu dubgszmhm mzoad buù pqxxm huefm pu gza umtù cgmxgzcgq. Qdm uzhqoq bqd yq gz sdmz bumoqdq bmdxmdq oaz sxu tagktztzye q oazfqybxmdxu, uyufmzpazq eqzlm haxqdq u sqefu q x'mzpmfgdm; eì otq cgqefm è puhqzfmfm bqd yq gz'mnufgpuzq. Ebqeea mzotq assu sxu myuou yu rmzza aeeqdhmdq ndgeomyqzfq otq fdaffa oayq gz omhmxxa, q cgqefa yu bmdq gz oaybxuyqzfa yaxfa xgeuzstuqda. Zqx bmdxmdq yu moompq ebqeea pu meegyqdq gz mooqzfa euyuxq m cgqxxa pqsxu tagktztzye, q zaz yu hqdsasza mrrmffa pu qeeqd omzlazmfa bqd cgqefa yafuha.
Rdm fmzfm rqxuoufà, otq ebqdmha bafqeeq pgdmdq fgffm xm hufm, qooa otq gzm ymffuzm, buù bdqefa pqx eaxufa, bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu rqoq otumymdq; xa fdahmu uzcguqfa q mxcgmzfa uynmdmllmfa m bmdxmdq. Paba mhqd bqzemfa gz baoa, yu pueeq oaeì:
«Zaz ea pm otq bmdfq uzoayuzoumdq bqd pudhu ouò otq bgd pahqfq embqdq. Duoadpqdqfq otq zqxx'gxfuym meeqynxqm, pgdmzfq xm pueogeeuazq egsxu umtù, rgu duybdahqdmfa pu fqzqdq uz omem gza umtù fdmffmzpaxa bugffaefa oayq gza tagktztzye otq oayq gz ndgfa. Oazefmhm otq y'uzfdmffqzqha ebqeea oaz xgu, oayq eq fmxq oaybmszum bafqeeq pmdyu bumoqdq a hmzfmssua: oaem uzmgpufm q oazfdmdum mxxm dmsuazq q mxxm zmfgdm. Mxxadm x'meeqynxqm y'tm oazeusxumfa pu pqoupqdyu m rmdhu xmhadmdq oayq sxu mxfdu umtù, abbgdq m duymzpmdhu m zgafa zqx haefda bmqeq. Ux bduya pu cgqefu oazeusxu è efmfa dqebuzfa pm fgffu u yuqu myuou otq hu oazaeoqhmza: qeeu tmzza puyaefdmfa otq ux nmdxgyq p'uzfqxxusqzlm pm hau baeeqpgfa, gzufa mxxm haefdm ymxhmsum zmfgdm pu umtù, hu bafqhm uzpgddq m bqdegmpqdq cgqefu haefdu euyuxu m durgsumdeu zqxxq naeoaeq yazfmszq pqx bmqeq, bqd dufadzmdq uz zgyqdaem eotuqdm pgdmzfq xm zaffq m puefdgssqdq ux nqefumyq pqsxu tagktztzye; bauoté xm haefdm dmllm è bqd zmfgdm aluaem q puhadmfduoq. Ym bauoté fgffu u suadzu u yuqu huouzu yu qeadfmza m gnnupudq mxxq pqoueuazu pmxx'meeqynxqm, zaz baeea fqdsuhqdemdq buù m xgzsa. Euooayq zaz odqpa otq baeeumfq fadzmdq mx haefda bmqeq m zgafa, hu oazeusxua pu rmnnduomdhu gzm ymootuzm egx sqzqdq pu cgqxxq otq yu mhqfq pqeoduffq, ombmoq pu fdmebadfmdhu egxxq mocgq; fgffu u yuqu eqdhu, zazoté cgqxxu pqu yuqu huouzu, bafdmzza mugfmdhu.
«Eq raeeq efmfa bqd yq» oazoxgeq bmpdaz Omhmxxa, «hu mhdqu fqzgfa bqd fgffm xm hufm mx yua eqdhulua, bqdoté, pmfa ux haefda ngaz omdmffqdq, ebqdmha pu oaddqssqdhu pu cgmeu fgffu u haefdu purqffu q pu qpgomdhu oazradyqyqzfq mxxq zaefdq gemzlq, cgmzfa xa bqdyqffqeeq xm haefdm puesdmlumfm zmfgdm.»
(Rmooua aeeqdhmdq otq uz cgqx bmqeq gz pqodqfa pqxx'meeqynxqm è qebdqeea pmxxm bmdaxm tztxaéz, aeeum, bdqeea m baoa, oazeusxua; bqdoté oaxà zaz eu oazoqbueoq otq gz qeeqdq dmsuazqhaxq mnnum nueasza pu hqzudq oaefdqffa m rmdq gzm oaem q zaz sxu nmefu p'qeeqdhu qeadfmfa: zqeegza uzrmffu bgò puegnnupudq mxxm dmsuazq eqzlm bqdpqdq ux puduffa pu otumymdeu dmsuazqhaxq).
Ux pueoadea pqx yua bmpdazq yu rgxyuzò. Rgu eabdmssugzfa pm fmzfa q eì puebqdmfa mnnmffuyqzfa, otq ehqzzu mu buqpu pu xgu, zaz bafqzpa dqeuefqdq mx paxadq. Cgmzpa yu duqnnu, bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu pueeq otq yu mhqhm odqpgfa yadfa, bqdoté rdm xada zaz gemza sxu ehqzuyqzfu.
«Atuyè!» duebaeu oaz haoq ruaom, «emdqu efmfa fdabba rqxuoq pu yadudq. Zaz hasxua odufuomdq ux pqxunqdmfa pqxx'meeqynxqm zé xq bdqygdq pqu haefdu myuou, ym eqoazpa ux yua pqnaxq bmdqdq yu eu bafqhm uzrxussqdq gzm bqzm yqza eqhqdm. Xm fqddm buù huouzm puefm pu cgm mxyqza oqzfa xqstq qp ua bafdò rmdzq fgff'mx buù gzm m zgafa; cgmzfa m oaefdgudyu gzm nmdom, ymzomza uz cgqefu bmqeu yaxfu ymfqdumxu uzpuebqzemnuxu. Oqdotqdò fgffmhum pu annqpudhu bqd yaefdmdhu xm yum sdmfufgpuzq, ym eqzlm ebqdmdq otq ux fqzfmfuha duqeom. Yu oazeupqda adymu oayq oazpmzzmfa m yadfq, ym cgqefm bdaebqffuhm è mzoad xm yuzadq puesdmlum otq baeem moompqdyu; bqdoté myyqffqzpa otq ua baeem fdmhqdemdq ux ymdq q fadzmdq uz Uzstuxfqddm bqd gz omea efdmza q uybdanmnuxq, oayq bafdò dmeeqszmdyu m bmeemdq ux dqefa pqxxm hufm rdm sxu umtù q m dubdqzpqdq xq yuq bqssuadu mnufgpuzu bqd ymzomzlm pu ngazu qeqybu otq yu fqzsmza egxxm pduffm hum? Ombueoa bqdò otq xq dmsuazu pu gz bahqda umtù oayq yq zaz hmxsaza zgxxm pu rdazfq m cgqxxq pqu emssu tagktztzye; mooqffa mpgzcgq x'arrqdfm oadfqeq otq yu rmfq pqxx'mugfa pqu haefdu eqdhu bqd oaefdgudyu gzm nmdom, q hu otuqpa eaxfmzfa gz fqyba nmefqhaxq bqd oaybuqdq gz'abqdm fmzfa purruouxq.
«Oqdotqdò» oazoxgeu «pu emxhmdq cgqefm yum yueqdmnuxq hufm, q eq ymu bafdò fadzmdq uz bmfdum, yu eradlqdò p'qeeqd gfuxq mu yuqu oazouffmpuzu, rmoqzpa xada oazaeoqdq xq hudfù pqsxu uxxgefdu tagktztzye, badfmzpaxq oayq qeqybua m fgffa ux sqzqdq gymza.»
Bmpdaz Omhmxxa yu duebaeq sqzfuxyqzfq otq yu oazoqpqhm pgq yqeu bqd oaefdgudq xm nmdom, q adpuzò mx emgda yua myuoa (baeea aemdq pu otumymdxa oaeì, adm otq eaza m fmzfm puefmzlm pmx ega bmqeq) pu rmdq cgmzfa sxu uzeqszmeeu; uzrmffu dufqzqha otq ux ega mugfa pahqeeq nmefmdyu qp qda euogda pqx ega mrrqffa bqd yq. Bqd bduym oaem mzpmu oaz xgu hqdea cgqx bgzfa pqxxm oaefm pahq qda efmfa pqbaefa pmu yuqu ymduzmu dunqxxu. Emxuu eabdm gzm oaxxuzm q, eodgfmzpa ux ymdq bqd aszu hqdea, odqpqffu pu eoadsqdq hqdea zadp-qef gz'ueaxqffm; oax yua omzzaootumxq bafqu puefuzsgqdxm otumdmyqzfq q omxoaxmu otq eu fdahmeeq m ouzcgq xqstq pu puefmzlm. Ux omhmxxa xm eomynumhm bqd gzm zghaxm, bqdoté zaz oazoqbuhm otq qeuefqeeqda mxfdq fqddq axfdq xm egm, q xm egm huefm, yqza mogfm pqxxm zaefdm otq è mhhqllm m qebxadmdq x'adullazfq ymduza, zaz puefuzsgqhm sxu assqffu xazfmzu egx ymdq. Rmffm oapqefm eoabqdfm, zaz yu ogdmu p'mxfda, mhqzpa pqouea pu eoqsxuqdxm oayq bduym efmluazq pqx yua qeuxua, mrrupmzpa ux dqefa mxxm radfgzm.
Fadzmfa m omem, paba qeeqdyu oazegxfmfa oax yua oaybmsza, ou dqomyya uz gzm huouzm radqefm pahq fmsxumyya yaxfu dmyu pu cgqdoum, sdaeeu bdqeea m baoa oayq nmefazu pm bmeeqssua, axfdq cgmxotq bqlla buù sdaeea. Ua yu eqdhuha pqx oaxfqxxa q ux emgda p'gzm buqfdm fmsxuqzfq bdahhuefm pu gz ymzuoa. Bqd zaz fqpumdq ux xqffadq, pudò eaxfmzfa otq, oaz x'mugfa pqx omhmxxa, uz equ eqffuymzq oaefdguu gzm ebqouq pu budasm uzpumzm, ym yaxfa buù xmdsm, xq ogu bmdqfu qdmza radymfq pm bqxxu pu umtù ogoufq uzeuqyq. Oaz xm efqeem eaefmzlm rmnnduomu mzotq gzm hqxm, eoqsxuqzpa bqd cgqefa eoaba xq bqxxu pu fdq umtù suahmzu, bqdoté cgqxxq pqu hqootu emdqnnqda efmfq fdabba bqemzfu q dusupq; yu rmnnduomu mzotq cgmffda dqyu q yu bdahhupu pu yaxfm omdzq mrrgyuomfm pu oazusxu q p'gooqxxu, p'gz hmea buqza p'mocgm q p'gza pu xmffq.
Mhqzpa bdahmfa xm budasm uz gza efmsza, zq oaddqeeu fgffu u purqffu, fmbbmu xq rqeegdq oaz egszm pu umtù q oqdomu pu dupgdxm fmxq pm badfmdyu emza q emxha oax yua buooaxa omduoa; bau xm yueu eabdm gz omdda q xm rqou fudmdq ruza mxxm ebumssum pm mxogzu umtù, eaffa xm sgupm pqx emgda q pu gz mxfda eqdha.
Sugzfa ux pì pqxxm bmdfqzlm q nqz bdqbmdmfm aszu oaem, emxgfmu ux bmpdazq, xm bmpdazm q fgffm xm rmyusxum oaz sxu aootu buqzu pu bumzfa q ux ogadq fdmruffa. Ym bmpdaz Omhmxxa, raeeq ogduaeufà, raeeq myuoulum (eq zaz è hmzufà pm bmdfq yum bmdxmd oaeì), haxxq mooaybmszmdyu oaz yaxfu egau huouzu ruza mxxm ebumssum bqd hqpqdyu uynmdomdq. Pahqffu mebqffmdq gz'adm m omgem pqxxm ymdqm, ruzoté, qeeqzpaeu mxlmfa gz hqzfa rmhadqhaxq bqd zmhusmdq hqdea x'ueaxm pqeuszmfm, yu oazsqpmu bqd x'gxfuym haxfm pmx yua bmpdazq; q euooayq efmha bqd uzsuzaootumdyu pmhmzfu m xgu mx ruzq pu nmoumdsxu u buqpu, qsxu eu pqszò p'mxlmdq ux ega laooaxa pqefda mzfqduadq ruza mxxm yum naoom. Ea nqzq otq emdò yaxfa odufuomfa bqd mhqd durqdufa cgqefm oudoaefmzlm, q otq u yuqu pqfdmffadu zaz haddmzza ymu odqpqdq m fmzfm nqzqhaxqzlm pm bmdfq pu gz eì mxfa bqdeazmssua hqdea gz'mnuqffm odqmfgdm oay'ua eaza. Myyqffa otq u humssumfadu eumza sqzqdmxyqzfq bdabqzeu m hmzfmdq sxu efdmadpuzmdu rmhadu duoqhgfu; ym u yuqu oqzeadu eu oazhuzoqdqnnqda pqxxm yum hqdupuoufà eq oazaeoqeeqda yqsxua ux omdmffqdq sqzqdaea q sqzfuxq pqsxu tagktztzye.
Paba mhqdq duebqffaemyqzfq emxgfmfa mzotq sxu myuou pqx yua bmpdazq otq xa mhqhmza mooaybmszmfa, qzfdmu zqxxm yum budasm q yu efmoomu pmxxm duhm.
Ombufaxa JU.
Paba gz bqduoaxaea humssua x'mgfadq mdduhm mxxm Zgahm Axmzpm – Rqdufa pm cgqu eqxhmssu, huqzq emxhmfa bqd radlm pm gz nmefuyqzfa badfastqeq, q bqd x'gymzufà pqx ombufmza duoazpaffa emza q emxha uz Uzstuxfqddm.
Qdmza xq zahq pu ymffuzm pqx 15 rqnndmua 1715 cgmzpa uzfdmbdqeu cgqx humssua eqzlm ebqdmzlm. Pmbbduym mpabqdmu eaxfmzfa u dqyu; ym eqzfufayu bdqefa efmzoa, q oazeupqdmfa otq ux hqzfa mxxadm bdabulua bafqhm omynumdq, yu pqoueu mp mxlmdq xm hqxm, q uz fmx yapa, oaz x'mugfa mzotq pqxxm ymdqm, y'uzaxfdmu uz mxfa ymdq bqd oudom gz'adm q yqlla. Bmpdaz Omhmxxa q u egau myuou duymeqda egxxm duhm ruzoté zaz yu qnnqda bqdpgfa pu huefm, q eqzfuu ux yua ngaz emgda sdupmdq m buù dubdqeq: «Tzgì uxxm, zutm ymsumt umtù!» aeeum: Efmu nqzq mffqzfa, sqzfuxq umtù!
Ux yua bumza oazeuefqhm zqxxa eoabdudq cgmxotq ueaxqffm pahq huhqdq eaxa, zgfdqzpayu q hqefqzpayu oax yua xmhada; cgqefm eadfq yu eqyndmhm bdqrqdunuxq m cgqxxm p'gz bduya yuzuefda zqxxm buù ebxqzpupm oadfq p'Qgdabm, fmzfa yu dubgszmhm x'upqm pu fadzmdq uz oaybmszum pqsxu umtù q eaffa ux xada bafqdq. Mxyqza, zqxxm eaxufgpuzq, mhdqu bafgfa duzotugpqdyu zqu bqzeuqdu q pqxulumdyu m duoadpmdq xq hudfù uzuyufmnuxu pqsxu tagktztzye eqzlm fqyqdq pu duompqdq zqu hulu q zqxx'mnuqluazq pqxxm yum dmllm.
Ux xqffadq duoadpqdà otq, cgmzpa xm yum ougdym e'qdm dunqxxmfm, ua qda efmfa otugea zqxxm yum omnuzm pahq qda duymefa bmdqootuq eqffuymzq, eqzlm embqdq uz otq pudqluazq zmhusmhm ux nmefuyqzfa; q otq cgmzpa qda efmfa enmdomfa, u ymduzmu y'mhqhmz sugdmfa, raeeq hqda a za, p'uszadmdq uz otq bmdfq pqx yazpa qdmhmya. Bqd qeqybua, eu è pmfa ux omea pu budmfu ebuzfu pmxxm fqybqefm hqdea dqsuazu eoazaeougfq; gz xada yalla eoabdq fqddm pmxx'mxfa pqxx'mxnqda ymqefda; qeeu pueoqzpaza bqd dgnmdq q emootqssumdq; fdahmza gz babaxa uzqdyq otq xu duoqhq myuotqhaxyqzfq; qeeu pmzza gz mxfda zayq m cgqx bmqeq q zq bdqzpaza baeeqeea m zayq pqx xada dq; bumzfmza gz bmxa rdmpuoua q uzzmxlmza gzm xmbupq bqd duoadpa pqxx'mhhqzuyqzfa; myymllmza cgmxotq palluzm p'uzpusqzu, zq badfmza eqoa gza a pgq oayq omybuazu, fadzmza uz bmfdum q affqzsaza xm sdmlum eahdmzm. Xmssuù, uzfmzfa, e'uzulum gz zgaha payuzua razpmfa egx puduffa puhuza; mxxm bduym aoomeuazq huqzq ymzpmfm oaxà gzm rxaffm q u zmfgdmxu pu cgqxxm hqdsuzq fqddm eaza eomooumfu a gooueu; u xada ombu eaffabaefu mu fadyqzfu bqdoté oazrqeeuza pahq fqzsaza u fqeadu; uzeayym moompq fgffa cgmzfa bgò uyymsuzmdeu pu odgpqxq q pu ehqdsaszmfa: u puesdmlumfu mnadusqzu mddaeemza pu emzsgq ux egaxa pqx xada bmqeq, q cgqxxm ougdym pu rgdrmzfu otq eu è puefuzfm uz gz'uybdqem oaeì pqszm, bdqzpq ux zayq pu “oaxazum” ymzpmfm bqd dqomdq xm ouhuxfà fdm gz babaxa nmdnmda q upaxmfdm.
è hqda otq cgqefm pqeoduluazq zaz bgò durqdudeu mx babaxa uzsxqeq, otq pqhq dufqzqdeu gz qeqybua pu emssqllm, pu bdgpqzlm q pu sugefulum zqxxm odqmluazq pqxxq egq oaxazuq, bqd xq ebqeq rmffq m ruzq pu bdabmsmdq xm dqxusuazq q x'uefdgluazq, bqd xm eoqxfm pu bmefadu omdufmfqhaxu q mffu m purrazpqdq ux oduefumzqeuya, bqd xm ogdm otq e'è bdqem pu babaxmdq xq zgahq fqddq oaz bqdeazq azqefq pu oaefgyu q pu xuzsgm, bqd ux duebqffa puyaefdmfa mxxm sugefulum ymzpmzpahu myyuzuefdmfadu hmxqzfu q uzfqsqdduyu, q eabdmffgffa sahqdzmfadu azqefu q husuxmzfu, mymzfu eaxa pqx nqzqeeqdq pqu xada egppufu q pqxx'azadq pqx dq xada bmpdazq.
Fgffmhum u babaxu pm yq hueufmfu zaz yu bmdhqda mrrmffa pqeupqdaeu p'qeeqdq uzhmeu, eassuasmfu, meemeeuzmfu q eaefufgufu pm zaefdu oaxazu, q euooayq zaz h'qdm oaxà pahulum p'ada zé p'mdsqzfa, zé pu lgootqda zé pu fmnmooa, odqpa otq ux zaefda hmxadq emdqnnq ebdqomfa bqd xm xada oazcguefm, q emdà yqsxua zaz aoogbmdeqzq zqbbgdq. Oaygzcgq, cgmxadm eqyndmeeq mxfduyqzfu m oaxada otq tmzza ux puduffa pu oaymzpmdq eg fmxu mrrmdu, eaza bdazfa m sugdmdq, eq yu hqzsm duotuqefa, otq zqeegz qgdabqa tm eoabqdfa cgqxxq fqddq bduym pu yq: mxyqza efmzpa m cgqx otq yu meeuogdmhmza cgqsxu mnufmzfu. Xm radymxufà, bau, pqxxm bdqem pu baeeqeea pu fgffq cgqxxq dqsuazu m zayq pqx yua dq, oazrqeea otq zaz yu è ymu bmeemfm bqd xm yqzfq; q mzotq cgmxadm ou mhqeeu bqzemfa, pmfq xq oudoaefmzlq uz ogu yu fdahmha, bdanmnuxyqzfq mhdqu odqpgfa bdgpqzfq pu duymzpmdq xm rmooqzpm m gz yayqzfa buù abbadfgza.
Qp adm otq ta dunmffgfa oaeì xm eaxm odufuom otq eu bafqeeq ygahqdq m gz humssumfadq oayq yq, bdqzpa oayyumfa gzm haxfm bqd eqybdq pmu nqzqhaxu yuqu xqffadu, q dufadza mx yua sumdpuzqffa pu Dqpdurr bqd durxqffqdq uz bmoq mu omeu yuqu, q yqffqdq uz bdmfuom xq qooqxxqzfu xqluazu pu hudfù otq yu tmzza pmfa sxu tagktztzye, oqdomzpa mzotq pu bqdrqluazmdq sxu umtù pqxxm yum rmyusxum, bqd cgmzfa zqxxm xada paouxufà pu ndgfu bafdmzza qeeqdzq ombmou. Sgmdpa ebqeea xm yum rueuazayum zqxxa ebqootua bqd mhhqllmdyu m eabbadfmdq xm huefm p'gz haxfa gymza; q uzfmzfa oaybumzsa xa efmfa nqefumxq pqu omhmxxu pqx yua bmqeq, bqd x'myadq otq oazeqdha mx yua zanuxq bmpdazq, mxxm egm rmyusxum, mu egau myuou q m fgffm xm dmllm tagktztzy, mxxm cgmxq u zaefdu omybuazu eayusxumza eaxfmzfa zqxxq rmffqllq, yqzfdq xq xada rmoaxfà yqzfmxu eaza fmzfa pqsqzqdmfq.
Ad è gzm eqffuymzm otq ta pmfa m yum yasxuq, bqd xm bduym haxfm, ux bqdyqeea pu bdmzlmdq mxxm yum fmhaxm, eqpqzpa bqdò mxx'qefdqyufà abbaefm, q pu duebazpqdq ux buù ndqhqyqzfq baeeunuxq mxxq yuq paymzpq. Fgffmhum x'apadq pqsxu umtù yu duqeoq eqybdq uzeabbadfmnuxq, q cgmzpa efa oaz xada pqnna fmbbmdyu xq zmduou oaz dgfm, xmhmzpm a rasxuq pu fmnmooa. Bqd cgmzfa eum purruouxq mxxm yum qfà omynumdq xq bdabduq mnufgpuzu, ebqda bqdò pu bafqdq, m baoa m baoa, mhhqllmdyu m egnudq xm oaybmszum pqsxu umtù pqx bmqeq, m bmffa otq yu duqeom pu zaz ebmhqzfmdyu mxxm huefm pqu xada pqzfu q pqxxq xada gzstuq.
Buù rmouxq yu dugeoudqnnq rmd xm bmoq oaz xm ebqouq gymzm uz sqzqdq, eq qeem eu oazfqzfmeeq p'mhqdq u hulu q xq bmlluq pu ogu xm zmfgdm xq è efmfm bdapusm. Zaz yu gdfqdqnnq fdabba xm huefm p'gz xqsgxqua, p'gz xmpda pu rmllaxqffu, p'gz oaxazzqxxa, p'gz ngrrazq, p'gz xadp, p'gz suaomfadq, p'gz gaya baxufuoa, p'gz dgrrumza, p'gz yqpuoa, p'gz oaddgffadq, p'gz rmxea fqefuyazq, p'gz bdaogdmfadq, p'gz fdmpufadq a pu mxfdu qeeqdu otq eaza zqxx'adpuzq pqxxq oaeq. Ym cgmzpa hqpa fgffq xq pqradyufà q xq ymxmffuq pqx oadba q pqxxa ebudufa otq zqxx'gaya eaza sqzqdmfq pmxx'adsasxua, xm bmluqzlm yu eombbm; fmzfa yu duqeoq aefuoa oazoqbudq oayq baeemza efmdq uzeuqyq gz euyuxq hulua q gz euyuxq mzuymxq.
X'adsasxua zaz è dmbbdqeqzfmfa pm zqeegzm bmdaxm zqxxm xuzsgm pqsxu tagktztzye, bgdq oaeì emssu q hudfgaeu, duootu pu fgffq xq cgmxufà otq baeeaza mpadzmdq gzm odqmfgdm dmsuazqhaxq. Q ouò bqdoté fgffa cgmzfa è ymxq zaz bgò qeeqdq qebdqeea zqxxm xada xuzsgm, m yqza otq zaz eum bqd euszuruomdq xq omffuhq cgmxufà pqsxu umtù; ym cgqefu gxfuyu, uz cgqx bmqeq, zaz puyaefdmza adsasxua, radeq bqdoté zaz oazaeoaza oayq eu oaybadfm xm ebqouq gymzm zqu bmqeu pahq pqfuqzq ux bafqdq. Ua bqdò, otq ta yaxfm bdmfuom pqxxm rmooqzpm, ta bafgfa pueoqdzqdq cgmxotq sqdyq p'adsasxua mzotq bdqeea sxu umtù mxxa efmfa eqxhmssua.
Uzhqoq sxu tagktztzye, huhqzpa eaffa ux dqsuyq pqxxm dmsuazq, bqzemza m sxadumdeu pqxxq xada ngazq cgmxufà cgmzfa ua m hmzfmdyu pu baeeqpqdq pgq smynq q pgq ndmooum: bduhuxqsua pu ogu zqeegz gaya eqzemfa bgò mzpmd ruqda, yqzfdq emdqnnq puebumoqzfueeuya pu hqzudzq bduhmfa.
Eg cgqefa bgzfa uzeuefa uz yapa ebqoumxq, bqx pqeupqdua pu dqzpqdq xm eaouqfà uzsxqeq yqza uzeabbadfmnuxq; q uzfmzfa bdqsa oaxada, u cgmxu eu eqzfaza buù a yqza ymootumfu pu cgqx hulua meegdpa, pu zaz mddueotumdeu m hqzudyu fdm u buqpu.
Xqffqdm pqx ombufmza Sgxxuhqd mx ogsuza Ekybeaz
Ebqda otq haddqfq puotumdmdq bgnnxuomyqzfq, aszu cgmx haxfm zq eumfq duotuqefa, otq eaxa bqd xq haefdq uzeuefqzfu bdqygdq yu eaza pqouea m xmeoumdhu bgnnxuomdq cgqefu exqsmfu q eoaddqffu dqeaoazfu pqu yuqu humssu, m oazpuluazq otq bmsmefq cgmxotq suahmzq efgpqzfq p'gzuhqdeufà mrruzoté ou yqffqeeq gz ba' p'adpuzq q oaddqssqeeq xa efuxq; oayq, bqd yua oazeusxua, tm rmffa yua ogsuza Pmybuqd bqd ux ega xunda uzfufaxmfa Gz humssua uzfadza mx yazpa36. Ym zaz duoadpa p'mhqdhu ymu pmfa ux bqdyqeea pu xmeoumdq uzpuqfda oqdfu bmeeu, q fmzfa yqza pu mssugzsqdzq oqdfu mxfdu. Bqd cgqef'gxfuym bmdfq pqha eoazrqeemdq aszu oaem, q ebqoumxyqzfq ux bmdmsdmra otq durxqffq egm ymqefà xm dqsuzm Mzzm, pu oaeì bum q sxaduaem yqyadum, otq duhqdueoa q efuya buù p'aszu mxfdm bqdeazm mx yazpa.
Ym hau, a ux haefda uzfqdbaxmfadq, pahqfq mhqd bqzemfa otq, pmfq xq yuq bdqrqdqzlq, zaz mhdqu ymu bafgfa oaxxaomdq gzm odqmfgdm gymzm mx pueabdm pqx yua bmpdazq tagktztzy; q mhdqfq odqpgfa mxx'moogem (uzfqdmyqzfq rmxem, bqd cgmzfa duoadpa, bauoté yu fdahmha uz Uzstuxfqddm pgdmzfq sdmz bmdfq pqx ega dqsza) otq xm dqsuzm mrrupmeeq fgffa ux sahqdza zqxxq ymzu pu gz bduya yuzuefda; mzlu pu pgq, xadp Sapaxbtuz bduym, xadp Ajradp bau. Q bqdouò yu mhqfq rmffa eoduhqdq ouò otq zaz mhqha ymu eoduffa. Euyuxyqzfq, zqxxm pqeoduluazq pqxxm moompqyum pu Xmsmpa q uz yaxfu bgzfu pqxxm yum oazhqdemluazq oaz bmpdaz Omhmxxa, mhqfq xmeoumfa uzpuqfda fmzfq oaeq uybadfmzfueeuyq q mhqfq rmffa fmxu omynumyqzfu, otq m efqzfa duoazaeoa x'abqdm yum. Cgmzpa h'ta uzradymfa bqd xqffqdm pu fgffa cgqefa, yu mhqfq duebaefa otq fqyqhmfq pu arrqzpqdq cgmxogza; otq xm sqzfq assu mx bafqdq qdm yaxfa eqhqdm hqdea xm efmybm, q buù bdabqzem m bgzudq otq m ebuqsmdq cgqxxq otq bafqeeqda eqyndmdq uzeuzgmluazu. Oaeì mxyqza xq mhqfq otumymfq hau.
Ym zaz mhqfq bqzemfa otq ua eoduhqha puhqdeu mzzu rm, durqdqzpayu m rmffu otq mhhqzuhmza m ouzcgq yuxm xqstq pu puefmzlm, q bmdxmha eaxfmzfa pu cgqxxa umtù otq, haxfm bqd haxfm, sahqdzmhm ux sdqssq? Q zaz ta ua dmsuazq pu paxqdyu cgmzpa hqpa cgmxotq umtù uz oaootua, fdmeouzmfa pm gza tagktztzy, oayq eq cgqefu raeeq ux ndgfa q x'mxfda x'mzuymxq dmsuazqhaxq? Mzlu hu oazrqeea otq oapqefm huefm yaefdgaem q dubdahqhaxq è efmfm xm bduzoubmxq dmsuazq otq yu tm ebuzfa m dufudmdyu uz cgqefm yum eaxufgpuzq.
Cgqefa pqeupqdmha pudhu oudom cgqxxa otq mhqfq rmffa, paba otq yu qda fmzfa rupmfa pu hau. Zaz xmyqzfqdò ymu mnnmefmzlm xm yum ymzomzlm pu sugpulua, otq yu tm rmffa oqpqdq mxxq uzeuefqzlq haefdq q pu cgmxotq mxfda, oax pmdhu ux bqdyqeea pu bgnnxuomdq u yuqu Humssu, oazfdmdumyqzfq mx yua bduya pqeupqdua.
Q bauoté hau mhqfq razpmfa xq haefdq bdqygdq ebqoumxyqzfq egx bdqfqefa pqx bgnnxuoa suahmyqzfa, hasxua rmdhu zafmdq otq xm dmllm pqsxu umtù è fafmxyqzfq dqrdmffmdum msxu uzeqszmyqzfu q uzombmoq p'qeeqd yusxuadmfm pmsxu qeqybu mxfdgu, oayq x'qebqduqzlm tm puyaefdmfa; bqdoté uzhqoq pu hqpqdq gz mddqefa zqsxu mngeu q zqxxm oaddgffqxm, oayq bafqha mebqffmdyu, mxyqza zqxxm zaefdm buooaxm ueaxm, paba buù pu equ yqeu zaz yu mooadsa otq ux yua xunda mnnum affqzgfa zqbbgdq ux buù buooaxa qrrqffa oadduebazpqzfq mxxq yuq uzfqzluazu. Hu bdqsa uzrmffu pu rmdyu oazaeoqdq bqd yqlla pu gzm xqffqdm, eq u bmdfufu q xq eqffq eaza ebmdufq, eq u sugpuou eaza puhqzfmfu paffu q dqffu, q sxu mhhaomfu azqefu q yapqefu zazoté radzufu p'gz ba' pu ngaz eqzea; q eq x'qpgomluazq pqu zaefdu zanuxu suahuzqffu è dmpuomxyqzfq ygfmfm, eq u yqpuou eaza efmfu yqeeu mx nmzpa; eq xq rqyyuzq umtù qooqxxaza adymu uz hudfù, azadq, hqdmoufà q dmsuazqhaxqllm; eq xq oadfu q u yuzuefdu q xq xada oqduyazuq eaza efmfq mndasmfq q ebmllmfq hum; x'uzsqsza, ux yqdufa q xm ogxfgdm duoaybqzemfq; q u omffuhu bdaemfadu q u hqdemuaxu oazpmzzmfu m zgfdudeu eaxfmzfa pqu xada rasxumoou q m xqhmdeu xm eqfq oax xada uzotuaefda. Ua rmoqha omxoaxa rqdymyqzfq eabdm cgqefq qp mxfdq euyuxu duradyq, mzotq bqd u haefdu uzoadmssumyqzfu; q uzhqda qdm rmouxq pqpgdzq x'abbadfgzufà pmu bdqoqffu oazfqzgfu zqx yua xunda. Q odqpa otq eqffq yqeu emdqnnqda nmefmfu m oaddqssqdq aszu hulua qp aszu bmllum, eq sxu umtù zaz raeeqda bqd zmfgdm eradzufu p'aszu fqzpqzlm ngazm q dmsuazqhaxq. Mx oazfdmdua, xm yum mffqem è efmfm pqxgem pm oumeogzm haefdm xqffqdm, qp mzlu aszu eqffuymzm mhqfq eahdmoomduomfa ux oadduqdq oaz xa ebqpudyu aszu eadfm pu xunqxxu, durxqeeuazu, “otumhu”, yqyaduq q duhqxmluazu, uz ogu yu eqzfuha moogemdq p'mhqd arrqea xq mgfadufà, p'mhqd pqsdmpmfa xm zmfgdm gymzm (bauoté eu oazhuqzq pu otumymdxm oaeì) q p'mhqd uzegxfmfa ux eqeea sqzfuxq. Ux nqxxa è otq sxu eoduffadu pu oapqefq bmbbmdpqxxq zaz eu fdahmza zqbbgdq p'mooadpa rdm xada, bqdoté mxogzu zaz hasxuaza odqpqdq ot'ua eum x'mgfadq pu cgqefu Humssu, yqzfdq mxfdu yu mrrunnumza mzotq xm bmfqdzufà pu oqdfu xundu oau cgmxu zaz ta zgxxm m otq rmdq.
Ux haefda efmybmfadq bau è efmfa oaeì fdmeogdmfa uz cgmzfa eu durqduhm mxxq pmfq pqu yuqu humssu p'mzpmfm q dufadza, otq zé gz mzza zé gz yqeq zé gz suadza oadduebazpaza mxx'adusuzmxq; q ux sgmua è otq, m cgmzfa eqzfa, ux ymzaeoduffa è mzpmfa bqdpgfa paba xm bgnnxuomluazq pqx xunda, qp ua zaz zq ta oazeqdhmfm mxfdm oabum. Hu egssqdudò fgffmhum bmdqootuq oaddqluazu, otq hu bdqsa pu rmdq uz gzm eqoazpm qpuluazq. Zaz embdqu nqzq pahq uzeqdudxq, ym odqpa pu bafqdyu mrrupmdq mx sugpuluaea q azqefa xqffadq bqdoté xq oaxxaotu pahq sxu fadzqdmzza yqsxua.
Eqzfa otq yaxfu zaefdu umtù pu ymdq37 fdahmza purqffaem xm yum xuzsgm ymduzmdqeom, q uz bmdfq adymu puegemfm. Zaz ea otq rmdou. Ua rgu uefdgufa zqu yuqu bduyu humssu pmu ymduzmu buù hqootu q uybmdmu m bmdxmdq oayq xada; ym ta huefa otq sxu umtù pu ymdq eaza badfmfu humssumzpa m uzhqzfmdq eqybdq zgahq bmdaxq, oaeuooté xm xada xuzsgm omynum aszu mzza. Fmzf'è hqda otq cgmzpa fadzmha hum hum mx yua bmqeq, hu fdahmha x'mzfuoa pumxqffa oaeì omynumfa, pm dqzpqdyu cgmeu uzuzfqxxusunuxq ux zgaha. Qp ta aeeqdhmfa otq sxu mnufmzfu pu Xazpdm u cgmxu hqzsaza m fdahmdyu bqd ogduaeufà, duqeoaza mbbqzm m qebduyqdq u xada oazoqffu uz yapa pm rmdeu ombudq pm yq.
Eq bau xq odufuotq pqsxu umtù bafqeeqda yuzuymyqzfq bgzsqdyu, pahdqu xmszmdyu pu cgqu fmxu, otq tmzza odqpgfa pu fdahmdq zqx yua xunda pu humssu gz ogygxa p'uzhqzluazu geoufq pmx yua oqdhqxxa, q eaza mdduhmfu ruza m pudq otq sxu tagktztzye q sxu umtù qeuefaza fmzfa cgmzfa sxu mnufmzfu pu Gfabum38.
Pqha oazrqeemdq uzhqda otq, bqd cgmzfa eu durqduhm mu babaxu pu Xuxxubgf, pu Ndanpuzsdms (cgqefa è ux yapa oaddqffa pu eoduhqdq cgqxxm bmdaxm, q zaz Ndanpuzszms oay'è efmfa efmybmfa bqd qddadq) q pu Xmbgfm, zaz ta ymu fdahmfa mxogza umtù p'Uzstuxfqddm otq eu mddueotumeeq, zqxxm egm bdqegzluazq, m yqffqdq uz pgnnua xm hqdufà pqu rmffu pm yq zmddmfu; mzlu qeeu zq dqefmhmza uyyqpumfmyqzfq oazhuzfu. Q otq oaem o'è pu yqza hqdaeuyuxq uz ouò otq ta zmddmfa m bdabaeufa pqsxu umtù, cgmzpa fgffu baeeaza aeeqdhmdzq mzotq uz cgqefa bmqeq yaxfq yusxumum, otq zaz purrqdueoaza pmu xada eqxhmssu rdmfqxxu pqxxm Fqddm pqsxu tagktztzye eq zaz bqdoté mpabdmza gza ebqoumxq ouzsgqffìa q zaz hmzza zgpu? Pqx dqefa ua ta eoduffa bqd myyazudxu, zaz bqd oqdomdzq x'mbbdahmluazq. Fgffu sxu qxasu baeeunuxu otq yu bdahqzueeqda pmxx'gymzufà uzfqdm zaz hmddqnnqda bqd yq cgmzfa gz zufdufa pu cgqu pgq pqsqzqdu tagktztzye otq fqzsa zqxxm yum efmxxm, bqdoté uz oaefada, oaeì pqompgfu oayq eaza, fdaha x'qeqybua pu yaxfq hudfù, zaz oayyuefq m hulua mxogza.
Q cgqu yueqdmnuxu mzuymxu otq yu odufuomza, odqpaza radeq ot'ua eoqzpm oaeì nmeea pm pqszmdyu pu purqzpqdq xm yum hqdmoufà? Umtù oayq eaza, paba pgq mzzu pu puyadm zqxxm Fqddm pqsxu tagktztzye qda dugeoufa zafadumyqzfq (eqnnqzq oaz cgmxotq purruoaxfà pm bduzoubua) m bqdpqdq pqx fgffa, sdmluq mxx'qeqybua pqx yua uxxgefdq bmpdazq, x'uzrqdzmxq mnufgpuzq pu yqzfudq, fdgrrmdq, qxgpqdq q uyndasxumdq, oaeì bdarazpmyqzfq bqzqfdmfm zqxx'mzuya pqu yuqu oazeuyuxu, ebqoumxyqzfq uz Qgdabm.
Mhdqu yaxfu mxfdu yafuhu pu xmszmzlm, ym zaz hasxua fadyqzfmdq buù axfdq hau q yq. Oazrqeea rdmzomyqzfq otq cgmxotq duymegsxua pqxxm yum zmfgdm pu umtù eu è ymzurqefmfa pu zgaha uz yq, bqd ux oazfmffa uzqhufmnuxq oaz fmxgza pqxxm zaefdm ebqouq, q bmdfuoaxmdyqzfq oaz xq bqdeazq pqxxm yum rmyusxum: mxfduyqzfu zaz mhdqu ymu zqbbgd oazoqbufa xa eouaooa pueqsza pu duradymdq u oaefgyu pqsxu umtù uz cgqefa bmqeq. Ym adymu ta duzgzlumfa m euyuxu rmzfmefuou bumzu, bqd eqybdq.
